MAT 1:1 Ikkaan tettaenin rhaepeton Jesus Kristus, iiy erhaep saengi David, iwe nge David erhaep saengi Abraham.
MAT 1:2 Nge Abraham semaen Isaac, nge Isaac semaen Jacob, nge Jacob semaen Judah me mwaaen kkewe pwiin.
MAT 1:3 Nge Judah semaen Peres me Zerah (itaen ineer nge Tamar), iwe nge Peres semaen Hezron, nge Hezron semaen Ram.
MAT 1:4 Nge Ram semaen Amminadab, nge Amminadab semaen Nahshon, nge Nahshon semaen Salmon.
MAT 1:5 Nge Salmon semaen Boaz (itaen inan nge Rahab), nge Boaz semaen Obed (itaen inan nge Ruth), nge Obed semaen Jesse,
MAT 1:6 nge Jesse semaen king David. Nge David semaen Solomon, iwe e naini me wooan niewe pwiuniuwaen Uriah,
MAT 1:7 nge Solomon semaen Rehoboam, nge Rehoboam semaen Abijah, nge Abijah semaen Asa.
MAT 1:8 Nge Asa semaen Jehoshaphat, nge Jehoshaphat semaen Jehoram, nge Jehoram semaen Uzziah.
MAT 1:9 Nge Uzziah semaen Jotham, nge Jotham semaen Ahaz, nge Ahaz semaen Hezekiah.
MAT 1:10 Nge Hezekiah semaen Manasseh, nge Manasseh semaen Amon, nge Amon semaen Josiah.
MAT 1:11 Nge Josiah semaen Jehoiachin me mwaaen kkewe pwiin ikkiwe re asiiur nong noan Babylon.
MAT 1:12 Mwirin aar asiiur noa Babylon: Jehoiachin semaen Shealtiel, nge Shealtiel semaen Zerubbabel.
MAT 1:13 Zerubbabel semaen Abiud, Abiud semaen Eliakim, nge Eliakim semaen Azor.
MAT 1:14 Azor semaen Zadok, Zadok semaen Achim, nge Achim semaen Eliud.
MAT 1:15 Eliud semaen Eleazar, Eleazar semaen Matthan, nge Matthan semaen Jacob.
MAT 1:16 Jacob semaen Joseph iwe pwiuniuwaen Maria, niewe a nainitiw Jesus iwe re faingi pwe Kristus.
MAT 1:17 Seig me faawu saeren aeremas saengi Abraham ngaeni David, pwan seig me faawu saeren aeremas saengi David ngaeni oaton aar asiiur noa noan Babylon, pwan seig me faawu saeren aeremas saengi oaton we re asiiur noa Babylon ngaeni wupwutiwen Kristus.
MAT 1:18 Ieen wunuunun aaen Jesus Kristus wupwutiw. Maria we inan a kkefoat ngaeni Joseph, nge igiwe resaaen pwiuppwiuniuw mwo nge a pwae pwe niewe a pwoopwo reen kkemenaen Espritu Santus.
MAT 1:19 Nge Joseph erhai mwaaen wenewen, ese mwerhaen aessaewa Maria me weni mmweer aeremas, iwe a niunniuwaennei epwene siusaengi, nge epwe feeori rhag noan mwoanomwoan.
MAT 1:20 Igiwe e rhiuwen niunniuwaennei wunuunun, erhai naiun Soamwoon angkenus a pwae ngaeni noan aan ttan nge a aengaeni pwe, “Joseph we tettaenin David, wosoapw mesag oamw wopwe pwiuniuwaeni Maria, pwe iiy a pwoopwo reen kkemenaen Espritu Santus.
MAT 1:21 Epwene naini erhai aetemwaaen, iwe wopwe aeita ngaeni Jesus, pwe iga iiy epwe aemenewaar naiun aeremas saengi aar monofit.”
MAT 1:22 A wen oanongaen minikkeei pwe epwe pwaeritae meeta we profeta a aepesa pwe mwaeniaei Soamwoon:
MAT 1:23 “Erhai aeterhooapwut epwene pwoopwo nge a naini erhai aetemwaaen, repwe aeitae ngaeni Immanuel”, (wewen nge “Deus eno reerh”).
MAT 1:24 Iwe oatowe Joseph a mmasetae, a feeori wunuunun miniwe angkenus we naiun Soamwoon e aepesa ngaeni. Iwe a pwiuniuwaeni Maria.
MAT 1:25 Nge Joseph ese maiur ngaeni Maria toori aan nainitiw aetewe naiun. Iwe, Joseph a aeita aetewe pwe Jesus.
MAT 2:1 Iwe, Jesus a wupwutiw noan Bethlehem we aepinoamwon Judea wene mweoiun king Erotes. Ese ssiunaei mwo mwirin, nge aaemweoi mwaaen saengi faniuwaen eotiw re metefaaegini wunuunun fiiu ra itto Jerusalem.
MAT 2:2 Ra aeiineo pwe, “Iya iga eno king we aar re Jews ee iwe a supw? Aeiweri taetaen fiiu we aeginnen aan ittae me eotiw. Iwe aeiya itto pwe aeipwe aesirowu.”
MAT 2:3 Oatowe king Erotes a rongorong iiy kkepas we, a toagun aenneew noa nee tipan, pwan oanongeer noa rhooan Jerusalem.
MAT 2:4 A faingiir oanongeer soamwooniir patere kkewe, me sinsein anniug kkewe nge a aeiineeor aere iya iga Kristus epwe wupwutiw ee.
MAT 2:5 Iwe nge ra iura pwe, “Epwe wupwutiw me noan Bethlehem noan Judea. Pwe ieei wunuunun miniwe profeta we e foatogi pwe:
MAT 2:6 ‘Een Bethlehem noan faniuwaen Judah, wosoapw foakkon sessoan me neeiin taeninimwaei Judah, pwe erhai soamwoon epwe toowow saengiug, epwe nemaeni naeyi re Israel.’ ”
MAT 2:7 Iwe Erotes a faingiir rhooan emwaamw kkewe re ittiw me eotiw pwe repwe sseoiu noan mwoanomwoan. Iwe Erotes a aeiineo firhiir oaton taetaen fiiu we.
MAT 2:8 Mwirin nge a aefengaar noa Bethlehem nge a aetiwenig ngaeniir pwe, “Oawpwe noa giutta firhiy iiy aetena. Nge aere oawwa weri, oawwa aengaeniaei, pwe ngaang ipwe pwan noa aesirowu.”
MAT 2:9 Mwirin aaen king we kkepas ngaeniir iwe nge ra noa. Iwe, oatowe re feffaaeraeg noa, ra pwan weri sefaaeniy fiiu we reweri mwo me eotiw, nge a gommw noa memmweer a noa iugiu noa me wooan iimw we aetewe eno ee.
MAT 2:10 Oatowe reweri fiiu we nge ra igin kker.
MAT 2:11 Iwe, ra toonong noan iimw we nge ra weri aetewe me Maria iwe inan, iwe ra foatotiw me mmwan nge ra aesirowu. Mwirin ra iseni tiw niffang kkewe aar: gold, frankincense me myrrh iwe ra fang ngaeni.
MAT 2:12 Iwe, Deus a kkepas ngaeniir noan aar ttan, pwe resoapw sefaaeniti Erotes, ina minne ra sefaaeniti faniuweer wooan eew noa aan.
MAT 2:13 Mwiriir rhooan emwaamw kkewe ra noa, nge erhai naiun Soamwoon angkenus a pwae ngaeni Joseph noan aan ttan nge a aengaeni pwe, “Erotes imwu e giutta aetena pwe epwe niiy noa. Rhimwitae wopwe pwigi aetena me niemwu inan nge oawwa kkewaeg noa Egypt. Oawpwe noa no iginaan toori oatona ipwe aengaeniug pwe oawpwene sefaaen.”
MAT 2:14 Iwe, Joseph a rhimwitae noan rhag pwongin we iwe a pwigi aetewe me niewe inan nge ra kkewaeg noa Egypt.
MAT 2:15 Ra noa no Egypt toori aaen Erotes mae noa. A wen minneei pwe epwe nnet miniwe profeta a aepesa pwe mwaeniaen Soamwoon, “Iya faingiwow mwaaen na Naeyi saengi Egypt.”
MAT 2:16 Oatowe Erotes enoa giuneei noa pwe rhooawe re ittiw me eotiw re oatupwu, nge a igin soong. Iwe, a akkiuneo pwe repwe niir noa oanongeer aetemwaaen kka a ruwowu raegiir aere wonigaet tiw me faar me noan Bethlehem me niugiun Bethlehem. A feeori minneei, pwe e ayiureoyiura ngaeni oaton taetaen fiiu we a giuneei saengiir rhooawe re ittiw me eotiw.
MAT 2:17 A wen minneei pwe epwe pwaeritae miniwe profeta Jeremiah e aepesa pwe:
MAT 2:18 “Aeremas ra rongorong mweireirei saeng me noan Ramah. Rachel a saengitiir aetekkewe naiun. Iwe esa rhipino, pwe naiun ra maenoa.”
MAT 2:19 Mwirin aaen Erotes maenoa, erhai naiun Soamwoon angkenus a pwae ngaeni Joseph noan aan ttan me Egypt
MAT 2:20 nge a aengaeni pwe, “Wopwe rhimwitae nge wa pwigi aetena me niemwu inan iwe, oawwa sefaaen noa wooan faniuwaen Israel, pwe rhooawe re niunniuwaennei repwe niiy noa aetena nge ra maenoa.”
MAT 2:21 Iwe Joseph a rhimwitae, a pwigi aetewe me niewe inan nge ra sefaaeniti Israel.
MAT 2:22 Nge oatowe Joseph a rongorong pwe Archelaus a ssiuweniy king Erotes we seman me noan Judea, iwe a mesag aan epwe noa igiwe. Noan aan ttan, Deus a pwan aetiwenig ngaeni iwe ina minne a noa wooan faniuwaen Galilee reen
MAT 2:23 nge a noa no noan aepinoamw we itan Nazareth. Iwe ieei minne epwe pwaeritae minikkiwe profeta kkewe re aepesa, “Epwe ffai pwe iiy re Nazareth.”
MAT 3:1 Reen oaton naan nge John Baptist a noa noan eew desert me noan Judea iwe a rhaepiy tae aan fenai.
MAT 3:2 Iwe, a iura pwe, “Oawpwe toagun saengi monofitimi, pwe Mweoiu Naaeng a arapeto.”
MAT 3:3 Iiy John miniwe profeta Isaiah e aepesa kkepesan iwe e iura pwe, “Erhai a iyaekkepwas me noan desert: ‘Oawpwe oamoannatae ennepaen Soamwoon; oawpwe awenecchera eew aan pwe epwe faaeraeg wooan.’ ”
MAT 3:4 John e memmengaag mengaag effeeor saengi iunaen camel, nge pwaanto na aan effeeor saengi ginin maan, nge anan mwongo ina manni neeiin waniwan ina nirhiugiunpweon me honey.
MAT 3:5 Aeremas ra maegeto reen saengi Jerusalem me oanongaen pwiuneoi me noan Judea, pwan saengi oanongaen pwiuneoi me niugiun pwupwu we Jordan.
MAT 3:6 Ra pwuwafayiuw noa monofitiir, nge John a paptismusaar noan pwupwu we Jordan.
MAT 3:7 Igiwe John a weriir towunepeer Pharisees me Sadducees kkewe re itto reen pwe epwe paptismusaar, a aengaeniir pwe, “Aaemi sowufaeng! Iyo e aengaenigaemi pwe oawpwe mmwenen kkewaeg saengi aaen Deus aegaeregaer iga epwe aefengato?
MAT 3:8 Oaw ssiuweniy wegitaegimi pwe epwe pwaeri noa pwe oawwa toagun saengi monofitimi.
MAT 3:9 Oawsoapw niunniuwaennei pwe oawwa taaw saengi aaen Deus aegaeregaer reen aaemi aepesa pwe Abraham minne rhaepetomi. Ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe Deus emmwenen feeori faai kaan pwe tettaenin Abraham!
MAT 3:10 Eew soapaen a oamoannatae pwe epwe gopiy tiw waniwan saengi waeran. Oanongaen waniwan kka ese gacch uwaan nge epwe gopogop tiw nge e aekkaerh nong noan aengaet.
MAT 3:11 “Ngaang iya paptismusaegaemi reen rhaan pwe pwaepwaenoan aaemi toagun saengi monofitimi. Iwe nge erhai ina epwe itto me mwiriy epwe paptismusaegaemi reen Espritu Santus me aengaet. Iiy ina e taegias saengiaei, nge ese fin mwo nge aaei ipwe pwigi nokkaan.
MAT 3:12 A kkemwarh aan sepwin pwe epwe aeyimweoiuw fesaenngiy faiun saengi peeon. Iwe, epwe ioni fengaenniy faiun nge a iseni nong noan aan imwaen iseis, nge peeon epwe oatoranong noan aengaet we ese mmwenen gunnoa.”
MAT 3:13 Noan oaton naan nge Jesus a itto me Galilee a itto reen pwupwu we Jordan, pwe John epwe paptismusa.
MAT 3:14 Nge John a menaen epwe ssiuweniy aan niunniuwaen. Iwe, a aengaeni pwe, “Iureoyiureon pwe een wopwe faer paptismusaeyaei, nge meeta een wa faer noa itto reei reen?”
MAT 3:15 Nge, Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Wopwe nigiti noa mwo ina. Pwe igina nge sipwe tapweei mwo oanongaen meeta tipaen Deus.” Iwe John a tipieew ngaeni.
MAT 3:16 Igiwe rhag Jesus a moann me paptismus noa, a teeotae me noan rhaan we. Iwe naaeng a sugaeg ngaeni nge a weri Espritu Santus aan ittiw nge eweei rhag erhai dove a ittiw soatiw wooan.
MAT 3:17 Iwe nge eew mangiungiu a ittiw me noan naaeng a aepesa pwe, “Ieei naeyi mwaaen aerhaengerhaeng, iye efin tipaei reen.”
MAT 4:1 Iwe Espritu a paeninoa Jesus noan desert we pwe epwe noa sessoat me reen Saetan.
MAT 4:2 Nge mwirin aaen Jesus aecchigipin noan faaeig raaen me faaeig pwoong, iwe a meyaefi aan pecchai.
MAT 4:3 Iwe, Saetan we a itto reen nge a aengaeni pwe, “Aere een Naiun Deus, wopwe aengaeniir faai kaan pwe repwe ssiuwen ngaeni fenoawa.”
MAT 4:4 Nge Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Saapw fenoawa rhag minne aeremas repwe menaw reen, pwe re menaw reen oanongaen kkepas kka Deus a aepesa.’ ”
MAT 4:5 Iwe Saetan we a paeninoa Jesus Jerusalem, aepinoamw we e santus, nge a noa aiuwtae pwiuneoi we oarosaen taegias me reen Temple we.
MAT 4:6 Iwe, a aengaeni pwe, “Aere een Naiun Deus, wa oatoroagotiw me igeei, pwe Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Deus epwe akkiuneeor naiun angkenus repwe aemmwenoag. Repwe ammwarhiug tae noan paiiur pwe pirhemw mwo nge ete woas ngaeni faai.’ ”
MAT 4:7 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Pwapwior we e Santus epwan aepesa pwe, ‘Wosoapw soatoni Deus na oamw Soamwoon.’ ”
MAT 4:8 Mwirin Saetan we a pwan paenitae Jesus wooan eew rhug igin taegias nge a pwaeri ngaeni mweoiun feoniufan me oanongaen minikkena nningen.
MAT 4:9 Iwe, a aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Oanongaen minikkeei ipwe ngaenneog, aere wopwe foatotiw me weni mmwaei nge wa oassotupw ngaeniaei.”
MAT 4:10 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Siunoa Saetan! Pwe Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Wopwe oassotupw ngaeni Deus na oamw Soamwoon nge iiy rhag wopwe engaang ngaeni.’ ”
MAT 4:11 Iwe rhag nge Saetan we a siusaengi Jesus, iwe nge angkenus ra itto tipaengi.
MAT 4:12 Igiwe Jesus a rongorong pwe ra iseni nong John noan kanepwus, iiy a noa Galilee.
MAT 4:13 Ese notiw noan Nazareth, pwe a noa no noan Capernaum, eew aepinoamw oaron meoneoiniuniun Galilee noan faniuwaen Zebulun me Naphtali.
MAT 4:14 A feeori minneen pwe epwe nnet miniwe profeta Isaiah e aepesa pwe,
MAT 4:15 “Faniuwaen Zebulun me faniuwaen Naphtali wooan aanna enoa ngaeni eew meoneoiniun, peiginoan pwupwu we Jordan me Galilee, faniuweer rhooawe re Gentiles!
MAT 4:16 Aeremas kkewe reno noan rorhappiung repwene weri eew seram faeregit, nge rhooakkena reno noan rorhappiungiun faniuwaen mae ina eew seram epwene ttinitiw wooar.”
MAT 4:17 Saengi iiy oatowe nge Jesus a rhaepiy tae aan fenai, “Oawpwe toagun saengi monofitimi, pwe Mweoiu Naaeng a arapeto!”
MAT 4:18 Nipwaen aaen Jesus a faaeraeg ngaerhei meoneoiniuniun Galilee, a weriir riiurhai rhooan fita nge re pwipwi, Simon (pwan itan Peter) me Andrew iwe pwiin, rewuug fetaen iig noan iiy meoneoiniun we.
MAT 4:19 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw itto tapweaei pwe ipwe oasuguuna ngaenigaemi wunuunun aaemi oawpwe fita aeremas.”
MAT 4:20 Oatowe rhag nge ra siusaengi wuug kkewe aar nge ra tapweei noa mwirin.
MAT 4:21 Jesus a pwan faaeraeg noa nge a pwan weriir riiurhai mwaaen pwipwi, James me John, ikkiwe naiun Zebedee. Reno wooan pwoot we waar reen mwaaen we semeer Zebedee, re aemmwena wow wuug kkewe aar. Iwe nge Jesus a faingiir.
MAT 4:22 Oatowe rhag nge ra siusaengi pwoot we waar me mwaaen we semeer nge re tapweei noa mwirin.
MAT 4:23 Iwe, Jesus a mwet fetaen wooan oanongaen Galilee, nge e fenai me noan wutteer Jews we nge e fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai we reen Mweoiu Naaeng, me pwan aecchipwaar aeremas kkewe eweriir mesemesaen semwaai.
MAT 4:24 Kkepesaen Jesus a rheeoi noa wooan oanongaen faniuwaen Syria, iwe aeremas ra pweipwog to oanongeer rhooa semwaai reen, rhooakka eweriir mesemesaen semwaai me metaeg, aeremas kka waen aniu, man ngong me aeremas kka re maemerhoar. Iwe, Jesus a aecchipwaar tae oanongeer.
MAT 4:25 Re towunap aeremas kka rettapw mwirin Jesus saengi Galilee me Decapolis, saengi Jerusalem me Judea me faniuw we eno epeig me reen pwupwu we Jordan.
MAT 5:1 Igiwe Jesus a weri pwuwaen aeremas kkewe, iwe a ittae wooan eew rhug a ittae mooat tiw. Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra itto reen.
MAT 5:2 Iwe, Jesus a rhaepetae aan fenai ngaeniir:
MAT 5:3 “Ra wenepwu rhooan giuneei pwe ngeoniiur e affayeo; pwe iir repwe mweoiuni Mweoiu Naaeng.
MAT 5:4 Ra wenepwu rhooa nee tip cchoaw nee tipeer, pwe Deus epwe rhipeer.
MAT 5:5 Ra wenepwu rhooa mesoan, pwe iir repwe faniuwaeni feoniufan.
MAT 5:6 Ra wenepwu rhooan mwerhaen feeori minne epwiung me faaen mesaen Deus, pwe Deus epwe fang ngaeniir minikkena re tipaeni.
MAT 5:7 Ra wenepwu rhooa ffayeo, pwe Deus epwe pwan ffayeo ngaeniir.
MAT 5:8 Ra wenepwu rhooa nimegacch nee tipeer, pwe iir repwe weri Deus.
MAT 5:9 Ra wenepwu rhooan engaengaen oapoas, pwe Deus epwe faingiir pwe iir naiun.
MAT 5:10 Ra wenepwu rhooa aewwaeiraes reen aar feeori nee tipaen Deus, pwe iir repwe mweoiuni Mweoiu Naaeng.
MAT 5:11 “Oaw wenepwu aaemi rhooana re ffeeoretae kkepesaemi, nge re aewwaeiraesigaemi, me aepesa aenneewagaemi pwe aegin ngaang.
MAT 5:12 Oawkker nge a mwamwaai nee tipaemi, pwe a yor paniuwaemi ina e igin faeregit me naaeng. Pwe ieei wunuunun aar pwan aewwaeiraesiir profeta kkewe regommw me mmwaemi.
MAT 5:13 “Aaemi oawwa taeppen rhag aesiig faaen iteer aeremesaen feoniufan. Pwe aere aesiig esa saaet no, esoapw mmwen sipwe aesaaeti sefaaeniy. Iwe esa yor no ipitan, epwe aekkaerh wow pwe aeremas repwe pwuri fetaeneei.
MAT 5:14 “Aaemi seremaen feoniufan. Eew aepinoamw ne eno wooan eew rhug esoapw mmwenen mwoanonoa.
MAT 5:15 Esooar erhai aeremas ne epwe figi eew oappwun nge a iseni nong faaen eew saepiy, pwe epwe faer iseni tae wooan nenien, pwe epwe aesseremaar rhooan iimw we.
MAT 5:16 Epwe ieei wunuunun seremaemi aan epwe ttin memmweer aeremas, pwe repwe giuneei aaemi wegitaeg mwamwaai iwe nge re aepingepinga Semaemi me wooai naaeng.
MAT 5:17 “Oawsoapw niunniuwaennei pwe iya itto pwe ipwe oamoai noa Anniug kkewe aaen Moses me aar profeta kkewe kkepesaen fenai. Ngaang ise itto pwe ipwe itto oamoai noa, pwe ifaer itto pwe ipwe pwaeritae minna wenewenen.
MAT 5:18 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe epat mwo aere efai mwo iirh me reen anniug eei nge esoapw aekkaerh noa toori aan toarop noa naaeng me soanop pwan toori aan epwe moann oanongaen meeta.
MAT 5:19 Iwe, ngaere erhai ese tapweei mwo nge eew anniug mwittig kkeei nge e oasuguuna ngaeniir aaemweoi pwe repwe pwan taeppen iiy, iiy epwe igin sessoan me noan Mweoiu Naaeng. Ngaere erhai epwe tapweei iiy anniug kkeei nge e oasuguuna ngaeniir aaemweoi pwe repwe pwan taeppen iiy, iiy epwe taegias me noan Mweoiu Naaeng.
MAT 5:20 Ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe aaemi oawpwe mmwenen toonong rhag noan Mweoiu Naaeng igine aaemi e mwamwaai wegitaegimi saengiir sinsein anniug me Pharisees kkewe.
MAT 5:21 “Oawwa rongorong aar aengaeniir aeremesaen mweoiwe pwe, ‘Wosoapw nni menaw aeremas. Iyo enni menaw aeremas epwe toonong noan nenien apwiung.’
MAT 5:22 Nge ngaang ipwene aengaenigaemi: iyo e esoong ngaeni pwiin nge epwe noa noan nenien apwiung, nge iyo e aengaeni pwiin pwe, ‘Een esooar ipitoamw,’ epwe noa noan nenien apwiung na e taegias, nge iyo e aengaeni pwiin pwe, ‘Een wopwurh,’ nge epwe noa noan aengaetaen nifierno.
MAT 5:23 Iwe aere wopwe pwigitae oamw oasoar ngaeni Deus wooan antar, nge a maeng ngaeniug pwe pwiimw ecchoaw tipan woamw,
MAT 5:24 wa nigiti mwo oasoar we oamw weni mmwan antar nge wa sefaaen, pwe oawpwe oamwusomwus fengaen. Mwirin wa sefaaeneto pwigitae oasoar we oamw ngaeni Deus.
MAT 5:25 “Aere erhai a mwerhaen pwigiug noa noan nenien apwiung, wopwe mwetekkaein saeneti ffin nipwaen iga e rhiuwen yor oaton, weni mmwaen iga wopwe toori nenien apwiung. Pwe oatona wopwe toori rhag nenien apwiung, ina nge een wopwene noa reen soaw apwiung we, nge iiy epwene aefengoag noa nee paiiur police, nge iir repwene iseniug nong noan kanepwus.
MAT 5:26 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe iginaan iga wopwe noa no e toori oamw wopwe piungiutiw oanongaen paniuwaen monofitimw.
MAT 5:27 “Oawwa rongorong pwe re aepesa pwe, ‘Wosoapw maiur ngaeni pwiuniuwaen erhai.’
MAT 5:28 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe: aere erhai mwaaen a pipiiy erhai rhooapwut nge a rig nee tipan ngaeni, iiy a fasiun monofit reen aan maiur ngaeni pwiuniuwaen erhai me noan nee tipan.
MAT 5:29 Iwe, aere ifirhin mesoamw e paeniug nong noan monofit, oannusuwow wa oatoranoa. Efaer gacch igine egiufet ireiren oanongoamw epwe ppiungiunoa, mmwaen igine wunusaen oanongoamw epwe aekkaerhnong noan nifierno.
MAT 5:30 Ngaere ifirhin poawumw e paeniug nong noan monofit, gopiy noa wa oatoranoa. Efaer gacch igine egiufet ireiren oanongoamw epwe ppiungiunoa, mmwaen igine wunusaen oanongoamw epwe toonong noan nifierno.
MAT 5:31 “Epwan aepesa pwe, ‘Erhai ne e asiuw noa pwiuniuwan nge epwe ngaenneei niewe erheo pwapwioron mweoinoa.’
MAT 5:32 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi: aere erhai mwaaen a mweoi saengi pwiuniuwan reen ese tiwegin meeta ppweoniun, nge soapw reen aaen niewe maiur ngaeni pwiuniuwaen erhai, iwe wonowe minne a monofit pwe a feeori niewe epwe oamonofit reen aan pwiuppwiuniuw sefaaen, nge iiy mwaaen na a pwiuniuwaeni, ina iiy a pwan feeori monofit.
MAT 5:33 “Oawwa pwan rongorong aar aengaeniir aeremesaen mweoiwe pwe, ‘Wosoapw misimis oamw aekkepan, nge wopwe faer feeori meeta e oamw aekkepan ngaeni Deus.’
MAT 5:34 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi: wosoapw aekkepan rhag. Wosoapw aekkepan faaen itaen naaeng, pwe ina nenien Deus,
MAT 5:35 nge soapw pwan faaen itaen soanop, pwe ina aaen Deus nenien aseoseon pirheen, nge soapw pwan faaen itaen Jerusalem, pwe ina aepinoamwon King we egin taegias.
MAT 5:36 Wosoapw pwan aekkepan mwo nge faaen itaen rhimwemw, pwe wosoapw mmwenen aepwerhepwerha aere oarhonaanoa eyaen aennirhimwemw.
MAT 5:37 Wopwe aepesa, ‘Ewaer,’ aere ‘Aapw,’ pwe ese tiwegin minne wonaaen aepesa nge e itto saengi Man Aenneew we.
MAT 5:38 “Oawwa rongorong pwe re aepesa pwe, ‘Aere erhai e aettiwow efai mesoamw nge paniuwaenin wa pwan aettiwow efai mesan, nge aere erhai e aettiwow efoarh ngiimw, nge paniuwaenin wa pwan aettiwow efoarh ngiin.’
MAT 5:39 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi: oawsoapw paniuwaeni aaen aeremas aenneew ngaenigaemi. Aere erhai e ppeosepa ne oawusupoamw me wooan peig mwaaenemw, pwan wegeti ngaeni ne oawusupoamw me wooan peig rhooapwutomw.
MAT 5:40 Aere erhai e pwigiug noa noan nenien apwiung pwe epwe pwigi mengaagiumw mengaag, faer pwan nigiti ngaeni siketa na pwe pwan mengaagiun.
MAT 5:41 Aere erhai sonotaw e akkiuneog pwe wopwe pwigi ngaeni pisaegin noan eew mile, faer pwigi ngaeni noan ruwowu miles.
MAT 5:42 Aere erhai a tingoareog meeta oamw, ngaenneei, ngaere erhai a mwerhaen aeyae mwo meeta pisaegimw, fang ngaeni.
MAT 5:43 “Oawwa rongorong pwe re aepesa pwe, ‘Oaw aerhaengiir rhooan weni oaromi, nge oaw oapwutaar rhooan oapwutaegaemi.’
MAT 5:44 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi: oawpwe aerhaengiir rhooan oapwutaegaemi nge oawwa maeipin faaen iteer rhooakkena re aewwaeiraesigaemi,
MAT 5:45 pwe oawpwe no pwe naiun minna Semaemi wooai naaeng. Pwe iya aettina feeorian aenet wooar aeremas aenneew me aeremas gacch, nge a apiungiutiw worhow wooar rhooakkena reffeeor mwamwaai me rhooakkena reffeeor aenneew.
MAT 5:46 Meeta faan Deus epwe fang niffengaemi aere oaw aerhaengiir rhag rhooa na re aerhaengigaemi? Pwan rhooan iyoiyon mwo tax nge refeeori minna.
MAT 5:47 Aere weni maereyaeremi rhag minne wogaen kekkepas ngaeniir, ina nge minna wofeeori nge ese pwan wen saengiir aaemweoi. Pwan re Gentiles mwo nge refeeori taeppen minna.
MAT 5:48 Iwe aaemi oawpwe igin menaw gacch pwe oawpwe taeppen rhag gacchiun minna Semaemi wooai naaeng.
MAT 6:1 “Oawpwe aefaenniy pwe oawsoapw feeori feoffeeoriun aaemi tiwegin faaen meseer aeremas pwe repwe weri meeta oawwa feeori. Pwe aere oawfeeori taeppen minneen nge oawsoapw pwigi paniuwaemi me reen minna Semaemi wooai naaeng.
MAT 6:2 “Iwe aere oawfang ngaeni erhai man affayeo eew aegiaeg, oawsoapw aeni oangonongon minne oawwa feeori, oawte taeppeer rhooa oatupwutupw kka refeeori noan wutteer Jews me pwan wooan ennap. Refeeori minneen pwe aeremas repwe ngonotiir. Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe ra moannon pwigi paniuweer.
MAT 6:3 Ngaere oawwa fang ngaeni erhai man affayeo eew meeta, oawpwe feeori noan mwoanomwoan, pwe rhooan oaromw mwo nge resoapw giuneei wunuunun.
MAT 6:4 Ina nge epwe mwoanomwoan meeta oawwa feeori. Nge Semaemi a weri minne oawwa feeori noan mwoanomwoan epwe aesefaaeni ngaenigaemi paniuwaenin.
MAT 6:5 “Igine oawpwe maeipin, oawsoapw taeppeer rhooa oatupwutupw kkewe. Re tipaeni repwe gaen iutae nge ra maeipin me noan wutteer Jews me noan oapwugopwugon ennap, pwe aeremas repwe weriir. Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe ra moann me pwigi paniuweer.
MAT 6:6 Ngaere aaemi oawpwe maeipin, oawpwe toonong noan aaemi sengkin, oawwa ttiy noa asam nge oawwa maeipin ngaeni Semaemi ina oawse weri. Iwe, Semaemi epwe weri minikka oawwa feeori noan mwoanomwoan epwe aesefaaeni ngaenigaemi paniuwaenin.
MAT 6:7 “Ngaere oaw maeipin, oawsoapw aeyae towunepaen petenaen kkepas kka esooar faan, taeppeer re Gentiles regaen feeori minneei, pwe re maengiy pwe aar deus repwe aiussaening aar maeipin pwe iga e igin faeremworh.
MAT 6:8 Oawsoapw taeppeer, pwe Semaemi a fasiun giuneei meeta aaemi mwerhaen weni mmwaen iga aaemi oawpwe tingoar ngaeni.
MAT 6:9 Iwe, epwe ieei wunuunun aaemi oawpwe maeipin: ‘Semmaem wooai naaeng, aemwo epwe ssoar minna itoamw ina e santus,
MAT 6:10 aemwo Mweoiumw epwe war, aemwo nee tipoamw epwe no wooan feoniufan wunuunun rhag noan naaeng.
MAT 6:11 Ngaennegemaem mwongoi raaeneei aeipwe mwongo igina.
MAT 6:12 Wopwe saeneti noa aemaem monofit, wunuunun pwan aemaem aeiya saenetiir noa rhooakkena re monofit ngaenigemaem.
MAT 6:13 Wosoapw oatonongegemaem noan sessoat, nge wopwe aengesagemaem saengi Man Aenneew we. [Pwe oamw rhag mweoi me manaman me nning esoapw iug. Amen.]’
MAT 6:14 “Aere oawpwe saeneti noa aar aeremas monofit, ina nge Semaemi wooai naaeng epwe pwan saeneti noa aaemi monofit.
MAT 6:15 Nge aere oawsoapw saeneti noa aar aeremas monofit, Semaemi esoapw pwan saeneti noa aaemi monofit.
MAT 6:16 “Ngaere oawpwe aecchigipin, oawsoapw mas affayeo taeppeer rhooa oatupwutupw kkewe regaen feeori. Ra mas affayeo noa, pwe aeremas repwe giuneei pwe ra aecchigipin. Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe ra faer moannon pwigi paniuweer.
MAT 6:17 Ngaere aaemi oaw aecchigipin, oawpwe woraes me kkomwuuw rhimwemi,
MAT 6:18 pwe aeremas resoapw giuneei pwe oawwa aecchigipin, pwe aaen manna rhag Semaemi ina oawse weri minne e giuneei. Nge Semaemi iwe e giuneei minne oawwa feeori noan mwoanomwoan epwe aesefaaeni ngaenigaemi paniuwaenin.
MAT 6:19 “Oawsoapw iseis wiinaemi wooai soanop, pwe manepwur me iyow repwe fereei noa, nge rhooa mwoarho repwe fereei nong nge ra pirifa.
MAT 6:20 Nge oawpwe faer iseis wenepwuwaemi wooai naaeng, iga manepwur me iyow resoapw mmwenen fereei, nge rhooa mwoarho resoapw mmwenen fereei nong nge ra pirifa.
MAT 6:21 Pwe pwunnomi epwe no rhag iga wenepwuwaemi eno ee.
MAT 6:22 “Maas eweei rhag oappwunon oanong. Pwe aere mesoamw effat, oanongan noa oanongoamw epwe seram.
MAT 6:23 Ngaere mesoamw ese ffat, oanongan noa oanongoamw epwe rorhappiung. Pwe aere minna aesseremaen oanongoamw ese seram, nge epwe ifa mwo rorhappiungiun minna nee tipaemi!
MAT 6:24 “Ese mmwen erhai epwe engaang ngaeniir riiurhai maasta. Ina epwe oapwuta erhai, nge aerhaengi iwe erhai, me ngaere epwe mwamwaai ngaeni erhai, nge a aenneew ngaeni erhai. Ese mmwen oawpwe engaangappag ngaeni Deus me senaapiy.
MAT 6:25 “Ina minne ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe oawsoapw aiunaeng reen mwongo me rhaan pwe oawpwe menaw reen, ngaere mengaagiun oanongaemi. Pwe meeta, ese rhaeng rhag menaw me mmwaen mwongo? Nge ese rhaeng noa rhag oanong me mmwaen mengaag?
MAT 6:26 Oaw pipiir man aeniaen: Rese foat faiun waniwan, me giniiy uwaan, pwe repwe seoiyeoninong noan soko, nge Semaemi wooai naaeng efang rhag aeneer. Pwe meeta, ese temoag noa egius rhaengimi memmweer man aeniaen?
MAT 6:27 Eyor neeimi epwe mmwenen enaenaei noa egius menewan reen aan aiunaeng?
MAT 6:28 “Meeta oaw aiunaeng reen mengaag reen? Oawfan ngaeni peeon waniwan wunuunun aar menawtae: rese engaang, nge rese pwan ffeeor mengaagiiur.
MAT 6:29 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe igiwe mwo king Solomon e menaw iwe erhai man ssow wiinan nge esooar mengaagiun ne enning noa me mmwaen peeon waniwan kaan.
MAT 6:30 Pwe Deus minne aememmengaagiur fetinen neeiin waniwan — fetin kka eyor igina, nge resoapw nonoa naiu, pwe ra figaeg noa newumw. Pwe meeta, Deus esoapw mmwenen aememmengaagiugaemi? Me gaen mwittiginen aaemi niugiuniug!
MAT 6:31 “Ieei minne oawsoapw aiunaeng nge aepesa pwe, ‘Meeta sipwe mwongo?’ aere ‘Meeta sipwe iuniumi?’ aere ‘Meeta sipwe memmengaag?’
MAT 6:32 (Pwe ikkaan minikka re Gentiles retip mwaramwar reen.) Semaemi wooai naaeng e giuneei pwe oawpwe ammweneni oanongaen minikkeei.
MAT 6:33 Nge oawpwe gommwaen giutta minna Mweoiun Deus me minikkena e mwerhaen pwe oawpwe feeori, iwe, iiy epwe ngaennegaemi oanongaen minikkeei.
MAT 6:34 Ieei minne oawsoapw aiunaengiy naiu reen, pwe naiu epwe sipegin feeori aiunaengin. Esooar ipitan sipwe oatomoga noa aiunaengiy noan eraaen me eraaen.
MAT 7:1 “Oawsoapw apwiungiu aeremas, pwe Deus ete pwan apwiungiugaemi.
MAT 7:2 Pwe Deus ina epwe pwan apwiungiugaemi taeppen rhag aaemi apwiungiiur aaemweoi, epwe pwan aeyae ngaenigaemi anniug kena oawpwan aeyae ngaeniir aaemweoi.
MAT 7:3 Meeta wa weri peipei na noan mesaen pwiimw, nge wose weri soapwon irae mwu noan mesoamw?
MAT 7:4 Epwe ifa wusun oamw wopwe aengaeni pwiimw pwe, ‘Itto ipwe tipwei wow peipei mwu noan mesoamw,’ iga een nge eno eew soapwon irae noan mesoamw?
MAT 7:5 Een erhai man oatupwutupw! Wopwe mmwaen tipwei wow soapwon irae mwu noan mesoamw, nge wopwe naaen weri gacchiuw oamw tipwei wow peipei na noan mesaen pwiimw.
MAT 7:6 “Oawsoapw ngaenneei gonaag minne essoar, pwe rete pwan toagun nge re giugaemi. Oawsaapw oatora ngaeniir sino aaemi faiun usowus eyor ipitan, pwe iir repwe pwuritiw faaen pirheer.
MAT 7:7 “Oawpwe tittingoar, ina nge epwe yo ngaenigaemi; oawpwe giutta, ina nge oawpwe weri; oawpwe apiungiupiung wooan asam, ina nge epwe sugaeg ngaenigaemi.
MAT 7:8 Pwe iyo a tittingoar nge epwe yo ngaeni, nge iyo a giutta epwe weri, nge asam epwe sugaeg ngaeni iyo na e apiungiupiung.
MAT 7:9 Iyo neeimi saam epwe ngaenneei naiun efai faai igine e tingoar fenoawa?
MAT 7:10 Ngaere epwe tingoar erhai iig, wopwe mmwenen ngaenneei erhai sowufaeng?
MAT 7:11 Iwe, inamwo aaemi aeremas aenneew, nge oawwa giuneei aaemi oawpwe fang ngaeniir naimi minikka e mwamwaai. Epwe pwan ifa mwo nepan aaen minna Semaemi wooai naaeng ngaenneer minikka e mwamwaai rhooakkena re tingoar ngaeni!
MAT 7:12 “Oawpwe feeori ngaeniir aeremas taeppen meeta na aaemi oaw mwerhaen pwe repwe feeori ngaenigaemi. Pwe ieei oawuton aaen Moses Anniug me aar profeta kkewe kkepesaen fenai.
MAT 7:13 “Oawtonong noan asam na e rheogit! Pwe aesemaen nifierno ina e rheonap, nge aan na eyan ngaeni nge e mererhaeg, nge towunepaen aeremas retaeri.
MAT 7:14 Nge aesemaen menaw ina e rheogit, nge aan na eyan ngaeni nge e waeiraes, nge fitiman rhag aeremas kka re rhuungi.
MAT 7:15 “Oawpwe aefaennigaemi reer profeta oatupwutupw kkewe, ra itto reemi taeppen rhag sheep, nge nee tipeer a aeffitaeg ngaeni rhag wolves kkewe re mwoarho.
MAT 7:16 Oawpwe giuneer reen meeta kka ra feeori. Aekkaew irae towfanfan resoapw uwaeni uwaen grape, nge fetin towfanfan resoapw uwaeni uwaen fig.
MAT 7:17 Efoarh waniwan gacch epwe uwa gacch, nge efoarh waniwan aenneew epwe uwa aenneew.
MAT 7:18 Efoarh waniwan gacch esoapw mmwenen uwa aenneew, nge efoarh waniwan aenneew esoapw mmwenen uwa gacch.
MAT 7:19 Nge oanongaen waniwan kka ese gacch uwaan repwe gopogop tiw pwe repwe aekkaerhnong noan aengaet.
MAT 7:20 Iwe ina aaemi oawpwene giuneer profeta oatupwutupw me reen minikka ra feeori.
MAT 7:21 “Saapw oanongeer rhooakka re faingiaei pwe ‘Soamwoon, Soamwoon,’ nge repwe toonong noan Mweoiu Naaeng, pwe rhooawe rhag refeeori nee tipaen minna Semaei wooai naaeng.
MAT 7:22 Ngaere enoa tooto Raaenin Apwiung, repwe gin ssow rhooa kkomwu repwe aengaeniaei pwe ‘Soamwoon, Soamwoon! Faaen itoamw minne aeiya fenaiuw minna oanoon Deus, faaen itoamw minne aeiya asiiur wow towunepeer aniu aenneew, nge pwan faaen itoamw minne aeiya feeori towunepaen kkeman.’
MAT 7:23 Iwe ngaang ipwene aengaeniir pwe, ‘Ngaang ise giunegaemi. Oawsiu noa me reei, aaemi man aenneew kena.’
MAT 7:24 “Iwe iyo kka re rongorong minikka mwaeniaei nge re tapweei, ina nge re taeppen mwaaen reepiy we e aiuwtae imwan wooan porow.
MAT 7:25 Iwe, a piung worhow, nge a pwurutae rhaan nge a igin ngiung aaeng. Nge iiy iimw we ese toaroponoa, pwe iga e kaiutae wooan porow.
MAT 7:26 “Iwe nge iyo kka re rongorong minikka mwaeniaei nge rese tapweei, ina nge ra taeppen erhai mwaaen tipoarorh, e aiuwtae imwan wooan ppiy.
MAT 7:27 Iwe, a piung worhow nge a pwurutae rhaan nge a igin ngiung aaeng. Nge enoa toarop iimw we, nge a ifa mwo nepaen aan ffeir noa!”
MAT 7:28 Igiwe Jesus a moann aan aepesa minikkaan nge pwuwaen aeremas ra mwaar reen wunuunun aan fenai,
MAT 7:29 pwe ese taeppen sinsein anniug kkewe, pwe iiy e fenai faaen minna nemaenian.
MAT 8:1 Igiwe Jesus a ittiw me wooan rhug we, re towunap aeremas kka re tapwetiw mwirin.
MAT 8:2 Iwe, erhai mwaaen eweri kaenepaai a itto reen Jesus, a foatotiw me mmwan nge a aengaeni pwe, “Menap, aere wo mwerhaen, wa aecchipwanoa aaei semwaai.”
MAT 8:3 Jesus e angenoa nge a geotteopa mwaaen we, nge a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaang i mwerhaen, wone cchipw noa!” Reen rhag oatowe nge a cchipw noa miniwe semwaaiun mwaaen we.
MAT 8:4 Iwe Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Pipiiy, wosoapw aengaeni mwo nge erhai minneei, nge wa faaeraeg uwen noa reen patere pwe epwe weriug. Iwe nge a feeori oasoar we Moses e akkiuneo, pwe epwe pwaeri ngaeniir aeremas pwe wa nimegacch noa.”
MAT 8:5 Oatowe Jesus a toonong noan Capernaum, erhai soamwoonin sonotawaen Rome a itto nge a tingoar maaw ngaeni,
MAT 8:6 iwe a iura pwe, “Soamwoon, naeyi rhooan engaang a no rhag nee iimw, ese mmwenen mwagiut, nge a pwan igin metaeg.”
MAT 8:7 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Ipwe noa pwe ipwe noa aecchipwa.”
MAT 8:8 Nge soamwoonin sonotaw we a aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, ngaang soapw erhai man yor ipitan reen oamw wopwe itto noan imwaei. Nge wopwe aepesa rhag epat kkepas, nge rhooan engaang we naeyi epwe mamaaw tae.
MAT 8:9 Ngaang mwo nge pwan ngaang erhai mwaaen ino faaen nemaeniaen erhai e soamwoon saengiaei, nge epwan yor sonotaw kka reno faaen nemaeniaei. Ipwe aengaeni inaan pwe, ‘Wopwe noa,’ iwe a noa; iya aengaeni inaan pwe, ‘Wopwe itto,’ iwe a itto; iwe iya aengaeni rhooan akkiuneo, ‘Feeori minneen,’ iwe a feeori.”
MAT 8:10 Igiwe Jesus a rongorong kkepas kkeei, a riutae reen nge a aengaeniir aeremas kkewe rettapw noa mwirin pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, ise giuneei mwo nge erhai me noan Israel epwe ieei wusun aan niugiuniug.
MAT 8:11 Ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe re towunap aeremas repwe itto saengi eotiw me netow nge repwe mooat oaron Abraham, Isaac me Jacob noan gupwunnap na noan Mweoiu Naaeng.
MAT 8:12 Nge rhooawe repwe no noan Mweoiu Naaeng repwe oatorawow noan rorhappiung, iga repwe sessaeng nge akkaarengi me ee.”
MAT 8:13 Iwe Jesus a aengaeni soamwoonin sonotaw we pwe, “Sefaaen noa noan imwoamw; meeta wa niugiuniug ngaeni, epwe pwan wen ngaeniug.” Iwe rhag nge rhooan engaang we naiun a mamaaw tae.
MAT 8:14 Iwe, Jesus a noa reen imwaen Peter. A noa giuneei niewe inaen pwiuniuwaen Peter ewon noan gien pwe a igin pwerhikkar ginin.
MAT 8:15 Jesus a geotteopa rhag paiun, nge esaer noa pwerhin niewe. Mwirin niewe a rhimwitae a ittae engaang ngaeni.
MAT 8:16 Igiwe a nee oatofaaef noa, aeremas ra pwigiir to reen Jesus pwuwaen aeremas kkewe eyor aniu aenneew wooar. Jesus a asiiur wow aniu aenneew reen petenaen mwaenian, nge a aemaemaewaar tae rhooawe re semwaai.
MAT 8:17 A feeori minneen pwe epwe pwaeritae miniwe profeta we Isaiah a aepesa pwe, “Iiy e arhiuwa aarh semwaai nge aiuferanoa mesemesaen aarh semwaai.”
MAT 8:18 Igiwe Jesus a giuneei pwuwaen aeremas kkewe me oaron, a aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe repwe fatiun noa epeig meoneoiniun we.
MAT 8:19 Iwe, erhai sinsein anniug a itto reen nge a aengaeni pwe, “Sinsei, ese tiwegin iga wopwe noa ee nge ngaang ipwe tapweog.”
MAT 8:20 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Fox eyor ngeteer, man aeniaen eyor feseer, iwe nge mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas esooar eew pwiuneoi ne epwe noa wonotiw aseoseo ee.”
MAT 8:21 Nge erhai mwaaen pwan iiy rhooan kkayeo a aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, mmwaen fang mwo ngaang ipwe sefaaen noa nipwaeni noa mwaaen na semaei.”
MAT 8:22 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Itto tapweaei nge wa nigitiir rhooa mae repwe sipegin nipwaeni aar mae.”
MAT 8:23 Jesus a teeotae wooan pwoot we nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra tapweei.
MAT 8:24 Ese mmwaei mwo nge eew mwoor enoa itto noan meoneoiniun we, nge pwoot we a arapakkaan aan epwene mweoiusiutiw. Nge Jesus e maiur.
MAT 8:25 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra noa reen, nge ra faingitae. Ra aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, aemenewaegemaem pwe sipwene mae!”
MAT 8:26 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta oawwa mesag reen? Me gaen mwittiginen aaemi niugiuniug!” Iwe a iutae nge a kkepas sseor ngaeni aaeng me noa pwe repwe poas noa, iwe rhag nge a niuwanoa wooai saaet.
MAT 8:27 Iwe, mwaaen kkewe ra riutae nge ra aepesa pwe, “Meeta taeppen aeremas een? Iye aaeng mwo me noa nge re tapweei mwaenian!”
MAT 8:28 Igiwe Jesus a toori faniuwaen Gadara eno epeig meoneoiniun we, a itto rhuungiir riiurhai mwaaen retowow me noan paeyi kkewe. Mwaaen kkeei nge ewartae aniu aenneew wooar, nge re igin aemmesag ina minne esooar ne e rhiuwen taeri aan een reen.
MAT 8:29 Reen rhag oaton een nge ra aekkepwastae pwe, “Naiun Deus, meeta minne wo tipaeni me remaem? Wa itto pwe wopwe itto aeppaetigimaem mmwaen oaton apwiung?”
MAT 8:30 Eno eew cchon sino re mwommwongo fetaen me peiginoar.
MAT 8:31 Iwe aniu aenneew kkewe ra aeffaenipirhe ngaeni Jesus pwe, “Aere wopwe asiugemaem, fangenoa aemaem neeiir sino kenaan.”
MAT 8:32 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawnoa!” Iwe ra toowow me wooar mwaaen kkewe nge ra noa wartae wooar sino kkewe. Iwe cchon sino kkewe ra fattapw tiw wenepeigin rhug we e ittiw noan meoneoiniun we ittiw moapw noa.
MAT 8:33 Mwaaen kkewe rhooan ffooanon sino ra fattapw noa ra ittiw nee aepinoamw, iwe ra ittiw fioangei oanongan meeta kkewe a wen ngaeniir mwaaen kkewe ewartae aniu aenneew wooar.
MAT 8:34 Iwe oanongeer rhooan aepinoamw we ra noa pwe repwe noa rhuungi Jesus. Nge igiwe ra weri, ra aeffaenipirhe ngaeni pwe epwe siusaengi miniwe faniuweer.
MAT 9:1 Jesus a teeotae wooan pwoot we nge a sefaaeniti miniwe aepinoamwon iwe eno epeig meoneoiniun we.
MAT 9:2 Aaemweoi aeremas ra pwigito reen erhai mwaaen e maemerhoar ewon noan epeo giegiy. Igiwe Jesus a weri nepaen aar niugiuniug rhooawe, a aengaeni mwaaen we e maemerhoar pwe, “Aetemaegin naeyi! Monofitimw a mwusunoa.”
MAT 9:3 Iwe aaemweoi sinsein anniug kkewe ra niuwaennei pwe, “Mwaaen een e aepesa aenneewa Deus!”
MAT 9:4 Nge Jesus a giuneei niunniuwaen kkewe aar nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta oaw niuwaennei minikkena e aenneew reen?
MAT 9:5 E mererhaeg pwe sipwe aepesa pwe, ‘Monofitimw a mwusunoa,’ aere sipwe aepesa pwe, ‘Iutae wa faaeraeg noa’?
MAT 9:6 Iwe, ngaang ipwe pwaeri ngaenigaemi pwe mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas eyor maemaewan wooan soanop pwe epwe oamwusa noa monofit.” Iwe, a aengaeni mwaaen maemerhoar we pwe, “Iutae, pwigi giemw nge wa noa noan imwoamw.”
MAT 9:7 Iwe mwaaen we a iutae nge a noa noan imwan.
MAT 9:8 Igiwe aeremas ra weri miniwe, ra mesag tae nge ra aepingepinga Deus reen aan ngaenneer aeremas taeppen mamaaw we.
MAT 9:9 Jesus a siusaengi igiwe nge a weri erhai rhooan iyoiyon tax itan Matthew, emooat noan aan office. Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Itto tapweaei.” Iwe Matthew a iutae nge a tapweei noa mwirin.
MAT 9:10 Igiwe Jesus a mwongo noan imwaen Matthew, nge re towunap rhooan iyoiyon tax me rhooa monofit ra itto tapweei Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun reen table we.
MAT 9:11 Oatowe aaemweoi Pharisees kkewe ra giuneei miniwe, ra aeiyegiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Meeta faan naimi sinsei a mwongo ngaeniir rhooan iyoiyon tax me rhooa monofit kena reen?”
MAT 9:12 Jesus a rongorong aar kkepas nge a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Rhooakka rese semwaai rese noa reer toagota, pwe rhooakka refaer semwaai.
MAT 9:13 Oawnoa giutta faaen kkepas een me noan Pwapwior we e Santus: ‘Faayeow minne ngaang i tipaeni, nge saapw maan kkena aar oasoar ngaeniaei.’ Ngaang ise itto pwe ipwe faingiir rhooa mwamwaai, pwe faer rhooa monofit.”
MAT 9:14 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun John Baptist ra itto reen Jesus nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta faan aemaem me Pharisees aeisooaw aecchigipin, nge rhooan kkayeo kkomwu noawumw rese aecchigipin reen?”
MAT 9:15 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oaw niuwaennei nge epwe aenneew tipeer rhooakkena re itto reen gupwunon appwiuniupai we igiwe bridegroom we e rhiuwen no reer? Aapw! Nge epwe itto raaenin na repwe pwigi saengiir bridegroom we, nge ina oatona repwene aecchigipin noa.
MAT 9:16 “Esooar erhai epwe aeyae mengaag ffeo aan epwe pinisa tae wooan erheo mengaag maerhiy, pwe mengaag ffeo we epwe fereei noa mengaag maerhiy we, nge miniwe taeringen epwene faer gin temoag noa.
MAT 9:17 Esooar erhai epwe aenianong wine ffeo noan nenien wine maerhiy, pwe ina epwe pwoanoa nge wine we e nipiwow nge nenien wine we epwe ffeir noa. Pwe faer wine ffeo epwe itinong noan nenien wine ffeo, pwe ina nge oanongaen repwe gacch.”
MAT 9:18 Igiwe Jesus e aepesa minneen, erhai soamwoonin Jews a itto reen, a foatotiw mmwan nge a aengaeni pwe, “Naeyi aeterhooapwut a maenoa igina, nge wopwe itto rhag iseni tae poawumw wooan, pwe epwe menaw.”
MAT 9:19 Iwe, Jesus a iutae nge a tapweei noa, nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra pwan tapweei.
MAT 9:20 Eno erhai rhooapwut neeiir eseiug aan peitaeg noa noan seig me ruwowu raeg, a itto me niugiusagiuriun Jesus nge a geotteopa soapwon mengaagiun.
MAT 9:21 A niuwaennei nong nee tipan, “Aere i geotteopa rhag mengaagiun nge ipwe mamaaw tae.”
MAT 9:22 Iwe, Jesus a toagun, a weri niewe nge a aengaeni pwe, “Naeyi, wopwe aetemaegin, oamw niugiuniug minne a aecchipwoag tae.” Reen rhag oatowe nge rhooapwut we a mamaaw tae.
MAT 9:23 Mwirin Jesus a noa noan imwaen soamwoon we. Nge a weriir rhooan arhiuwerhiuw kkewe me pwuwa we ra igin saeng,
MAT 9:24 a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawtowow oanongaemi! Aeterhooapwut een nge ese mae, pwe aan rhag maiur!” Iwe ra kekkaei aegini.
MAT 9:25 Nge igiwe aeremas ra toowow niugiun, Jesus a toonong noan sengkin we aaen aeterhooapwut we nge a ammwarhiu tae paiun, iwe a rhimwitae.
MAT 9:26 Iwe, fioangon miniwe a rheeoi noa wooan oanongaen faniuw we.
MAT 9:27 Oatowe Jesus a siusaengi pwiuneoi we, riiurhai mwaaen masparh ra pwan tapweei noa mwirin. Ra aepwesaegini pwe, “Naiun David, wopwe faayeogemaem!”
MAT 9:28 Iwe, igiwe Jesus a toonong noan iimw we, mwaaen masparh kkewe ra itto reen. Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Oaw niugiuniug pwe ngaang ipwe mmwenen aeffetanoa mesaemi?” Iir ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Ooa, menap.”
MAT 9:29 Iwe Jesus a geotteopa meseer nge aepesa pwe, “Meeta oaw niugiuniug ngaeni, epwe pwan wen ngaenigaemi.”
MAT 9:30 Iwe, a ffatenoa meseer. Nge Jesus a igin ammwir ngaeniir pwe resoapw aengaeni mwo nge erhai miniwe a wen.
MAT 9:31 Nge iir ra faer noa arheoiuwa noa wunuunun Jesus wooan oanongaen faniuw we.
MAT 9:32 Igiwe mwaaen kkewe ra noa, aaemweoi aeremas ra pwigito reen Jesus erhai mwaaen ese mmwenen kkepas pwe ewartae aniu aenneew wooan.
MAT 9:33 Reen rhag oaton we Jesus a oatowowuw aniu aenneew we saengi mwaaen we, nge a mmwenen kkepas. Oanongeer aeremas kkewe ra mwaar reen nge ra aepesa pwe, “Esaaen yor mwo giuneyarh taeppen minneei me noan Israel.”
MAT 9:34 Nge Pharisees kkewe ra aepesa pwe, “Soamwoonin aniu aenneew minne efang maemaewan pwe epwe asiiur noa aniu aenneew.”
MAT 9:35 Jesus a faaeraeg fetaen wooan oanongaen aepinoamw me pwugos kkewe. E fenaiuw me noan wutteer Jews, e fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai we reen Mweoiu Naaeng me pwan aecchipwaar aeremas kkewe eweriir mesemesaen semwaai.
MAT 9:36 Nge igiwe a weriir pwuwaen aeremas kkewe, nge a igin faayeeor, pwe ra no noan affayeo me waeiraes taeppen sheep kkewe esooar no rhooan neginegiir.
MAT 9:37 Iwe a aengaeniir naiun rhooan kkayeo pwe, “A towunap uwaen menaai, nge re fitiman rhag rhooan gin.
MAT 9:38 Oaw maeipin ngaeni soamwoonin maat we pwe epwe fangenoa rhooan engaang pwe repwe giniiy oanongaen uwaen maat we aan.”
MAT 10:1 Jesus a faingi fengaenniir rhooawe seig me riiurhai rhooan kkayeo nge a ngaenneer maemaeweer pwe repwe asiuw aniu aenneew me aecchipwaar tae aeremas kka eweriir mesemesaen semwaai.
MAT 10:2 Ikkaan iteer oapostonus kkewe seig me riiurhai: mmwan nge Simon (pwan itan Peter) me Andrew we pwiin; James we pwiin John, ikkiwe naiun Zebedee;
MAT 10:3 Philip, Bartholomew, Thomas me Matthew iwe rhooan iyoiyon tax; James we naiun Alphaeus iwe me Thaddaeus;
MAT 10:4 Simon, iwe erhai man menat, me Judas Iscariot, iwe e fangenoa tinnimaen Jesus.
MAT 10:5 Jesus a fangenoa rhooawe seig me riiurhai nge a ammwir ngaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw noa noan faniuweer re Gentiles aere noan aepinoamwoor re Samaria.
MAT 10:6 Nge oawpwe faer noa reer aeremesaen Israel pwe iir minne ra weer sheep kkewe ra mwaenirh noa.
MAT 10:7 Oawnoa nge oawwa fenaiuw kkepas een, ‘Mweoiu Naaeng a arapeto!’
MAT 10:8 Oaw aecchipwaar rhooa semwaai, oaw aemenewaar tae manimae, oaw aecchipwaar rhooa kaenepaai iwe me oatowowuur aniu aenneew. Oawwa pwigi minneei me reei nge esooar paniuwan, nge oawpwene noa fang nge esoapw pwan yor paniuwan.
MAT 10:9 Nge oawsoapw pweipwog eew taeppen senaapiy noan pwoarsaemi;
MAT 10:10 oawsoapw pwan pweipwog pwetoaw me ssiuwenin mengaagiumi me nokka me yomi. Pwe rhooan engaang ina epwe toowow paniuweer.
MAT 10:11 “Ngaere oawwa toori eew aepinoamw aere pwugos, oawwa pipiiy iyo e tipaeni epwe aetiwaegaemi, iwe oawwa noa no reen toori aaemi oawpwene siusaengi pwiuneoi we.
MAT 10:12 Ngaere oawtonong noan eew iimw, oawwa aengaeniir pwe, ‘Oapoas epwe no reemi.’
MAT 10:13 Aere aeremesaen iimw we re aetiwaegaemi, nigititiw kkepesaen oapoas we aaemi reer. Nge aere rese aetiwaegaemi, nge oawwa pwigi sefaaeniy kkepesaen oapoas we aaemi.
MAT 10:14 Iwe, aere rhooan eew aepinoamw me aere eew iimw rese aetiwaegaemi aere aiussaening ngaenigaemi, oaw siusaengi pwiuneoi we nge oawwa iurhiugi noa ppweoniun me wooan pirhemi.
MAT 10:15 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe noan Raaenin Apwiung nge Deus epwe faayeow re Tyre me Sidon memmweer aeremesaen aepinoamw naan.
MAT 10:16 “Aiussaening, ngaang ipwene aefengaegaemi wow taeppeer sheep reno neeiir cchon wolves. Nge oawpwe aetipaecchemegaemi taeppen sowufaeng nge oawpwan tipipoas taeppeer doves.
MAT 10:17 Oawpwan aefaennigaemi pwe imwu eyor aeremas kka repwe torofigaemi nge re paenigaemi nong noan nenien apwiung, nge repwe pwan wirhigaemi me noan wutteer Jews.
MAT 10:18 Pwe reen minne itaei, minne repwene paenigaemi noa mmweer soamwoon me king, pwe oawpwe aengaeniir me re Gentiles Kkepas Mwamwaai we.
MAT 10:19 Iwe aere ra isenigaemi nong noa nenien apwiung, oawsoapw pireiir reen meeta oawpwe aepesa me wunuunun aaemi aepesa, pwe petenaen kkepas kka oawpwe aepesa epwe toorigaemi noan oaton naan.
MAT 10:20 Pwe saapw aaemi minne oaw kkepas, pwe Ngeoniun minna Semaemi minne oawwa aepesa mwaenian.
MAT 10:21 “Aeremas repwene afangmaei noa pwiir ngaeni maenoa, nge saam repwe pwan feeori taeppen minneen ngaeni naiiur; nge naiiur repwene pwan appaniuwaeni semeer me ineer nge re fangenoa iir pwe repwe noa niir noa.
MAT 10:22 Oanongeer aeremas nge repwe oapwutaegaemi pwe faaen itaei. Nge iyo na e aetemaegin ngaeni minna oarosan nge epwe menaw.
MAT 10:23 Iwe, aere re aewwaeiraesigaemi me noan eew aepinoamw, siunoa noan ina eew. Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe epwe itto mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas nge aaemi oaw sogoppaen moann reen aaemi engaang wooan oanongaen aepinoamwon Israel.
MAT 10:24 “Esooar erhai aeteei suguun epwe taegias saengi aan sinsei, nge esooar erhai rhooan akkiuneo epwe taegias saengi aan maasta.
MAT 10:25 Ieei minne erhai aeteei suguun epwe kker tipan aan epwe aeffitaeg ngaeni aan sinsei, nge erhai rhooan akkiuneo epwe kker tipan aan epwe aeffitaeg ngaeni aan maasta. Aere ra aeita ngaeni soamwoonin aeinang we pwe Beelzebul, epwe ifa mwo aenneewan aar repwe faingi ngaeniir oanongeer rhooan aeinang we.
MAT 10:26 “Iwe, oawsoapw mesagiiur aeremas. Pwe oanongaen meeta ewop epwene pwae noa, iwe me oanongaen kkepas mwoanomwoan repwene giuneei.
MAT 10:27 Meeta ngaang iya aengaenigaemi noan rorhappiung, oawpwe aepesatae noan seram. Nge meeta oaw rongorong noan saeningaemi oawpwe aekkepwas aegini noa me wooan wungaen iimw.
MAT 10:28 Oawsoapw mesagiiur rhooamwu regaen niiy noa oanongaemi, pwe ina resoapw mmwenen niiy noa ngeoniumi. Nge oawpwe faer mesagiu Deus, iwe emmwenen niiy noa oanongaemi me ngeoniumi noan nifierno.
MAT 10:29 Reen efai rhag checcha nge wa mmwenen chuwaiuw riiurhai nicchok, nge erhai mwo nge ese ppiungiutiw nee ppweon aere Semaemi ese iura.
MAT 10:30 Iwe nge aaemi, oanongaen aennirhimwemi mwo nge Deus e paengi.
MAT 10:31 Ina oawsoapw mesag, pwe aaemi ina eyor ipitaemi memmweer towunepeer nicchok!
MAT 10:32 “Rhooakka re aepesa pwe iir naeyi me neeiir aeremas, ngaang ipwe pwan feeori ngaeniir me weni mmwaen Semaei wooai naaeng.
MAT 10:33 Nge iyo kena resaep saengiaei me neeiir aeremas, ngaang ipwe pwan saep saengiir me weni mmwaen Semaei wooai naaeng.
MAT 10:34 “Oawsoapw maengiy pwe iya itto pwe ipwe pwigito oapoas wooan soanop. Aapw, ise itto pwe ipwe pwigito oapoas, pwe faer efoarh saeitan.
MAT 10:35 Pwe ngaang itto ipwe feeoriir aetemwaaen repwe aengimaaw ngaeniir semeer, me aeterhooapwut repwe aengimaaw ngaeniir ineer, pwiuniuwaen naiiur repwene aengimaaw ngaeniir inaen pwiuniuweer;
MAT 10:36 nge rhooan oapwutoag repwe itto saengi rhag rhooan oamw famini.
MAT 10:37 “Rhooakka e temoag aerhaengerhaengin semeer me ineer me mmwaei, ese fin repwe no pwe naeyi rhooan kkayeo. Nge rhooakka e temoag aerhaengerhaengin naiiur me mmwaei, ese pwan fin repwe no pwe naeyi rhooan kkayeo.
MAT 10:38 Iwe, rhooakka rese aiufera aar kurus nge re tapweeito mwiriy, nge ese fin repwe no pwe naeyi rhooan kkayeo.
MAT 10:39 Nge rhooakkena re maengiy repwe kkemwarh wooan meneweer, epwe ppiung saengiir, nge rhooakkena eppiung saengiir meneweer pwe faaen itaei nge repwe weri sefaaeniy.
MAT 10:40 “Iyo e aetiwaegaemi, e aetiwaeyaei, nge iyo a aetiwaeyaei, a pwan aetiwa iwe efangeto ngaang.
MAT 10:41 Iyo a aetiwa erhai profeta pwe iga iiy erhai profeta, epwe yor paniuwaenin me reen minna paniuwaen. Nge iyo a aetiwa erhai aeremas mwamwaai pwe iga iiy erhai aeremas mwamwaai, epwe yor paniuwaenin taeppen erhai aeremas mwamwaai.
MAT 10:42 Aere erhai a aiuniu ngaeni erhai man sessoan kka rhoaniuwaei eew kkepaen rhaan patapat pwe iga iiy erhai rhoaniuwaei, ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, iiy epwe yo ngaeni minna paniuwaenin.”
MAT 11:1 Igiwe Jesus a moannon akkiuneeor rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun iwe seig me riiurhai, a noa saengi pwiuneoi we iwe a noa fenai me oaronga fetaeneei wooan oanongaen aepinoamw kkewe pwiuneoi we.
MAT 11:2 Nge oatowe John Baptist a rongorong me noan imwaen kanepwus wunuunun engaang kkewe Kristus a feeorin, a fangenoa aaemweoi rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun reen.
MAT 11:3 Iwe, ra aeiineow Jesus pwe, “Een miniwe re iura pwe epwe itto, aere aeipwe wewweti erhai?”
MAT 11:4 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Oaw sefaaen noa oawwa aengaeni John minne oawwa rongorong me weri:
MAT 11:5 rhooa masparh ra ffatenoa, rhooa pirhemae ra faaeraeg, rhooa kaenepaai ra gacch noa, rhooa saeningapiung ra rongorong, rhooa mae ra menawtae, nge Kkepas Mwamwaai we a fenai ngaeniir rhooa affayeo.
MAT 11:6 Ifa mwo wenepwuweer rhooa se tip mwaramwar reei!”
MAT 11:7 Oatowe rhooawe naiun John ra noa, Jesus a kkepas ngaeniir aeremas kkewe reen wunuunun John: “Igiwe oawwa noa reen John noan desert we, meeta minne oaw niuwaennei pwe oawpwe noa weri? Efoarh fetin e mwoaroro reen aaeng?
MAT 11:8 Meeta minne oawnoa pwe oawpwe weri? Erhai mwaaen e memmengaag tae mengaag nning? Aeremas kka e ina wusun mengaagiiur nge reno noan imwaen king!
MAT 11:9 Aengaeniaei, meeta rhag oawnoa pwe oawpwe weri? Erhai profeta? Ooa, ennetaen, oawwa weri erhai e taegias saengi erhai profeta.
MAT 11:10 Pwe John miniwe Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, ‘Deus a kkepas, ngaang ipwene fangetiw naeyi rhooan pweipwogin kkepas me weni mmwoamw pwe epwe noa maeneti ennepoamw.’
MAT 11:11 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe John Baptist ina e taegias saengiir aeremas towunap kka reno wooan soanop. Iwe nge manna oarosaen git me noan Mweoiu Naaeng ina e taegias saengi John.
MAT 11:12 Saengi rhag oaton we John Baptist a rhaepetae aan fenai toorito igina nge miniwe Mweoiu Naaeng a toonong noan waeiraes pwe aeremas aenneew ra fiiow wooan pwe repwe nemaeni.
MAT 11:13 Toorito oatowe John a no, oanongeer profeta me Anniug kkewe aaen Moses ra aepesa wunuunun miniwe Mweoiu Naaeng;
MAT 11:14 nge aere oawwa niugiuw aar fenai, John nge iiy Elijah, iwe ra fasiun aepesa noa pwe epwe itto.
MAT 11:15 Iyo eyor saeningan, epwe rongorong!
MAT 11:16 “Iwe, meeta ipwe aweweei ngaeniir aeremesaen mweoi e igina? Ra aeffitaeg ngaeniir rhag wonigaet kkewe remooat noan nenien chuwaai. Eew mwiirh nge re iyaekkepwas ngaeniir aaemweoi,
MAT 11:17 ‘Aemaem aeiya pwan kker ngaenigaemi, nge aaemi oawse maan! Aemaem aeiya arhiuwerhiuw, nge aaemi oawse saeng!’
MAT 11:18 Igiwe John a itto, e aecchigipin nge ese pwan iun wine, nge aeremas ra aepesa pwe, ‘Iiy eyor aniu aenneew wooan!’
MAT 11:19 Nge igiwe Naiun Aeremas e itto, a mwommwongo nge e iun, nge aeremas ra aepesa pwe, ‘Oaw pipiiy mwaaen een! Iiy erhai mwaaen mwongonap me iun wine, nge maereyaereer rhooan iyoiyon tax me rhooa monofit.’ Iwe nge minna repiaen Deus reepiy a pwae noa pwe ennet reen meeta a feeori.”
MAT 11:20 Aeremesaen aepinoamw kkewe Jesus a feeori towunepaen kkeman kkewe aan me ee ina rese toagun saengi aar monofit, iwe Jesus a soong ngaeniir.
MAT 11:21 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi rhooan Chorazin me Bethsaida! Aere kkeman kka refeeori me wooan igeei minne refeeori me wooan Tyre me Sidon, ina nge aeremesaen aepinoamw kenaan a ssiunaei rhag aar memmengaag tutu nge re oamworomwor tae fenang wooar, pwe epwe pwae noa aar toagun saengi monofit!
MAT 11:22 Ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe noan Raaenin Apwiung nge Deus epwe faayeow re Tyre me Sidon me mmwaemi.
MAT 11:23 Nge een Capernaum! Wo tipaeni wopwe tooritae naaeng? Een wopwe ppiungiutiw noan nifierno! Aere kkeman kkewe effeeor me reemw epwan ffeeor me noan Sodom, epwe rhiuwen no rhag igina.
MAT 11:24 Ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe noan Raaenin Apwiung nge Deus epwe faayeow re Sodom me mmwoamw.”
MAT 11:25 Reen oatowe nge Jesus a aepesa pwe, “Semaei, Soamwoonin naaeng me soanop, iya ngaenneog oamw aerhigerhig, pwe wa oapanoa minikkeei saengiir rhooa reepiy me metefaaegini, nge wa pwaeri ngaeniir rhooa kkewe reweer wonigaet.
MAT 11:26 Ennet, Semaei, pwe ina minna wo tipaeni epwe wen.”
MAT 11:27 “Semaei a ngaenneaei oanongaen meeta. Esooar erhai ne e giuneei minna Naiun, pwe aeggaen minna Seman rhag, nge esooar erhai e giuneei minna Seman, pwe iiy rhag minna Naiun, iwe me iyo kena minna Naiun a finiir tae pwe epwe pwaeri ngaeniir.
MAT 11:28 “Oaw itto reei oanongaemi rhooakkena oawwa aerhig reen pweipwogin mini cchoaw, pwe ngaang ipwe asseoseogaemi.
MAT 11:29 Oaw pwigi yoke e aaei nge oawwa iseni tae woami, nge oawwa kapwiung saengiaei, pwe ngaang itip maniuweniuw nge i mesoanosoan; pwe ina nge aaemi oawpwe meyaefi aseoseo.
MAT 11:30 Pwe yoke e ngaang ipwene fang ngaenigaemi iye e mererhaeg, nge minne ipwe iseni tae woami oawpwe aiufera iye eppaen.”
MAT 12:1 Ese ssiunaei weni mwirin aaen Jesus faaeraeg nong noan aekkaew maetaen wheat wooan raaenin Sabbath. Nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra pecchai, iwe ra rhaepetae aar ferhiy iuwoapwon wheat kkewe nge ra angi minikkewe faiun.
MAT 12:2 Nge igiwe Pharisees kkewe ra weri miniwe, ra aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Pipiiy, ese gacch ngaeni aarh anniug pwe rhooan kkayeo kkomwu noawumw repwe feeori minna wooan Sabbath!”
MAT 12:3 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oawse aeraegi mwo miniwe David efeeori noan oaton we iiy me rhooa kkewe naiun ra pecchai?
MAT 12:4 A toonong noan imwaen Deus, nge iiy me mwaaen kkewe rhoaniuwan ra mwongo fenoawa kkewe ra aeni oasoar ngaeni Deus, inamwo igiwe e aenneew ngaeni anniug pwe repwe mwongo, pwe patere rhag minne emmwen pwe repwe mwongo fenoawa kkewe.
MAT 12:5 Aere oawse aeraegi miniwe effoat noan aaen Moses anniug pwe oanongaen raaenin Sabbath nge patere kkena noan Temple we re fereei anniugiun Sabbath, nge rese monofit?
MAT 12:6 Ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe erhai minne eno igeei e taegias saengi Temple.
MAT 12:7 Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, ‘Faayeow minne ngaang i tipaeni, nge saapw maan kkena aar oasoar ngaeniaei.’ Aere aaemi oaw giuneei faaen kkepas een, ina nge oawsoapw oamonofitiir aeremas kena rese monofit.
MAT 12:8 Pwe mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas minne Soamwoonin Sabbath.”
MAT 12:9 Iwe, Jesus a noa saengi pwiuneoi we nge a toonong noan wutteer Jews we,
MAT 12:10 nge eno erhai mwaaen e maemerhoar paiun. Aaemweoi aeremas repwan no igiwe, ra giutta aekkaew rhaepin minikka repwe oaturu Jesus wooan. Iwe ra aeiineow Jesus pwe, “E mwamwaai ngaeni aarh anniug pwe repwe aecchipwa erhai wooan raaenin Sabbath?”
MAT 12:11 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Epwe ifa aere erhai naimi sheep a ppiungiunong noan eew niipw wooan raaenin Sabbath? Oawsoapw pwigi pwe oawpwe taiuwtae?
MAT 12:12 Pwe erhai aeremas nge eyor ipitan mmwaen erhai sheep! Iwe aarh anniug a saeneti aarh sipwe feeori minne e mwamwaai wooan raaenin Sabbath.”
MAT 12:13 Mwirin Jesus a aengaeni mwaaen we e maemerhoar paiun pwe, “Aeitiwow poawumw.” Iwe, a aeitiwow paiun nge a mamaaw noa pwan taeppen rhag ina epai.
MAT 12:14 Iwe Pharisees kkewe ra siunoa pwiungiuw wunuunun aar repwe niiy noa Jesus.
MAT 12:15 Oatowe Jesus a rongorong pwiungiupwiung we aar, a noa saengi pwiuneoi we, nge pwuwaen aeremas ra ttapw noa mwirin. Iwe a aecchipwaar oanongeer rhooa semwaai
MAT 12:16 nge a aengaeniir pwe resoapw fioangei ngaeniir aeremas wunuunun iiy.
MAT 12:17 A feeori minneen, pwe epwe pwaeritae miniwe Deus a aengaeni profeta Isaiah:
MAT 12:18 “Ieen naeyi rhooan akkiuneo iya finitae, iiy minne i aerhaengi, iya igin kker reen. Ngaang ipwene fangetiw aaei Espritu wooan, nge iiy epwe arheoiuwa noa wunuunun aaei apwiung ngaeniir oanongaen faniuw.
MAT 12:19 Esoapw aengimaw aere apwas, aere kkepas temoag wooan aan.
MAT 12:20 Esoapw gopiy mwo nge efoarh fetin ppwoar, me pwan gunuw noa naam na e oamoaruporup. Iiy epwe oarhorho ngaeni toori ssiaaen aan mmwen ngaeni oapoas na efin pwe epwe yo ngaeni oanongaen faeinaengiy.
MAT 12:21 Ina nge oanongaen faniuw repwene aeisetip wooan.”
MAT 12:22 Iwe aaemweoi aeremas ra pwigito reen Jesus erhai mwaaen parh nge ese pwan mmwenen kkepas, pwe ewartae aniu aenneew wooan. Jesus a aecchipwa mwaaen we, iwe a mmwenen kkepas me fannoa.
MAT 12:23 Pwuwaen aeremas kkewe ra riutae reen miniwe Jesus a feeori nge ra aeiineo pwe, “Meeta, epwe ieei mwaaen we naiun David?”
MAT 12:24 Igiwe Pharisees ra rongorong kkepas kkewe, ra aepesa pwe, “Emmwenen asiiur noa aniu aenneew pwe iga rhag Beelzebul we soamwoonin aniu aenneew minne efang maemaewan.”
MAT 12:25 Jesus a giuneei aar niunniuwaen nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Aere eew faniuw a ginigin fesaeng me fiiow fengaen, faniuw een esoapw ssiunaei. Aere rhooan eew aepinoamw aere eew famini repwe ginigin fesaeng me fiiow fengaen, nge repwe mwetoar fesaeng.
MAT 12:26 Iwe aere rhooan mweoiun Saetan ra fiiow fengaen ina nge ra fasiun mwetoarotoar, nge minna mweoiun epwe iug noa!
MAT 12:27 Ngaere igine e ieei wunuunun aaei asiiur noa, iwe nge e ifa wusun aar rhooa kkomwu rhoaniuwaemi asiiur noa aniu aenneew? Rhooa kkomwu rhoaniuwaemi ra pwaeritae pwe oaw mwaerhei!
MAT 12:28 Aapw, pwe Ngeoniun Deus a ngaenneaei maemaewaei aaei ipwe asiiur noa aniu aenneew. Ieei minne a pwaeri noa pwe minna Mweoiun Deus a faer toorigaemi.
MAT 12:29 “Esooar erhai epwe tongaeni toonong noan imwaen erhai mwaaen mamaaw pwe epwe pwigi noa pisaegin; aere epwe mmwaen geoni noa mwo mwaaen we, ina nge epwapw mmwenen piraf me noan iimw we.
MAT 12:30 “Erhai ne ese tapweaei, nge iiy rhooa aenneew ngaeniaei, nge erhai ese tipaengiaei reen ioi, iiy erhai rhooan oammwoatoar.
MAT 12:31 Faaen minneei ipwe aengaenigaemi: aeremas repwe mmwenen oamwusa noa ese tiwegin monofitiir, me pwan kkepas aenneew kka re aepesa; nge aere erhai e kkepas aenneew ngaeni Espritu Santus nge esoapw mwusunoa.
MAT 12:32 Iyo e kkepas aenneew ngaeni Naiun Aeremas epwe mmwenen mwusunoa. Nge iyo e kkepas aenneew ngaeni Espritu Santus esoapw mmwenen mwusunoa igina toori nee soapw noan.
MAT 12:33 “Aere eyor waniwan gacch, uwaan repwan gacch, nge aere a yor waniwan e aenneew, uwaan repwan aenneew. Pwe sigaen giuneei meeta taeppen waniwan we me reen rhag uwaan.
MAT 12:34 Aaemi sowufaeng! Epwe ifa wusun aaemi aepesa min mwamwaai nge aaemi aeremas aenneew. Pwe iga aaw e aepesa meeta kkena esseog noan pwunn.
MAT 12:35 Erhai aeremas gacch epwe oatowowuw mini gacch saengi gacchiun noan tipan, nge erhai aeremas aenneew epwe oatowowuw mini aenneew saengi aenneewaen noan tipan.
MAT 12:36 “Nge ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe noan Raaenin Apwiung nge aeremas repwe aengaeni oanongaen kkepas kka esooar ipitan ikka re aepesa.
MAT 12:37 Pwe reen oamw kkepas minne Deus epwe apwiungiug reen, epwe pwaeritae aere een minne wo mwamwaai aere wo monofit.”
MAT 12:38 Iwe aaemweoi sinsein anniug me rhooawe Pharisees ra aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Sinsei, aemaem aei mwerhaen weri oamw feeori eew kkeman.”
MAT 12:39 Nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “A ifa mwo aenneewan me aar se niugiuniug aeremesaen mweoi e igina! Oawwa tingoar ngaeniaei pwe ipwe feeori eew kkeman? Nge esoapw yor eew kkeman epwe pwae ngaenigaemi me niugiunoan kkeman we aaen profeta Jonah.
MAT 12:40 Epwe wunuunun rhag aaen Jonah no aegini eoniuraen me eoniupwoong noan upwaen erhai iig faeregit we, ina minne Naiun Aeremas epwe no eoniuraen me eoniupwoong noan faeinaengiy.
MAT 12:41 Noan Raaenin Apwiung re Nineveh repwe iutae nge ra oamonofiti aeremesaen mweoi e igina, pwe iga iir re toagun saengi monofitiir oatowe re rongorong fenai kkewe aaen Jonah; nge ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe erhai e taegias saengi Jonah eno igeei!
MAT 12:42 Noan Raaenin Apwiung nge Queen reen Sheba epwe iutae nge a oamonofiti aeremesaen mweoi e igina; pwe iiy a itto saengi faniuwaen taaw noa, pwe epwe itto aiussaening ngaeni aaen king Solomon kkepesaen reepiy; nge ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe erhai e taegias saengi Solomon eno igeei!
MAT 12:43 “Igine erhai aniu aenneew a toowow me wooan erhai aeremas, nge ina epwene faaeraeg fetaen wooan faniuw paenekka pwe egiut nenien aan aseoseo. Aere esooar eew neniy e rhuungi,
MAT 12:44 nge ina epwene aengaeni oanongan pwe, ‘Ipwene sefaaen noa reen imwaei iwe i siusaengi.’ Iwe a sefaaen nge a noa rhuungi iimw we pwe a peo, nge a pwan nimegacch noa noan pwe oanongaen aegiaeg nge a wonopaeg noa nenien.
MAT 12:45 Iwe epwe noa nge a noa paeniir to fiusiuman aniu aenneew kena re igin kkaein aar aenneew saengi, nge ra itto no pwiuneoi we. Iwe igiwe a moann oanongan noa, nge wunuunun aeremas we a faer igin aenneew saengi mmwaen miniwe rhaepetaen. Ieei wunuunun minne epwe wen ngaeniir aeremas aenneewan mweoi e igina.”
MAT 12:46 Jesus e rhiuwen kekkepas ngaeniir aeremas kkewe, nge miniwe inan me rhooawe pwiin ra war. Ra iu niugiun iimw we nge ra tingoar pwe repwe kkepas ngaeni.
MAT 12:47 Iwe erhai aeremas kkewe a aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Pipiiy, inoamw me rhooawe pwiimw re iu niugiun nge re mwerhaen kkepas ngaeniug.”
MAT 12:48 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Iyo inaei me iyo pwiiy?”
MAT 12:49 Iwe a aeitiiti ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a iura pwe, “Pipiiy! Ikkaan iir inaei me pwiiy!
MAT 12:50 Pwe iyo na a feeori nee tipaen Semaei wooai naaeng, iir pwiiy me mwengeaei me inaei.”
MAT 13:1 Iwe noan rhag raaenin we Jesus a siusaengi iimw we a noa reen meoneoiniun we, iwe a noa mooat tiw wenepeigin.
MAT 13:2 Nge aeremas towunap kkewe ra itto reen, iwe a teeotae wooan efoarh pwoot a ittae mooat wooan. Nge rhooawe ra iu nee ppiy.
MAT 13:3 Jesus a fioang awewe ngaeniir towunepaen aegiaeg, iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Erhai mwaaen a noa pwe epwe noa aeperes faiun foat.
MAT 13:4 Igiwe e aeperes fetaen foat kkewe, nge aekkaefai ra ppiungiutiw wenepeigin aan we, nge man aeniaen ra itto anginoa.
MAT 13:5 Aekkaefai ra ppiungiutiw wooan kaenefai, igiwe ese maniueon ppweon ee. Faiun kkewe ra mwetekkaein pwaechetae, pwe igiwe rese no ppweon ttonoa.
MAT 13:6 Nge igiwe aenet a ttinitae, nge a aeppwesa noa foat kkewe; pwe igiwe waeran foat kkewe ese nennoan noa, iwe a mwetekkaein mae noa.
MAT 13:7 Aekkaefai ra ppiungiutiw neeiin irae towfanfan. Iwe irae towfanfan kkewe ra menawtae nge ra fittitae wooar iwe ra maenoa.
MAT 13:8 Nge aekkaefai ra ppiungiutiw noan ppweon mwamwaai, iwe ra uuwa: aekkaefai ra uwaeni epwiugiuw, aekkaefai woneig, nge aekkaefai eniig.”
MAT 13:9 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Iyo eyor saeningan, epwe rongorong!”
MAT 13:10 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra itto reen Jesus nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta wo kkepas noan fioangon awewe iga wo kkepas ngaeniir reen?”
MAT 13:11 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Deus a fang ngaenigaemi pwe oawpwe giuneei kkepas mwoanomwoanon minna Mweoiu Naaeng, nge ikka aaemweoi ese ngaenneer.
MAT 13:12 Pwe iyo a yor meeta aan nge repwe pwan fang ngaeni iwe epwene igin ssow noa aan, nge iyo ese yor meeta aan nge repwe pwigi saengi mwo nge iwe egius iwe eyor reen.
MAT 13:13 Faaen aaei kkepas ngaeniir noan fioangon awewe, pwe iga re pipiiy noa nge rese weri, nge repwe aiussaening nge rese rongorong, nge rese pwan metaf reen.
MAT 13:14 Iwe a pwae pwe ennet minikkiwe mwaeniaen profeta Isaiah: ‘Oawpwe aiussaening me aiussaening nge oawsoapw metaf; oawpwe pipiiy me pipiiy nge oawsoapw weri.
MAT 13:15 Pwe aar niunniuwaen rhooakkeei nge a pwurh, nge ra pineyinoa saeningeer, nge ra ammaiur noa meseer. Ngaere ese ieei wusuur, ina nge meseer epwe weriwer nge saeningeer epwe rongorong, epwe metaf noan pwunnoor, iwe nge repwe toagun ngaeniaei, nge ngaang ipwe aemaemaewaar tae.’ Ieei minne mwaeniaen Deus.
MAT 13:16 “Nge aaemi oawwa wenepwu! Pwe mesaemi ra weriwer nge saeningaemi ra rongorong.
MAT 13:17 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe towunap profeta me aeremas mwamwaai ra mwerhaen weri meeta kka aaemi oawwa weri, nge iir rese weri. Ra pwan mwerhaen rongorong meeta kka aaemi oawwa rongorong, nge iir rese rongorong.
MAT 13:18 “Iwe oaw aiussaening, pwe oawpwe metaf reen fioangon awewen rhooan foat we.
MAT 13:19 Rhooa kkewe re rongorong kkepesaen Mweoiu Naaeng, nge rese metefaaegini, ra taeppen rhag faiun foat kkewe re ppiungiutiw wenepeigin aan we. Iwe Man Aenneew we a itto pwigi saengiir minne a toonong nee tipeer.
MAT 13:20 Nge faiun kkewe re ppiungiutiw wooan kaenefai, ra aeffitaeg ngaeni rhooawe re aetiwa miniwe kkepesaen Deus noan kker reen rhag oaton we ra rongorong.
MAT 13:21 Nge kkepas we ese waaraar me nee tipeer, iwe ese ssiunaei wooar. Nge aere a yor fitigogo me waeiraes faaen itaen miniwe kkepesaen Deus, ra mwetekkaein fangetae.
MAT 13:22 Nge faiun kkewe re ppiungiutiw neeiin irae towfanfan, ra aeffitaeg ngaeniir rhooawe re rongorong kkepesaen Deus, nge aiunaeng reen menaw e igina me mwecheniaen pisaegin feoniufan ra oamoapwu miniwe kkepesaen Deus, pwe esoapw mmwenen uuwa.
MAT 13:23 Nge faiun kkewe re ppiungiutiw wooan ppweon mwamwaai, ra aeffitaeg ngaeniir rhooawe re rongorong miniwe kkepesaen Deus nge ra metaf reen: iwe, ra uuwa, aaemweoi ra uwaeni epwiugiuw, aaemweoi woneig, nge pwan aaemweoi eniig.”
MAT 13:24 Jesus a pwan fioangei ngaeniir pwan eew fioangon awewe: “Mweoiu Naaeng a aeffitaeg ngaeni minneen. Erhai mwaaen a aeperes faiun foat gacch noan aan menaai.
MAT 13:25 Noan eew pwongin, igiwe aeremas ra maiur, erhai man aenneew a itto aeperes pwuger mwaaen neeiin maat we, iwe, a noa.
MAT 13:26 Oatowe faiun foat kkewe ra menawtae nge ra uuwa, iwe nge a noa pwae noa pwuger mwaaen kkewe.
MAT 13:27 Mwaaen kkewe naiun rhooan engaang ra itto reen nge ra aengaeni pwe, ‘Menap, saapw faiun foat gacch miniwe wofoat noan menaai we oamw?. Nge iya rhag pwuger mwaaen ra noa itto me ee?’
MAT 13:28 A paniuwaeniir pwe, ‘Erhai man aenneew a feeori minneei.’ Iwe, rhooawe rhooan engaang ra aeiineow pwe, ‘Wo mwerhaen aeipwe noa wiytae pwuger mwaaen kenaan?’
MAT 13:29 Iwe a paniuwaeniir pwe, ‘Aapw, pwe aere oawpwe wiytae pwuger mwaaen kenaan nge emmwen pwe faiun foat kkewe repwe pwan wisaegtae.
MAT 13:30 Oaw nigitiir pwe repwe menaw ppagtae toori oaton ee sipwene gin. Iwe nge ngaang ipwe naaen aengaeni rhooan affeeoriun repwe mmwaen wiytae pwuger mwaaen kkewe, ra geoni fengaenniy nge ra figiir noa. Iwe ra ioni fengaenniy faiun foat kkewe nge ra iseniir nong noan aaei imwaen soko.’ ”
MAT 13:31 Iwe, Jesus a fioangei ngaeniir pwan eew fioangon awewe: “Mweoiu Naaeng a aeffitaeg ngaeni minneen. Erhai mwaaen a pwigi efai faiun mustard a noa foatogi noan aan menaai.
MAT 13:32 Iiy minne oarosaen mwittigin me neeiir faiun irae, nge igine a menawtae nge iiy minne oarosaen temoag me neeiin irae me noan menaai we. A ssiuwen ngaeni efoarh irae faeregit, pwe man aeniaen repwe itto ffeeor feseer wooan raaen.”
MAT 13:33 Iwe, Jesus a fioangei ngaeniir pwan eew fioangon awewe: “Mweoiu Naaeng a aeffitaeg ngaeni minneen. Erhai rhooapwut a pwigi egius yeast nge a nofiti fengaenniy me enuuw pwaecchin fenoawa emas toori aan pwo tae fenoawa we.”
MAT 13:34 Jesus a aeyae fioangon awewe aan epwe aepesa ngaeniir pwuwaen aeremas oanongaen minikkeei; esoapw aepesa mwo nge epat aegiaeg ngaeniir igine ese aeyae fioangon awewe.
MAT 13:35 A feeori minneei pwe epwe pwaeritae pwe ennet miniwe profeta a aepesa pwe, “Ngaang ipwe aeyae fioangon awewe iga ipwe kkepas ngaeniir. Ngaang ipwe aepesa ngaeniir minikka rese giuneei saengi rhaepetaen feoniufan.”
MAT 13:36 Iwe igiwe Jesus a noa saengi pwuwaen aeremas kkewe nge a toonong noan eew iimw, rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra itto reen nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Wopwe aemmetefa ngaenigemaem meeta faaen fioangon awewen fetin we noan menaai we.”
MAT 13:37 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Mwaaen we aeperes faiun foat kkewe egacch nge ina iiy Naiun Aeremas;
MAT 13:38 menaai we ina feoniufan; faiun foat kkewe regacch ina aeremesaen Mweoiu Naaeng; nge pwuger mwaaen kkewe, ina iir naiun Man Aenneew we;
MAT 13:39 nge man aenneew we e foatogi pwuger mwaaen kkewe ina Saetan. Nge oaton gin nge ina nee soapwonoan feoniufan, nge rhooan affeeoriun gin we ina iir angkenus.
MAT 13:40 Wunuunun pwuger mwaaen kkewe ra ioni fengaenniy nge ra figiir tae wooan aengaet, nge ina wunuunun minne epwe wen nee soapwonoan feoniufan.
MAT 13:41 Miniwe Naiun Aeremas epwene fangenoa naiun angkenus pwe repwe ioniir iyo kkewe reno noan Mweoiun iwe re paeni ngaeniir monofit, pwan rhooawe refeeori wegitaeg aenneew,
MAT 13:42 nge repwe oatoranong noan nenien aengaet, iga repwe sessaeng nge akkaarengi me ee.
MAT 13:43 Iwe rhooa mwamwaai repwene ttin taeppen aenet noan Mweoiun Semeer. Iyo eyor saeningan, epwe rongorong!
MAT 13:44 “Mweoiu Naaeng a pwan weei minneen. Erhai mwaaen enoa rhuungi eew pisaeg kooap egin rhaeng me wooan eew maat. A pwaniuw sefaaen noa nge noan aan kker a noa ameow noa oanongaen minikkena pisaegin, nge a sefaaen noa nge a noa meoni maat we.
MAT 13:45 “Mweoiun Naaeng a pwan weei minneen. Erhai mwaaen rhooan chuwaai nge e kiukkiutta fetaen faiun usowus kka nning,
MAT 13:46 nge igine a giuneei efai min igin yor ipitan, a noa ameow noa oanongaen pisaegin nge a meoni faiun usowus we.
MAT 13:47 “Mweoiun Naaeng a pwan weei minneen. Aaemweoi rhooan fita ra aekkaerh wow aar wuug noan meoneoiniun we nge ra niyap mesemesaen iig.
MAT 13:48 Oatowe wuug we a sseog reen iig, nge ra iuriunong nee ppiy, mwirin ra mooat tiw pwe repwe aemegena fesaenngiy iig kkewe: iig gacch ra iseni nong noan rhiug, nge iig kkewe re aenneew ra oatoranoa.
MAT 13:49 Epwe ieei wunuunun nee soapwonoan feoniufan. Angkenus repwene noa aeyimweoiuw fesaenngiy aeremas aenneew saengiir aeremas mwamwaai.
MAT 13:50 Repwe oatoranong aeremas aenneew noan nenien aengaet, iya repwe sessaeng nge akkaarengi me ee.”
MAT 13:51 Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Oaw metefaaegini oanongaen minikkaan?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Ooa.”
MAT 13:52 Iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Ina nge faaen minneei ina oanongeer sinsein anniug kka repwe no pwe rhooan kkayeo noan Mweoiun Naaeng ra taeppen rhag soaw iimw we e oatowowuw pisaeg mini ffeo me min maerhiy me noan soko we aan.”
MAT 13:53 Igiwe Jesus a moann aan fioangei fioangon awewe kkewe, a noa saengi pwiuneoi we
MAT 13:54 nge a noa nee pwugusan. A fenai noan wutteer Jews we, nge rhooawe re rongorong ngaeni ra riutae reen. Ra aeiineo, “Iya woneei a pwigi me ee aan tipaecchem me kkeman kka aan?
MAT 13:55 Ifa wusun, soapw woneei miniwe naiun taikusang we? Saapw Maria miniwe inan? Me saapw James, Joseph, Simon me Judas nge pwiin?
MAT 13:56 Soapw oanongeer mwengeyan nge reno igeei? Iya woneei a pwigi oanongaen minikkeei me ee?”
MAT 13:57 Iwe resa aetiwa no iiy. Jesus a aengaeniir, “Erhai profeta eyor aesirowun me noan oanongaen pwiuneoi, nge ese yor aesirowun me noan sipegin taeninimwan aere noan imwan.”
MAT 13:58 Pwe iga esooar aar niugiuniug, ina minne Jesus ese feeori towunepaen kkeman kkewe aan me igiwe reen.
MAT 14:1 Noan oatowe Erotes iwe soamwoonin Galilee a rongorong wunuunun Jesus.
MAT 14:2 A aengaeniir rhooan engaang kkewe naiun pwe, “Ieei iiy John Baptist, nge a menaw sefaaen. Ina faaen minne eyor maemaewan pwe epwe feeori kkeman kkeei reen.”
MAT 14:3 Pwe mmwan nge Erotes a akkiuneo pwe repwe torofi John nge ra geoni iwe ra oatoranong noan kanepwus. Erotes a feeori minneei faaen itaen Herodias iwe pwiuniuwaen Philip we pwiin.
MAT 14:4 Pwe John Baptist a fasiun aepini ngaeni Erotes pwe, “Ese fin ngaeniug oamw wopwe pwiuniuwaeni Herodias.”
MAT 14:5 Erotes e mwerhaen pwe epwe niiy noa John, nge e mesagiiur Jews pwe iga re iseni John pwe erhai profeta.
MAT 14:6 Nge raaenin gupwunon wupwutiwen Erotes, nge niewe naiun Herodias epwaai me weni mmweer rhooawe. Nge Erotes igin kker,
MAT 14:7 a ppwon ngaeni niewe pwe, “Iya aekkepan, pwe ngaang ipwe ngaenneog ese tiwegin meeta wo tingoar.”
MAT 14:8 Miniwe inan a akkiuneow pwe epwe tingoareei Erotes pwe, “Igina rhag nge wopwe ngaenneaei rhimwen John Baptist noan eew saepiy!”
MAT 14:9 Iwe rhag nge e aenneew noa tipaen king we, nge pwonno igiwe a aekkepan weni mmweer waseona kkewe, a aepesa pwe mwerhaen we aaen rhooapwut we naiun epwe mmwen.
MAT 14:10 Iwe a akkiuneo pwe repwe noa gopiy noa iiuwaen John me noan kanepwus.
MAT 14:11 Iwe, ra pwigito miniwe rhimwen John noan eew saepiy nge ra ngaenneei aeterhooapwut we, iwe niewe a pwigi noa reen niewe inan.
MAT 14:12 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun John ra itto pwigi miniwe oanongan nge ra noa paeia noa. Iwe nge ra noa aengaeni Jesus.
MAT 14:13 Igiwe Jesus a rongorong miniwe kkepesaen John, a tapweei efoarh pwoot saengi igiwe nge a noa ngaeni eew pwiuneoi ne iiy noa rhag. Nge igiwe aeremas ra rongorong miniwe, ra noa saengi aepinoamwoor nge ra tapweei noa mwirin me weni faniuw.
MAT 14:14 Jesus a teeotiw me wooan pwoot we, nge a giuneei pwuwaen aeremas kkewe, nge a igin faayeeor iwe a aecchipwaar tae rhooawe re semwaai me neeiir.
MAT 14:15 Noan faefin we nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra itto reen nge ra aengaeni pwe, “E igin anniug noa igeei, nge a pwan pwoong. Aefengaar noa aeremas kaan nee aepinoamw pwe repwe noa sipegin chuwaai aeneer mwongo.”
MAT 14:16 Nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Inamwo me rese noa, aaemi oawpwe ngaenneer meeta repwe mwongo!”
MAT 14:17 Nge iir ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Minne eyor remaem nge niffai rhag fenoawa me riiurhai iig.”
MAT 14:18 Iwe, Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Iwe oaw pwigito reei.”
MAT 14:19 Iwe nge a aepesa ngaeniir rhooawe pwe repwe mooat tiw wooan fetin kkewe. Iwe a pwigi fenoawa kkewe niffai me iig kkewe riiurhai, a fattae naaeng nge a fang aan maeipinen aerhigerhig Iwe a giniiy fenoawa kkewe nge a ngaenneer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun, nge iir ra inetiy ngaeniir aeremas kkewe.
MAT 14:20 Oanongeer nge ra maegin mwongo iwe ra faeyemwaai noa. Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra oawuta seig me ruwowu rhiug reen nuseg kkewe.
MAT 14:21 Iwe nepeer mwaaen kkewe re mwongo nge nimingeras, nge rese paaepae rhooapwut me wonigaet.
MAT 14:22 Iwe rhag nge Jesus a aepekkaar rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe repwe teeotae wooan pwoot we, nge ra gommwonoa epeig meoneoiniun we, nge iiy a aefengaar noa aeremas kkewe.
MAT 14:23 Mwirin aan aefengaar noa aeremas kkewe, Jesus a ittae wooan rhug we nge iiy rhag, pwe epwe noa maeipin. Igiwe a pwongonoa, a iiy noa rhag igiwe.
MAT 14:24 Reen oateen nge pwoot we a taaw saengi faniuw, a nuponup pwoot we reen tettemoagon noa, nge igiwe repwan maeyi ngaeni aaeng.
MAT 14:25 Enoa nepetaen enuuw me wonowu konook nee oatosor Jesus a itto reer rhooan kkayeo kkewe, enoa faaeraegto weei saaet.
MAT 14:26 Igiwe ra giuneei aan faaeraegto weei saaet, ra igin mesag. Ra aekkepwas pwe, “Erhai aniu!”
MAT 14:27 Noan rhag oaton een nge Jesus a kkepas ngaeniir pwe, “Oaw aemenetaegaemi! Ngaang minneei, oawte mesag!”
MAT 14:28 Iwe Peter a aepesa pwe, “Soamwoon, aere een minna, aengaeniaei pwe ipwe faaeraeg wow reemw wooan saaet.”
MAT 14:29 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Itto!” Iwe Peter a teeotiw me wooan pwoot we nge a faaeraeg noa reen Jesus weei saaet.
MAT 14:30 Nge igiwe a weri maemaewaen aaeng we, a mesag nge a rhaepetae aan mwotupwutiw. Iwe, a aekkepwas pwe, “Aemenewaeyaei Soamwoon!”
MAT 14:31 Iwe rhag nge Jesus a aeiti noa paiun, a ammwarhiu Peter nge a aengaeni pwe, “Me gaen mwittiginen oamw niugiuniug! Meeta wotip mwaramwar reen?”
MAT 14:32 Iwe ra teeotae wooan pwoot we, iwe nge aaeng we a maseoseotiw.
MAT 14:33 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe reno wooan pwoot we ra aesirowu Jesus nge ra aepesa pwe, “Ennetaen pwe een Naiun Deus!”
MAT 14:34 Iwe ra seraeg noa epeig meoneoiniun we nge ra noa itto noan me Gennesaret.
MAT 14:35 Aeremesaen pwiuneoi we re aeginna Jesus iwe ra aepesa noa wooan oanongaen faniuw pwe Jesus a no. Iwe aeremas ra pwigiir to oanongeer rhooa semwaai reen Jesus.
MAT 14:36 Ra tingoar ngaeni pwe aere uwen aar mwo man semwaai geotteopa soapwon mengaagiun. Iwe oanongeer iyo kkewe re geotteopa ra mamaaw noa.
MAT 15:1 Iwe aaemweoi Pharisees me sinsein anniug ra itto reen Jesus saengi Jerusalem nge ra aeiineow pwe,
MAT 15:2 “Meeta rhooan kkayeo kkomwu noawumw rese tapweei aar fenai rhaepeto kkewe aarh reen? Rese tapweei wunuunun toatoan pai mmwaen aar repwe mwongo!”
MAT 15:3 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Iwe ina meeta oawse tapweei aaen Deus anniug reen pwe oawwa tapweei ina kkomi?
MAT 15:4 Pwe Deus a aepesa pwe, ‘Wopwe aesirowuur semoamw me inoamw’ iwe me, ‘Iyo e oari seman aere inan nge repwe niiy noa.’
MAT 15:5 Nge aaemi oawwa aengaeniir aeremas pwe aere eyor minne erhai epwe tipaengi ngaeni seman aere inan, nge a iura pwe, ‘Ieen aaen Deus,’
MAT 15:6 nge ese aenneew igine ese aesirowu no seman. Ieei minne oawwa oatoranoa aaen anniug Deus pwe aaemi oawpwe feeori minna kkomi.
MAT 15:7 Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! A gin weneeti minne we Isaiah e fenaiuw pwe wunuunumi!
MAT 15:8 ‘Deus a aepesa pwe: Aeremas kkeei ra oassoamwooniaei rhag reen aar kkepas, nge nee tipeer a igin taaw saengiaei.
MAT 15:9 Esooar ipitaen aar aesirowuwaei, pwe re fenaiuw aar aeremas anniug, nge ra feeori pwe aetae gaen aaei anniug!’ ”
MAT 15:10 Iwe Jesus a faingiir to pwuwaen aeremas kkewe nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw aiussaening pwe oawpwe metaf!
MAT 15:11 Saapw meeta kka etonong noan ewaemi minne epwe aenimaenneewagaemi, pwe faer meeta kka etowow me noan minne a aenimaenneewagaemi.”
MAT 15:12 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra itto reen Jesus nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Wa giuneei pwe ra soong Pharisees kkewe reen meeta we wo aepesa?”
MAT 15:13 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oanongan waniwan kka miniwe Semaei noan naaeng ese foatogi epwe wiwiytae.
MAT 15:14 Oawsoapw niunniuwaenneer iir! Iir ikkomwu rhooa parh nge re paaepae rhooa parh. Ngaere erhai man parh e paeni pwan erhai man parh, nge iir me riiurhai repwe ppiungiunong nee niipw.”
MAT 15:15 Peter a aengaeni pwe, “Wopwe aemmetefa ngaenigemaem meeta faaen kkepas eei.”
MAT 15:16 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawsaaen metaf noa mwo?
MAT 15:17 Oawse metaf? Pwe meeta kka a toonong noan ewaemi pwan toonong noan upwaemi, mwirin a toowow me noan oanongaemi.
MAT 15:18 Nge meeta kka retowow saengi ewaemi rhaep saengi pwunnomi, nge ikkaan minikka e aenimaenneewagaemi.
MAT 15:19 Pwe saengi noan pwunnomi a toowow niunniuwaen aenneew taeppen, nni menaw, maiur ngaeni pwiuniuwaen erhai, ffeeor aenneew, mwoarho, oatupwutupw me aenneewa noa iteer aaemweoi.
MAT 15:20 Ikkaan minikka e aenimaenneewagaemi. Iwe nge erhai e mwongo nge ese tapweei wunuunun toatoan pai, minneen esoapw aenimaenneewagaemi.”
MAT 15:21 Jesus a noa saengi pwiuneoi we nge a noa noan faniuw kkewe oaron aepinoamwon Tyre me Sidon.
MAT 15:22 Erhai rhooapwuton Canaan e nonno pwiuneoi we a itto reen, nge a aepwesaegini pwe, “Soamwoon, Naiun David! Faayeowaei! Rhooapwut na naeyi a wartae aniu aenneew wooan nge a igin cchoaw noa.”
MAT 15:23 Nge Jesus ese aengaeni mwo eew petenaen kkepas. Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra itto reen nge ra tingoar gacch ngaeni pwe, “Aefenganoa nieei! Ettapw fetaen rhag me mwirirh nge e igin soaw oacchorong!”
MAT 15:24 Iwe Jesus a aepesa pwe, “Deus e aefengaeyaei to rhag pwe reer re Israel kkewe ra weer sheep kkewe re mwaenirh noa.”
MAT 15:25 Iwe rhag nge rhooapwut we a itto foatotiw weni mmwan nge a iura pwe, “Soamwoon, tipaengiaei!”
MAT 15:26 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ese mwamwaai pwe sipwe pwigi aeneer wonigaet mwongo nge sa oatora ngaeniir gonaag.”
MAT 15:27 Iwe niewe a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ennet minna, Soamwoon, nge gonaag mwo nge re angi peipeyin mwongo ppiungiutiw saengi aar maasta table.”
MAT 15:28 Iwe Jesus a paniuwaeni niewe pwe, “Een erhai rhooapwut e igin faeregit oamw niugiuniug! Meeta na oamw mwerhaen nge epwe yo ngaeniug.” Iwe noan rhag oaton we nge rhooapwut we naiun a takketae.
MAT 15:29 Jesus a noa saengi pwiuneoi we nge a noa faaeraeg ngaerhen meoneoiniuniun Galilee. A ittae wooan eew rhug a ittae mooat tiw.
MAT 15:30 Towunepaen aeremas kkewe ra itto reen, pwigito rhooawe re pirhemae, rhooa parh, rhooa maemerhoar, rhooa se kkepas, me pwan towunepaen aeremas kka re semwaai ra itto iseniir tiw oaron pirheen Jesus; iwe a aecchipwaar tae oanongeer.
MAT 15:31 Aeremas ra mwaar reen meeta we ra weri pwe igiwe rhooawe rese kkepas ra kkepas, rhooawe re maemerhoar ra mamaaw noa, rhooawe re pirhemae ra faaeraeg, pwan rhooawe reparh ra weri mmweer. Iwe, ra aepingepinga Deus we naiiur re Israel.
MAT 15:32 Jesus a faingiir to rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Ngaang iya faayeeor aeremas kaan, pwe ra no reei noan eoniuraen nge esooar meeta minne repwe angi. Ngaang ise mwerhaen aefengaar noa noan aar pecchai, pwe repwe tongaeni niyoarorhrorh iga repwe faaeraeg ngaeni imweer.”
MAT 15:33 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra aeiineow pwe, “Iya me noan pwiuneoi anniug noa eei minne sipwe weriwer mwongo me ee pwe epwe nap ngaeniir towunepeer aeremas kaan?”
