MAT 15:34 Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Fitifai fenoawa eyor reemi?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Fiusiufai fenoawa me fitiman iig mwittig.”
MAT 15:35 Iwe Jesus a aepesa ngaeniir aeremas kkewe pwe repwe mooat tiw weni ppweon.
MAT 15:36 A pwigi fenoawa kkewe fiusiufai me iig kkewe nge a fang ngaeni Deus aan aerhigerhig, a giniytiw nge a ngaenneer rhooan kkayeo kkewe, nge rhooan kkayeo ra ngaeniir aeremas kkewe.
MAT 15:37 Oanongeer ra mwongo nge ra faeyemwaai. Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra oawuta fisuuw rhiug reen nusegin mwongo kkewe.
MAT 15:38 Nneogeoiiur mwaaen kkewe re mwongo nge faangeras, nge rese paaepaenong rhooapwut me wonigaet.
MAT 15:39 Iwe Jesus a fangenoa aeremas kkewe, nge a teeotae wooan pwoot we nge a saei ngaeni miniwe faniuwaen Magadan.
MAT 16:1 Aaemweoi Pharisees me Sadducees ra itto reen Jesus pwe repwe aegina, iwe ra tingoareei pwe epwe feeori eew kkeman, pwe epwe pwae noa pwe Deus e tipieew ngaeni.
MAT 16:2 Nge Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Iga aenet epwe tupwutiw oawwa aepesa, ‘Epwe igin gacch raaen naiu, pwe a ccha noa noan naaeng.’
MAT 16:3 Nge nee oatosor moawugowug oawwa aepesa pwe, ‘Epwe igin piung worhow raaeneei, pwe a ccha me roorh noa noan mann.’ Oawwa mmwenen aepesa wunuunun raaen mwaai me raaen aenneew reen aaemi weri noan mann, nge oawsoapw mmwenen aweweei minikka aeginnen mweoi kkeei!
MAT 16:4 A ifa mwo aenneewan me aar se niugiuniug aeremesaen mweoi e igina! Oawwa tingoar ngaeniaei pwe ipwe feeori eew kkeman. Nge esoapw yor eew kkeman epwe pwae ngaenigaemi me niugiunoan kkeman we kkemenaen profeta Jonah.” Iwe nge Jesus a nigitiir a noa taaw noa.
MAT 16:5 Igiwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra noa epeig meoneoiniun we, ra maniuwegi noa pwe repwe pweipwog fenoawa.
MAT 16:6 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw atapeonneogiugaemi nge aefaennigaemi reen yeast we aar Pharisees me Sadducees.”
MAT 16:7 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra rhaepetae reen kkepas fengaen nee fineer, “A aepesa kkepas eei pwe iga sise pweipwog fenoawa.”
MAT 16:8 Jesus a giuneei meeta we ra aepesa, iwe a aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta oawwa fioangei nee finaemi aan esooar fenoawa reemi reen? Me gaen mwittiginen aaemi niugiuniug!
MAT 16:9 Meeta, oawsaaen metaf mwo? Oawse maengiy igiwe i giniiy niffai fenoawa wooar rhooawe nimingeras? Fitowu rhiug oawwa oawuta reen minikkewe nusegin mwongo?
MAT 16:10 Nge oatowe i giniiy fenoawa kkewe fiusiufai wooar rhooawe faangeras, fitowu rhiug oaw oawuta reen minikkewe nusegin mwongo?
MAT 16:11 Ifa wusun imwu oawse metaf pwe ise kkepesaen fenoawa ngaenigaemi? Oawpwe aefaennigaemi reen aar yeast Pharisees me Sadducees!”
MAT 16:12 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra metefaaegini pwe Jesus ese kkepesaen pwe repwe aefaenniir reen yeast we eno noan fenoawa, pwe saengi aar Pharisees me Sadducees fenai.
MAT 16:13 Jesus a noa ngaeni pwiuneoi we e arap ngaeni aepinoamwon Caesarea Philippi, igiwe a aeiineeor rhooan kkayeo kkewe me ee pwe, “Iyo ee aeremas ra aepesa pwe iiy Naiun Aeremas?”
MAT 16:14 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Aaemweoi re iura pwe John Baptist, nge aaemweoi re iura pwe Elijah, nge aaemweoi re iura pwe Jeremiah aere aaemweoi profeta.”
MAT 16:15 Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Nge aaemi, oaw iura pwe ngaang iyo?”
MAT 16:16 Simon Peter a paniuwaeni pwe, “Een Kristus iwe Naiun Deus iwe e menaw.”
MAT 16:17 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Wenepwu ngaeniug, Simon naiun John! Pwe kkepas eei ese itto reemw me reer aeremas, pwe Semaei noan naaeng minne e pwaeri ngaeniug.
MAT 16:18 Iwe ipwe aengaeniug pwe een Peter: een efai faai. Nge wooan wungaen fai een ipwe aiuwtae aaei keneisia wooan, nge maenoa mwo nge esoapw tongaeni oatoaropa.
MAT 16:19 Ngaang ipwe ngaenneog kkiaen Mweoiun Naaeng; minne oawwa feoti me feoniufan epwe pwan feofeo me wooan naaeng, nge minne oawwa saeneti me wooan feoniufan epwe pwan saenetaeg me wooan naaeng.”
MAT 16:20 Iwe Jesus a aetiwenig ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe pwe resoapw aengaeni mwo nge erhai pwe iiy miniwe Kristus.
MAT 16:21 Saengi rhag oatowe nge Jesus a rhaepetae aan aemmetefa ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Ipwene noa Jerusalem, nge ipwene noa waeiraes me reer mwaaen kkewe aar, me soamwoonin patere kkewe me rhooawe sinsein anniug. Repwe niaei noa, nge mwirin enuuw raaen nge ipwe menaw sefaaen.”
MAT 16:22 Iwe Peter a wummwuw noa egius nge a noa soong ngaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, esoapw ina minna! Esoapw mmwenen wen ngaeniug minna!”
MAT 16:23 Nge Jesus a toagun ngaeni Peter nge a aengaeni pwe, “Rhiuw me oaroi, Saetan, een rhooan pineyiaei. Pwe oamw niunniuwaen ese itto me reen Deus, pwe e itto me reen aeremas.”
MAT 16:24 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Aere erhai a mwerhaen tapweaei, epwe aerheei noa niunniuwaennen wooan oanongan, a aiufera aan kurus nge tapweeito mwiriy.
MAT 16:25 Pwe iyo e mwerhaen ammwarhiu menewan, epwe ppiung saengi; nge iyo eppiung saengi menewan pwonno ngaang, epwe giuneei menaw.
MAT 16:26 Epwe meeta ipitan aaen yo faeinaengiy nniuw noa ngaeni erhai, nge ese yo ngaeni menewan? Esooar ngaere! Esoapw yor meeta erhai epwe tongaeni fangenoa pwe epwe pwigi sefaaeniy menewan.
MAT 16:27 Pwe Naiun Aeremas epwe war noan nningen minna Seman me angkenus kkewe naiun. Enoa oatonaan nge a aesefaaeni ngaeni erhai me erhai aeremas wunuunun aan feoffeeor.
MAT 16:28 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe eyor aaemweoi aeremas igeei resoapw mae, toori oatona repwe weri Naiun Aeremas epwe wareto pwe King.”
MAT 17:1 Iwe mwirin wonowu raaen, Jesus a paenitae Peter me mwaaen pwipwi kkewe riiurhai James me John nge a wummwuur tae wooan eew rhug taegias, nge a iir noa rhag ee.
MAT 17:2 Igiwe re rhiuwen oawruru Jesus, nge a ssiuwen noa wunuunun: wooan mesan a weei seremaen ttinen aenet, nge mengaagiun a igin pwerheraeg noa.
MAT 17:3 Iwe nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe eoniurhai ra weri Moses me Elijah pwe re kekkepas fengaen me Jesus.
MAT 17:4 Iwe, Peter a aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Soamwoon, a igin gacch pwe sino igeei. Aere wo tipaeni, ipwe aiuwtae enuuw iimw tampwoning igeei, eew imwoamw, eew imwaen Moses, me eew imwaen Elijah.”
MAT 17:5 Igiwe Peter e rhiuwen kekkepas, eew toapw seram a itto pwaniiur noa, nge eew mangiungiu saengi toapw we a aepesa pwe, “Ieei Naeyi mwaaen aerhaengerhaeng, iye efin tipaei reen, oaw aiussaening ngaeni!”
MAT 17:6 Igiwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra rongorong kkepas kkewe, ra igin mesag, iwe ra tororhap tiw wooan ppweon.
MAT 17:7 Iwe Jesus a itto reer nge a geotteopaar nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawpwaetae, oawsoapw mesag!”
MAT 17:8 Iwe renoa fattae nge esooar ne re rhiuwen weri pwe a Jesus noa rhag.
MAT 17:9 Igiwe ra ittiw me wooan rhug we, Jesus a aetiwenig ngaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw aengaeni mwo nge erhai meeta oawwa weri, toori aaen mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas epwe menaw sefaaen me reen maenoa.”
MAT 17:10 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra aeiineow Jesus pwe, “Meeta sinsein anniug ra aepesa pwe Elijah epwe mmwaen itto reen?”
MAT 17:11 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Epwe fasiun gommwoto Elijah pwe epwe oamoannatae oanongaen aegiaeg.
MAT 17:12 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe Elijah a fasiun itto, nge aeremas rese aeginna, pwe refeeori ngaeni minne re tipaeni. Epwan ina rhag aar aeppaeti mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas.”
MAT 17:13 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra metaf pwe Jesus a kkepas ngaeniir reen wunuunun John Baptist.
MAT 17:14 Igiwe ra sefaaen ngaeniir pwuwaen aeremas kkewe, erhai mwaaen a itto reen Jesus, a foato pwiugiuwtiw me mmwan
MAT 17:15 nge a aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, faayeow aetemwaaen e naeyi! Egaen ngong nge a igin waeiraes nge a faaen ssow aan ppiungiunong noan aengaet me ne rhaan.
MAT 17:16 Iya pwigito reer rhooan kkayeo kkewe noawumw, nge iir rese mmwenen aecchipwatae.”
MAT 17:17 Iwe Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ifa mwo aaemi se niugiuniug me ruguppin faaen oateei! Epwe ifa ssiunaein aaei ipwe no reemi? Epwe ifa wusun aaei noaneenaei reemi? Oaw pwigito aetena reei!”
MAT 17:18 Jesus a aerh ngaeni aniu aenneew we, iwe a toowow me reen aet we, nge noan rhag oatowe nge aet we a cchipw tae.
MAT 17:19 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra itto reen Jesus igiwe a iir noa rhag nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta aemaem aeise mmwenen oatowowuw aniu aenneew we reen?”
MAT 17:20 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Pwonno iga e mwittig aaemi niugiuniug. Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe aere aaemi niugiuniug eweei nepaen faiun mustard een, emmwen oawpwe aengaeni rhug een pwe, ‘Wopwe mwagiut saengi igeei nge wa noa iginaan!’ nge epwe mwagiut. Emmwen oawpwe feeori ese tiwegin meeta.”
MAT 17:21 [Nge maeipin me aecchigipin rhag minne emmwen epwe asiuw wow taeppen een; esooar pwan eew meeta ne emmwen.]
MAT 17:22 Oatowe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra rhu fengaen me noan Galilee, Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas epwene yonong nee paiiur aeremas,
MAT 17:23 repwe niiy noa, nge mwirin enuuw raaen epwe menaw sefaaen.” A igin aenneew noa noan tipeer rhooan kkayeo kkewe.
MAT 17:24 Igiwe Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra toori Capernaum, rhooan iyoiyon tax reen Temple we ra itto reen Peter nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Ifa wusun, sinsei mwu naimi esoapw fang tax reen Temple we?”
MAT 17:25 Peter a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ewaer, epwe fang.” Oatowe Peter a toonong noan iimw we, Jesus a mmwaen kkepas, “Simon, meeta oamw niunniuwaen? Iyo epwe pey aegini ngaeniir kingaaen faniuw tax? Naiiur aeremas aere waseona?”
MAT 17:26 Peter a paniuwaeni pwe, “Waseona.” Iwe Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Aere ina, nge aeremesaen faniuw resoapw fang aar tax.
MAT 17:27 Nge sise mwerhaen sipwe aenneewa nee tipeer aeremas kaan. Iwe wonoa noan meoneoiniun we wa noa aerheei nong oamw ooa noan. Iwe nge mmwaen iig na wopwe nipaeni, wopwe sugi noa ewan, nge wa pwigi faiun senaapiy ina eno noan e nnaaf ngaeniaei tax reen Temple me oamw. Pwigi nge wa fang ngaeniir pwe aarh tax.”
MAT 18:1 Noan oatowe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra itto reen Jesus nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Iyo e oarosaen taegias me noan minna Mweoiu Naaeng?”
MAT 18:2 Iwe Jesus a faingito erhai wonigaet nge aiuwtae me weni mmweer.
MAT 18:3 Nge a aepesa pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, aere oawse ssiuwen pwe oawpwe weer rhag wonigaet, oawsoapw mmwenen toonong noan minna Mweoiu Naaeng.
MAT 18:4 Iyo na oarosaen taegias me noan minna Mweoiu Naaeng, nge iiy minne e oasossonaetiw pwe epwe aeffitaeg ngaeni wonigaet een.
MAT 18:5 Nge iyo e aetiwa erhai wonigaet faaen itaei, iiy epwan aetiwaeyaei.
MAT 18:6 “Aere erhai efeeori pwe erhai maan mwittig kaan epwe ppiung noa aan niugiuniug reei, nge efaer gacch pwe epwe geeogeeotae efai fai temoag faaen iiuwan nge ra noa oamoapwu noa nee metaw.
MAT 18:7 Ifa mwo aenneewaen faeinaengiy iga eyor rhag minikka e affeeori pwe epwe ppiung noa aar aeremas niugiuniug! Taeppen minikkaan nge repwe fasiun wen, nge ifa mwo aenneewan aeremas na erhaepiy tae minikkeei!
MAT 18:8 “Aere poawumw aere pirhemw re affeeori pwe epwe ppiung noa oamw niugiuniug, wa gopiy noa wa oatoranoa! Egacch oamw wopwe toonong noan menaw na esooar iyaenin wooan oamw pai efoarh me pirhe efoarh, mmwaen oamw wopwe pai riiufoarh aere pirhe riiufoarh nge ra aerheog nong noan aengaet we esooar iaenin.
MAT 18:9 Me ngaere mesoamw a affeeori pwe epwe ppiung noa oamw niugiuniug, wopwe oannusuwow wa oatoranoa! Efaer gacch oamw wopwe toonong noan menaw na esooar iyaenin reen oamw maseyefai, mmwaen oamw wopwe maseriufai nge ra aerheog nong noan aengaetaen nifierno.
MAT 18:10 “Oaw aefaenniy pwe oawsoapw aeffaeioapwut mwo nge erhai me neeiir aet mwittig kaan. Pwe ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe angkenusuur aetekkaan repwe wewweri rhag mesaen minna Semaei noan naaeng.
MAT 18:11 [Pwe Naiun Aeremas a itto, pwe epwe aemenewaar rhooawe re mwaenirh noa.]
MAT 18:12 “Meeta aaemi niunniuwaen? Aere erhai mwaaen eyor epwiugiuw naiun sheep, nge erhai neeiir a mwaenirh noa, iiy epwe nigititiw ikkiwe tiweig me tiweman wooan rhug we pwe epwe noa giutta iwe erhai e mwaenirh noa.
MAT 18:13 Ngaere a weri iwe erhai, ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, iiy epwe igin kker reen iwe erhai mmwaen ikkiwe tiweig me tiweman rese mwaenirh noa.
MAT 18:14 E aeffitaeg ngaeni rhag iga Semaemi noan naaeng ese mwerhaen pwe erhai mwo me neeiir man mwittig kaan repwe mwaenirh noa.
MAT 18:15 “Aere pwiimw a monofit ngaeniug, wopwe noa reen pwe wopwe noa pwaeri ngaeni meeta na teren, nge noan mwoanomwoan nepetaemi rhag riiurhai. Ngaere e aiussaening ngaeniug, een wa pwini sefaaeniy pwiimw.
MAT 18:16 Ngaere ese aiussaening ngaeniug, wopwe paeni erhai aere riiurhai rhinoamw, ‘pwe oanongaen kkepas nge rhooa na riiurhai aere eoniurhai repwe aenneta aere ennet,’ taeppen miniwe effoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus.
MAT 18:17 Iwe, aere ese mwerhaen aiussaening ngaeniir, wopwe pwaeri ngaeni rhooan keneisia. Aere keneisia mwo nge ese aiussaening ngaeni, iwe ina nge wopwe feeori ngaeni wunuunun minna wopwe feeori ngaeni erhai mane ese niugiuw Deus aere erhai rhooan iyoiyon tax.
MAT 18:18 “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi: minne oawwa feoti me feoniufan epwe pwan feofeo me wooan naaeng, nge minne oawwa saeneti me wooan feoniufan epwe pwan saenetaeg me wooan naaeng.
MAT 18:19 “Iwe, ipwe pwan aengaenigaemi pwe: aere riiurhai neeimi wooan feoniufan ra tipieew fengaen wooan aekkaew minne repwe maeipin wooan, epwe toorigaemi mmwenen me reen Semaei wooai naaeng.
MAT 18:20 Pwe iga riiurhai aere eoniurhai ra rhu fengaen pwe faaen itaei, ngaang ipwan no reer.”
MAT 18:21 Iwe Peter a itto reen Jesus nge aeiineow pwe, “Soamwoon, aere pwiiy a gaen monofit ngaeniaei, faaen fitowu ngaang ipwe saeneti noa aan monofit? Epwe faaen fisuuw?”
MAT 18:22 Nge Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Aapw, saapw faaen fisuuw rhag, pwe faaen fisiig me fisuuw.
MAT 18:23 Ieei minne Mweoiu Naaeng a aeffitaeg ngaeni. Erhai king a mwerhaen pwe naiun rhooan engaang repwene itto aera monofitiir ngaeni.
MAT 18:24 Oatowe ennaen rhaepetae ne feeori iiy miniwe, nge ra pwigito erhai nge e monofitini fitasenn mwo senaapiy.
MAT 18:25 Iwe iga rhooan engaang we ese mmwenen aera miniwe monofitin, iwe king we a aepesa pwe repwe ameow noa fengaen me pwiuniuwan me naiun me oanongaen meeta pisaegiir pwe epwe mmwenen aera minikkewe monofitin.
MAT 18:26 Iwe rhooan engaang we a foato pwiugiuwtiw me mmwaen king we nge aeffaenipirhe ngaeni pwe, ‘Faayeowaei, pwe wopwe tipenaei ngaeniaei. Ngaang ipwe aera sefaaeniy oanongaen monofitiy ngaeniug.’
MAT 18:27 Iwe king we a igin faayeow rhooan engaang we, iwe a saeneti noa aan monofit nge a fang pwe epwene noa.
MAT 18:28 “Mwirin rhooan engaang we a noa weri erhai rhinan rhooan engaang e monofit ngaeni fitowu rhag senaapiy. Iwe a torofi mwaaen we, a fiengi worongan nge a aengaeni pwe, ‘Wopwe aera sefaaen monofitimw ngaeniaei.’
MAT 18:29 Iwe rhooan engaang we a aesirowu tiw nge tingoar maaw ngaeni, ‘Wose mwerhaen wopwe faayeow ngaeniaei, ngaang ipwapw pey monofitiy ngaeniug!’
MAT 18:30 Nge mwaaen we ese mwerhaen. A aepesa pwe repwe oatoranong noan imwaen kanepwus toori aan epwe pey aegini monofitin.
MAT 18:31 Igiwe rhooan engaang kkewe rhinan ra giuneei meeta we a wen, ra igin soong iwe ra noa reen king we ra noa aengaeni oanongaen meeta we a wen.
MAT 18:32 Iweking we a faingito rhooan engaang we nge a aengaeni pwe, ‘Een erhai rhooan engaang kkewe re aenneew! Ngaang iya saeneti noa oanongaen oamw monofit ngaeniaei faaen itaen oamw tingoar ngaeniaei.
MAT 18:33 Meeta wose faayeow ngaeni rhinoamw rhooan engaang reen, taeppen rhag meeta ngaang iya feeori ngaeniug?’
MAT 18:34 Noan aaen king we igin soong, a fangenoa rhooan engaang we noan kanepwus toori aan epwe pey aegini oanongaen monofit kkewe aan ngaeni.
MAT 18:35 “Epwe ieen taeppen minne Semaei noan naaeng epwe feeori ngaeni erhai me erhai neeimi, aere oawsoapw saeneti noa monofitin pwiimi me noan tipaemi.”
MAT 19:1 Igiwe Jesus a moann aan aepesa oanongaen minikkeei, nge a siusaengi Galilee pwe noa ngaeni faniuwaen Judea me wenepeiginoan pwupwu we Jordan.
MAT 19:2 Pwuwaen aeremas kkewe rettapw noa mwirin, a aecchipwa tae me pwiuneoi we.
MAT 19:3 Aaemweoi Pharisees ra itto reen pwe repwe soatoni, nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Egacch me noan aarh anniug pwe erhai mwaaen epwe mweoi saengi pwiuniuwan reen minne rhag e tipaeni?”
MAT 19:4 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oawse aeraegi miniwe effoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus, pwe saengi rhaepetaen nge Deus a feeoriir aeremas pwe mwaaen me rhooapwut?
MAT 19:5 Nge Deus a aepesa pwe, ‘Ieei minne erhai mwaaen epwe nigiti seman me inan nge a noa rhuu ngaeni pwiuniuwan, pwe repwene eew rhag.’
MAT 19:6 Ina minne iir resoapw rhiuwen riiurhai no, pwe ra erhai rhag. Esooar erhai aeremas ne epwe mweoiti fesaenngiy meeta e Deus a oarhuw fengaenniy.”
MAT 19:7 Iwe, rhooawe Pharisees ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta rhag Moses a feeori anniug we pwe erhai mwaaen epwe mmwenen ngaenneei pwiuniuwan pwapwioron mweoinoa reen?”
MAT 19:8 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Moses a saeneti pwe aaemi mwaaen oawpwe mweoi saengi pwiuniuwaemi faaen itaen aaemi se rongorong ngaeni aan fenai. Nge ese ina wusun saengi rhaepetaen igiwe Deus efeeori feoniufan.
MAT 19:9 Nge ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi: aere erhai mwaaen a mweoi saengi pwiuniuwan faaen itaen aekkaew aegiaeg, nge soapw reen aaen niewe maiur ngaeni pwiuniuwaen erhai, iiy mwaaen we epwan feeori monofit aere a pwiuniuwaeni pwan erhai rhooapwut.”
MAT 19:10 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra aengaeni pwe, “Aere epwe ieei wusun nepetaen erhai mwaaen me pwiuniuwan, epwe faer gacch aarh sisoapw pwiuppwiuniuw.”
MAT 19:11 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Fenai eei nge ese noa ngaeniir oanongeer aeremas, pwe rhooawe rhag Deus a ngaenneer.
MAT 19:12 Pwe e towunap faan minne mwaaen rese gaen pwiuppwiuniuw reen: aaemweoi re wupwutiw pwe epwe ina wusuur, aaemweoi nge aeremas minne refeeoriir pwe resoapw pwiuppwiuniuw, nge pwan aaemweoi rese mwerhaen pwiuppwiuniuw pwonno faaen itaen minna Mweoiu Naaeng. Iyo e metefaaegini fenai een ina epwe metaf reen.”
MAT 19:13 Aaemweoi aeremas ra pwigiir to wonigaet reen Jesus, pwe epwe iseni tae paiun wooar nge a maeipinaar, nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra soong ngaeniir.
MAT 19:14 Nge Jesus a iura pwe, “Fangeto aetekkena reei, nge oawsoapw aiugiiur, pwe minna Mweoiu Naaeng ina aar aeremas kka reweer wonigaet.”
MAT 19:15 Iwe a iseni tae paiun wooar, iwe a mwet saengiir.
MAT 19:16 Eew oaton nge erhai mwaaen a itto reen Jesus nge a aeiineow pwe, “Sinsei, meeta min mwamwaai ipwe feeori pwe epwe yo ngaeniaei menaw na esooar iaenin?”
MAT 19:17 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Meeta wa faer aeiineowaei minne e mwamwaai reen? Erhai rhag minne e mwamwaai. Aere wo mwerhaen weri menaw, tapweei oasoapwosoapw kkeei.”
MAT 19:18 A aeiineo pwe, “Oasoapwosoapw kkefa?” Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Wosoapw nni aeremas, wosoapw ffeeor manetemwaai, wosoapw mwoarho, wosoapw oatupwutupw tae kkepas wooan erhai.
MAT 19:19 Wopwe aesirowu semoamw me inoamw, wopwe aerhaengi rhooan weni oaromw taeppen rhag oamw sipegin aerhaengi oanongoamw.”
MAT 19:20 Iwe anian we a aengaeni pwe, “Ngaang iya fasiun tapweei oanongaen oasoapwosoapw kkeei. E rhiuwen pwan yor meeta isaaen feeori mwo?”
MAT 19:21 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Aere wa mwerhaen wopwe oanongonniuwaen gin gacch, wa noa ameow noa oanongaen pisaegimw, nge wa fang senaapian ngaeniir rhooa affayeo, ina nge epwe yor wiinoamw me wooai naaeng. Iwe nge wa itto tapweaei.”
MAT 19:22 Igiwe anian we a rongorong miniwe, a siunoa noan aan tip aenneew, pwe igiwe iiy erhai man naiwiis.
MAT 19:23 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi: epwe waeiraes pwe aeremas kka re pisaegisaeg repwe toonong noan minna Mweoiu Naaeng.
MAT 19:24 Ipwe aepini sefaaeniy ngaenigaemi, egin mererhaeg aaen erhai camel epwe toonong noan ngetaen efoarh oaguwa, me mmwaen aaen erhai mwaaen pisaegisaeg epwe toonong noan minna Mweoiun Deus.”
MAT 19:25 Igiwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra rongorong kkepas we, ra igin riutae reen nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Iwe, iyo rhag epwe mmwenen menaw?”
MAT 19:26 Nge Jesus a fan wenewen ngaeniir nge a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Minneei ese mmwen ngaeni aeremas, nge oanongaen meeta nge emmwen ngaeni Deus.”
MAT 19:27 Iwe Peter a iura, “Pipiiy, aemaem aeiya siusaengi oanongaen aegiaeg nge aeiya itto tapweog. Iwe meeta aeipwe aeni?”
MAT 19:28 Jesus a aengaeniir, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe oatona mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas epwe mooat wooan nenien mooat na aan ina enning noan mweoi ffeo eei, nge aaemi rhoaniuwaei oawpwe pwan mooat wooan seig me ruwowu nenien mooat pwe oawpwe nemaeniir aeinang kkewe seig me ruwowu ikkiwe aaen Israel.
MAT 19:29 Nge iyo e siusaengi imwan, aere pwiin, aere mwengeyan, aere seman, aere inan, aere naiun, aere faniuwan, faaen itaei, epwe pwigi meoniun epwe temoag saengi epwiugiuw, nge epwe pwan pwigi menaw na esooar iaenin.
MAT 19:30 Pwe towunepeer rhooawe re amwirimwir repwene gommw, nge towunepeer rhooawe regommw repwene amwirimwir.
MAT 20:1 “Minna Mweoiu Naaeng eweei minneen. Eno erhai mwaaen a wugusoronoa epwe noa giut rhooan engaang pwe repwe engaang wooan aan maetaen grape.
MAT 20:2 A tipieew ngaeniir rhooan engaang kkewe pwe paniuweer nge epwe efai faiun silver noan eew raaen, iwe a fangenoa pwe repwe noa engaang wooan maetaen grape we aan.
MAT 20:3 Enoa tiwowu konook a sefaaen noa reen nenien chuwaai we nge a noa weriir aaemweoi mwaaen re iu fetaen, nge esooar meeta refeeori,
MAT 20:4 iwe a aengaeniir pwe, ‘Oawpwe pwan noa engaang noan maetaen grape na aaei, pwe ipwe ngaennegaemi paniuwaemi iye egacch.’
MAT 20:5 Iwe ra noa. Iwe nge enoa seig me ruwowu konook iwe pwan enuuw konook nge a pwan feeori taeppen rhag miniwe a feeori mmwan.
MAT 20:6 Enoa aerepa nimowu konook nee oanowas, a pwan noa noan nenien chuwaai we, nge a noa weriir aaemweoi mwaaen repwan iu fetaen igiwe. Iwe, a aeiineeor pwe, ‘Meeta oawwa iu fetaen rhag igeei, nge oawse engaang?’
MAT 20:7 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, ‘Esooar erhai ne e mwerhaen aengaengagemaem.’ Iwe, a aengaeniir pwe, ‘Oawnoa engaang noan maetaen grape na aaei.’
MAT 20:8 “Nge igiwe a pwoong noa, nge mwaaen we aan maat we a aengaeni soamwooniir rhooan engaang kkewe pwe, ‘Faingiir to rhooan engaang kkewe nge wa pey aeginiir, rhaepetae me reer rhooawe re amwirito toori rhooawe regommwoto.’
MAT 20:9 Mwaaen kkewe re rhaepetaen aar engaang reen nimowu konook, ra pey aeginiir reen efai silver nge paniuwaen erhai.
MAT 20:10 Iwe nge igiwe mwaaen kkewe regommw ra war pwe repwe pwigi paniuweer, ra niuwaennei pwe epwe temoag paniuweer saengiir, nge repwan fang rhag efai silver ngaeni erhai me erhai iir.
MAT 20:11 Igiwe ra pwigi paniuweer nge ra rhaepetae aar ngiuniungiuniuw wonowe aan maat we.
MAT 20:12 Ra aepesa pwe, ‘Mwaaen kkewe re amwirito, re engaang noan eew rhag awa, nge aemaem aeiya engaang waeiraes faaen aenet noan ffoarhon raaeneei, nge wa pwan aeffitaegiy rhag paniuweer ngaeni paniuwaemmaem!’
MAT 20:13 Iwe wonowe aan maat we a aengaeni erhai neeiir, ‘Maereyaerei, ngaang ise oatupwug. Een wo tipieew ngaeniaei pwe wopwe engaang noan eew raaen faaen itaen efai silver.
MAT 20:14 Igina pwigi paniuwoamw nge wa noa reen imwoamw. Ngaang i tipaeni ipwe pey aegini mwaaen enaaen itto nepaen rhag miniwe ngaang i ngaenneog.
MAT 20:15 Meeta, esooar maemaewaei pwe ipwe feeori meeta tipaei ngaeni naeyi senaapiy? Ngaere wopwai iga ngaang igin mmwoon?’ ”
MAT 20:16 Iwe Jesus a soapwei noa nge a aepesa pwe, “Ina minne rhooawe re amwirimwir repwene gommw, nge rhooawe regommw repwene amwirimwir.”
MAT 20:17 Igiwe Jesus a ittae Jerusalem, a paeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai nge a kkepas ngaeniir igiwe a iir noa rhag reen aar faaeraeg.
MAT 20:18 Iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw aiussaening. Sipwe ittae Jerusalem, nge aeremas repwene fangenoa miniwe Naiun Aeremas nee paiiur soamwoonin patere kkewe me sinsein anniug kkewe. Repwene apwiungiu pwe epwe maenoa,
MAT 20:19 nge ra fangenoa nee paiiur Gentiles, nge repwe aeni aegekkaei, repwe wirhiy nge re kurusuw noa; nge mwirin enuuw raaen epwe menaw sefaaen.”
MAT 20:20 Iwe niewe pwiuniuwaen Zebedee me mwaaen riiurhai kkewe naiun ra itto reen Jesus, rhooapwut we a foatotiw me mmwan nge a aengaeni tingoar we aan.
MAT 20:21 Jesus a aeiineow pwe, “Meeta wo tipaeni?” Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Wopwe ppwon ngaeniaei, pwe mwaaen riiurhai kka naeyi repwe mooat peig mwaaenemw me peig rhooapwutomw, iga aere wopwene no pwe een king.”
MAT 20:22 Jesus a aengaeniir rhooawe riiurhai pwe, “Aaemi oawse giuneei minne oawwa tingoar. Oawmmwenen iun me reen kkepaen aewwaeiraes e ngaang ipwe iuniumi?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Ooa, emmwen ngaenigemaem.”
MAT 20:23 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ooa, oawpwe mmwenen iun me noan kkap e aaei, nge soapw ngaang minne ipwe finitae iyo epwe mooat peig mwaaeneei me peig rhooapwutoi. Neniy kkeei nge nenieer rhooakkena minna Semaei a fasiun feeori pwe nenieer.”
MAT 20:24 Nge igiwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig ra rongorong kkepas kkewe, ra igin soong wooar mwaaen pwipwi kkewe riiurhai.
MAT 20:25 Iwe Jesus a faingiir oanongeer nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Aaemi oaw giuneei pwe rhooakka re nemaeniir re Gentiles ina eyor maemaeweer wooar, nge soamwoon kena aar minne re nemaeni ppagiiur noa.
MAT 20:26 Nge esoapw ieei wunuunun nee finaemi. Pwe iyo a mwerhaen taegias me neeimi, iiy epwe no pwe naimi rhooan engaang ngaenigaemi oanongaemi,
MAT 20:27 nge iyo a mwerhaen epwe gommw me neeimi, iiy epwe slave ngaenigaemi.
MAT 20:28 Epwe taeppen rhag Naiun Aeremas iye ese itto pwe aeremas repwe engaang ngaeni, pwe efaer itto pwe epwe engaang ngaeniir aeremas me fangenoa menewan faaen iteer towunepaen aeremas.”
MAT 20:29 Igiwe Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra mwet saengi Jericho, eew pwuwaen aeremas ra ttapw to mwiriir.
MAT 20:30 Iwe nge riiurhai mwaaen parh remooat wenepeigin aan we ra rongorong pwe Jesus a faaeraeg wooan aan we, iwe ra rhaepetae reen aar iyaekkepwas, “Naiun David, faayeogemaem menap!”
MAT 20:31 Nge rhooa towunap we ra soong ngaeniir nge ra aengaeniir pwe repwe anniug noa. Nge iir ra faer egius mwo nge oatomoga noa aar iyaekkepwas, “Naiun David, faayeogemaem menap!”
MAT 20:32 Jesus a iug noa nge a faingiir to. A aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta oawwa mwerhaen pwe ipwe feeori ngaenigaemi?”
MAT 20:33 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Menap, aei mwerhaen pwe wopwe aeffetanoa mesaemmaem!”
MAT 20:34 Jesus a igin faayeeor iwe a geotteopa meseer; reen rhag oatowe nge a ffatenoa meseer, iwe ra tapweei noa mwirin Jesus.
MAT 21:1 Igiwe Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra arap ngaeni Jerusalem, ra itto reen Bethphage reen rhugun Olives. Iwe nge Jesus a fangenoa riiurhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe
MAT 21:2 iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawpwe noa noan pwugos mwu mmwaemi, nge oawpwe noa weri erhai donkey e feotaeg iginaan fengaen me minna naiun eno oaron. Oawpwe pwaeisiir nge oawwa wummwuur to reei.
MAT 21:3 Nge aere erhai epwe aepesa eew meeta ngaenigaemi, oawpwe aengaeni pwe, ‘Soamwoon e mwerhaen waawa’; ina rhag nge epwe fangenoa iir.”
MAT 21:4 A wen minneen pwe epwe pwaeri noa miniwe profeta e aepesa:
MAT 21:5 “Aengaeni aepinoamwon Zion pwe: Emwaeri, a itto king we noawumw! Etip sessoan nge e waawa erhai donkey, erhai donkey mwittig, naiun erhai donkey.”
MAT 21:6 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra noa feeori meeta miniwe Jesus a aengaeniir.
MAT 21:7 Ra pwigito donkey we me miniwe naiun donkey we, ra iseni tae mengaagiiur wooar, nge Jesus a teeotae wooan.
MAT 21:8 Iwe rhooa towunap we ra mmeraeg noa mengaagiiur wooan aan we, nge aaemweoi ra gopogop tiw paeiniu pwe enenaen wooan aan we.
MAT 21:9 Towunepeer aeremas kkewe regommw me mmwaen Jesus, pwan rhooawe re tapweto mwirin ra aekkepwas pwe, “Sipwe aepingepinga Naiun David! Deus epwe aewenepwuwa aeremas na epwe itto faaen itaen Soamwoon! Aepingepinga Deus na oarosaen taegias!”
MAT 21:10 Igiwe Jesus a toonong noan Jerusalem, oanongaen aepinoamw we ra riu pwurhopwurh fetaen reen. Ra aeiineo pwe, “Iyo mwaaeneei?”
MAT 21:11 Aaemweoi aeremas ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Iiy profeta we Jesus saengi Nazareth noan Galilee.”
MAT 21:12 Igiwe Jesus a toonong noan Temple we, nge a asiiur wow rhooawe re chuwaai me ameomeo pisaeg me igiwe. A aerheppa noa table kkewe aar rhooan ssiuwen senaapiy me nenien mooat kkewe aar rhooan chuwaai pigeons,
MAT 21:13 nge a aengaeniir pwe, “E foatofoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus pwe Deus a aepesa pwe, ‘Temple e aaei epwe ffai pwe imwaen maeipin,’ nge aaemi oawwa ssiuweniy ngaeni eew nenien wopoor rhooa mwoarho.”
MAT 21:14 Iwe rhooa kkewe re masparh me rhooa pirhemae ra itto reen Jesus noan Temple we, nge a aecchipwaar tae.
MAT 21:15 Nge soamwoonin patere kkewe me sinsein anniug kkewe ra igin soong reen min amwaraar kkewe Jesus a feeorin, me pwan aar wonigaet kkewe re iyaekkepwas me noan Temple we pwe, “Sipwe aepingepinga Naiun David!”
MAT 21:16 Iwe ra aeiineow Jesus pwe, “Wo rongorong minikka wonigaet kaan ra aepesa?” Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ewaer, iya rongorong. Oawsaaen aeraegi mwo miniwe a foat noan Pwapwior we e Santus? ‘Aaemi oawwa oasuguunaar wonigaet me goagoa pwe repwe oassoara itoamw.’ ”
MAT 21:17 Iwe Jesus a nigitiir me Jerusalem, a noa ngaeni aepinoamwon Bethany. Iwe a noa no aegini epwoong igiwe.
MAT 21:18 Igiwe a sefaaeniti aepinoamw we noan soran we, nge Jesus a pecchai.
MAT 21:19 A weri waniwan we fig eno wenepeigin aan we iwe a faaeraeg ngaeni, nge a weri pwe esooar uwaan pwe rheon rhag. Iwe a aengaeni waniwan we pwe, “Esooar faaen eew ne wopwe rhiuwen uwa!” Noan rhag oaton we nge waniwan we a ppwass noa.
MAT 21:20 Igiwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra weri miniwe nge ra riutae nge ra iura pwe, “E ifa wusun rhag nge a noa mwetekkaein ppwass noa waniwan fig een?”
MAT 21:21 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe aere oaw niugiuniug, nge oawse tip mwaramwar, oawpwe mmwenen feeori meeta ngaang iya feeori ngaeni waniwan we fig. Nge saapw minneen rhag, pwe oawpwe pwan mmwenen aengaeni rhug een pwe, ‘Mwagiut saengi igeei nge wa noa oatoranoa oanongoamw nee metaw,’ nge epwe mmwen.
MAT 21:22 Aere oaw niugiuniug, nge oawpwe pwigi oanongaen meeta oaw tingoar noan aaemi maeipin.”
MAT 21:23 Igiwe Jesus a sefaaen nong noan Temple we, nge a fenai, nge soamwooniir patere kkewe me mwaaen kkewe aar ra itto reen nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta nemaenioamw pwe wopwe feeori minikkeei? Iyo a ngaenneog oamw nemenem?”
MAT 21:24 Jesus a paniuwaeniir, “Ngaang ipwe aeiineogaemi eew kkepas aeiineo, nge aere oaw paniuwaeni, ngaang ipwe pwan aengaenigaemi iya iga i pwigi aaei nemenem me ee pwe ipwe feeori minikkeei.
MAT 21:25 Iya e itto aaen John nemenem pwe epwe paptismus fetaen: saengi Deus aere saengi aeremas?” Iwe, ra rhaepetae aar aengimaw fengaen wooar, “Meeta sipwe iura? Aere sipwe iura pwe, ‘Saengi Deus,’ nge iiy epwe aeiineogirh pwe, ‘Meeta rhag oawse niugiuniug ngaeni John reen?’
MAT 21:26 Nge aere sipwe iura pwe, ‘Saengi aeremas,’ si mesagiiur aeremas, pwe oanongeer re niugiuniug pwe John nge erhai profeta.”
MAT 21:27 Iwe ra paniuwaeni Jesus pwe, “Aeise giuneei.” Jesus a aengaeniir, “Iwe ngaang isoapw pwan aengaenigaemi iya iga i pwigi me ee nemaeniaei pwe ipwe feeori minikkeei.
MAT 21:28 “Igina meeta aaemi niunniuwaen? Eno erhai mwaaen eyor riiurhai naiun mwaaen. A noa reen mwaaen we e tugufaeyi nge a aengaeni pwe, ‘Naeyi, wonoa engaang noan maetaen grape igina.’
MAT 21:29 Iwe nge iiy a paniuwaeni pwe, ‘Ngaang ise tipaeni ipwe noa.’ Nge mwirin a ssiuwen noa aan niunniuwaen nge a noa.
MAT 21:30 Iwe wonowe semeer a noa reen erhai naiun nge a noa aengaeni taeppen rhag iwe e aengaeni iwe erhai. Nge a paniuwaeni, ‘Ooa menap, ngaang ipwe noa,’ nge ese noa.
MAT 21:31 Iwe iyo neeiir rhooa ee riiurhai efeeori miniwe semeer e tipaeni?” Iwe, ra paniuwaeni, “Iwe e faeregit.” Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe rhooawe rhooan iyoiyon tax me rhooapwutoi chuwaai kkewe nge repwe toonong noan Mweoiun Deus me mmwaemi.
MAT 21:32 Pwe John Baptist a itto reemi nge a pwaeri ngaenigaemi aan na e mwamwaai, nge aaemi oawse niugiuniug reen. Nge rhooawe rhooan iyoiyon tax me rhooapwutoi chuwaai kkewe ra niugiuniug reen. Inamwo iga oawwa weri minneen, nge aaemi oawse ssiuweniy aaemi niunniuwaen pwe oawpwe niugiuniug ngaeni.”
MAT 21:33 Iwe Jesus a iura pwe, “Oaw aiussaening ngaeni pwan eew fioangon awewe. A yor erhai mwaaen e foatogi eew maetaen grape, a feeori gurun niugiun, a genengi eew niipw pwe nenien wongowongin uwaen grape we nge a aiuwtae eew imwaen poos taegias me noan. Mwirin a ngaenneer aaemweoi rhooan maat pwe repwe aefaenniy. Iwe rhag nge a saei taaw noa.
MAT 21:34 Nge igiwe a toori oaton gin, a fangenoa naiun rhooan akkiuneo reer rhooan maat kkewe pwe repwe noa pwigito inetin me reen uwaen grape kkewe.
MAT 21:35 Iwe nge rhooan maat kkewe ra torofi rhooan akkiuneo kkewe nge ra wirhiy erhai, ra niiy noa erhai nge ra tera iwe erhai.
MAT 21:36 Mwirin nge mwaaen we a pwan fangenoa aaemweoi rhooan akkiuneo re towunap saengi rhooawe mmwan, nge rhooan maat kkewe ra pwan feeori ngaeniir wunuunun meeta kkewe ra feeori ngaeniir rhooawe regommw.
MAT 21:37 Oarosan nge a fangenoa mwaaen we naiun reer, nge a iura pwe, ‘I niugiuw nge repwe aesirowu mwaaen e naeyi.’
MAT 21:38 Nge igiwe rhooan maat kkewe ra weri miniwe naiun, ra aepesa fengaenniy nee fineer pwe, ‘Ieen mwaaen we naiun mwaaen we aan maat eei iwe epwe pwugusaeni minneei. Oaw itto sipwe niiy noa, pwe sipwe pwigi minne pwugusaen pwe pwugusarh!’
MAT 21:39 Iwe ra torofi, ra oatorawow me niugiun maat we nge ra niiy noa.”
MAT 21:40 Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Igina, ngaere mwaaen we aan maat we a war, meeta epwe feeori ngaeniir rhooan maat kkewe?”
MAT 21:41 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Epwe niir noa rhooawe re aenneew nge a ngaenneer aaemweoi maat we iyo kka repwe mmwenen fang inetin uwaen grape kkewe oaton gin.”
MAT 21:42 Iwe, Jesus a aengaeniir, “Oawsaaen pwan aeraegi mwo meeta kkewe Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa? ‘Fai we rhooan kaiu iimw re aerheei noa, nge faer ina fai we egin yor ipitan me mmwaen oanongan. Minneen nge feeoriaen Soamwoon, a inamwo amwaraeran nningen!’
MAT 21:43 “Iwe, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe minna Mweoiun Deus nge repwe pwigi saengigaemi pwe repwe ngaenneer aeremas kka epwe mmwen epwe feeori uuwan.
MAT 21:44 [Iyo a ppiungiutiw wooan faai een nge epwe mwetoarotoar noa, nge aere faai een epwe ppiungiutiw wooan erhai, epwe aepettatiw.]”
MAT 21:45 Igiwe soamwooniir patere kkewe me Pharisees ra rongorong fioangon awewe kkewe, nge re giuneei pwe e aepesaar,
MAT 21:46 iwe ra aegina pwe repwe torofi. Nge re mesagiu pwuwaen aeremas kkewe, pwe iir re iseni Jesus pwe erhai profeta.
MAT 22:1 Iwe, Jesus a pwan kkepas ngaeniir aeremas kkewe noan fioangon awewe.
MAT 22:2 “Mweoiu Naaeng eweei minneen. Eno erhai king e oamoannatae aaen mwaaen we naiun gupwunon appwiuniupai.
MAT 22:3 A fangenoa naiun rhooan engaang pwe repwe noa faingiir to waseona kkewe repwe itto tapweei gupwun we, nge rese mwerhaen itto.
MAT 22:4 Mwirin a pwan fangenoa aaemweoi rhooan engaang pwe repwe noa aengaeniir aeremas pwe: ‘Igina, aaei gupwun a moannotae; naeyi wakke me man pwetaei kkewe naiiur ra niir noa, iwe oanongan nge a moannotae. Oaw itto tapweei gupwuneen.’
MAT 22:5 Nge rhooawe re faingiir rese tepa, iwe ra siunoa: erhai a noa ngaeni aan menaai, nge erhai a noa ngaeni aan nenien chuwaai,
MAT 22:6 nge pwan aaemweoi ra torofiir rhooan engaang kkewe, ra wirhiir nge ra niir noa.
MAT 22:7 Iwe king we a igin soong, iwe a fangenoa sonotaw kkewe pwe repwe noa niir noa rhooawe renni menaw iwe me figinoa aepinoamwoor.
MAT 22:8 Iwe a faingiir to rhooan engaang kkewe naiun nge a aengaeniir pwe, ‘Aaei gupwunon appwiuniupai a moannotae, nge waseona kkewe i faingiir pwe repwe itto tapweei gupwuneen nge ese fin pwe repwe itto.
MAT 22:9 Iwe oawnoa wooan ennap temoag kena pwe oawpwe faingiir to oanongeer aeremas kka oaw rhuungiir.’
MAT 22:10 Iwe rhooan engaang kkewe ra faaeraeg wow wooan ennap kkewe nge ra faingiir oanongeer aeremas kka re rhuungiir, ese tiwegin aere aeremas gacch aere aeremas aenneew, iwe a sseog noa imwaen gupwun we reer waseona.
MAT 22:11 “Igiwe king we a toonong noan iimw we pwe epwe pipiiy rhooan gupwun kkewe, a weri erhai mwaaen ese memmengaag min mwamwaai to reen appwiuniupai we.
MAT 22:12 Iwe king we a aeiineow pwe, ‘Maereyaerei, ifa wusun oamw toonong igeei, nge wose memmengaag min mwamwaai to reen appwiuniupai eei?’ Nge mwaaen we ese paniuwaeni.
MAT 22:13 Iwe king we a aengaeniir rhooan engaang kkewe pwe, ‘Oaw geoni paiun me pirheen nge oawwa oatorawow noan rorhappiung, iga epwe sessaeng nge akkaarengi me ee.’ ”
MAT 22:14 Nge Jesus a iura pwe, “Re towunap rhooawe re faingiir, nge fitiman rhag re finiir.”
MAT 22:15 Pharisees kkewe ra noa nge ra pwiungiuw fengaenniy pwe repwe aettefaeti reen aar kkepas aeiineo.
MAT 22:16 Ra fangenoa aaemweoi rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiiur reen Jesus me aaemweoi rhinaen Erotes. Nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Sinsei, aemaem aei giuneei pwe een wo aepesa minikka ennet. Wa fenaiuw minikka ennet pwe wunuunun nee tipaen Deus ngaeniir aeremas, nge wose niuwaennei minikka aeremas ra aeni niunniuwaen, nge wose niuwaennei wunuunun erhai me erhai.
MAT 22:17 Iwe, aengaenigemaem meeta oamw niunniuwaen. E mwamwaai aarh sipwe fang tax ngaeni Soamwoonin Rome, aere aapw?”
MAT 22:18 Nge Jesus e giuneei aar niunniuwaen aenneew, iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Meeta oaw mwerhaen pwe oawpwe soatoniaei reen?
MAT 22:19 Oaw pwaeri ngaeniaei senaapiy mwu oawpwe fang pwe tax!” Iwe, ra pwigito reen efai senaapiy.
MAT 22:20 Nge Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Mesaen iyo me itaen iyo een?”
MAT 22:21 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Soamwoonin Rome.” Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Iwe, oawfang ngaeni Soamwoonin Rome meeta aaen Soamwoonin Rome, nge oawfang ngaeni Deus meeta aaen Deus.”
MAT 22:22 Oatowe re rongorong kkepas we, ra mwaar noa reen, iwe ra siusaengi.
MAT 22:23 Noan raaenin we rhag nge aaemweoi Sadducees ra itto reen Jesus ra iura pwe aeremas resoapw menaw sefaaen me reen mae.
MAT 22:24 Iwe, ra aepesa pwe, “Sinsei, Moses a iura pwe ngaere erhai mwaaen a maenoa nge esooar naiun, ina nge mwaaen we pwiin epwe pwiuniuwaeni rhooapwut we pwe epwe yor naiun pwe epwe ffai pwe naiun mwaaen we a mae.
MAT 22:25 Iwe, eyor fiusiuman pwipwi re fasiun nonno igeei. Iwe mwaaen we e tugufaeyi a pwiuniuwaeni erhai rhooapwut, nge a maenoa nge esooar naiun, iwe a nigiti niewe ngaeni wonowe pwiin.
MAT 22:26 Taeppen rhag meeta we ewen ngaeni iwe ariiurhaiun me iwe aeiniurhaiun toori oanongeer noa rhooawe fiusiuman.
MAT 22:27 Mwirin noan, nge rhooapwut we a maenoa.
MAT 22:28 Iwe, noan raaenin na manimae repwene menaw sefaaen, iyo me neeiir rhooawe fiusiuman minne pwiuniuwaen rhooapwut we? Igiwe oanongeer nge re pwiuniuwaeni niewe.”
MAT 22:29 Nge Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Aaemi oawwa mwaerhei, pwe iga aaemi oawse giuneei oawton Pwapwior we e Santus ngaere minikkena maemaewaen Deus.
MAT 22:30 Pwe oate rhooa mae repwe menaw sefaaen, repwene aeffitaeg ngaeniir rhag angkenusun naaeng nge resoapw pwiuppwiuniuw no.
MAT 22:31 Iwe nge reer manimae iga repwe menaw sefaaen tae: esaaen yor mwo aaemi aeraegi meeta we Deus e aengaenigaemi? Iwe e aepesa pwe,
MAT 22:32 ‘Ngaang aaen Abraham Deus, aaen Isaac Deus me aaen Jacob Deus.’ Iiy aar Deus rhooakka re menaw, nge saapw aar Deus rhooakka remae.”
MAT 22:33 Igiwe pwuwaen aeremas kkewe ra rongorong kkepas kkewe, ra mwaar noa reen aan fenai.
MAT 22:34 Oatowe Pharisees ra rongorong noa pwe Sadducees kkewe ra iugiu noa pwe resa giuneei no minne repwe paniuwaeni ngaeni Jesus, iir ra rhu fengaen,
MAT 22:35 nge erhai me neeiir, erhai sinsein anniug, a aegina ne soatoni Jesus reen aan kkepas aeiineo.
MAT 22:36 A aeiineow pwe, “Sinsei, ifa oasoapwosoapw e oarosaen taegias me neeiin oanongaen Anniug?”
MAT 22:37 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Wopwe aerhaengi Soamwoon na oamw Deus reen oanongaen nee tipoamw, reen oanongaen ngeoniumw pwan reen oanongaen oamw niunniuwaen.
MAT 22:38 Ieei minne e oarosaen taegias me yor ipitan me neeiin oanongan oasoapwosoapw.
MAT 22:39 Nge oaruwowwaen oasoapwosoapw epwan taegias nge: ‘Wopwe aerhaengiir rhooan weni oaromw taeppen rhag oamw sipegin aerhaengi oanongoamw.’
MAT 22:40 Oanongaen aaen Moses Anniug me aar profeta kkewe pwapwior nge re oanongonong rhag wooan oasoapwosoapw kka ruwowu.”
MAT 22:41 Igiwe aaemweoi Pharisees ra rhu fengaen, Jesus a aeiineeor pwe,
MAT 22:42 “Meeta oaw niuwaennei reen Kristus? Iiy teoteeon iyo?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Iiy teoteeon David.”
MAT 22:43 Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta rhag nge Espritu Santus a aemeyaefi ngaeni David aan epwe faingi pwe ‘Soamwoon’? Iwe David a aepesa,
MAT 22:44 ‘Soamwoon a aengaeniaei Soamwoon pwe: Mooat tiw peig mwaaeneei toori aaei ipwe iseniir tiw rhooan oapwutoag faaen pirhemw.’
MAT 22:45 Iwe, ngaere David e faingi ngaeni pwe iiy ‘Soamwoon’, ifa wusun nge Kristus epwe no pwe teoteeon David?”
MAT 22:46 Esooar erhai ne emmwenen paniuwaeni kkepas aeiyeg kkewe aaen Jesus, iwe saengi rhag noan raaenin we nge esooar no ne e rhiuwen mwerhaen pwe epwe aeiineow aekkaew kkepas aeiineo.
MAT 23:1 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir pwuwaen aeremas me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe,
MAT 23:2 “Sinsein anniug me Pharisees kkewe minne rhooan aweweei Anniug kkewe aaen Moses.
MAT 23:3 Iwe oawpwe tapweei nge oawfeeori oanongaen meeta ra aengaenigaemi; nge oawsoapw appiuriu aar wegitaeg, pwe rese pomwoni meeta ra aeni fenai.
MAT 23:4 Re geonitae wooan sagiuriiur aeremas minikka ecchoaw nge e waeiraes pwe repwe aiufera, nge rese mwerhaen mwo nge repwe saeregi egatt aiuttiun paiiur pwe repwe tipaengiir reen aiufar.
MAT 23:5 Refeeori oanongaen meeta pwe aeremas repwe weriir. Oaw pipiiy minikkena eno wegisin Pwapwior we e Santus wooan ina ra geonitae wooan rhimweer me paiiur, nge e igin tettemoagon! Oaw pipiiy enaeyin minikkena maetetteren weni ngaerhen mengaagiiur!
MAT 23:6 Re aerhaengi neniy kkena egacch noa me noan gupwun me pwan neniy kkena nenieer rhooa taegias me noan wutteer Jews,
MAT 23:7 repwan aerhaengi aar aeremas repwe aewenimmwaar me aesirowuur me noan imwaen chuwaai, me aar aeremas repwe faingiir pwe ‘Sinsei’.
MAT 23:8 Nge aaemi oawsoapw ffai pwe ‘Sinsei’, pwe erhai rhag aaemi Sinsei, nge oanongaemi nge oaw pwipwi.
MAT 23:9 Oawsoapw faingi mwo nge erhai me wooan soanopeei pwe ‘Saam’, pwe iga erhai rhag Semaemi eno wooai naaeng.
MAT 23:10 Oawsoapw pwan ffai pwe aaemi ‘Rhooan a Wen’, pwe iga pwan erhai rhag aaemi rhooan a wen imwu iiy Kristus.
MAT 23:11 Iyo e egin taegias noa me neeimi nge iiy epwe no pwe naimi rhooan akkiuneo.
MAT 23:12 Pwe iyo na e aetaegiasa tae epwe sessoanotiw, nge iyo na epwe oasossonaetiw epwe taegias tae.
MAT 23:13 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi sinsein anniug me Pharisees! Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Oawttiy noa aesemaen Mweoiu Naaeng saengiir aeremas. Nge aaemi oawse toonong noan, oawse pwan fang ngaeniir mwo nge rhooawe re tipaeni repwe toonong.
MAT 23:14 [Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi sinsein anniug me Pharisees! Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Oaw oapwurhaar rhooapwut kka a mae pwiuniuweer, nge oawwa pwigi saengiir imweer, nge oawwa oangonongon ngaeniir aeremas aaemi maeipin enaei. Reen minneei minne Deus epwe fang ngaenigaemi aegaeregaer na oarosaen cchoaw.]
MAT 23:15 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi sinsein anniug me Pharisees! Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Aaemi oawwa seraeg fetaen nee metaw pwan wooan oanongaen faniuw pwe minni oawpwe wegiti tipaen erhai aeremas ngaeni aaemi namanam; nge aere iga emmwen minneen, aaemi oawwa feeori pwe iiy epwe faer kkaein noa aaen aegaeregaer me mmwaemi me noan nifierno.
MAT 23:16 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi rhooan afan parh! Oaw aepesa pwe, ‘Aere erhai a aekkepan faaen itaen Temple we, miniwe nge esooar ipitan. Nge aere a aekkepan faaen itaen goon we noan Temple we, iiy epwene feeori meeta we a aeni ppwon.’
MAT 23:17 Aaemi masepwurh masparh! Ifa minne e igin yor ipitan, goon aere Temple we efeeori goon we pwe epwe pin?
MAT 23:18 Aaemi oawpwan aepesa pwe, ‘Aere erhai a aekkepan faaen itaen antar we, miniwe nge esooar ipitan. Nge aere a aekkepan faaen itaen niffang kkewe wooan antar we, iiy epwene feeori meeta we a aeni ppwon.’
MAT 23:19 Masperhaemi! Meeta e igin yor ipitan, niffang we aere antar we efeeori niffang we pwe epwe pin?
MAT 23:20 Iwe, ngaere erhai a aekkepan faaen itaen antar we, a aekkepan faaen itaen antar we me oanongaen niffang kena eno wooan.
MAT 23:21 Nge ngaere erhai a aekkepan faaen itaen Temple, a aekkepan faaen itaen Temple we nge a pwan aekkepan faaen itaen Deus iwe eno noan.
MAT 23:22 Nge ngaere erhai a aekkepan faaen itaen naaeng, ina a aekkepan faaen itaen nenien mooat we aaen Deus me pwan faaen itaen Deus iwe emooat wooan.
MAT 23:23 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi sinsein anniug me Pharisees! Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Oaw ngaenneei Deus eew ginigin me noan seig reen mint me dill me cumin. Iwe nge oaw aerheei noa Anniug kkewe eyor ipitan me reen oasoapwosoapw, taeppen awewe mwamwaai me faayeow me ennet. Ikkeei anniug kka oawpwe pomwoni, nge oawsoapw nigiti noa ikkina aekkaew.
MAT 23:24 Aaemi rhooan afan parh! Oaw tipwei wow erhai nnoang me noan minimwu iuniumaemi, nge oawwa faer woromi noa erhai camel!
MAT 23:25 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi sinsein anniug me Pharisees! Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Oaw toafi gacchiuw niugiun aaemi kkap me saepiy, nge noan a sseog noa reen fitigogo me tipinap.
MAT 23:26 Masperhaemi, aaemi Pharisees! Oawpwe mmwaen toafi gacchiuw noan kkap we pwe ina nge niugiun epwan nimegacch noa.
MAT 23:27 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi sinsein anniug me Pharisees! Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Oawweei rhag taeppen pwerheraegin paeyi kka enning niugiun, nge noan a sseog noa reen rhiun aeremas me pwotoron manimae.
MAT 23:28 Epwan taeppen rhag aaemi: me niugiun oawnning faaen meseer aeremas, nge noan nge a sseog noa reen oatupwutupw me monofit.
MAT 23:29 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi, aaemi sinsein anniug me Pharisees! Aaemi rhooa oatupwutupw! Oawfeeori paeyieer rhooawe profeta pwe epwe gacch, nge oawwa awweoniuwa faiun paeyieer rhooawe rhooa mwamwaai.
MAT 23:30 Oawwa aepesa pwe, ‘Aere aemaem aei menaw noan oaton we rhaepetomaem re rhiuwen menaw, aemaem aeisoapw tapweer reen niir noa profeta kkewe.’
MAT 23:31 Iwe oawwa sipegin pwaeritae pwe aaemi teoteeor rhooawe reniir noa profeta kkewe!
MAT 23:32 Iwe oawnoa pwan soapwei noa meeta minikkewe aaemi rhaepeto rerhaepiy tae!
MAT 23:33 Aaemi sowufaeng me naiiur sowufaeng! Epwe ifa wusun aaemi kkewaeg saengi aaemi aegaeregaer noan nifierno?
MAT 23:34 Ieei minne ipwe fang wow reemi profeta me soaw tipaecchem me sinsei; aaemi oawpwe niir noa aaemweoi, oaw kurusuur noa aaemweoi, oawpwan wirhiy aaemweoi me noan wutteer Jews nge oaw fattapweer noa me reen eew me eew aepinoamw kkena.
MAT 23:35 Ieei minne epwe ittiw woami eew aegaeregaer faaen iteer rhooa kkewe mwamwaai iwe oawniir noa, saengi nni menaw noan mwaaen mwamwaai we Abel toori Zechariah iwe naiun Berechiah, mwaaen we oawniiy noa me nepetaen Temple we me antar we.
MAT 23:36 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi: aegaeregaerin oanongaen nni menaw kkewe nge epwe tooriir aeremesaen mweoi e igina.
MAT 23:37 “Jerusalem, Jerusalem! Wa niir noa profeta kkewe nge wo teraar rhooan pweipwogin kkepas kkewe Deus efangeto reemw! A faaen fiteig aaei mwerhaen pwe ipwe ioni fengaenniy noawumw aeremas, taeppen maniug a ioni fengaenniy naiun faaen paiun, nge een wose mwerhaen pwe ipwe feeori!
MAT 23:38 Iwe Temple we aaemi ina aeremas repwe siusaengi iwe peonoa.
MAT 23:39 Pwe ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe saengi igina oawsoapw rhiuwen weriaei no toori oawpwe iura pwe, ‘Deus epwe aewenepwuwa aeremas na epwe itto faaen itaen Soamwoon.’ ”
MAT 24:1 Igiwe Jesus a siusaengi Temple we, rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra itto reen nge ra pwaeri ngaeni iimw kkewe noan Temple we.
MAT 24:2 Nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ooa, oawwa weri oanongan minikkaan. Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi: esooar efai faai kaan ne epwe notiw nenien; oanongan noa nge repwene toaropotiw.”
MAT 24:3 Igiwe Jesus a mooat wooan miniwe rhugun Olives, rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra itto reen nge iir noa rhag. Ra aeiyeg ngaeni pwe, “Aengaenigemaem ineeta minikkeei epwe wen, me meeta aegin epwe pwaeri noa oamw itto me soapwonoan feoniufan?”
MAT 24:4 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oaw aefaennigaemi, pwe esoapw yor erhai epwe oatupwugaemi.
MAT 24:5 Towunepeer aeremas repwe itto faaen itaei nge re aepesa pwe, ‘Ngaang Kristus!’ Iwe, repwe oatupwuur noa pwuwaen aeremas.
MAT 24:6 Oawpwe rongorong oacchorongon moawun arapeto me kkepesaen moawun taaw noa, nge oawsoapw mesag. Oatokkeei nge minikkeei nge repwe fasiun wen, nge saapw reen a arapeto ne soapwonoan.
MAT 24:7 Faniuw me faniuw repwe fiiow fengaen, nge mweoi me mweoi repwe pwan moawun fengaen. Epwe yor naengeta me fanemwar oanongaen pwiuneoi.
MAT 24:8 Oanongaen minikkaan nge eweei pweoneotaen metaegin erhai rhooapwut iga epwe nainai.
MAT 24:9 “Iwe repwe torofigaemi nge refang noa aaemi repwe noa aewwaeiraesigaemi nge ra nigaemi noa. Oanongeer aeremas repwe oapwutaegaemi pwonno faaen itaei.
MAT 24:10 Reen oatona nge towunepeer repwene fangetae aar niugiuniug; nge re afangmaei erhai nge re kkoapwut fengaen nee fineer.
MAT 24:11 Iwe towunepeer profeta oatupwutupw repwe itto nge ra oatupwuur noa pwuwaen aeremas.
MAT 24:12 Pwonno iga a temoag noa feoffeeor aenneew, aerhaengerhaeng we nepetaen aeremas epwene mwittig noa.
MAT 24:13 Nge iyo e aetemaegin toori nee soapwonoan nge epwe menaw.
MAT 24:14 Nge Kkepas Mwamwaai we reen Mweoiu Naaeng repwe noa fenaiuw wooan oanongaen faniuw, pwe epwe pwae ngaeniir oanongaen aeremas, iwe mwirin epwapw itto nee soapwonoan.
MAT 24:15 “Oawpwe weri eew Min Oarosaen Aemmesagsag, iwe profeta Daniel a kkepas faaen itan. Epwe no noan pwiuneoi we epin.” (Ngaeni rhooan aeraegraeg: metefaaegini minneen!)
MAT 24:16 “Iwe rhooawe reno Judea repwe fattapwetae weei rhug.
MAT 24:17 Erhai ne eno wooan wungaen iimw, esoapw teeotiw pweipwog pisaegin me nee iimw.
MAT 24:18 Nge erhai ne eno noan maat, esoapw sefaaen ngaeni imwan pwe epwe pweipwog mengaagiun.
MAT 24:19 Epwe ifa mwo aar affayeo rhooapwut pwoopwo me ikka re nayigit noan oaton naan!
MAT 24:20 Oawpwe maeipin ngaeni Deus pwe aaemi siunoa esoapw itto noan oaton patapat aere noan raaenin Sabbath!
MAT 24:21 Pwe waeiraesin oatonaan ina epwe faer igin kkaein saengi oanongaen waeiraes kka enoa itto reen oatowe supwuton faniuw toorito igina. Nge esoapw rhiuwen yor taeppen epwe rhiuwen itto.
MAT 24:22 Nge Deus a fasiun oamworhomworha nepaen raaen; ngaere ese feeori, nge esooar ne epwe menaw. Nge pwonno faaen iteer rhooawe a finiir tae, Deus a oamworhomworhanoa nepaen raaen.
MAT 24:23 “Iwe, ngaere erhai e aepesa ngaenigaemi pwe, ‘Pipiiy, ieei iiy Kristus!’ aere ‘Inaan iiy!’ oawsoapw niugiuniug ngaeni.
MAT 24:24 Pwe aaemweoi aeremas repwene oatupwutupw pwe iir Kristus, aere erhai profeta, nge repwene feeori min amwaraar me manaman tettemoag, pwe repwe oatupwu rhooawe Deus a finiir tae aere repwe mmwenen feeori.
MAT 24:25 Oaw rongorong! Ngaang iya fasiun pwaeri ngaenigaemi oanongaen minikkeei mmwaen aar repwe wen.
MAT 24:26 “Iwe aere erhai epwe aengaenigaemi pwe, ‘Pipiiy, a no noan desert!’, oawsoapw noa iginaan. Ngaere re aepesa, ‘Pipiiy, iiy ewop igeei!’, oawsoapw niugiuniug ngaeni.
MAT 24:27 Pwe mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas epwe itto taeppen rhag weriwer iga e ffiunoa noan naaeng saengi rhag eotiw toori netow.
MAT 24:28 “Ese tiwegin igine epwe yor erhai manimae ee, nge witiyas repwe mweoiuto reen.
MAT 24:29 “Mwirin rhag moanno noan aewwaeiraesin noan raaenin kkewe, aenet epwene rorhonoa, meram esoapw rhiuwen ttin, nge fiiu repwene ppiungiutiw me noan naaeng, nge minikkiwe maemaewaen noan naaeng repwene mwagiut saengi nenieer.
MAT 24:30 Iwe nge miniwe aeginnen Naiun Aeremas epwe pwae noa me noan naaeng; nge oanongeer aeremesaen faniuw repwe sessaeng aar repwe giuneei miniwe Naiun Aeremas aan itto wooan toapw noan minna maemaewan me nningen ina e temoag.
MAT 24:31 Nge epwe fangenoa naiun angkenus reen nngiun ttigin rappwa we, nge repwene ioni fengaenniy rhooawe Deus a finiir saengi faawu pwaeisiisin faeinaengiy, saengi esoapw naaeng toori esoapw.
MAT 24:32 “Oawpwe kapwiung saengi waniwan e fig. Oate minikkena raaen ra arawaraw me mechecchoar noa nge a pwiugiuw wow rheon, oawwa giuneei pwe a arapeto neraeg.
MAT 24:33 Epwan taeppen rhag, igine oawweri minikkeei pwe a wen, oawpwene giuneei pwe oatowe ina a arapeto, oamoannatae pwe epwene rhaep.
MAT 24:34 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe oanongaen minikkeei nge epwe wen weni mmwaen iga aeremesaen igina repwe maenoa.
MAT 24:35 Naaeng me soanop repwe soapwonoa, nge aaei kkepas esoapw soapwonoa.
MAT 24:36 “Esooar erhai ne e giuneei raaenin aere awa aan epwe itto, angkenusun naaeng mwo nge resoapw giuneei, aere miniwe Naiun, pwe aaen Saam rhag.
MAT 24:37 Pwe itton mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas epwe taeppen rhag meeta a wen noan oaton Noah.
MAT 24:38 Noan raaenin kkewe mmwaen noataer we, aeremas re mwommwongo nge kukkupwun, mwaaen me rhooapwut re pwiuppwiuniuw toori noan raaenin we Noah a teeotae wooan pwoot we.
MAT 24:39 Rese giuneei minne epwe wen toori aaen noataer we itto niir noa oanongeer. Ina wunuunun minne epwe wen oate Naiun Aeremas epwe war.
MAT 24:40 Iwe nge riiurhai mwaaen re engaang wooan maat: erhai repwe pwigi noa nge erhai epwe notiw.
MAT 24:41 Riiurhai rhooapwut repwe ammaat mwongo; erhai repwe pwigi noa nge erhai epwe notiw.
MAT 24:42 Ieei minne oawpwe aefaennigaemi reen, pwe oawsoapw giuneei noan raaen fa minne aaemi Soamwoon epwe wareto.
MAT 24:43 Nge oawpwe metaf pwe ngaere soaw iimw we e giuneei ineet rhooa mwoarho we epwe itto, pwe iiy epwe mmas noa rhag, nge esoapw fang ngaeni rhooa mwoarho we aan epwe fereeinong iimw we imwan.
MAT 24:44 Ieei minne pwan aaemi, oawpwe moannotae, pwe mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas epwe noa itto reen eew oat ina aaemi oawse tapeonneog reen.
MAT 24:45 “Iwe, iyo rhag rhooan akkiuneo we e wenewen nge e reepiy? Iiy minne maasta we a fang ngaeni pwe epwe nemaeniir rhooan akkiuneo kkewe nge e ngaenneer mwongo noan oaton efin.
MAT 24:46 Ifa mwo wenepwuwaen rhooan akkiuneo we, aere maasta we aan e itto giuneei aan feeori minikkeei igiwe ewar.
MAT 24:47 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe maasta we epwe ngaenneei rhooan akkiuneo we pwe epwe nemaeni oanongaen minikkewe pisaegin.
MAT 24:48 Nge aere rhooan akkiuneo we e aenneew, epwe niuwaennei nong noan tipan, ‘Maasta we aaei epwe mmwaei aan sefaaeneto,’
MAT 24:49 nge epwene rhaepetae aan wirhiir rhooan akkiuneo kkewe rhinan, nge e mwongo me gupwun fengaen me aaemweoi man pwunaas.
MAT 24:50 Mwirin maasta we epwe sefaaeneto noan raaenin we rhooan akkiuneo we ese niuwaennei, me eew oaton esoapw giuneei.
MAT 24:51 Iwe maasta we epwene fena kititiw nge efang noa neeiir rhooawe rhooa oatupwutupw. Igiwe epwe sessaeng me akkaarengi me ee.
MAT 25:1 “Reen oaton naan nge minna Mweoiu Naaeng epwe aeffitaeg ngaeni minneen. Eno seig rhooapwut anian re pwigi aar oappwun nge ra noa soawuni erhai bridegroom.
MAT 25:2 Nimman me neeiir re tipoarorh, nge nimman re tipaecchem.
MAT 25:3 Rhooawe re tipoarorh ra pwigi aar oappwun, nge rese pwigi oatoawun rhaniun oappwun kkewe aar,
MAT 25:4 nge ikkiwe re tipaecchem ra pwigi aar oappwun fengaen me neon rhaniun oappwun kkewe aar.
MAT 25:5 Iwe igiwe bridegroom e mmwaei aan itto, iwe ra cchoaw iwe ra maiur noa.
MAT 25:6 “Igiwe a nugaenipwoong noa nge a yor eew aekkepwas, ‘Ieen iiy bridegroom we! Oaw itto oawpwe rhuungi!’
MAT 25:7 Iwe rhooapwut kkewe seig ra mmasetae nge ra oamoannatae oappwun kkewe aar.
MAT 25:8 Iwe, rhooawe re tipoarorh ra aengaeni rhooawe re tipaecchem pwe, ‘Oawfang ngaenigemaem egius rhaniun oappwun, pwe oappwun kka aemaem nge repwene gunnoa.’
MAT 25:9 Nge rhooawe re tipaecchem ra paniuwaeniir pwe, ‘Ese mmwen, pwe iye esoapw nnaaf aaemi me pwan aemaem. Oawnoa sitowa oawpwe noa chuwaai aaemi rhaniun oappwun.’
MAT 25:10 Iwe rhooawe re tipoarorh ra noa pwe repwe noa chuwaai aar rhaniun oappwun. Nge igiwe ra noa, iwe nge bridegroom we a war. Iwe, rhooawe nimman rhooapwut re moannotae ra tapweei nong noan imwaen gupwun we, iwe mwirin iwe a titti noa asam we.
MAT 25:11 “Mwirin nge rhooapwut kkewe aaemweoi ra pwan war. Iwe, ra iyaekkepwas, ‘Soamwoon, soamwoon, sugi ngaenigemaem asam.’
MAT 25:12 “Iwe nge bridegroom we a paniuwaeniir pwe, ‘Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, ise giunegaemi.’ ”
MAT 25:13 Iwe Jesus a soapwei noa nge a iura pwe, “Oawpwe atapeonneogiugaemi, pwe oawse giuneei raaenin me awaan.
MAT 25:14 “Noan oaton naan nge Mweoiu Naaeng epwe aeffitaeg ngaeni minneen. Eno erhai mwaaen epwene noa waeii; a faingiir rhooan engaang kkewe naiun nge a aengaeniir pwe repwe nemaeni oanongaen minikkewe pwugusan.
MAT 25:15 A ngaenneei erhai me erhai iugiugiun minne epwe mmwen ngaeni: a ngaenneei erhai nimingeras faiun senaapiy, nge a ngaenneei pwan iwe erhai riiungeras, nge iwe erhai eew sengeras. Iwe a noa waeii noa.
MAT 25:16 Iwe rhag nge rhooan engaang we e pwigi nimingeras faiun senaapiy a mwetekkaein noa aengaenga iwe reen, iwe a pwan pwigi sefaaeniy pwan nimingeras menewan.
MAT 25:17 Epwan ina rhag wunuunun iwe e pwigi riiungeras pwe a pwan pwigi sefaaeniy pwan riiungeras menewan.
MAT 25:18 Nge rhooan engaang we e pwigi sengeras faiun senaapiy, a noa genengi eew niipw nge a nipwaeni noa faiun senaapiy we naiun maasta we aan noan.
MAT 25:19 “A ssiunaei noa mwirin nge maasta we a sefaaen to nge a aeiyegiir senaapiy kkewe naiun.
MAT 25:20 Iwe rhooan engaang we e pwigi nimingeras faiun senaapiy a itto nge a iseni tiw pwan nimingeras. A aepesa pwe, ‘Maasta, een wo ngaenneaei nimingeras faiun senaapiy. Pipiiy, a pwan yo ngaeniaei nimingeras faiun senaapiy pwe menewan.’
MAT 25:21 Maasta we a aengaeni pwe, ‘Egacch, een erhai rhooan engaang mwamwaai me wenewen. Een wo menaw wenewen reen oamw nemaeni minikka e mwittig, ina minne ipwe faer ngaenneog minikka e tettemoag pwe wopwe nemaeni. Itto tapweaei reen apwapwa e aaei.’
MAT 25:22 Iwe rhooan engaang we e pwigi riiungeras faiun senaapiy a toonong nge aepesa pwe, ‘Maasta, een wa ngaenneaei riiungeras faiun senaapiy. Pipiiy, a pwan yo riiungeras faiun senaapiy pwe menewan.’
MAT 25:23 Maasta we a aengaeni, ‘Egacch, een erhai rhooan engaang mwamwaai me wenewen. Een wo menaw wenewen reen oamw nemaeni minikka e mwittig, ina minne ipwe faer ngaenneog minikka e tettemoag pwe wopwe nemaeni. Itto tapweaei reen apwapwa e aaei.’
MAT 25:24 Iwe rhooan engaang we e pwigi sengeras faiun senaapiy a toonong nge aepesa pwe, ‘Maasta, i giuneei pwe een erhai mwaaen sosoong. Wo giniiy uwaen foat inamwo iga wose foat, wa ioni fengaenniy uwaen irae inamwo wose oamworomwor faiun.
MAT 25:25 Iya mesag, ina minne iya noa nipwaeni noa senaapiy we noawumw faaen ppweon reen. Pipiiy, ieen senaapiy we noawumw.’
MAT 25:26 Iwe maasta we a paniuwaeni pwe, ‘Een erhai rhooan engaang aenneew me gagu! Wo giuneei pwe ngaang iya giniiy ikka ise foat, iya pwan ioni fengaenniy uwaan ikka ise oamworomwor faiun ee?
MAT 25:27 Iwe, meeta wose faer iseni nong senaapiy mwu naeyi noan bank reen? Ina nge ipwe pwigi sefaaeniy fengaen me menewan igine iya sefaaen to.
MAT 25:28 Igina, oaw pwigi saengi senaapiy kkomwu reen nge oawwa ngaenneei imwu eyor seig sengeras faiun senaapiy reen.
MAT 25:29 Pwe iyo a yor meeta aan nge repwe pwan fang ngaeni, iwe epwene igin ssow noa aan; nge iyo ese yor meeta aan nge repwe pwigi saengi mwo nge iwe egius iwe eyor reen.
MAT 25:30 Nge reen rhooan engaang e esooar ipitan, oaw oatorawow niugiun noan rorhappiung, iga epwe sessaeng nge akkaarengi me ee.’
MAT 25:31 “Ngaere igine mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas epwene war noan nningen pwe king nge oanongeer angkenus repwe tapweei, nge epwe mooat wooan minna nenien king,
MAT 25:32 iwe, nge oanongeer aeremesaen faeinaengiy nge repwe rhu fengaen me weni mmwan. Nge epwe aeyimweoiuw fesaenngiir noan ruwowu mwiirh, taeppen rhag erhai rhooan neginegin maan e aeyimweoiuw fesaenngiir sheep saengiir goat.
MAT 25:33 Epwe iseniir nong sheep peig mwaaenen, nge goat peig rhooapwuton.
MAT 25:34 Nge king we epwene aengaeniir rhooawe reno peig mwaaenen, ‘Oaw itto, aaemi rhooa wenepwu me reen Semaei! Oawpwe mweoiuni mweoi e oamoannatae faaen itaemi saengi rhaepetaen feoniufan.
MAT 25:35 Pwe ngaang iya pecchai nge aaemi oawwa oamwongowaei, iya moar nge aaemi oawwa aiuniuwaei, iya waseona nge aaemi oawwa aetiwaeyaei noan imwaemi.
MAT 25:36 Ise memmengaag nge aaemi oawwa fang mengaagiuy, iya semwaai nge aaemi oawwa aefaenniaei, iya no noan kanepwus nge aaemi oawwa itto rhuungiaei.’
MAT 25:37 Iwe rhooawe rhooa wenewen repwene paniuwaeni, ‘Soamwoon, ineet aeiya giuneei pwe wa pecchai nge aeiya oamwongog, ineet wa moar, nge aeiya aiuniug?
MAT 25:38 Ineet aeiya giuneei pwe wa waseona, nge aeiya aetiwoag nong noan imwaemmaem, aere ineet aeiya giuneei pwe esooar mengaagiumw, nge aeiya fang mengaagiumw?
MAT 25:39 Ineet aeiya giuneei pwe wo semwaai aere no noan kanepwus, nge aeiya itto rhuungiug?’
MAT 25:40 Iwe, king we epwene paniuwaeni pwe, ‘Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, ese tiwegin minne oawwa feeori ngaeni erhai neeiir rhooakka rewen pwiiy ikka re igin sessoan, nge oawpwan feeori ngaeniaei.’
MAT 25:41 “Iwe epwan aengaeniir rhooawe reno peig rhooapwuton, ‘Oawpwe siu saengiaei, aaemi rhooawe Deus epwene fang aaemi aegaeregaer, oawpwe noa noan aengaet we esooar iaenin a faer oamoannatae faaen iteer Saetan me naiun angkenus!
MAT 25:42 Pwe iya pecchai, nge aaemi oawse oamwongowaei; iya moar, nge aaemi oawse ainiuwaei.
MAT 25:43 Iya waseona, nge aaemi oawse aetiwaeyaei noan imwaemi; ise memmengaag, nge aaemi oawse fang mengaagiuy; iya semwaai me no noan kanepwus, nge aaemi oawse aefaenniaei.’
MAT 25:44 Iwe repwene paniuwaeni pwe, ‘Soamwoon, ineet aemaem aeiya giuneei pwe wa pecchai aere moar, aere waseona, aere wose memmengaag, aere semwaai, aere no noan kanepwus, nge aeise aefaenniug?’
MAT 25:45 Nge king we epwene paniuwaeniir pwe, ‘Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi: ese tiwegin minne oawse feeori ngaeni erhai neeiir rhooakka re rewen pwiiy ikka re igin sessoan, oawse pwan feeori ngaeniaei.’
MAT 25:46 Iwe, rhooakkeei repwe noa ngaeni aegaeregaer we esooar iaenin, nge rhooawe rhooa wenewen repwe noa ngaeni menaw na esooar ssiaaenin.”
MAT 26:1 Oatowe Jesus a moann aan fenaiuw oanongaen minikkeei, a aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe,
MAT 26:2 “Aaemi oaw giuneei pwe a faei riiuraaen nge epwene gona miniwe gupwunon Passover, nge miniwe Naiun Aeremas epwene toonong nee paiiur aeremas pwe repwene noa kurusuw noa.”
MAT 26:3 Iwe soamwooniir patere me mwaaen kkewe aar ra mwiirh fengaen noan imwaen Soamwoonin Patere we itan Caiaphas,
MAT 26:4 nge ra pwiungiuw wunuunun aar repwe torofi Jesus noan mwoanomwoan pwe repwe noa niiy noa.
MAT 26:5 Nge ra aepesa pwe, “Sisoapw feeori minneei oaton gupwunon Passover, pwe aeremas rete aefitigogo tae.”
MAT 26:6 Jesus a noa Bethany noan imwaen Simon, erhai mwaaen kaenepaai mwo igiwe.
MAT 26:7 Nge oaton we Jesus a mwongo, erhai rhooapwut a itto reen faaen eew neo effeeor saengi alabaster nge e oawut ngaeni neoningas e igin cchoaw paniuwan, a itto aeniatiw neo we wooan rhimwen Jesus.
MAT 26:8 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra giuneei miniwe, nge ra soong. Ra aepesa pwe, “Meeta mwo oasonopaen neoningas eei?
MAT 26:9 Pwe neoningas een emmwen erhai epwe chuwaiuw ngaeni senaapiy temoag nge ra ngaenneer man affayeo!”
MAT 26:10 Jesus e giuneei meeta kkewe ra aepesa, iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta oaw amwagiutiu nieen reen? Egin mwamwaai minne a feeori ngaeniaei.
MAT 26:11 Pwe rhooa affayeo repwe fasiun yor reemi oanongaen oat, nge ngaang isoapw no rhag reemi oanongaen oat.
MAT 26:12 Minne efeeori iga e aeniatae neoningas wooan oanongaei, nge a faer oamoannayaei tae ngaeniaei nipwaenipw.
MAT 26:13 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe ese tiwegin iga repwe fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai een me ee, nge minne nieei a feeori nge aeremas repwene fioangei pwe aemaengimaengin faaen itan.”
MAT 26:14 Iwe erhai me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai, iwe itan Judas Iscariot, a noa reen soamwoonin patere kkewe
MAT 26:15 nge a aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta oawpwe ngaenneaei aere ipwe fangenoa tinnimaen Jesus?” Ra paengiwow eniig faiun senaapiy silver nge ra ngaenneei.
MAT 26:16 Saengi rhag oatowe nge Judas a giutta eew oaton ne egacch aan epwe fang ngaeniir Jesus.
MAT 26:17 Noan aeyewaen raaenin Gupwunon Fenoawa we esooar Yeast reen, rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra itto reen Jesus nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Iya iga wo mwerhaen pwe aeipwe oamoannatae mwongoon Passover me ee?”
MAT 26:18 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawnoa noan aepinoamw na reen erhai mwaaen nge oawwa aengaeni, ‘Sinsei e iura pwe, A arapeto oatoi nge rhooan kkayeo kena naeyi me ngaang pwe feeori mwongoon Passover me noan imwoamw.’ ”
MAT 26:19 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra feeori wunuunun meeta we Jesus a aengaeniir, nge ra oamoannatae mwongoon Passover we.
MAT 26:20 Igiwe a nee oatofaaef noa, Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai ra mooat tiw reen table we.
MAT 26:21 Iga ra mwongo, nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe erhai me neeimi epwene fangenoa tinnimaei.”
MAT 26:22 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe a igin aenneew noa nee tipeer reen kkepas we nge ra rhaepetae ne kkepas aeiyeg ngaeni, erhai me erhai ra aepesa pwe, “Soamwoon, saapw ngaang?”
MAT 26:23 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Erhai ne e tapweaei reen rhirinong anan fenoawa noan saepiy een, ina iiy epwe fangenoa tinnimaei.
MAT 26:24 Minna Naiun Aeremas epwe maenoa taeppen rhag meeta we Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa, nge epwe ifa mwo aenneewaen mwaaen na iiy e afangmaei noa mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas! Egacch rhag igine rese nainitiw mwaaen een!”
MAT 26:25 Judas iwe e afangmaei noa Jesus a kepastae, “Sinsei, saapw ngaang?” Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Een minimwu wo aepesa minna.”
MAT 26:26 Igiwe ra mwongo, Jesus a pwigi eew fenoawa, a fang aan maeipinen aerhigerhig, iwe a giniiy nge a ngaenneer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a aepesa pwe, “Oaw pwigi pwe oawpwe angi, pwe ieen minne oanongaei.”
MAT 26:27 Mwirin a pwigi eew kkap, a fang aan maeipinen aerhigerhig, iwe, a ngaenneer nge a aepesa pwe, “Oaw iuniumi minneen oanongaemi,
MAT 26:28 pwe ieen minne cchaei iye epwene no pwe tiweginin ppwon we aaen Deus ngaenigaemi, nge minne cchaei epwene nipiwow pwe arhiuwerhiuwen aar monofit aeremas.
MAT 26:29 Ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe isoapw rhiuwen iuniumi wine een toori raaenin na ipwe iuniumi wine na effeo me noan minna Mweoiun Semaei.”
MAT 26:30 Mwirin ra aeni erheo keoniun aerhigerhig, nge ra toowow ngaeni miniwe rhugun Olives.
MAT 26:31 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Nee pwongiy nge oanongaemi oawpwe nigitiaei noa, pwe iwe Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Deus epwe niiy noa rhooan neginegin sheep we, nge sheep kkewe repwene toaropas fetaen.’
MAT 26:32 Nge mwirin aaei menaw sefaaen, ipwe gommwonoa Galilee me mmwaemi.”
MAT 26:33 Iwe, Peter a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaang isoapw nigitiug noa, inamwo me oanongeer nge re nigitiug noa!”
MAT 26:34 Jesus a aengaeni Peter pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaeniug pwe mmwaen aaen maniug we epwe keokkeok nee pwongiy, nge epwe faaen enuuw oamw iura pwe wose giuneaei.”
MAT 26:35 Peter a paniuwaeni pwe, “Esooar faaen eew ipwe aepesa minna, inamwo aere ipwe tapweog reen maenoa.” A pwan ina rhag meeta re iura rhooan kkayeo kkewe aekkaerhai.
MAT 26:36 Iwe Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra noa noan eew neniy itan Gethsemane, iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawmooat tiw igeei, pwe ngaang ipwe noa maeipin iginaan.”
MAT 26:37 A paeninoa Peter me mwaaen riiurhai kkewe naiun Zebedee. Waeiraes me nee tip cchoaw a tooto reen,
MAT 26:38 iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Waeiraesin noan minne nee tipaei egin temoag, arapakkaan rhag epwe niaei noa. Oawno igeei oawpwe tapweaei reen metenaeg.”
MAT 26:39 Jesus a mwet noa egius mmwan, a won rhappetiw nee ppweon nge maeipin, “Semaei, aere emmwen, wopwe pwigi saengiaei kkepaen waeiraes een; nge saapw minne ngaang i tipaeni, pwe minne een wo tipaeni.”
MAT 26:40 Iwe a sefaaeneto reer rhooan kkayeo kkewe eoniurhai we naiun, nge a giuneer pwe ra maiur. Iwe a aengaeni Peter pwe, “Ifa wusun, aaemi mwo nge ese mmwen oawpwe mmas ngaeniaei noan eew rhag awa?
MAT 26:41 Oaw mmas nge oaw maeipin pwe oawte ppiungiunong noan sessoat. Ngeon a mwerhaen, nge oanong a apwangapwang.”
MAT 26:42 Jesus a pwan sefaaen noa maeipin, “Semaei, aere wosoapw pwigi saengiaei kkepaen waeiraes een pwe ipwe iuniumi, nge minna tipoamw minne epwe mmwen.”
MAT 26:43 Jesus epwan sefaaen nge a giuneer pwe ra pwan maiur, pwe ra igin cchoaw.
MAT 26:44 Iwe, Jesus a pwan mwet saengiir, a sefaaen noa maeipin reen aeinuwaen, nge epwan aeni rhag maeipin we e aeni me mmwan.
MAT 26:45 Iwe a sefaaeneto reer rhooan kkayeo kkewe nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw rhiuwen maiur me aseoseo rhag? Pipiiy, a toori oaton repwene fangenoa Naiun Aeremas nee paiiur rhooa monofit.
MAT 26:46 Oaw rhimwitae, oaw sia noa. Pipiiy, ieei iiy mwaaen we e fangenoa menewaei!”
MAT 26:47 Oatowe Jesus e rhiuwen kekkepas, Judas iwe erhai me neeiir rhooawe seig me riiurhai a war. Pwuwaen aeremas kkewe re tapweei faaen naiiur saeitan me soapwon irae, nge re itto faaen iteer soamwoonin patere me mwaaen kkewe aar.
MAT 26:48 Rhooan afangmaei noa we a fang aeginn ngaeniir pwuwa we: “Mwaaen na ipwe faeisongei ina mwaaen na oaw tipaeni. Oaw torofi!”
MAT 26:49 Judas a faaeraeg wenewen ngaeni Jesus nge a aengaeni pwe, “Sirow woamw, Sinsei,” iwe a faeisongei.
MAT 26:50 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Pwiiy, feeori meeta wo itto reen.” Iwe ra mwet ngaeni, ra torofi Jesus nge ra ammwarhiu.
MAT 26:51 Nge erhai me neeiir rhooawe rhoaniuwaen Jesus a waeitiwow naiun saeitan, nge a fena rhooan akkiuneo we naiun Soamwoonin Patere iwe gopiy noa eew saeningan.
MAT 26:52 Iwe, Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Wopwe aesefaaeninong saeitan mwu noawumw noan nenien. Pwe rhooakkena re pweipwog saeitan repwe maenoa wooan saeitan.
MAT 26:53 Oawse giuneei, pwe ngaang ina emmwen ipwe tingoar ngaeni Semaei pwe epwe tipaengiaei, pwe epwe mwetekkaein fang ngaeniaei seig me ruwowu mwirhaen sonotawaen angkenus?
MAT 26:54 Nge ngaere epwe wen minneei, epwe ifa wusun nge epwe nnet miniwe e foatofoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus, iwe e iura pwe ieei meeta epwe fasiun wen?”
MAT 26:55 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir aeremas towunap kkewe pwe, “Meeta oawnoa itto faaen naimi saeitan me soapwon irae pwe oawpwe torofiaei, pwe iga aetae ngaang erhai man mwoarho? Raaen me raaen nge ngaang imooat reemi nge i fenai noan Temple, nge aaemi oawse torofiaei.
MAT 26:56 Nge ina oanongaen minikkeei nge epwe wen pwe epwe nnet ngaeni minikkiwe profeta ra foatogitiw noan Pwapwior we e Santus.” Iwe oanongeer rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra siusaengi Jesus nge ra fattapw noa.
MAT 26:57 Rhooawe re torofi Jesus ra paeninoa reen Soamwoonin Patere itan Caiaphas, iwe me sinsein anniug kkewe me mwaaen kkewe aar ra mwiirh fengaen ee.
MAT 26:58 Nge Peter e tettapw to mwirin Jesus me itaaw toorito niugiun imwaen Soamwoonin Patere we. A toonong noan wororaen iimw we nge a mooat tiw reer rhooan poos kkewe pwe epwe giuneei meeta epwe wen.
MAT 26:59 Rhooawe soamwooniir patere me oanongeer rhooan council we ra giutta eew min oatupwutupw ne repwe tipi ngaeni Jesus pwe repwe niiy noa,
MAT 26:60 nge esooar meeta ne reweri, inamwo igiwe re towunap aeremas kka ra itto iutae nge re pwaeritae aar oatupwutupw reen. Mwirin riiurhai mwaaen ra iutae
MAT 26:61 nge ra aepesa pwe, “Mwaaen een aepesa pwe, ‘Ngaang immwenen fereeitiw aaen Deus Temple, nge noan enuuw raaen ipwe aiusefaaeniy tae.’ ”
MAT 26:62 Soamwoonin Patere a iutae nge a aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Esooar minne wopwe paniuwaeni ngaeni kkepas kka mwaaen kaan ra tipi ngaeniug?”
MAT 26:63 Nge Jesus a anniug noa rhag. Iwe Soamwoonin Patere a pwan aepesa ngaeni Jesus pwe, “Wopwe ppwon faaen itaen Deus na e menaw nge wa aengaenigemaem aere een Kristus, Naiun Deus.”
MAT 26:64 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Een minne wo iura. Nge ipwe aengaenigaemi: saengi igina oawpwene giuneei Naiun Aeremas epwe mooat peig mwaaenen iwe e oarosaen Mamaaw, nge epwe ittiw me weei naaeng wooan toapw.”
MAT 26:65 Iwe Soamwoonin Patere we a fereeitiw mengaagiun nge a iura pwe, “A aepesa aenneewa Deus! Meeta si rhiuwen pwigiir to rhooan oatuttur reen? Pipiiy, oawwa sipegin rongorong aan aepesa aenneewa Deus.
MAT 26:66 Meeta aaemi niunniuwaen?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Iiy e monofit nge epwe mae.”
MAT 26:67 Mwirin ra oattuffa mesan nge re wirhiy, nge ikkiwe re peosepa
MAT 26:68 ra aepesa pwe, “Aengaenigemaem, Kristus! Iyo we e wirhiug!”
MAT 26:69 Igiwe Peter emooat noan wororaen iimw we imwaen Soamwoonin Patere, iwe erhai rhooapwut naiun rhooan engaang a itto reen nge a aengaeni pwe, “Een pwan erhai rhoaniuwaen Jesus saengi Galilee.”
MAT 26:70 Peter a paniuwaeni memmweer oanongeer, nge a iura pwe, “Ngaang ise giuneei meeta mwu wo aepesa,”
MAT 26:71 iwe a faaeraeg wow me noan asam we. Iwe erhai rhooapwut rhooan engaengaen igiwe a giuneei Peter nge a aengaeniir mwaaen kkewe igiwe pwe, “Mwaaen een eno reen Jesus re Nazareth we.”
MAT 26:72 Iwe, Peter a pwan iura pwe ese giuneei nge a aepesa pwe, “Iya aekkepan pwe ise giuneei mwaaen naan!”
MAT 26:73 Faeiyegius noa mwirin nge rhooawe re iu igiwe ra itto reen Peter nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Ennet, een pwan erhai rhoaniuwaen mwaaen naan, pwe aei giuneei rhag me reen ngingin oamw kkepas.”
MAT 26:74 Iwe Peter a iura pwe, “Iya aekkepan pwe ngaang i aepesa minne ennet! Deus epwe apwiungiuwaei aere i oatupwutupw! Ngaang ise giuneei mwaaen naan.” Iwe rhag nge e keokkeok noa maniug we,
MAT 26:75 iwe Peter a maengiy miniwe Jesus e aengaeni: “Weni mmwaen epwe keokkeok maniug, een wopwe aepesa faaen enuuw pwe wose giuneaei.” Iwe a toowow niugiun nge a igin noa saeng.
MAT 27:1 Enoa nee oatosor moawugowug, oanongeer soamwoonin patere kkewe me mwaaen kkewe aar ra pwiungiuw wunuunun aar repwe niiy noa Jesus.
MAT 27:2 Ra geoni noa nge ra paeninoa reen Pilate, iwe iiy minne governor.
MAT 27:3 Igiwe Judas, iwe efang noa menewaen Jesus, a giuneei pwe ra aettiweginiy pwe Jesus epwene mae, a ssiuwen aan niunniuwaen iwe a aesefaaeni ngaeniir soamwoonin patere me mwaaen kkewe aar faiun senaapiy we eniig.
MAT 27:4 Nge a aepesa pwe, “Ngaang iya monofit reen aaei fangenoa menewaen erhai mwaaen se monofit.” Iwe, ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Meeta faan ngaenigemaem? Feeori pwe oamw engaang.”
MAT 27:5 Judas a oatoranong senaapiy kkewe noan Temple we nge a noa, iwe a noa nnoma noa iiuwan.
MAT 27:6 Soamwoonin patere kkewe ra pwigi faiun senaapiy kkewe nge ra aepesa pwe, “Senaapiaen meoniun ccha minneen, nge e aenneew ngaeni aarh anniug pwe sipwe oarhuw nong noan senaapiaen Temple.”
MAT 27:7 Ra tipieew fengaen wooan senaapiy we, iwe ra meoni eew faniuw itan Potter’s Field, pwe eew nenien paeyieer waseona.
MAT 27:8 Ina minne ra aeita ngaeni pwe “Faniuwaen Ccha” toorito igina.
MAT 27:9 Iwe a pwae noa pwe ennet meeta we profeta Jeremiah e aepesa: “Ra pwigi eniig senaapiy silver, nepaen miniwe re Israel ra tipieew wooan pwe repwe pey aegini ngaeni mwaaen we,
MAT 27:10 nge ra naini senaapiy een ne meoni ngaeni Potter’s Field, taeppen miniwe Soamwoon e anniugiu ngaeniaei.”
MAT 27:11 Iwe Jesus a iu me mmwaen governor we nge a aeiyegiy Jesus pwe, “Een minne aar king re Jews?” Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Een minimwu wo aepesa.”
MAT 27:12 Iwe esa paniuwaeni no meeta kkewe soamwoonin patere me mwaaen kkewe aar ra aepesa pwe teren.
MAT 27:13 Iwe Pilate a aengaeni pwe, “Wose rongorong towunepaen kkepesaen oatuttur kkomwu ra oaturug rhag reen?”
MAT 27:14 Nge Jesus ese paniuwaeni mwo nge eew, iwe governor we a igin mwaar noa reen.
MAT 27:15 Reen oanongaen oaton gupwunon Passover, nge governor egaen saeneti noa erhai rhooan kanepwus ina aeremas towunap re tingoar.
MAT 27:16 Nge noan oaton naan nge eno erhai rhooan kanepwus itan nge Barabbas, nge oanongeer aeremas nge re giuneei.
MAT 27:17 Iwe igiwe rhooa towunap kkewe ra maegin rhu fengaen, nge Pilate a aeiineeor pwe, “Iyo e oaw tipaeni pwe ipwe saeneti ngaenigaemi, Barabbas aere Jesus we re faingi pwe Kristus?”
MAT 27:18 E fasiun giuneei pwe ra fang nong Jesus nee paiun faaen itaen aar noanowo ngaeni.
MAT 27:19 Iwe igiwe Pilate e rhiuwen mooat wooan nenien mooaton apwiung we aan, nge niewe pwiuniuwan a fangenoa reen eew kkepas: “Esooar meeta wopwe feeori ngaeni mwaaen mwamwaai na, pwe noan aaei ttan nee pwoong we nge iya igin waeiraes noa faaen itan.”
MAT 27:20 Iwe soamwooniir patere kkewe me mwaaen kkewe aar ra igin aetemaeginiy ngaeniir aeremas pwe repwe tingoareei Pilate pwe epwe saeneti noa Barabbas, nge a niiy noa Jesus.
MAT 27:21 Nge governor we a aeiineeor aeremas pwe, “Iyo neeiir rhooa riiurhai een oaw tipaeni pwe ipwe saeneti ngaenigaemi?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Barabbas!”
MAT 27:22 Pilate a aeiineeor pwe, “Nge meeta ipwe feeori ngaeni Jesus, iwe itaen Kristus?” Oanongeer noa ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Kurusuw noa!”
MAT 27:23 Nge Pilate a aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta taeppen wegitaeg aenneew e a feeori?” Nge iir ra pwan oatomoga aar iyaekkepwas pwe, “Kurusuw noa!”
MAT 27:24 Igiwe Pilate a giuneei pwe esooar ipitan aan epwe kkepas ngaeniir, pwe ina nge epwene rhaepetae eew fitigogo, a pwigi rhaan nge a toafi paiun memmweer aeremas kkewe nge a aepesa pwe, “Esooar monofitiy reen cchaaen mwaaen een aan mae. Pwe faer aaemi.”
MAT 27:25 Aeremas towunap kkewe ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Cchaan epwe itto woamaem me wooar naimaem!”
MAT 27:26 Iwe Pilate a saeneti Barabbas ngaeniir, nge ra wirhiy Jesus nge a fangenoa pwe repwene noa kurusuw noa.
MAT 27:27 Iwe sonotaw kkewe naiun Pilate ra paeni nong Jesus noan imwaen governor, nge ra faingiir oanongeer sonotaw kkewe nge ra itto roangei noa oaron.
MAT 27:28 Ra pwiniti saengi mengaagiun nge ra aememmengaagiu ngaeni erheo mengaag ccha.
MAT 27:29 Iwe ra fiti eew mwaer saengi irae towfanfan nge ra ngaettae wooan rhimwen, nge ra pwan iseni nong efoarh soapwon irae noan pai mwaaenen; nge ra foatotiw me mmwan nge ra aeni fetaeneei aegekkaei. Ra gaen aepesa pwe, “Sirow woamw, Kingaen Jews.”
MAT 27:30 Ra oattuffa, ra pwigi irae we saengi nge ra wirhiy ngaeni rhimwen.
MAT 27:31 Nge igiwe ra moann me aeni aegekkaei, ra pwiniti saengi mengaag ccha we nge ra aememmengaagiu sefaaeniy ngaeni ikkiwe sipegin mengaagiun. Iwe ra paeninoa pwe repwene noa kurusuw noa.
MAT 27:32 Igiwe ra nennoa, nge ra rhuungi erhai mwaaen itan Simon saengi Cyrene; nge sonotaw kkewe ra aengimaw ngaeni pwe epwe aiufera kurus we aaen Jesus.
MAT 27:33 Nge ra tooto reen eew pwiuneoi itan Golgotha, wewen nge “Nenien Peopeoi Rhimw”.
MAT 27:34 Igaan iga ra itto aiuniu ngaeni Jesus wine min nofit me meras. Nge mwirin aan nnaeri, nge ese mwerhaen iuniumi.
MAT 27:35 Mwirin aar kurusuw noa Jesus, nge ra itto aekkaerh dice pwe repwe inetiy minikkewe mengaagiun wooar.
MAT 27:36 Iwe ra mooat tiw igiwe nge ra pipiiy.
MAT 27:37 Wooan tae rhimwen ra aepperhatae aaemweoi foatofoat e pwaeritae meeta we ra tipi ngaeni, e iura pwe: “Ieei Jesus, Kingaen Jews.”
MAT 27:38 Iwe ra pwan kurusuur noa riiurhai rhooa mwoarho oaron Jesus, erhai me peig rhooapwuton, nge erhai me peig mwaaenen.
MAT 27:39 Aeremas kkewe re faaeraeg noa me oaron Jesus ra gaen aepesa aenneewa, nge re iurhiugi rhimweer
MAT 27:40 nge re aepesa pwe, “Een miniwe wo iura pwe wopwe fereeitiw Temple we nge wa aiusefaaeniy tae noan enuuw raaen! Aemenewoag aere een Naiun Deus, nge wa teeotiw me wooan kurus na!”
MAT 27:41 Epwan ina rhag wunuunun soamwoonin patere kkewe me sinsein anniug me mwaaen kkewe aar re aeni aegekkaei Jesus nge re iura pwe,
MAT 27:42 “A aemenewaar aaemweoi, nge ese mmwenen aemenewa oanongan! Saapw i miniwe kingaaen Israel? Aere epwe teeotiw saengi kurus naan igina, ina nge sipwe niugiuniug ngaeni.
MAT 27:43 E niugiuniug ngaeni Deus, nge e aepesa pwe iiy Naiun Deus. Iwe, sipwe pipiiy aere Deus epwe mwerhaen aemenewa igina!”
MAT 27:44 Pwan rhooa mwoarho kkewe mwo re tapweei reen kurus nge repwan aessaewa reen aar kkepas ngaeni.
MAT 27:45 Saengi nugunupaen oanowas a noa, a rorhappiung noa wooan oanongaen faniuw we noan enuuw konook.
MAT 27:46 Enoa enuuw konook nge Jesus a aekkepwas temoag tae pwe, “Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani?” wewen, “Aaei Deus, aaei Deus, meeta wa nigitiaei noa reen?”
MAT 27:47 Aaemweoi aeremas kkewe re iu igiwe ra rongorong miniwe nge ra iura pwe, “A faingi Elijah!”
MAT 27:48 Erhai me neeiir a mwetekkaein fattapweto reen, a pwigi eew faerewa nge a rhirinong noan eew wine emwaenn, a iseni tae nee soapwon efoarh irae nge a aiuniu ngaeni Jesus.
MAT 27:49 Nge aaemweoi re iura pwe, “Weti sipwe pipiiy aere Elijah epwe itto aemenewa.”
MAT 27:50 Nge Jesus a pwan aekkepwas temoag tae faaen eew, iwe a fangetae ngeoniun.
MAT 27:51 Iwe nge mengaag we e tteoraeg noan Temple we mwo nge a taeringatiw faaen ruwowu, saengi wooan ittiw faan. A fanemwar faniuw, nge faai ra tiningaeg fesaeng,
MAT 27:52 nge paeyi ra sugaeg, nge towunap rhooa maenoa kkewe naiun Deus ra menaw sefaaen.
MAT 27:53 Ra siusaengi paeyieer nge mwirin aaen Jesus menaw sefaaen nge ra noa noan aepinoamw we e santus, igiwe pwuwaen aeremas ra noa giuneer me ee.
MAT 27:54 Igiwe soamwoonin sonotaw we me sonotaw kkewe re pippipiiy Jesus ra giuneei fanemwar me oanongaen minikkiwe a wen, ra igin riutae iwe nge ra aepesa pwe, “Ennetaen pwe iiy Naiun Deus!”
