MAR 12:33 Nge een wopwe aerhaengi Deus reen oanongaen nee tipoamw, reen oanongaen oamw niunniuwaennen me oanongaen maemaewoamw, me wopwe pwan aerhaengi rhooan weni oaromw taeppen rhag oamw sipegin aerhaengi oanongoamw. E igin yor ipitan aaen erhai epwe aiussaening firhiy anniug kka ruwowu, mmwaen aan epwe aeni oasoar maan wooan antar me mesemesaen oasoar ngaeni Deus.”
MAR 12:34 Jesus e meyaefi gacchiun paniuwaenin kkepas kkewe aan, iwe a aengaeni pwe, “Een wose taaw saengi miniwe Mweoiun Deus.” Mwirin nge ra mesag repwe rhiuwen kkepas aeiineo ngaeni Jesus.
MAR 12:35 Igiwe Jesus e fenai noan Temple we, a aeiineo eew kkepas, “Epwe ifa wusun nge sinsein anniug kkewe repwe aepesa pwe Kristus nge iiy teoteeon David?
MAR 12:36 Espritu Santus minne e aemeyaefi ngaeni David pwe epwe aepesa: ‘Soamwoon a aengaeniaei Soamwoon: Mooat tiw peig mwaaeneei toori aaei ipwe iseniir tiw rhooan oapwutoag faaen pirhemw.’
MAR 12:37 David wooan oanongan e sipegin faingi Kristus pwe iiy ‘Soamwoon’, iwe epwe ifa wusun nge Kristus epwe no pwe teoteeon David?” Ekker tipeer aeremas towunap kkewe re aiussaening ngaeni aaen Jesus fenai.
MAR 12:38 Igiwe e fenaiuw ngaeniir pwe, “Oawpwe aefaennigaemi reer sinsein anniug kkewe re aerhaengi aar faaeraeg fetaen faaen mengaagiiur min enaenaei, nge re aerhaengi aar aeremas repwe aewenimmwaar me aesirowuur me noan imwaen chuwaai,
MAR 12:39 nge re fini rhag neniy kkena nenieer rhooa taegias me noan wutteer Jews me pwiuneoi mwamwaai me noan gupwun.
MAR 12:40 Re oapwurhaar rhooapwut kka ra mae pwiuniuweer nge ra pirifa saengiir pwuguseer, nge re oangona ngaeni aeremas aar maeipin enaei. Iwe nge aegaeregaeriir ina epwene igin waeiraes!”
MAR 12:41 Igiwe Jesus emooat oaron nenien maenigaech we me noan Temple we, a pippipiir aeremas kkewe re iseis nong aar maenigaech. Towunepeer aeremas kkewe re naiwiis re iseis nong towunepaen naiiur senaapiy;
MAR 12:42 nge erhai rhooapwut mwaenene pwe a mae pwiuniuwan a itto iseis nong riiufai manfaifai, ina epwe aeffitaeg ngaeni oawton efai checcha.
MAR 12:43 Jesus a faingiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe miniwe rhooapwut mwaenene we efang nge e temoag saengi aar oanongeer aeremas towunap kkewe.
MAR 12:44 Pwe oanongeer nge re iseni nong nusegin wiineer, nge rhooapwut een inamwo iga e igin affayeo nge a fangenoa oanongaen meeta eno reen — a fangenoa oanongaen minikka epwe menaw wooan.”
MAR 13:1 Igiwe Jesus a siusaengi Temple we, erhai me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun a iura pwe, “Sinsei, pipiiy nningen faai me iimw kaan!”
MAR 13:2 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Woweri iimw faeregit kaan? Esooar efai faai kaan ne epwe notiw nenien; oanongan noa nge repwene toaropotiw.”
MAR 13:3 Jesus emooat wooan miniwe rhugun Olives peiginoan Temple we, igiwe Peter, James, John me Andrew renoa reen nge iir noa rhag.
MAR 13:4 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Aengaenigemaem ineeta minikkeei epwe wen, me aengaenigemaem meeta minne epwe pwaeri noa pwe oaton minikkeei nge epwene wen.”
MAR 13:5 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw aefaennigaemi, pwe esoapw yor erhai epwe oatupwugaemi.
MAR 13:6 Towunepeer aeremas repwene itto faaen itaei nge repwe aepesa pwe, ‘Ngaang iiy!’ Iwe nge pwuwaen aeremas repwe tupw noa reer.
MAR 13:7 Oawsoapw mesag igine oaw rongorong oacchorongon moawun arapeto aere kkepesaen moawun taaw noa. Oanongaen minikkeei nge repwe mmwaen wen, nge saapw reen a arapeto ne soapwonoan.
MAR 13:8 Faniuw me faniuw repwe fiiow fengaen nge mweoi me mweoi repwe pwan moawun fengaen. Epwe yor fanemwar oanongaen pwiuneoi me naengeta. Minikkaan nge eweei pweoneotaen metaegin erhai rhooapwut iga epwe nainai.
MAR 13:9 “Aaemi wooan oanongaemi oawpwe sipegin aefaennigaemi. Repwe torofigaemi nge re pwigigaemi nong noan nenien apwiung. Repwe wirhigaemi me noan wutteer Jews; oawpwe iutae mmweer soamwoonin anniug me king kkewe faaen itaei, pwe oawpwe aengaeniir Kkepas Mwamwaai we.
MAR 13:10 Nge weni mmwaen epwe tooto minna nee soapwonoan, nge Kkepas Mwamwaai een epwe gommwaen fenai ngaeniir oanongeer aeremesaen feoniufan wunus.
MAR 13:11 Aere ra torofigaemi nge re isenigaemi nong noan nenien apwiung, oawsoapw pireiir reen meeta oawpwe aepesa; pwe oatona epwe noa toori oatonaan, nge oawpwe aepesa meeta na eno reemw. Pwe petenaen kkepas kena oaw aepesa nge saapw mwaeniaemi, pwe e itto me reen Espritu Santus.
MAR 13:12 Aeremas repwene afangmaei noa pwiir ngaeni maenoa, nge saam repwe pwan feeori taeppen minneen ngaeni naiiur. Nge naiiur repwene pwan appaniuwaeni semeer me ineer nge re fangenoa iir repwe noa niir noa.
MAR 13:13 Oanongeer aeremas nge repwene oapwutaegaemi faaen itaei. Nge iyo e aetemaegin toori nee soapwonoan nge epwe menaw.
MAR 13:14 “Aaemi oawpwe weri eew Min Oarosaen Aemmesagsag epwe iu eew pwiuneoi saapw fasiun nenien. (Ngaeni rhooan aeraegraeg: metefaaegini minneen!) Iwe rhooawe reno Judea repwe fattapwetae weei rhug.
MAR 13:15 Erhai ne eno wooan wungaen iimw, esoapw teeotiw noan imwan pwe epwe ittiw pweipwog meeta me ee.
MAR 13:16 Nge erhai ne eno noan maat, esoapw sefaaen ngaeni imwan pwe epwe pweipwog mengaagiun.
MAR 13:17 Epwe ifa mwo aar affayeo rhooapwut pwoopwo me ikka re nayigit noan oaton naan!
MAR 13:18 Oawpwe maeipin ngaeni Deus pwe minikkeei nge esoapw wen noan oaton patapat.
MAR 13:19 Pwe waeiraesin noan raaenin kkewe epwe faer igin waeiraes saengi me mmwaen ikkiwe rhaepetaen igiwe Deus a feeori feoniufan toorito igina. Nge esoapw rhiuwen yor taeppen epwe rhiuwen itto.
MAR 13:20 Pwe Soamwoon a oamworhomworha nepaen raaen; ngaere ese feeori, nge esooar ne epwe menaw. Nge pwonno faaen iteer rhooawe a finiir tae a oamworhomworhanoa nepaen raaen.
MAR 13:21 “Iwe ngaere erhai e aepesa ngaenigaemi pwe, ‘Pipiiy, ieei iiy Kristus!’ aere ‘Pipiiy, inaan iiy!’ oawsoapw niugiuniug ngaeni.
MAR 13:22 Pwe aaemweoi aeremas repwene oatupwutupw pwe iir Kristus, aere erhai profeta, nge repwene feeori min amwaraar me manaman, pwe repwe oatupwu rhooawe Deus a finiir tae aere repwe mmwenen feeori.
MAR 13:23 Oawpwe aefaennigaemi! Ngaang iya pwaeri ngaenigaemi minikkeei mmwaen aar repwe wen.
MAR 13:24 “Noan raaenin kkewe mwirin oaton waeiraes, aenet epwene rorhonoa, meram esoapw rhiuwen ttin,
MAR 13:25 nge fiiu repwene ppiungiutiw me noan naaeng, nge minikkiwe maemaewaen noan naaeng repwene mwagiut saengi nenieer.
MAR 13:26 Iwe nge miniwe Naiun Aeremas epwene pwaeto me neeiin toapw reen maemaewan me nningen.
MAR 13:27 Epwene fangenoa angkenus reen oanongaen pwaeisiisin faeinaengiy pwe repwe ioni fengaenniy rhooawe Deus a finiir me reen esoapw feoniufan toori esoapw.
MAR 13:28 “Oaw kapwiung saengi waniwan e fig. Oate minikkena raaen ra arawaraw me mechecchoar noa nge a pwiugiuw wow rheon, oawwa giuneei pwe a arapeto neraeg.
MAR 13:29 Epwan taeppen rhag, igine oawweri minikkeei pwe a wen, oawpwene giuneei pwe oatowe ina a arapeto, oamoannatae pwe epwene rhaep.
MAR 13:30 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe oanongaen minikkeei nge epwe wen weni mmwaen iga aeremesaen igina repwe maenoa.
MAR 13:31 Naaeng me soanop repwe soapwonoa, nge aaei kkepas esoapw soapwonoa.
MAR 13:32 “Esooar erhai e giuneei raaenin aere awa na epwe wen minikkeei reen, angkenusun naaeng mwo nge resoapw giuneei, aere miniwe Naiun, pwe aaen Saam rhag.
MAR 13:33 Oaw mmas nge atapeonneogiugaemi, pwe oawse giuneei ineet oatona epwe itto noan.
MAR 13:34 Epwe taeppen rhag aaen erhai mwaaen saei saengi pwugusan nge a siusaengi naiun rhooan engaang pwe repwe nemaeni oanongaen, mwirin a fang ngaeni erhai me erhai aan engaang, nge a anneogiu ngaeni poosun asam we pwe epwe pippipiir.
MAR 13:35 Iwe ina minne oawpwe atapeonneogiugaemi reen, pwe oawse giuneei ineet mwaaen we imwan epwe war, aere epwe war nee oatofaaef, aere nugaenipwoong, aere weni mmwaei raaen, aere nee oatosor.
MAR 13:36 Aere epwe mwetekkaein itto, ese gacch aan epwe werigaemi pwe oaw maiur.
MAR 13:37 Meeta iya aengaenigaemi, iya pwan aengaeniir oanongeer: Oaw atapeonneogiugaemi.”
MAR 14:1 Igina nge a no rhag ruwowu raaen mmwaen miniwe gupwunon Passover me gupwunon fenoawa we esooar yeast reen. Nge soamwooniir patere me sinsein anniug kkewe ra pwiungiuw noan mwoanomwoan wunuunun aar repwe torofi Jesus, pwe repwe noa niiy noa.
MAR 14:2 Ra iura pwe, “Sisoapw feeori minneei oaton gupwunon Passover pwe aeremas rete aefitigogo tae.”
MAR 14:3 Jesus eno noan Bethany noan imwaen Simon, erhai mwaaen kaenepaai mwo igiwe. Oaton we Jesus a mwongo, erhai rhooapwut a toonong faaen eew neo effeeor saengi alabaster nge e oawut ngaeni neoningas e igin cchoaw paniuwan effeeor saengi eew irae itan nard. Rhooapwut we a ripiy neo we iwe a aeniatiw wooan rhimwen Jesus.
MAR 14:4 Aaemweoi aeremas kkewe reno reer ra soong iwe ra kkepas fengaen nee fineer, “Meeta ipitan aan oasonopa noa neoningas naan?
MAR 14:5 Aere efaer chuwaiuw noa nge epwe nigiti eniupwiugiuw senaapiy we silver nge ra ngaenneer man affayeo!” Iwe iir ra igin aepesa aenneewa rhooapwut we.
MAR 14:6 Nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw siusaengi rhooapwut na! Meeta oaw amwagiutiu reen? Egin mwamwaai minne a feeori ngaeniaei.
MAR 14:7 Pwe rhooa affayeo repwe fasiun yor reemi oanongaen oat, nge oatona rhag oaw tipaeni oawpwe tipaengiir iwe oawwa feeori. Nge ngaang isoapw no rhag reemi oanongaen oat.
MAR 14:8 A feeori iugiugiun meeta a mmwen ngaeni; a aeniatiw neo we wooan oanongaei pwe epwe oamoann ngaeni oaton aaei nipwaenipw.
MAR 14:9 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe ese tiwegin iga repwe fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai een me ee, nge minne nieei a feeori nge aeremas repwene fioangei pwe aemaengimaengin faaen itan.”
MAR 14:10 Iwe Judas Iscariot, erhai me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai, a noa reer soamwoonin patere kkewe faaen itaen aan epwene fangenoa tinnimaen Jesus.
MAR 14:11 Ra igin kker reen meeta we a aengaeniir, nge ra ppwon ngaeni pwe repwe ngaenneei naiun senaapiy. Iwe Judas a giutta eew oaton ne egacch pwe epwe fang ngaeniir Jesus.
MAR 14:12 Noan aeyewaen raaenin gupwunon fenoawa we esooar Yeast reen, noan raaenin we ra niir noa lambs kkewe pwe mwongoon Passover we, rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra aeiineow pwe, “Iya iga wo mwerhaen pwe aeipwe noa oamoannatae mwongoon Passover me ee?”
MAR 14:13 Iwe Jesus a fangenoa riiurhai me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawpwe noa noan aepinoamw na, nge oawpwe rhuungi erhai mwaaen e pwigi eew ruumen rhaan. Oawwa tapweei noa
MAR 14:14 noan iimw na epwe noa toonong noan, nge oawwa aengaeni mwaaen na imwan iimw naan pwe: ‘Sinsei e iura pwe: Ifa sengkin na rhooan kkayeo kena naeyi me ngaang aeipwe mwongoon Passover me ee?’
MAR 14:15 Ina epwene pwaeri ngaenigaemi eew sengkin faeregit ina wooan tae, ina a fasiun moannotae noan, nge ina igina oawpwene noa oamoannatae me ee.”
MAR 14:16 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra noa noan aepinoamw we, ra noa weri oanongaen meeta we Jesus e aengaeniir; iwe ra oamoannatae mwongoon Passover we.
MAR 14:17 Igiwe a pwoongtiw, Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai ra itto.
MAR 14:18 Igiwe remooat reen table we pwe re mwongo, Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, erhai me neeimi epwene fangenoa tinnimaei, mwaaen naan nge e tapweaei reen mwongo igina.”
MAR 14:19 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe a aenneew noa nee tipeer reen kkepas kkewe, nge erhai me erhai a rhaepetae aan aeiineo ngaeni Jesus, “Saapw ngaang?”
MAR 14:20 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Epwe erhai me neeimi rhooamwu seig me riiurhai, iiy e tapweaei reen rhirinong anan fenoawa noan saepiy een.
MAR 14:21 Minna Naiun Aeremas epwe maenoa taeppen rhag meeta we Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa; nge epwe ifa mwo aenneewaen mwaaen na iiy e afangmaei noa mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas! Egacch rhag igine rese nainitiw mwaaen een!”
MAR 14:22 Igiwe re rhiuwen mwongo, Jesus a pwigi fenoawa we, a fang aan maeipinen aerhigerhig, iwe a giniiy nge a ngaenneer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a iura pwe, “Oaw pwigi, pwe ieen minne oanongaei.”
MAR 14:23 Mwirin a pwigi eew kkap, a fang aan maeipinen aerhigerhig, nge a fang ngaeniir; iwe oanongeer ra iun me reen.
MAR 14:24 Jesus a aepesa pwe, “Ieen minne cchaei epwe nipinoa pwe faaen iteer towunepeer aeremas, minne cchaei epwene no pwe tiweginin ppwon we aaen Deus ngaenigaemi.
MAR 14:25 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe isoapw rhiuwen iuniumi wine een toori raaenin na ipwe iuniumi wine na effeo me noan minna Mweoiun Deus.”
MAR 14:26 Mwirin ra aeni erheo keoniun aerhigerhig, nge ra toowow ngaeni miniwe rhugun Olives.
MAR 14:27 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oanongaemi nge oawpwe nigitiaei noa, pwe Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Deus epwe niiy noa rhooan neginegin sheep we, nge sheep kkewe repwene toaropas fetaen.’
MAR 14:28 Nge mwirin aaei menaw sefaaen, ipwe gommwonoa Galilee me mmwaemi.”
MAR 14:29 Peter a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaang isoapw nigitiug noa, inamwo me oanongeer nge re nigitiug noa!”
MAR 14:30 Jesus a aengaeni Peter pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaeniug, pwe nee pwongiy mmwaen aaen maniug we epwe keokkeok faaen ruwowu, nge epwe faaen enuuw oamw iura pwe wose giuneaei.”
MAR 14:31 Peter a egius mwo nge e aengimaaw ngaeni, “Esooar faaen eew ipwe aepesa minna, inamwo aere ipwe tapweog reen maenoa!” Nge oanongeer a pwan ina rhag meeta re iura.
MAR 14:32 Iwe ra itto reen eew pwiuneoi itan Gethsemane, nge Jesus a aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Oawmooat igeei iga ngaang ipwe maeipin.”
MAR 14:33 A paeniir noa Peter, James me John. Waeiraes me nee tip cchoaw a itto reen,
MAR 14:34 nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Waeiraesin noan minne nee tipaei egin temoag, arapakkaan rhag epwe niaei noa. Oawno igeei nge oawwa mmas.”
MAR 14:35 A sooar mwet saengiir egius, a oatoratiw nee ppweon nge a maeipin, aere emmwen pwe esoapw toonong noan oaton waeiraes.
MAR 14:36 Iwe a maeipin, “Saam, Semaei! Oanongaen meeta nge emmwen ngaeniug. Pwigi saengiaei kkepaen waeiraes een. Nge soapw minna ngaang i tipaeni, pwe minna een wo tipaeni.”
MAR 14:37 Iwe a sefaaen nge a rhuungiir rhooawe eoniurhai pwe ra maiur. Iwe a aengaeni Peter pwe, “Simon, wa maiur? Ese mmwen mwo nge wopwe mmas noan eew rhag awa?
MAR 14:38 Oaw mmas nge oawwa maeipin pwe oawte ppiungiunong noan sessoat. Ngeon a mwerhaen, nge oanong a apwangapwang.”
MAR 14:39 A pwan sefaaen noa maeipin nge epwan aeni rhag taeppen kkepas kkewe e aeni mmwan.
MAR 14:40 Iwe a sefaaenitiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe nge a pwan giuneer pwe ra pwan maiur; pwe ra igin cchoaw. Nge rese giuneei meeta repwe aengaeni.
MAR 14:41 Enoa aeinuwaen aan sefaaeneto, a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw rhiuwen maiur me aseoseo? A gacch nepan! Awa we ina a tooto! Pipiiy, miniwe Naiun Aeremas ina repwene fangenoa nee paiiur rhooa monofit.
MAR 14:42 Oaw rhimwitae, oaw sia noa. Pipiiy, ieei iiy mwaaen we e fangenoa menewaei!”
MAR 14:43 Jesus e rhiuwen kekkepas, nge Judas iwe erhai me neeiir rhooawe seig me riiurhai a war. Pwuwaen aeremas kkewe re tapweei faaen naiiur saeitan me soapwon irae. Nge re itto faaen iteer soamwoonin patere me sinsein anniug me mwaaen kkewe aar.
MAR 14:44 Rhooan afangmaei noa we a fang aeginn ngaeniir pwuwa we: “Mwaaen na ipwe faeisongei ina mwaaen na oaw tipaeni. Oaw torofi nge oawwa paeninoa nge oawwa posuw.”
MAR 14:45 Igiwe rhag Judas a tooto, a faaeraeg wenewen ngaeni Jesus nge a aengaeni pwe, “Sinsei!”, nge a faeisongei.
MAR 14:46 Iwe ra torofi Jesus nge ra ammwarhiu neogiuw.
MAR 14:47 Nge erhai me neeiir rhooawe re iu a waeitiwow naiun saeitan, nge a fena rhooan akkiuneo we naiun Soamwoonin Patere iwe gopiy noa eew saeningan.
MAR 14:48 Jesus a kkepas tae nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta oawnoa itto faaen naimi saeitan me soapwon irae pwe oawpwe torofiaei, pwe iga aetae ngaang erhai man mwoarho?
MAR 14:49 Raaen me raaen nge ngaang ino reemi i fenai noan Temple we, nge aaemi oawse torofiaei. Nge ina nigiti pwe meeta we e foatofoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus epwe nnet noa.”
MAR 14:50 Iwe rhag nge oanongeer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra siusaengi nge ra fattapw noa.
MAR 14:51 Erhai anian e memmengaag eew mini mmis, e tettapw noa mwirin Jesus. Igiwe ra menaen pwe repwe torofi,
MAR 14:52 a fattapw noa wooan aan esooar mengaagiun, pwe a siusaengi tiw.
MAR 14:53 Iwe ra paeninoa Jesus noan imwaen Soamwoonin Patere we. Iwe soamwoonin patere kkewe, me mwaaen kkewe aar me sinsein anniug ra mwiirh fengaen.
MAR 14:54 Peter e tapweei noa mwirin Jesus me taaw noa nge a noa toonong noan wororaen iimw we imwaen Soamwoonin Patere we. A mooat tiw reer rhooan poos kkewe nge a raengiy reen aengaet we.
MAR 14:55 Soamwooniir patere me oanongeer rhooan council kkewe re giutta meeta eew teren Jesus, pwe repwe niiy noa, nge esooar meeta ne reweri.
MAR 14:56 Towunap rhooa oatupwutupw tae kkepas wooan Jesus, nge aar kkepesaen oatupwutupw nge ese aeffitaeg fengaen.
MAR 14:57 Aaemweoi mwaaen ra iutae nge ra oatupwutupw tae kkepas wooan Jesus, nge ra iura pwe,
MAR 14:58 “Aemaem aeiya rongorong aan aepesa pwe, ‘Ngaang ipwe fereei Temple eei feeorieer aeremas, nge mwirin enuuw raaen ipwe aiusefaaeniy tae pwan eew nge soapw feeorieer aeremas.’ ”
MAR 14:59 Pwan iir mwo nge ese aeffitaeg fengaen mwaenieer.
MAR 14:60 Soamwoonin Patere we a iutae memmweer oanongeer nge aeiineow Jesus, “Esooar minne wopwe paniuwaeni ngaeni kkepas kka mwaaen kaan ra tipi ngaeniug?”
MAR 14:61 Nge Jesus a anniug noa rhag nge esooar no eew kkepas ne e iura. Iwe Soamwoonin Patere we a pwan aeiineo sefaaeniy, “Een minne Kristus, Naiun Deus na Esooar?”
MAR 14:62 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ooa ngaang. Aaemi oawpwene giuneei Naiun Aeremas epwene mooat mwaaenen firhin iwe e oarosaen Mamaaw nge epwe ittiw me weei naaeng wooan toapw.”
MAR 14:63 Iwe Soamwoonin Patere we a fereeitiw mengaagiun nge a iura pwe, “Meeta si rhiuwen pwigiir to rhooan oatuttur reen?
MAR 14:64 Oawwa sipegin rongorong aan aepesa aenneewa Deus. Meeta aaemi mwerhaen?” Oanongeer nge ra pwiungiuw pwe: iiy e monofit nge epwe mae noa.
MAR 14:65 Aaemweoi me neeiir a rhaepetae aar oattuffa, nge re pwaniuw noa mesan nge re peosepa. “Iura iyo e peosepoag!” aar aepesa. Nge poos kkewe ra noa peosepa.
MAR 14:66 Peter eno rhag noan wororaen iimw we nge erhai rhooapwut naiun Soamwoonin Patere we rhooan engaang a itto reen.
MAR 14:67 Igiwe a weri Peter pwe a raengiy oanongan, a fan wenewen ngaeni nge a iura pwe, “Een pwan rhoaniuwaen Jesus rhooan Nazareth we.”
MAR 14:68 Nge iiy a iura pwe, “Aapw, ise giuneei aere metefaaegini meeta mwu wo aepesa,” iwe a toowow niugiun. Iwe rhag nge e keokkeok noa maniug we.
MAR 14:69 Rhooapwut we rhooan engaang a pwan weri sefaaeniy Peter me igiwe nge a pwan aepini ngaeniir rhooawe oaron pwe, “Iiy erhai rhoaniuwaar!”
MAR 14:70 Nge Peter a pwan aepesa pwe ese nnet. Ese ssiunaei noa mwo nge rhooawe oaron ra pwan aengaeni Peter pwe, “Ennet, een pwan erhai rhoaniuwaen mwaaen naan, pwe een pwan erhai re Galilee.”
MAR 14:71 Nge Peter a iura pwe, “Iya aekkepan pwe ngaang i aepesa minne ennet! Deus epwe apwiungiuwaei aere i oatupwutupw! Ise giuneei mwaaen mwu oaw iyaepesa.”
MAR 14:72 Iwe rhag nge a keokkeok maniug we oaruwowwan, nge Peter a maengiy meeta we Jesus e aengaeni, “Weni mmwaen epwe keokkeok maniug, nge een wopwe aepesa faaen enuuw pwe wose giuneaei.” Eppwoar tiw rhag nge esaeng.
MAR 15:1 Nee oatosor moawugowug nge soamwooniir patere me mwaaen kkewe aar ra mwiirh fengaen me sinsein anniug me iir ikkiwe aaemweoi oawuton Council we re pwiungiuw meeta repwene feeori. Ra geoni Jesus nge ra noa fangenoa reen Pilate.
MAR 15:2 Iwe Pilate a aeiineow pwe, “Een minne aar king re Jews?” Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Een minimwu wo aepesa.”
MAR 15:3 Soamwooniir patere kkewe ra tipitae wooan Jesus towunepaen aegiaeg,
MAR 15:4 iwe Pilate a pwan aeiyegiy sefaaeniy pwe, “Wosoapw paniuwaeni? Wo rongorong oanongaen kkepesaen oatuttur kka ra tipi ngaeniug!”
MAR 15:5 Jesus esa paniuwaeni no, nge Pilate a mwaar noa.
MAR 15:6 Oanongaen raeg reen gupwunon Passover, Pilate egaen saeneti noa erhai rhooan kanepwus, iyo we aeremas re tingoar.
MAR 15:7 Noan oaton naan nge eno erhai mwaaen noan kanepwus itan Barabbas, eno neeiir aaemweoi rhooa aenneew iwe resooaw nni aeremas faei oaton moawun.
MAR 15:8 Igiwe aeremas towunap ra rhu fengaen, ra tingoar ngaeni Pilate pwe epwe feeori wunuunun minne a fasiun feoffeeori,
MAR 15:9 iwe Pilate a aeiineeor pwe, “Oaw mwerhaen pwe ipwe saeneti ngaenigaemi kingaaen Jews een?”
MAR 15:10 Pilate e giuneei pwe soamwooniir patere kkewe minne re fangenoa Jesus reen pwe epwe noa apwiung faaen itaen aar noanowo ngaeni.
MAR 15:11 Nge soamwooniir patere kkewe ra aetemaeginiy ngaeniir aeremas kkewe pwe repwe tingoareei Pilate, pwe epwe saeneti ngaeniir Barabbas.
MAR 15:12 Iwe Pilate a pwan aeiineo sefaaen ngaeniir pwe, “Nge meeta ipwe feeori ngaeni aeremas e oaw faingi pwe kingaaen Jews?”
MAR 15:13 Ra iyaekkepwas temoag tae, “Kurusuw noa!”
MAR 15:14 Pilate a pwan aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta taeppen wegitaeg aenneew e a feeori?” Nge iir ra pwan oatomoga aar iyaekkepwas pwe, “Kurusuw noa!”
MAR 15:15 Pilate e tipaeni pwe epwe amwamwaaiuw nee tipeer aeremas kkewe, iwe a saeneti ngaeniir Barabbas, nge ra wirhiy Jesus nge a fangenoa pwe repwe noa kurusuw noa.
MAR 15:16 Sonotaw kkewe ra paeninoa Jesus noan wororaen iimw we imwaen governor nge ra faingiir to oanongeer sonotaw kkewe rhoaniuwaar.
MAR 15:17 Ra aememmengaagiu ngaeni erheo mengaag siungiurhoan, nge ra pwan fiti eew mwaer saengi irae towfanfan iwe ra ngaettae wooan rhimwen.
MAR 15:18 Iwe ra rhaepetae ne aesirowu: “Sirow woamw, Kingaen Jews!”
MAR 15:19 Ra wirhiy rhimwen ngaeni efoarh irae, nge ra oattuffa, nge ra foatotiw nge ra aesirowu ngaeni.
MAR 15:20 Igiwe ra moann reen aar aeni aegekkaei, ra pwiniti saengi mengaag siungiurhoan we, nge ra aememmengaagiu ngaeni ikkiwe sipegin mengaagiun. Iwe ra paeninoa pwe repwene noa kurusuw noa.
MAR 15:21 Igiwe re faaeraeg noa wooan aan we, nge ra noa rhuungi erhai mwaaen itan Simon saengi Cyrene, e itto saengi eew soapw pwe epwe toonong noan taeninimw we, nge sonotaw kkewe ra aengimaw ngaeni pwe epwe aiufera kurus we aaen Jesus. (Simon semaen Alexander me Rufus.)
MAR 15:22 Ra paeninoa Jesus reen eew pwiuneoi itan Golgotha, wewen nge “Nenien Peopeoi Rhimw.”
MAR 15:23 Igaan iga ra itto aiuniu ngaeni Jesus eew wine e nofit fengaen me aekkaew saefei itan myrrh, nge ese mwerhaen iuniumi.
MAR 15:24 Ra kurusuw noa Jesus, nge ra inetiy mengaag kkewe wooar, nge re aekkaerh dice wooar ngaere iyo epwe pwigi ifa.
MAR 15:25 A kiung tiwowu nee oatosor iga re kurusuw noa.
MAR 15:26 Foatofoaton minne ra tipi ngaeni e iura pwe: “Ieei Kingaen Jews.”
MAR 15:27 Repwan kurusuw noa riiurhai rhooa mwoarho oaron Jesus, erhai peig mwaaenen, nge erhai peig rhooapwuton.
MAR 15:28 [Ieei wunuunun pwe epwe pwaenoan miniwe Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, “Refeeori pwe iiy erhai aeremas aenneew.”]
MAR 15:29 Aeremas kkewe re faaeraeg noa me oaron Jesus re iurhiugi rhimweer nge re aepesa aenneewa Jesus, “Aa! Een miniwe wo iura pwe wopwe fereeitiw Temple we nge wa aiusefaaeniy tae noan enuuw raaen!
MAR 15:30 Iwe teeotiw me wooan kurus na pwe wopwe aemenewoag!”
MAR 15:31 Epwan ina rhag wunuunun soamwoonin patere me sinsein anniug kkewe re aeni aegekkaei Jesus reen aar aepesa pwe, “A aemenewaar aaemweoi, nge ese mmwenen aemenewa oanongan!
MAR 15:32 Oawsa pipiiy Kristus een, iwe Kingaen Israel, aan epwe teeotiw saengi kurusuna igina, ina nge sipwe niugiuniug ngaeni!” Nge pwan rhooa kkewe re tapweei reen kurus repwan aessaewa Jesus.
MAR 15:33 Saengi nugunupaen oanowas nge oanongaen faniuw we a rorhappiung noa noan enuuw konook.
MAR 15:34 Igiwe a enuuw konook nge Jesus a iyaekkepwas temoag tae pwe, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabachthani?” faan nge, “Aaei Deus, aaei Deus, meeta wa nigitiaei noa reen?”
MAR 15:35 Aaemweoi aeremas kkewe re iu oaron ra rongorong kkepas kkewe, ra iura pwe, “Oaw rongorong, a faingi Elijah!”
MAR 15:36 Erhai me neeiir a fattapweto reen faaen eew faerewa, a rhirinong noan wine emwaenn, nge a iseni tae nee soapwon efoarh irae. A aeititae irae we ngaeni ewaen Jesus nge a iura pwe, “Weti sipwe pipiiy aere Elijah epwe itto ateeotiwei me wooan kurus na!”
MAR 15:37 E apwas temoag noa rhag faaen eew, nge a nurh noa aan ngasangas.
MAR 15:38 Mengaag we e tteoraeg noan Temple we mwo nge e taeringatiw faaen ruwowu, saengi wooan ittiw faan.
MAR 15:39 Erhai soamwoonin sonotaw e iu mmwaen kurus we eweri wunuunun aaen Jesus maenoa, a iura pwe, “Ennetaen pwe mwaaen een nge Naiun Deus!”
MAR 15:40 Aaemweoi rhooapwut reno igiwe, re oawruruto me itaaw. Neeiir rhooapwut kkewe nge Maria Magdalene, Maria we inaen James me Joseph iwe me pwan Salome.
MAR 15:41 Re tapweei Jesus me noan Galilee reen aar tittipaengi. Towunepeer rhooapwut kkewe re tapweeito Jesus me Jerusalem repwan no igiwe.
MAR 15:42 A faaeraeg ngaeni nee oatofaaef nge Joseph re Arimathea we a tooto. Iiy erhai e regin oawoai me noan Council we, iwe e wewweti itton minna Mweoiun Deus. A raaenin Aenimowu miniwe (eew raaen mmwaen raaenin Sabbath), noan maemaewaen nee tipaen Joseph a itto reen Pilate a itto tingoar miniwe oanongaen Jesus.
MAR 15:44 Nge Pilate a riutae igiwe e rongorong pwe Jesus a fasiun maenoa. A tengaeg soamwoonin sonotaw we nge a aeiineow aere a ssiunaei aaen Jesus maenoa.
MAR 15:45 Mwirin aan rongorong meeta we sonotaw we e iura reen mmwenen Jesus, Pilate a aengaeni Joseph pwe epwe noa pwigi mini oanongaen Jesus.
MAR 15:46 Joseph meoni erheo mengaag pwerh ffeo, a iseni tiw miniwe oanongan Jesus me wooan kurus we nge a tiugiumi ngaeni mengaag we, a oawnanong noan paeyi we ekken wow me neeiin faai. Iwe a oasoagopeniy to efai faai gin temoag reen aesemaen paeyi we.
MAR 15:47 Maria Magdalene me Maria we inaen Joseph re pipiiy nge ra giuneei iya re paeiaeni miniwe oanongaen Jesus ee.
MAR 16:1 Mwirin raaenin Sabbath, nge Maria Magdalene, Maria we inaen James iwe me Salome ra chuwaai neoningas, pwe repwe noa aepiti miniwe oanongaen Jesus.
MAR 16:2 Weni mmwaei raaenin Sunday, oatowe aenet epwene teeotae, ra noa reen paeyi we.
MAR 16:3 Wooan aar faaeraeg noa, ra kkepas fengaen nee fineer, “Iyo epwe peniy ngaenigirh fai we mesaen paeyi we?” (Egin faeregit fai we.) Nge renoa fannoai paeyi we, ra giuneei pwe fai we a faer mwagiut saengi aesemaen paeyi we.
MAR 16:5 Igiwe ra toonong noan paeyi we, ra weri erhai mwaaen anian emooat peig mwaaenen paeyi we, e memmengaag min pwerhepwerh, nge ra mesag reen.
MAR 16:6 A aengaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw mesag. I giuneei pwe oaw giutta Jesus re Nazareth we re kurusuw noa. Esa nono igeei, a menaw sefaaen! Oaw pipiiy, igaan igiwe re oawnatiw ee.
MAR 16:7 Iwe oawnoa aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun me pwan Peter: ‘Iiy ina epwene gommw noa Galilee me mmwaemi; iginaan minne oawpwene noa weri me ee, taeppen rhag meeta we e aengaenigaemi.’ ”
MAR 16:8 Iwe ra toowow nge ra fattapw saengi paeyi we, noan aar mesag me riu. Nge rese aepesa ngaeni mwo nge erhai, pwe ra igin mesag.
MAR 16:9 [Mwirin aaen Jesus menaw sefaaen nee oatosoron raaenin Sunday we, egommwaen pwae ngaeni Maria Magdalene, iwe e oatowowuw fiusiuman aniu aenneew me reen.
MAR 16:10 Niewe a noa iwe a noa aengaeniir rhooawe rhinaan. Rhooawe re sessaeng reen aenneewaen nee tipeer;
MAR 16:11 nge igiwe ra rongorong pwe Jesus a menaw sefaaen pwe iiy a weri, nge rese niugiuniug ngaeni.
MAR 16:12 Mwirin minneei nge Jesus a pwaenoan pwan eew taeppen wegitaeg ngaeniir riiurhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe igiwe re faaeraeg ngaeni aepinoamw we.
MAR 16:13 Ra sefaaen nge ra aengaeniir ikkiwe aaemweoi, nge iir rese niugiuniug reer.
MAR 16:14 Oarosan noa nge Jesus a pwae ngaeniir rhooawe seig me erhai igiwe iir re mwongo. A songetiir, pwe esooar aar niugiuniug, ra pwan tipoarorh, pwe rese niugiur rhooawe ra weri pwe Jesus a menaw sefaaen.
MAR 16:15 Iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawnoa wooan oanongaen faniuw oawpwe noa fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai een ngaeniir oanongeer aeremas.
MAR 16:16 Iyo e niugiuniug nge a paptismus nge epwe menaw, nge iyo ese niugiuniug nge epwe aegaeregaer.
MAR 16:17 Rhooakka re niugiuniug repwe fang maemaeweer pwe repwe feeori manaman: repwe asiiur aniu aenneew faaen itaei; nge repwe kkepesaen noa eew me eew faniuw,
MAR 16:18 ngaere repwe pweipwog sowufaeng aere iun pwoisiun, nge resoapw woas; nge repwe iseni tae paiiur wooar rhooa semwaai nge repwe cchipw tae.”
MAR 16:19 Mwirin aaen Soamwoon Jesus kkepas ngaeniir, a ittae naaeng a ittae mooat peig mwaaenen Deus.
MAR 16:20 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra noa fenai wooan oanongaen pwiuneoi, nge Soamwoon e engaang neeiir nge e pwaeri noa aar fenai pwe ennet reen oanongaen manaman kkewe ra feeori.] [Rhooapwut kkewe ra noa reen Peter me rhooawe rhinan ra noa fioangei ngaeniir oanongaen meeta kkewe re rongorong. Mwirin minneei nge Jesus wooan oanongan a fang wow rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe repwe noa fenai fetaeneei saengi eotiw toori netow kkepas mwamwaai we kkepesaen menaw na esooar ssiaaenin.]
LUK 1:1 Aerhaengerhaeng Theophilus: Aeremas towunap re oarhorho pwe repwe foatogi kkepesaen meeta kka a wewwen me neeimaem.
LUK 1:2 Iir ra foatogi meeta kka e itto ngaeniir me reer rhooakka ra fasiun weri minikkeei me nee rhaepetaen nge ra aepesa iiy kkepas mwamwaai we.
LUK 1:3 Iwe een pwonno iga iya wori firhiy oanongaen minikkeei saengi pweoneotaen, iya niuwaennei pwe epwe mwamwaai pwe ipwe foatogi wunuunun aetettaeniin ngaeniug.
LUK 1:4 Iya feeori minneei pwe een wopwe giuneei gacchiuw minna wenewenen oanongaen meeta kkewe ra kapwiung ngaeniug.
LUK 1:5 Noan oatowe Erotes eno pwe kingaaen Judea, eno erhai patere itan Zechariah, iiy e tapweei tettaenin patereen Abijah. Itaen rhooapwut na rhooan ngaenneyan nge Elizabeth; nge iiy epwan itto saengi eew faminiin patere.
LUK 1:6 Iir me riiurhai nge e igin mwamwaai noan meneweer faaen mesaen Deus nge re tapweei gacchiuw oanongaen aaen Soamwoon anniug me akkiuneo.
LUK 1:7 Iir esooar naiiur pwe Elizabeth ese mmwenen nainai, nge igina mwo nge ra igin tugufaeyi.
LUK 1:8 Eraaen nge Zechariah a itinong feeori aan engaang noan Temple we, pwe a toori oaton ginigin we aan epwe engaang noan raaenin we.
LUK 1:9 Noan peigin aaen engaang patere, nge iiy minne ra fini pwe epwe fifi oappwongesaen wooan antar. Iwe a toonong noan Temple we aaen Soamwoon,
LUK 1:10 nge rhooa towunap kkewe reno niugiun pwe re maeipin reen oatowe iiy e fifi oappwongas kkewe.
LUK 1:11 Angkenus we naiun Soamwoon a pwae ngaeni, nge e iu peig mwaaenen antar we igiwe oappwongas we eno ee.
LUK 1:12 Oatowe Zechariah a weri mwaaen we, a riu nge a mesag tae.
LUK 1:13 Angkenus we a aengaeni pwe, “Wosoapw mesag, Zechariah! Deus a rongorong oamw maeipin, iwe Elizabeth we reemw epwene naini erhai aetemwaaen. Wopwe aeitae ngaeni pwe John.
LUK 1:14 Epwene ifa mwo oamw wenepwu me pwapwa, iwe me aar aaemweoi wenepwu reen aan supwutiw.
LUK 1:15 John epwene igin taegias me faaen mesaen Deus. Esoapw iun wine me aerhi. Saengi rhag aan wupwutiw epwene sseog reen Espritu Santus,
LUK 1:16 nge iiy epwene pwigiir towunepeer re Israel ngaeni Soamwoon we aar Deus.
LUK 1:17 Iiy epwe gommw me weni mmwaei Soamwoon, pwe e mamaaw pwe taeppen rhag profeta we Elijah. Epwe aesefaaeni fengaenniir saam me naai pwe repwe eew rhag; iiy epwe wegiti sefaaeniir rhooa serong feon ngaeni niunniuwaen mwamwaai; nge epwe oamoannaar tae aeremas weni mmwaei Soamwoon.”
LUK 1:18 Zechariah a aengaeni angkenus we pwe, “Epwe ifa wusun nge iya giuneei pwe ennet minneei? Ngaang iya tugufaeyi, nge manna pwiuniuwaei nge a pwan tugufaeyi.”
LUK 1:19 “Ngaang Gabriel,” mwaeniaen angkenus we. “Ngaang iyiu weni mmwaen Deus, iwe iiy minne efang ngaang pwe ipwe pwigito kkepas mwamwaai een reemw.
LUK 1:20 Nge een wose niugiuniug ngaeni mwaeniaei, nge minneei epwe noa pwaetae minna wenewenen noan oaton naan. Iwe nge iga wose niugiuniug, een wosoapw mmwenen kkepas no; wopwene anniug noa rhag toori aan itto iiy raaenin na iya fasiun ppwoneei ngaeniug.”
LUK 1:21 Noan oateei nge aeremas re wewweti Zechariah nge ra niunniuwaennei aere meeta a igin itinong pwongiy noan Temple we reen.
LUK 1:22 Enoa toowow, nge esa mmwenen kkepas ngaeniir no, nge ra giuneei pwe eyor minne a itinong weri me noan Temple we. Igiwe esa mmwenen kkepas no, iwe a taenepom ngaeniir rhag.
LUK 1:23 Oatowe a moanno noa engaang we aan noan Temple we, Zechariah a sefaaen noa nee iimw.
LUK 1:24 Enoa eew oaton nge Elizabeth a pwoopwo nge a no rhag nee iimw noan nimowu meram.
LUK 1:25 “Ennaen igina minne Deus a tipaengiaei,” mwaeniaen niewe. “A arhiuwa saengiaei aessaewaei me neeiir rhooanap!”
LUK 1:26 Noan oawonowuwaen meremaen Elizabeth Deus a fangetiw angkenus we Gabriel noan eew aepinoamwon Galilee itan Nazareth.
LUK 1:27 Eyor eew aan kkepesaen oarong ngaeni erhai rhooapwut a kkefoat ngaeni mwaaen we itan Joseph, iwe itto saengi teeo we aan king David. Itan nge Maria.
LUK 1:28 Angkenus we a itto reen niewe nge a iura pwe, “Oapoas epwe no reemw! Soamwoon eno reemw nge a aewenepwuwoag.”
LUK 1:29 Maria a gin riutae reen miniwe mwaeniaen angkenus we, nge a niuwaennei meeta faan iiy kkepas kkewe.
LUK 1:30 Angkenus we a aengaeni niewe pwe, “Wosoapw mesag, Maria; pwe Deus minne e igin mwamwaai ngaeniug.
LUK 1:31 Wopwene pwoopwo nge wa nainitiw erhai aetemwaaen, nge wa aeitae ngaeni pwe Jesus.
LUK 1:32 Epwe igin taegias nge epwe ffai pwe iiy naiun Deus na oarosaen taegias. Soamwoon Deus epwene feeori pwe iiy king taeppen rhag David we aan rhaepeto,
LUK 1:33 nge epwe no pwe king reen teeo we aaen Jacob oanongaen oat; minna mweoiun ina esooar aigiugiun!”
LUK 1:34 Maria a aengaeni angkenus we pwe, “Ngaang erhai piirgo. Epwe ifa wusun rhag nge a mmwen minneei?”
LUK 1:35 Angkenus we a iura pwe, “Espritu Santus epwene ittiw woamw, nge minna kkaeinen Deus ina oarosaen taegias a no woamw. Nge faaen minneei nge aetena esooar epwene ffai pwe Naiun Deus.
LUK 1:36 Wo maengiy rhag Elizabeth we re pwugusoamw? Iwe re iura pwe esoapw mmwenen nainai no, nge igina nge a wonowu mereman, inamwo iga a igin tugufaeyi.
LUK 1:37 Pwe esooar eew meeta ne Deus esoapw mmwenen feeori.”
LUK 1:38 “Ngaang erhai naiun Soamwoon rhooan akkiuneo,” aaen Maria iura. “Nigiti pwe epwe wen ngaeniaei petenaen kkepas mwu wa iura.” Iwe angkenus we a siusaengi niewe.
LUK 1:39 Ese mmwaei mwo me weni mwirin nge Maria a oamoannatae epwe mwekkaei noa reen eew aepinoamw eno neeiin rhugun Judea.
LUK 1:40 A noa reen imwaen Zechariah pwe epwe noa koapwong ngaeni Elizabeth.
LUK 1:41 Igiwe Elizabeth a rongorong aaen Maria koapwong nge aetewe naiun a mwagiut me noan upwan. Elizabeth a sseog reen Espritu Santus
LUK 1:42 iwe a aekkepwas faeregit tae nge a iura pwe, “Een minne wa oarosaen wenepwu me neeiir rhooapwut, nge epwan wenepwu aetena wopwe naini!
LUK 1:43 Meeta ppweoniun aaen min mwamwaai eei aan epwe itto wen ngaeniaei, iye nie inaen soamwoon a itto sengaeriaei?
LUK 1:44 Pwe igiwe rhag i rongorong oamw koapwong, iwe nge aete noan upwaei a mwagiut reen aaen kker.
LUK 1:45 Ifa mwo oamw kker pwe wa niugiuw pwe kkepas we aaen Soamwoon ngaeniug nge epwe nnet noa!”
LUK 1:46 Maria a iura pwe, “Nee tipaei a aepingepinga Soamwoon;
LUK 1:47 ngeoniuy apwapwa pwe aegin Deus iiy aaei Rhooan Aemenaw,
LUK 1:48 pwe iya maengiaei ngaang naiun rhooan akkiuneo man sessoan! Saengi igina oanongeer aeremas nge repwene faingiaei pwe ngaang wenepwu,
LUK 1:49 pwe reen min mwamwaai kka Deus na oarosaen kkeman a feeori ngaeniaei. Minna itan ina essoar;
LUK 1:50 saengi eew me eew saaer e pwaeri aan ffayeo ngaeniir rhooan oassoara.
LUK 1:51 A aeiti noa paiun na e kkeman nge e oamwotoraar noa rhooana re namanam taegias noan aar niunniuwaen.
LUK 1:52 A oatoraar tiw king kka re mamaaw me wooan nenien mooatoor, nge e saeregiir tae ikka re sessoan.
LUK 1:53 A oamwongoor rhooa pecchai ngaeni min mwamwaai, nge a aefengaar noa rhooa pisaegisaeg nge esooar oawton paiiur.
LUK 1:54 Iiy e ammwarhiuto rhag ppwon we aan ngaeniir rhooawe rhaepetorh, nge a itto pwe epwe fang tipaengieer rhooawe re Israel iwe naiun rhooan akkiuneo. Iiy e maengiy rhag pwe epwe pwaeri ffaayeo we aan ngaeni Abraham me oanongeer rhooan teowe aan iwe esooar iaenin!”
LUK 1:56 Epwe enuuw meram aaen Maria no aegini reen Elizabeth nge a sefaaeniti pwugusan.
LUK 1:57 Enoa tooto oatowe Elizabeth epwene nainai, nge a timenewaegini erhai aetemwaaen.
LUK 1:58 Rhooan weni oaron me rhooa kkewe repwugusan ra rongorong ifa mwo aaen soamwoon mwamwaai ngaeni, iwe iir ra maegin tapweei reen aan pwapwa.
LUK 1:59 Igiwe aetewe a eew week aan no, ra itto repwe circumcise aegini, nge repwene aeitae ngaeni pwe Zechariah, aeiteitaen mwaaen we seman.
LUK 1:60 Nge rhooapwut we inan a iura pwe, “Aapw! Epwe itaeni John.”
LUK 1:61 Nge ra aengaeni niewe pwe, “Aetae esooar re pwugusoamw ne e ina itan!”
LUK 1:62 Nge iir ra taenepom ngaeni mwaaen we seman, meeta e mwerhaen pwe aetewe epwe itaeni.
LUK 1:63 Zechariah a tingoar eew pwapwior nge a foatogitiw pwe, “Itan nge John.” Ifa mwo aar riutae rhooawe!
LUK 1:64 Reen oatonaan rhag nge Zechariah a mmwenen kkepas, a rhaepetae aan aepingepinga Deus.
LUK 1:65 Rhooan no oaroor ra igin mesag, nge kkepesaen minikkeei a rheeoi noa wooan rhugun aepinoamwon Judea.
LUK 1:66 Rhooan rongorong kkepas we ra gaen niunniuwaennei nge ra aeiyeg pwe, “Meeta aeteei epwene no pwe iiy?” Pwe igiwe epwae noa pwe maemaewaen Soamwoon eno wooan.
LUK 1:67 Zechariah we semaen John a sseog noa reen Espritu Santus, nge a aepesa wow kkepesaen oarongorong we aaen Deus:
LUK 1:68 “Sipwe aepingepinga Soamwoon iwe aaen Israel Deus! A itto epwe fang tipaengiaen naiun aeremas nge aessaenetaegiir noa.
LUK 1:69 A fang ngaenigirh naiurh rhooan aemenaw e igin kkeman, rhooan teowe aaen David iwe naiun rhooan akkiuneo.
LUK 1:70 A ppwon ngaeniir profeta kkewe mweoiwe
LUK 1:71 pwe iiy epwe aemenewaegirh saengiir rhooan kkoapwut ngaenigirh, saengi maemaeweer rhooakkena re aeni giirh aeffaeioapwut.
LUK 1:72 E iura pwe epwe pwaeri ngaeniir rhooakkena rhaepetorh ffaiyeo iwe me e maengiy ppwon ssoar we aan.
LUK 1:73 Noan aan aekkepan ngaeni Abraham we rhaepetorh iiy eppwon pwe epwe aemenewaegirh saengiir rhooan oapwutaegirh, iwe nge e nigiti ngaenigirh pwe sisoapw mesag noan aarh engaang ngaeni,
LUK 1:75 pwonno giirh sipwe ssoar nge si mwamwaai me weni mmwan noan oanongaen raaenin aarh menaw.
LUK 1:76 “Een naeyi, wopwene ffai pwe profeta we naiun Deus na oarosaen taegias. Een wopwene mmweei Soamwoon wopwene oamoannatae ennepan,
LUK 1:77 wopwe aengaeniir naiun aeremas repwene menaw igine emwus noa monofitiir.
LUK 1:78 Naiurh Deus ina e sseogiun ffayeo nge etip mererhaeg. Epwe feeori pwe seremaen menaw epwe ttinitiw wooarh
LUK 1:79 nge seremaen wooan naaeng epwe ttin noa wooar rhooa no noan rorhappiungiun maenoa, pwe epwe aeitiiti mesaen gupworh noan ennepaen oapoas.”
LUK 1:80 Iwe a temoag tae aetewe iwe a mamaaw noa oanongan me ngeoniun. Iwe a no noan desert we e toori noan raaenin we a pwae ngaeniir re Israel.
LUK 2:1 Noan oatonaan nge Soamwoonin Rome we Augustus a akkiuneo pwe epwe yor paaepaen fainaaw noan oanongaen faniuw kka nemaeniaen Rome.
LUK 2:2 Reen igiwe aeyewaen paaepae a rhaepetae nge Quirinius minne eno pwe governor reen Syria.
LUK 2:3 Erhai me erhai nge enoa foatogi itan reen aan taeninimw.
LUK 2:4 Joseph a noa saengi Nazareth noan Galilee a noa ngaeni Bethlehem noan Judea, igiwe esiupwutiw king David me ee. Joseph a noa igiwe pwe igiwe iiy teoteeon David.
LUK 2:5 A noa pwe enoa foatogi iteer me Maria, rhooapwut we a no pwe kkefoaton. Niewe a pwoopwo,
LUK 2:6 oatowe reno Bethlehem, a toori oaton aan supw aetewe naiun.
LUK 2:7 Niewe a timenewaegini aetemwaaen we mesaemmwaei naiun, nge a tiugiumi nong noan mengaag nge e oana nong noan miniwe nenien anan maan, pwe igiwe esooar no nenieer me noan imwaen waseona we.
LUK 2:8 Eyor aekkaerhai rhooan neginegin sheep reno wooan menaai nee pwoong re aefaenniir naiiur maan.
LUK 2:9 Erhai naiun Soamwoon angkenus a pwae ngaeniir, nge nningen Soamwoon a ttinitiw wooar. Ra igin mesag,
LUK 2:10 nge angkenus we a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw mesag! Ngaang iya pwigito eew kkepas mwamwaai reemi, kkepas een epwe pwigito eew kker temoag ngaeniir oanongeer aeremas.
LUK 2:11 Raaenin eei noan aepinoamw we aepinoamwon David rhooan aemenaw we aaemi a supw — Kristus we Soamwoon!
LUK 2:12 Ieen minne epwe aniugiuniugiuw ngaenigaemi: oawpwe noa rhuungi erhai wonigaet e tiugiutiug noan mengaag nge ewon noan nenien anan maan.”
LUK 2:13 Ese mmwaei mwo nge eew mwirhaen angkenus a pwae noa me oaron angkenus we erhai, ra aepingepinga Deus noan aar keon:
LUK 2:14 “Sia fang ssoar ngaeni Deus na eno wooai naaeng, nge oapoas enoa ngaeniir rhooakkena e mwamwaai nee tipan wooar!”
LUK 2:15 Oatowe angkenus kkewe ra nigitiir ra sefaaen noa naaeng, rhooan neginegin sheep kkewe ra kkepas fengaen nee fineer pwe, “Sa noa Bethlehem sipwe noa weri meeta minne a wen, minne Soamwoon a aengaenigirh.”
LUK 2:16 Iwe ra siu mwetekkaei noa me igiwe, nge ra noa weri Maria me Joseph iwe nge reweri wonigaet we ewon noan nenien anan maan.
LUK 2:17 Oatowe ra weri aetewe, nge ra aengaeniir rhooawe meeta we angkenus e iura reen aetewe.
LUK 2:18 Oanongeer iyo kkewe re rongorong miniwe nge ra mwaar reen miniwe mwaenieer rhooawe rhooan neginegin sheep kkewe.
LUK 2:19 Maria a maeng ngaeni oanongaen minikkeei nge a niuwaennei nong rhag nee tipan.
LUK 2:20 Rhooan neginegin sheep ra sefaaen, nge ra aepingepinga Deus reen igiwe meeta kkewe ra rongorong nge ra weri; nge taeppen rhag miniwe angkenus we a aengaeniir.
LUK 2:21 Enoa eew week weni mwirin, reen oatowe aetewe epwene circumcise, ra aeita ngaeni pwe Jesus, itiwe angkenus a fasiun ngaenneer weni mmwaen aan supw.
LUK 2:22 A toori oatowe Joseph me Maria repwe feeori eew pwaengepwaengin aenimenim, pwe ina miniwe oasoapwosoapw we aaen Moses e aepesa. Iwe ra pwigi noa aetewe Jerusalem pwe repwe noa pwaeri ngaeni Soamwoon,
LUK 2:23 pwe ina miniwe effoat noan oasoapwosoapw we aaen Soamwoon pwe, “Oanongaen mesaemmwaei naiiur aetemwaaen nge repwe aeyimweoiiur ngaeni Soamwoon.”
LUK 2:24 Ra pwai noa pwe repwe noa aeni maenigaech riiurhai dove aere riiurhai aeppaen pigeons, pwe ina miniwe e fasiun no noan oasoapwosoapw we aaen Soamwoon.
LUK 2:25 Noan oatonaan nge eno erhai mwaaen itan Simeon eno noan Jerusalem. Iiy erhai mwaaen reepiy nge e mwamwaai noan menewan nge e wewweti oatona epwe cchipw Israel. Espritu Santus a teeotiw wooan
LUK 2:26 nge a aniugiuniugiuw ngaeni pwe iiy esoapw mae weni mmwaen epwe weri Kristus we Soamwoon e ppwoneei.
LUK 2:27 Espritu Santus a paeni Simeon a itinong noan Temple we. Oatowe rhooawe inan me seman ra pwigito goagoa we noan Temple we pwe repwe feeori ngaeni meeta we oasoapwosoapw e iura,
LUK 2:28 Simeon a ammwarhiu aetewe noan paiun nge a fang aerhigerhig ngaeni Deus:
LUK 2:29 “Igina Soamwoon, een wa iseni ppwon we oamw, nge wa mwiuti ngaeni noawumw rhooan akkiuneo pwe epwe noa noan oapoas.
LUK 2:30 Iya weri ngaeni mesaei oamw engaengaen menaw,
LUK 2:31 iwe een wa oamoannatae me weni mmweer oanongeer aeremas:
LUK 2:32 eew seram epwe pwaeri ngaeniir re Gentiles mwerhaen na oamw iwe me pwigito nning ngaeniir noawumw re Israel.”
LUK 2:33 Rhooawe inan me seman aetewe ra mwaar reen meeta kkewe Simeon e iura reen aetewe.
LUK 2:34 Simeon a aepiniir nge a aengaeni Maria, iwe inaen aetewe, “Aeteei a ffin tae me reen Deus pwe epwe oatoaropa nge e aemenewaer towunepaen re Israel. Iiy epwe no pwe eew aeginn me reen Deus pwe towunepaen aeremas repwe appaniuwaeni noan aar kkepas,
LUK 2:35 iwe a pwaeritae noan niunniuwaen mwoanomwoan kena aar. Nge niemaam eweei kaengin saeitan, epwe fereei pwunnomw.”
LUK 2:36 Eno erhai profeta tugufaeyi itan Anna nge a mae noa pwiuniuwan. Nge iiy naiun Phanuel saengi aeinang we aaen Asher. Fisuuw raeg aan pwiuppwiuniuw nge emae noa pwiuniuwan. Nge igina a waniig me faawu raegin. Iiy ese nigiti Temple we; pwoong me raaen nge e aesirowu noa rhag Deus, e aecchigipin nge e memmaeipin.
LUK 2:38 Noan rhag awa we e tooto nge a fang aerhigerhig ngaeni Deus nge a fioangei mmwenen aetewe ngaeniir oanongeer rhooa kkewe re iya wetiwet ngaeni Deus pwe epwe saeneti noa Jerusalem.
LUK 2:39 Igiwe Joseph me Maria ra moannon feeori minikkewe eno noan anniug we aaen Soamwoon, nge ra sefaaen ngaeni miniwe aepinoamwoor iwe Nazareth me noan Galilee.
LUK 2:40 A tootae aetewe nge amamaaw noa, nge a sseog noan reepiy nge Deus a no wooan.
LUK 2:41 Oanongaen raeg nge rhooawe inaen me seman Jesus ra noa Jerusalem pwe repwe noa tapweei gupwunon Passover we.
LUK 2:42 Oatowe a seig me ruwowu raegin Jesus nge ra noa tapweei gupwun we taeppen rhag miniwe regaen feoffeeori.
LUK 2:43 Enoa moanno noa gupwun we, rhooawe ra sefaaen noa nee pwuguseer, nge Jesus a notiw noan Jerusalem. Rhooawe inan me seman rese giuneei minneei;
LUK 2:44 iir re niuwaennei pwe eno reer rhooanap we, iwe eraaen nniuw aar nennoa nge a rhaepetae aar kiukkiutta fetaeneei aetewe me neeiir aei oaroor me maereyaereer.
LUK 2:45 Nge iir rese weri, iwe ra sefaaen noa giutta me Jerusalem.
LUK 2:46 Wooan ayeoniuraenin aar giut nge ra noa weri me noan Temple we, emooat neeiir sinsein Jews kkewe, e aiussaening ngaeniir nge e kekkepas aeiineo ngaeniir.
LUK 2:47 Oanongeer rhooa kkewe re rongorong mwaenian nge remwaar noa reen aesefaaenin kkepas aeiyeg kkewe aan.
LUK 2:48 Rhooawe inan me seman re riutae reen igiwe ra noa weri, iwe nge rhooapwut we inan a aengaeni pwe, “Naeyi, meeta wa feeori ngaenigemaem minneei reen? Pwe ngaang me mwaaen e semoamw aeiya gin noanineeng reen aemaem giutta fetaeneog.”
LUK 2:49 Nge iya paniuwaeniir nge a iura pwe, “Meeta aaemi oawnoa giutta fetaeneaei reen? Oawse giuneei pwe ngaang ipwe no noan imwaen minna Semaei?”
LUK 2:50 Nge iir rese metaf reen miniwe e iura.
LUK 2:51 Iwe Jesus a tapweei sefaaeniir noa Nazareth, nge a noa aiussaening ngaeniir. Miniwe inaan a iseni nong rhag oanongan nee tipan.
LUK 2:52 Jesus a temoag tae wooan oanongan me aan reepiy me temoagon rhaengiin me reen Deus me aeremas.
LUK 3:1 Noan miniwe seig me nimowu raeg aan Soamwoonin Rome we Tiberius nemenem, nge Pontius Pilate minne governor reen Judea, nge Erotes minne soamwoonin Galilee, iwe nge Philip we pwiin minne soamwoonin faniuwaen Iturea me Trachonitis; iwe nge Lysanias minne soamwoonin Abilene,
LUK 3:2 iwe nge Annas me Caiaphas minikka Patere taegias — noan oatonaan nge Deus a fang to kkepas reen John iwe naiun Zechariah me noan desert we.
LUK 3:3 Iwe John a noa fenai fetaen noan faniuwaen rhan pwupwu na Jordan, “Toagun saengi monofitimi nge oawpwe paptismus, ina nge Deus epwe saeneti noa monofitimi.”
LUK 3:4 Miniwe effoat noan pwapwior we aaen profeta Isaiah pwe: “Erhai aeremas e iyaekkepwas me noan desert we nge e iura pwe: ‘Oawpwe oamoannatae ennepaen Soamwoon; oawpwe awenecchera eew aan pwe epwe faaeraeg wooan!
LUK 3:5 Oanongaen mwoattotiw nepetaen rhug nge sipwe oawutaeni tae, oanongaen taeiit me rhug nge epwe soan eew noa rhag. Oanongaen aan pwoar nge epwe aewwen noa, oanongaen aan toarumwrumw nge epwe arhannenoa.
LUK 3:6 Oanongeer aeremas nge repwe weri menaw na Deus epwene fangetiw!’ ”
LUK 3:7 Aeremas towunap ra maeg wow reen John pwe epwe noa paptismus aeginiir. Nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Aaemi sowufaeng! Iyo e aengaenigaemi pwe oawpwe mmwenen kkewaeg saengi aaen Deus aegaeregaer iga epwe aefengato?
LUK 3:8 Oaw ssiuweniy wegitaegimi pwe epwe pwaeri noa pwe oawwa toagun saengi monofitimi. Oawsoapw niunniuwaennei pwe oawwa taaw saengi aaen Deus aegaeregaer reen aaemi aepesa pwe Abraham minne rhaepetomi. Ngaang ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe Deus emmwenen feeori faai kaan pwe tettaenin Abraham!
LUK 3:9 Eew soapaen a oamoannatae pwe epwe gopiy tiw waniwan saengi waeran. Oanongaen waniwan kka ese gacch uwaan nge epwe gopogop tiw nge e aekkaerh nong noan aengaet.”
LUK 3:10 Aeremas ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta minne aeipwe feeori?”
LUK 3:11 A paniuwaeniir pwe, “Iyo na riiuwapeo mengaagiun nge epwe fangenoa epeo pwe mengaagiun manna esooar mengaagiun, iwe nge iyo na eyor mwongo reen nge epwe fang ngaeniir aaemweoi.”
LUK 3:12 Aaemweoi rhooan iyoiyon tax re itto pwe repwe paptismus, iwe nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Sinsei, meeta aemaem aeipwe feeori?”
LUK 3:13 Nge iiy a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw iyoiy tax temoag saengi minna eno noan oasoapwosoapw.”
LUK 3:14 Aaemweoi sonotaw ra pwan aeiineow pwe, “Iwe nge aemaem? Meeta aemaem aeipwe feeori?” Nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw pweipwog senaapiy saengiir aeremas noan amamaaw ngaere oatupwutupw tae kkepas wooan erhai. Oawsoapw tipinap saengi minikkena paniuwaemi noan engaang.”
LUK 3:15 Aar aepiniugiuniug aeremas a tettemoag noa reen miniwe mwaenian, iwe nge a rhaepetae aar niunniuwaennei ngaere teorh maeni pwe John minne Kristus.
LUK 3:16 John a aengaeniir oanongeer noa pwe, “Ngaang iya paptismusaegaemi reen rhaan, iwe nge erhai ina epwe itto nge e taegias me mmwaei. Ngaang mwo nge ese fin ipwe pwaeisi geeogeeon nokkaan. Iiy epwe paptismusaegaemi ngaeni Espritu Santus me aengaet.
LUK 3:17 A kkemwarh aan sepwin pwe epwe aeyimweoiuw fesaenngiy faiun saengi peeon. Iwe, epwe ioni fengaenniy faiun nge a iseni nong noan aan imwaen iseis, nge peeon epwe oatoranong noan aengaet we ese mmwenen gunnoa.”
LUK 3:18 E towunap mesemesaen aaen John fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai we ngaeniir aeremas nge e aemaemaewa ngaeniir pwe repwe ssiuweniy meneweer.
LUK 3:19 Iwe nge John a soong ngaeni Governor Erotes, pwe igiwe e rhooan ngaenne aeni Herodias, iwe rhooan ngaenneyaen mwaaen we pwiin, iwe me igiwe e towunap min aenneew kkewe efeeori.
LUK 3:20 Iwe egius mwo nge Erotes a faer gin feeori aenneewa noa pwe a iseni nong John noan kanepwus.
LUK 3:21 Mwirin aar oanongeer aeremas paptismus, Jesus a pwan paptismus. Nugunupaen aan maeipin nge a susu noa naaeng,
LUK 3:22 iwe nge Espritu Santus a ittiw wooan eweei rhag erhai dove. Iwe nge eew mangiungiu a ittiw me noan naaeng nge a aepesa pwe, “Een naeyi mwaaen aerhaengerhaeng. Iye efin tipaei reen.”
LUK 3:23 Oatowe Jesus a rhaepetae aan engaang, nge a eniig raegin. Aeremas re niuwaennei pwe iiy naiun Joseph, iwe naiun Heli,
LUK 3:24 iwe naiun Matthat, iwe naiun Levi, iwe naiun Melchi, iwe naiun Jannai, iwe naiun Joseph,
LUK 3:25 Iwe naiun Mattathias, iwe naiun Amos, iwe naiun Nahum, iwe naiun Esli, iwe naiun Naggai,
LUK 3:26 iwe naiun Maath, iwe naiun Mattathias, iwe naiun Semein, iwe naiun Josech, iwe naiun Joda,
LUK 3:27 iwe naiun Joanan, iwe naiun Rhesa, iwe naiun Zerubbabel, iwe naiun Shealtiel, iwe naiun Neri,
LUK 3:28 iwe naiun Melchi, iwe naiun Addi, iwe naiun Cosam, iwe naiun Elmadam, iwe naiun Er,
LUK 3:29 iwe naiun Joshua, iwe naiun Eliezer, iwe naiun Jorim, iwe naiun Matthat, iwe naiun Levi,
LUK 3:30 iwe naiun Simeon, iwe naiun Judah, iwe naiun Joseph, iwe naiun Jonam, iwe naiun Eliakim,
LUK 3:31 iwe naiun Melea, iwe naiun Menna, iwe naiun Mattatha, iwe naiun Nathan, iwe naiun David,
LUK 3:32 iwe naiun Jesse, iwe naiun Obed, iwe naiun Boaz, iwe naiun Salmon, iwe naiun Nahshon,
LUK 3:33 iwe naiun Amminadab, iwe naiun Admin, iwe naiun Arni, iwe naiun Hezron, iwe naiun Perez, iwe naiun Judah,
LUK 3:34 iwe naiun Jacob, iwe naiun Isaac, iwe naiun Abraham, iwe naiun Terah, iwe naiun Nahor,
LUK 3:35 iwe naiun Serug, iwe naiun Reu, iwe naiun Peleg, iwe naiun Eber, iwe naiun Shelah,
LUK 3:36 iwe naiun Cainan, iwe naiun Arphaxad, iwe naiun Shem, iwe naiun Noah, iwe naiun Lamech,
LUK 3:37 iwe naiun Methuselah, iwe naiun Enoch, iwe naiun Jared, iwe naiun Mahalaleel, iwe naiun Kenan,
LUK 3:38 iwe naiun Enosh, iwe naiun Seth, iwe naiun Adam, iwe naiun Deus.
LUK 4:1 Enoa sefaaeneto Jesus me reen pwupwu we Jordan nge a sseog noa reen Espritu Santus iwe nge Espritu Santus a paeninoa noan desert,
LUK 4:2 nge Saetan a noa soatoni me ee noan faaeig raaen. Noan oanongaen raaenin kkewe nge ese mwongo, ina miniwe a meyaefi pecchai reen.
LUK 4:3 Saetan a aengaeni pwe, “Ngaere een Naiun Deus, wopwe aengaeniir faai kaan pwe repwe ssiuwen ngaeni fenoawa.”
LUK 4:4 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Saapw fenoawa rhag minne aeremas repwe menaw reen.’ ”
LUK 4:5 Iwe Saetan a pwigitae weei naaeng nge a noa pwaeri ngaeni reen rhag eew oat oanongaen mweoi me noan faeinaengiy.
LUK 4:6 Saetan a aengaeni pwe, “Ipwe ngaenneog oanongaen mamaaw kkeei me oanongaen mmwen kkeei. Oanongaen nge nemaeniaei, nge ipwe fang ngaeni iyo iye tipaei ipwe ngaenneei.
LUK 4:7 Oanongaen minikkeei nge epwe no pwe oamw igine wopwe oassotupw ngaeniaei.”
LUK 4:8 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Wopwe oassotupw ngaeni Deus na oamw Soamwoon nge iiy rhag wopwe engaang ngaeni. ’”
LUK 4:9 Iwe Saetan a pwigi noa Jerusalem nge a noa iseni tae pwiuneoi we oarosaen taegias me reen Temple we, nge a aengaeni pwe, “Ngaere een Naiun Deus nge wa oatoroagotiw me igeei.
LUK 4:10 Pwe iwe Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Deus epwe akkiuneeor naiun angkenus repwe aemmwenoag.’
LUK 4:11 Nge epwan aepesa pwe, ‘Repwe ammwarhiug tae noan paiiur pwe pirhemw mwo nge ete woas ngaeni faai.’ ”
LUK 4:12 Iwe nge Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa pwe, ‘Wosoapw soatoni Deus na oamw Soamwoon.’ ”
LUK 4:13 Weni mwirin aaen Saetan soatoni Jesus, iwe nge a nigiti noa mwo.
LUK 4:14 Iwe Jesus a sefaaen ngaeni Galilee, iwe nge miniwe maemaewaen Espritu Santus eno reen. Miniwe fioangon a rheeoi fetaen wooan oanongan noa faniuw we.
LUK 4:15 A fenai fetaen noan wutteer Jews nge oanongaen aeremas ra mwaar reen.
LUK 4:16 Jesus a noa Nazareth, igiwe effooan me ee, nge wooan Sabbath a noa noan wutteer Jews we taeppen rhag miniwe egaen feeori. A iutae pwe epwene aeraegi Pwapwior we e Santus,
LUK 4:17 nge ra ngaenneei pwapwior we aaen profeta Isaiah. A suginoa pwapwior we nge a weri pwiuneoi we effoat me ee,
LUK 4:18 “Kkemenaen Soamwoon a no wooai pwe iya ffin tae ipwe pwigito Kkepas Mwamwaai eei reer rhooa affayeo. Iya fangenoa ngaang ipwe oaronga ngaeniir rhooan kanepwus pwe iir ra saenetaeg nge i aecchipwaar rhooa parh pwe repwe ffat noa, me pwan aengesaar noa rhooa waeiraes
LUK 4:19 iwe me ipwe oaronga ngaeniir aeremas pwe a toori oatowe Soamwoon epwe aemenewaar naiun aeremas.”
LUK 4:20 Jesus a oawunnu noa pwapwior we, a ateeow sefaaeniy ngaeni aeremas we e tipaengi, iwe nge a mooat tiw. Oanongeer aeremas kkewe noan wutteer Jews we nge a meseer ngaeni rhag,
LUK 4:21 Iwe nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Soapwon kkepas e noan Pwapwior we e Santus iye igina nge a pwae noa pwe ennet, iye oawwa rongorong ngaeni.”
LUK 4:22 Ra piungiun mwaar reen nge ra maengi noannei nong mwamwaaiun ititin aan kkepas. Ra iura pwe, “Saapw iiy mwaaen we naiun Joseph?”
LUK 4:23 A aengaeniir pwe, “I giuneei firhiy pwe oawpwe aengaeni sefaaeniaei kkepas een, ‘Toagota, aecchipwa oanongoamw.’ Oawpwe akkiuneowaei pwe ipwe feeori me nee pwugusaei minikkewe oaw rongorong pwe i fasiun gaen feeori me noan Capernaum.”
LUK 4:24 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi, pwe profeta nge ese gacch aar aewenimmwaar me noan pwuguseer.
LUK 4:25 Aiussaening ngaeniaei: regin towunap rhooapwut kka ra mae rhooan ngaenneyeer me wooan Israel noan oatowe oaton Elijah, oatowe esooar worhow noan enuuw me esoapw raeg iwe a itto eew naengeta gin oarosaen temoag wooan oanongaen faniuw we.
LUK 4:26 Inamwo nge esooar erhai ne re fangenoa Elijah reen me wooan Israel, pwe aeggaen erhai rhag rhooapwut a mae rhooan ngaenneyan eno wooan Zarephath me wooan faniuw na Sidon.
LUK 4:27 Iwe nge ra gin ssow rhooa affayeo reen kaenepaai kka reno wooan Israel reen oatowe oaton Elisha; nge inamwo nge erhai mwo me neeiir nge ese cchipw, pwe aeggaen Naaman we erhai re Syria.”
LUK 4:28 Igiwe aeremas kkewe reno noan wutteer Jews we ra rongorong miniwe nge a gin teeo ngaeniir aar soong.
LUK 4:29 Ra iutae rhag, iuriutepa wow Jesus me noan aepinoamw we, nge ra pwigitae wooan wungaen rhug we eno miniwe aepinoamwoor wooan. Re menaen pwe repwe aerheei noa me wooan rhug we,
LUK 4:30 iwe nge iiy etowow rhag me nugunupaen pwuwa we nge a faaeraeg noa.
LUK 4:31 Iwe Jesus a noa wooan Capernaum, eew aepinoamwon Galilee, a noa fenai ngaeniir aeremas wooan Sabbath.
LUK 4:32 Ra mwaar reen aan fenai, pwe igiwe eyor kkemenaen aan fenai.
LUK 4:33 Noan wutteer Jews we nge eyor erhai mwaaen eyor aniu aenneew wooan; a gin aekkepwas temoag tae,
LUK 4:34 “Ah! Meeta oamw mwerhaen ngaenigemaem, Jesus re Nazareth? Wa itto igeei pwe wopwe oatoaropagemaem? Ngaang i giuneei een iyo: een mwaaenessoar we rhooan pweipwogin kkepas we aaen Deus!”
LUK 4:35 Jesus a anniugiu ngaeni aniuwe pwe, “Wopwe anniug noa nge wa siunoa me wooan mwaaen na!” Iwe nge aniu aenneew we a aerheei tiw mwaaen we weni mmweer rhooawe nge a teeowow me wooan, nge esooar minne e oawoasu ngaeni.
LUK 4:36 Aeremas ra piungiun mwaar nge ra kkepas fengaen wooar pwe, “Meeta taeppen kkepas kkeei? Eyor kkemenaen me maemaewaen aaen mwaaen een kkepas ngaeniir aniu aenneew nge ra siu!”
LUK 4:37 Iwe miniwe fioangon Jesus a rheeoi fetaen wooan faniuw we.
LUK 4:38 Jesus a siusaengi wutteer Jews we iwe a noa reen miniwe pwugusaen Simon. Niewe inaen pwiuniuwaen Simon e semwaai pwe egin pwerhikkar ginin, iwe ra kkepas ngaeni Jesus reen mmwenen.
LUK 4:39 A noa iwe a noa iu oaron niewe iwe nge a aengaeni pwerhikkar we pwe epwe siusaengi niewe. Iwe rhag nge esaer noa miniwe pwerhin niewe, iwe niewe a rhimwitae pwe a ittae feor fetaen minne epwe tipaengi ngaeniir.
LUK 4:40 Enoa mwirin tupwunoan aenet nge oanongeer rhooawe eyor rhooa semwaai reer nge ra pwigiir to reen Jesus. E iseni tae paiun wooar oanongeer nge a aecchipwaar tae.
LUK 4:41 Mwuniaan mwo nge re piungiun teeowow me wooar rhooa towunap we nge ra itiwow aekkepwas pwe, “Een mwaaen we Naiun Deus!” Jesus a kkepas sseor ngaeniir aniu aenneew kkewe pwe resoapw kkepas, pwe igiwe re giuneei pwe iiy miniwe Kristus.
LUK 4:42 Weni mmwaei raaen Jesus a nigiti aepinoamw we iwe a noa eew pwiuneoi ne iiy noa rhag. Aeremas a rhaepetae aar giutta fetaeneei, iwe nge renoa weri, nge ra aegina aar ammwarhiu tiw pwe ete rhiuwen siunoa.
LUK 4:43 Iwe nge iya aengaeniir pwe, “Ngaang ipwan noa fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai we reen Mweoiun Deus me noan aepinoamw kena aekkaew, pwe ina minne Deus efang ngaang pwe ipwe noa feeori.”
LUK 4:44 Iwe a noa fenaiuw noan oanongan noa wutteer Jews me wooan faniuw we.
LUK 5:1 Eraaen nge Jesus e iu reen meoneoiniun we Gennesaret nipwaen aar aeremas aekkaetemaegin to pwe repwe itto rongorong miniwe kkepesaen Deus.
LUK 5:2 A weri riiufoarh pwoot pwe ra iuriiur tae weni ppiy: nge rhooan fita kkewe ra nigiti pwe ra noa wupwuuw noa wuug kkewe naiiur.
LUK 5:3 Jesus a toonong noan efoarh pwoot kkewe — pwoot we waen Simon — nge a tingoareei ngaere epwe mmwenen amman saengi egius mwoarhoisaet. Jesus a mooat noan pwoot we nge a fenai ngaeniir rhooa towunap we.
LUK 5:4 Enoa moann aan mwaenieniy, nge a aengaeni Simon pwe, “Ammaan ffoarh wow igina e nennoan ee, nge een me rhooa kkomwu rhinoamw oawwa aerheei tiw wuug mwu naimi pwe oawpwe fita.”
LUK 5:5 Simon a paniuwaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, efoarh ngaeni nee pwoong we aemaem fita nge esooar iig e aei nipaeni. Iwe ngaere ina minimwu wo iura, ina nge iya iseni tiw wuug kka naimaem.”
LUK 5:6 Ra iseni tiw wuug kkewe nge ra igin niyap iig nge aetae epwene ffeir wuug kkewe.
LUK 5:7 Iwe nge ra taenepom ngaeniir rhooa kkewe rhoaniuwaar wooan pwoot we efoarh pwe repwe itto tipaengiir. Re itto iwe ra itto oawuta pwoot kkewe waar e sseogtae reen iig aetae pwoot kkewe repwene mweoius.
LUK 5:8 Oatowe Simon Peter a weri miniwe a wen, a foatotiw weni mmwaen Jesus nge a iura pwe, “Siu saengiaei Soamwoon! Ngaang erhai mwaaen monofit!”
LUK 5:9 Iiy me rhooa kkewe ra riutae reen towunepaen iig kkewe ra nipaeni.
LUK 5:10 Pwan ina rhag miniwe ewen ngaeniir James me John, mwaaen kkewe naiun Zebedee. Jesus a aengaeni Simon pwe, “Wosoapw mesag: saengi igina a noa een wopwene niyap aeremas.”
LUK 5:11 Ra iuriutae pwoot kkewe waar weni ppiy, nigititiw oanongaen aegiaeg, nge ra tapweei noa Jesus.
LUK 5:12 Eew oat nge Jesus eno noan eew aepinoamw igiwe erhai mwaaen eweri eew kaenepaai eno ee. Igiwe eweri Jesus, a foatotiw wooan ppweon nge a aeffaenipirhe ngaeni pwe, “Menap, aere wo mwerhaen, wa aecchipwanoa aaei semwaai!”
LUK 5:13 Jesus e angenoa nge a geotteopa mwaaen we, nge a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaang i mwerhaen, wone cchipw noa!” Reen rhag oatowe nge kaenepaai we a rhiuw saengi mwaaen we.
LUK 5:14 Jesus a ammwir ngaeni pwe, “Esooar ne wopwe aengaeni minneei, nge faaeraeg uwen noa reen patere pwe epwe weriug. Iwe nge a feeori oasoar we Moses e akkiuneo, pwe epwe pwaeri ngaeniir aeremas pwe wa nimegacch noa.”
LUK 5:15 Miniwe kkepesaen Jesus a rheeoi fetaen, iwe pwuwaen aeremas ra maegeto repwe itto aiussaening ngaeni nge e aecchipwa aar semwaai.
LUK 5:16 Iwe nge egaen noa pwiuneoi e esooar aeremas ee, nge a noa maeipin ee.
LUK 5:17 Eraaen nge Jesus e fenai, nge aaemweoi Pharisees me sinsein anniug remooat igiwe, nge re itto me wooan aepinoamwon Galilee me Judea me Jerusalem. Kkeman we aaen Soamwoon eno wooan Jesus pwe epwe mmwenen aecchipwaar rhooa semwaai.
LUK 5:18 Aaemweoi mwaaen re pwigito erhai mwaaen e maemerhoar wooan eew giegiy, re aegina pwe repwe pwigi nong noan iimw we nge ra oawnatiw weni mmwaen Jesus.
LUK 5:19 Pwonno reen pwuwaen aeremas we, iwe rese mmwenen repwe toori Jesus. Iwe ra teeotae wooan iimw we, ra feingi noa aekkaew oason iimw we, nge re atairaetiw mwaaen we noan giegiy we nugunupaen pwuwa we me weni mmwaen Jesus.
LUK 5:20 Igiwe Jesus a weri nepaen aar niugiuniug rhooawe, a aengaeni mwaaen we pwe, “Naeyi, monofitimw a mwusunoa.”
LUK 5:21 Sinsein anniug kkewe me Pharisees kkewe a rhaepetae aar niuwaennei fengaen wooar pwe, “Iyo mwaaen e aepesa aenneewa Deus! Deus rhag minne emmwen epwe oamwusa noa monofit!”
LUK 5:22 Jesus e giuneei niunniuwaen kkewe aar nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta oaw niuwaennei minikkena e aenneew reen?
LUK 5:23 E mererhaeg pwe sipwe aepesa pwe, ‘Monofitimw a mwusunoa,’ aere sipwe aepesa pwe, ‘Iutae wa faaeraeg noa’?
LUK 5:24 Ipwe pwaeri ngaenigaemi pwe mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas eyor maemaewan wooan soanop pwe epwe oamwusa noa monofit.” Iwe a aengaeni mwaaen maemerhoar we pwe, “Ipwe aengaeniug, iutae, pwigi giemw wa noa noan imwoamw!”
LUK 5:25 Iwe rhag mwaaen we a iutae me weni mmweer rhooawe, a pwigi miniwe gien iwe ewon wooan, a noa nee pwugusan, a noa aepingepinga Deus.
LUK 5:26 Oanongeer rhooawe ra gin riutae reen aar mesag, nge ra aepingepinga Deus nge ra iura pwe, “A inamwo aemwaeraeran minikka sa weri noan raaeneei!”
LUK 5:27 Mwirin minneei, Jesus a noa weri erhai rhooan iyoiyon tax itan Levi, emooat noan aan office. Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Itto tapweaei.”
LUK 5:28 Iwe Levi a iutae nigiti oanongaen aegiaeg nge a tapweei noa mwirin.
LUK 5:29 Oatona nge Levi a feeori eew gupwun gin temoag me reen iimw na imwan pwe aaen Jesus, iwe nge neeiir rhooan itto tapweei gupwun we nge regin ssow rhooan iyoiyon tax me pwan aaemweoi aeremas.
LUK 5:30 Aaemweoi Pharisees me sinsein anniug re appaniuwaen ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun Jesus re iura pwe, “Meeta oaw iun nge oaw mwongo ngaeniir rhooan iyoiyon tax me rhooa aenneew wegitaegiir kkomwun reen?”
LUK 5:31 Jesus a paniuwaeniir a iura pwe, “Rhooakka rese semwaai rese noa reer toagota, pwe rhooakka refaer semwaai.
LUK 5:32 Ngaang ise itto pwe ipwe faingiir rhooa mwamwaai, pwe faer rhooa monofit pwe repwe toagun saengi monofitiir.”
LUK 5:33 Aekkaaemweoi aeremas re aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun John regaen aecchigipin ffoarh noa rhag nge re maeipin ffoarh, pwan ina rhag rhooan akkiuneo kka naiiur Pharisees; nge rhooan kkayeo kkomwu noawumw re mwongo noa rhag me re iun noa rhag.”
LUK 5:34 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oaw niuwaennei pwe epwe mmwen oawsoapw oamwongoor aeremas kkewe re itto reen gupwunon appwiuniupai igiwe bridegroom we e rhiuwen no reer? Aapw!
LUK 5:35 Nge epwe itto raaenin na repwe pwigi saengiir bridegroom we, nge ina oatona repwene aecchigipin noa.”
LUK 5:36 Jesus a pwan aengaeniir fioangon awewe een: “Oawsoapw taeringa eew mengaag ffeo pwe oawpwe pinisa ngaeni eew mengaag maerhiy. Esooar ipitan oawpwe feeori. Iwe ngaere epwe ina, oawwa taeringa mwaenenei noa mengaag ffeo we pwe ikka mengaag ffeo we ese aeffitaeg ngaeni mengaag maerhiy we.
LUK 5:37 Oawsoapw pwan aenianong wine ffeo noan nenien wine maerhiy, pwonno wine ffeo we epwe taeringatiw nenien wine maerhiy we, iwe a nipi noa wine we nge nenien wine we a ffeir noa.
LUK 5:38 Wine ffeo ina oawpwan ngoannong rhag noan nenien wine ffeo!
LUK 5:39 Nge esooar erhai ne epwe iun wine maerhiy nge epwe pwan rhiuwen iun wine ffeo. Pwe e iura pwe, ‘Wine kka e ssiunaei minne enneo.’ ”
LUK 6:1 Jesus a feffaaeraeg noa neeiin maetaen wheat wooan raaenin Sabbath. Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra ginigin iuwoapwon wheat kkewe, ra mwunuti fetaeneei noan paiiur, nge re angi minikkewe faiun.
LUK 6:2 Aekkaerhai Pharisee kkewe ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta oawwa feeori miniwe oasoapwosoapw we aarh e iura pwe oawsoapw feeori wooan Sabbath reen?”
LUK 6:3 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oawse aeraegi mwo miniwe David efeeori noan oaton we iiy me rhooa kkewe naiun ra pecchai?
LUK 6:4 Iwe etonong noan imwaen Deus, nge a pwigi fenoawa kkewe re aeni oasoar ngaeni Deus, nge a angi nge a pwan ngaenneer mwaaen kkewe rhoaniuwan. Miniwe nge e aenneew ngaeni aarh oasoapwosoapw pwe aeremas repwe angi pwe aeggaen patere rhag.”
LUK 6:5 Iwe nge Jesus a soapwei noa pwe, “Minna Naiun Aeremas minne Soamwoonin Sabbath.”
LUK 6:6 Wooan eew noa raaenin Sabbath nge Jesus a noa noan wutteer Jews a noa fenai. Erhai mwaaen eno ee nge e maemerhoar pai mwaaenen.
LUK 6:7 Aaemweoi sinsein anniug me aaemweoi Pharisees re giutta aekkaew rhaepin minikka repwe oaturu Jesus wooan, iwe ina faan ra pipiiy gacchiuw Jesus aere epwe aecchipwaar aeremas wooan Sabbath.
LUK 6:8 Nge Jesus e giuneei niunniuwaen kkewe aar nge a aengaeni mwaaen we pwe, “Iutae nge wa itto iu weni mmwan.” Mwaaen we a iutae nge a itto iu igiwe.
LUK 6:9 Iwe nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ipwe aeiineogaemi: meeta aarh anniug e aengaenigirh sipwe mmwenen feeori noan raaenin Sabbath? Meeta aarh anniug e aengaenigirh sipwe mmwenen feeori noan raaenin Sabbath? Sipwe tipaengi aeremas ngaere sipwe oawoasuur? Sipwe aemenewaar, aere sipwe niir noa?”
LUK 6:10 A fan fetaen neeiir oanongeer, iwe nge a aengaeni mwaaen we pwe, “Aeitiwow poawumw.” Iwe mwaaen we a aeitiwow paiun, iwe a mamaaw sefaaen.
LUK 6:11 A gin teoteeo aar soong rhooa kkewe iwe ra pwiungiuwwoar meeta e repwene feeori ngaeni Jesus.
LUK 6:12 Oatonaan nge Jesus a ittae wooan eew taeiit epwe ittae maeipin, iwe a ittae no aegini noa epwoong reen aan ittae maeipin ngaeni Deus.
LUK 6:13 Enoa raaen tae, a faingiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe nge a finiir seig me riiurhai me neeiir, nge a aeita ngaeniir pwe oapostonus:
LUK 6:14 Simon (iwe a aeita ngaeni pwe Peter) iwe nge Andrew we pwiin; James me John, Philip me Bartholomew,
LUK 6:15 Matthew me Thomas, James we naiun Alphaeus, iwe me Simon (iwe regaen iura pwe man menat),
LUK 6:16 Judas we naiun James, iwe me Judas Iscariot, iwe e fangenoa tinnimaen Jesus.
LUK 6:17 Igiwe Jesus enoa ittiw me wooan taeiit we iiy me oapostonus kkewe, a ittiw iunoa nefenapi reen eew mweoiuyaen rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun. Eew pwuwaen aeremas temoag a no ee, nge re maegeto me Judea me Jerusalem me aepinoamw kkewe wenepeigin faniuwaen Tyre me Sidon;
LUK 6:18 re maegeto repwe itto aiussaening ngaeni me repwe itto aecchipwa aar semwaai. Oanongeer rhooakka eteeotae mwuniaan wooar nge re maegeto nge a aecchipwaar.
LUK 6:19 Oanongeer aeremas nge re aetemaegin repwe geotteopa, pwe miniwe kkemenan e itiwow me wooan nge a aecchipwaar noa oanongeer.
LUK 6:20 Jesus a toagun ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a iura pwe, “Oaw wenepwu aaemi rhooa mwaenene; pwe minna Mweoiun Deus a no pwe aaemi!
LUK 6:21 Oaw wenepwu aaemi rhooa pecchai igina; pwe aaemi oawpwene faeyemwaai! Oaw wenepwu aaemi rhooa nee tip cchoaw; pwe aaemi oawpwene kekkaei!
LUK 6:22 “Oaw wenepwu aaemi igine re aeserhoawuna gaemi, asiugaemi, aessaewa gaemi, aepesa gaemi pwe oaw aenneew, pwe faaen ngaeni mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas!
LUK 6:23 Oawkker igine a wen minna ngaenigaemi nge oaw ittae maan fetaen reen aaemi mesaeig, pwe a yor paniuwaemi ina e igin faeregit me naaeng. Pwe rhooa kkewe rhaepetoor repwan feeori taeppen minneei ngaeniir profeta kkewe.
LUK 6:24 Nge ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi aaemi rhooamwu oawwiin igina; oawwa gaen aemmererhaeg rhag igina!
LUK 6:25 Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi rhooamwu oawwa igin faeyemwaai igina; oawpwene pecchai! Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi rhooamwu oaw aemweireyiir fetaen igina; oawpwene nee tip cchoaw me saeng!
LUK 6:26 “Ifa mwo aenneewan ngaenigaemi igine oanongeer aeremas repwe aepesa gacchiumi; pwe rhooawe rhaepetoor ina rhag miniwe repwan aepesa reer profeta oatupwutupw kkewe.
LUK 6:27 “Nge ipwe aengaenigaemi aaemi rhooan aiussaening ngaeniaei: aerhaengiir rhooa oapwutaegaemi, ffeeor mwamwaai ngaeniir rhooa aeserhoawuna gaemi,
LUK 6:28 oaw aewenepwuwaar rhooan soong ngaenigaemi, nge oaw maeipinaar rhooa feoffeeor aenneew ngaenigaemi.
LUK 6:29 Ngaere erhai e pigiri epeig ne oawusupoamw, wa wegeti ngaeni peig na epeig pwe epwe pwan pigiri; ngaere erhai e pwigi noa mengaagiumw, wa pwan ngaenneei pwan epeo.
LUK 6:30 Ngaenneer iyo kena rhooan tingoareog aegiaeg, me ngaere erhai e pwigi pisaegimw nge wosoapw rhiuwen tingoar sefaaen no.
LUK 6:31 Oawpwe feeori ngaeniir aeremas taeppen meeta na aaemi oaw mwerhaen pwe repwe feeori ngaenigaemi.
LUK 6:32 “Aere oaw aerhaengiir rhag rhooa na re aerhaengigaemi, meeta faaen aaemi oawpwe pwigi eew wenepwu? Rhooa kkewe mwo rhooa monofit nge repwan aerhaengiir rhooa kkewe re aerhaengiir!
LUK 6:33 Ngaere igine oawffeeor mwamwaai ngaeniir rhag rhooakkena reffeeor mwamwaai ngaenigaemi, meeta faaen aaemi oawpwe pwigi eew wenepwu? Rhooa monofit kkewe mwo nge repwan feeori taeppen rhag!
LUK 6:34 Ngaere oawfang pisaegimi ngaeniir rhag rhooakkena oaw niunniuwaennei pwe repwe aesefaaeni niuwenin, meeta faaen aaemi oawpwe pwigi eew wenepwu? Rhooa monofit mwo nge repwan mmwoon ngaeniir rhag rhooa monofit, pwe repwe pwan pwigi rhag nepaen miniwe refang!
LUK 6:35 Aapw! Aerhaengiir rhooan oapwutaegaemi me ffeeor mwamwaai ngaeniir; oawfang ngaeniir pisaegimi nge oawsoapw niunniuwaennen repwe aesefaaenin. Ina nge minna wenepwuwaemi epwe temoag noa, nge oawpwe no pwe aaemi naiun Deus na oarosaen taegias. Pwe iiy nge e mwamwaai ngaeniir rhooa kkewe re sonap me aeremas aenneew.
LUK 6:36 Oawpwe faayeow taeppen rhag aaen Semaemi faayeow ngaenigaemi.
LUK 6:37 “Oawsoapw apwiungiu aeremas, nge ina nge Deus esoapw pwan apwiungiugaemi; oawsoapw oamonofitiir aaemweoi, nge ina nge Deus esoapw pwan oamonofitigaemi; oaw oamwusaar noa aaemweoi, nge ina nge Deus epwe pwan oamwusagaemi.
LUK 6:38 Oawpwe fang ngaeniir aaemweoi, pwe ina nge Deus epwe pwan fang ngaenigaemi. Ewaer, pwe ammwenemi ina epwene igin towunap, ina esoapw faer noan paimi iga oawpwe ammwarhiu fengaenniy. Nepaen minna oaw aeyae ngaeniir aaemweoi, nge ina nepaen minne Deus epwe pwan aeyae ngaenigaemi.”
LUK 6:39 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir eew fioangon awewe: “Erhai mwaaen parh mesan esoapw mmwenen wummwuw erhai ne epwan parh. Ngaere e wummwuw, nge repwe ppiung nong ne niipw iir me riiurhai.
LUK 6:40 Esooar erhai aeteei suguun epwe taegias saengi aan sinsei; pwe oanongeer aeteei suguun nge epwe noa moann ngaeniir aar suguun nge repwe naaen aeffitaeg ngaeniir aar sinsei.
LUK 6:41 “Meeta wa weri peipei na noan mesaen pwiimw, nge wose weri soapwon irae mwu noan mesoamw?
LUK 6:42 Epwe ifa wusun oamw aengaeni pwiimw, ‘Moawwerh pwiiy, itto ipwe tipwei wow peipei mwu noan mesoamw,’ nge wose weri soapwon irae mwu noan mesoamw een? Een erhai man oatupwutupw! Mmwaen tipwei wow soapwon irae mwu noan mesoamw, nge wopwe naaen weri gacchiuw oamw tipwei wow peipei na noan mesaen ina pwiimw.
LUK 6:43 “Efoarh waniwan mwamwaai esoapw uwa aenneew, nge efoarh waniwan aenneew esoapw uwa mwamwaai.
LUK 6:44 Oanongaen mesemesaen waniwan nge si giuneei reen minikkena uwaan; wosoapw mmwenen gin fig me reen irae towfanfan ngaere gin grape saengi fetin towfanfan.
LUK 6:45 Erhai aeremas gacch epwe oatowowuw mini gacch saengi gacchiun noan tipan, nge erhai aeremas aenneew epwe oatowowuw mini aenneew saengi aenneewaen noan tipan. Pwe iga aaw aepesa meeta kena esseog noan pwunn.
LUK 6:46 “Meeta faan oaw faingi ngaeniaei pwe, ‘Soamwoon, Soamwoon,’ nge oawse feeori minne i aengaenigaemi reen?
LUK 6:47 Erhai ne e itto reei nge e aiussaening minikka mwaeniaei nge e tapweei — ngaang ipwe pwaeri ngaenigaemi meeta na iiy eweei.
LUK 6:48 Iiy eweei erhai mwaaen e aiuwtae imwan, e genengitiw nipwan taeyifan iimw we imwan nge enoa ssaenitae me wooan porow. Iwe enoa itto pwur we itto parengi iimw we nge ese ffeir iimw we, pwe igiwe egin mamaaw kaiun.
LUK 6:49 Nge erhai ne e rongorong mwaeniaei nge ese tapweei, ina nge iiy epwe weei rhag mwaaen we e aiuwtae imwan nge ese ffeeor taeyifan; iwe enoa itto pwur we itto parengi iimw we iwe toarop noa, ifa mwo nepaen aan ffeir noa!”
LUK 7:1 Oatowe Jesus a moannon aepesa oanongaen minikkeei ngaeniir aeremas kkewe, nge a noa Capernaum.
LUK 7:2 Erhai soamwoonin sonotawaen Rome eno erhai naiun rhooan engaang ne egin aerhaengi; nge rhooan engaang we naiun a gin semwaai nge epwene oaropaen mae.
LUK 7:3 Oatowe soamwoonin sonotaw we a rongorong wunuunun Jesus, a aefengaar noa mwaaen kkewe aar re Jews repwe noa faingito Jesus pwe epwe itto aecchipwa tae rhooan engaang we naiun.
LUK 7:4 Ra noa reen Jesus nge ra noa aeffaenipirhe ngaeni, “Mwaaen een nge yor ipitan wopwe tipaengi.
LUK 7:5 Egin ffayeo ngaeniir aeremesarh nge iiy wooan oanongan a aiuwtae eew wutteer Jews pwe aarh.”
LUK 7:6 Iwe Jesus a tapweer noa rhooawe. Ese taaw saengi iimw we igiwe soamwoonin sonotaw we a aefengaar noa rhooawe maereyaeren pwe repwe noa aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, wosoapw aewwaeiraesiug. Pwe saapw ngaang erhai aeremas yor ipitan reen oamw wopwe itto toonong reei noan imwaei,
LUK 7:7 nge saapw ngaang erhai aeremas yor ipitan reen aaei ipwe itto ngaeniug. Wopwe aepesa rhag epat kkepas nge rhooan engaang e naeyi epwe mamaaw tae.
LUK 7:8 Ngaang mwo nge pwan ngaang erhai mwaaen ino faaen nemaeniaen erhai e soamwoon saengiaei, nge epwan yor sonotaw kka reno faaen nemaeniaei. Ipwe aengaeni inaan pwe, ‘Wopwe noa!’ iwe a noa; iya aengaeni inaan pwe, ‘Wopwe itto!’ iwe a itto; iwe iya aengaeni rhooan akkiuneo, ‘Feeori minneen!’ iwe a feeori.”
LUK 7:9 Jesus a mwaar oatowe e rongorong minneen; a saep sefaaen ngaeniir mwirhaen aeremas we rettapw to mwirin nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe, noan mwo Israel nge isaaen weri mwo taeppen niugiuniug een me ee!”
LUK 7:10 Iwe rhooawe maereyaeren soamwoonin sonotaw we ra sefaaen noa reen miniwe imwan nge ra noa weri pwe rhooan engaang we naiun a mamaaw noa.
LUK 7:11 Weni mwirin rhag oatowe nge Jesus a noa reen eew aepinoamw itan Nain, nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun me eew pwuwaen aeremas re tapweto mwirin.
LUK 7:12 Iwe oatowe a tooto reen wororaen aepinoamw we, nge ra pwigiwow erhai manimae. Mwaaen we emae i rhag naiun erhai rhooapwut iwe a mae pwiuniuwan, towunepaen aeremesaen aepinoamw we re tapweei niewe.
LUK 7:13 Igiwe Soamwoon Jesus a weri niewe, iwe a gin faayeow, nge a aengaeni pwe, “Wosoapw saeng.”
LUK 7:14 Iwe a faaeraeg noa a noa geotteopa kakoonaen manimae we, iwe mwaaen kkewe re pwigi ra iug noa. Jesus a iura pwe, “Anian een! Rhimwitae!”
LUK 7:15 Iwe manimae we a mooat tae iwe a ittae kkepas fetaen, iwe Jesus a fang sefaaen ngaeni niewe inan.
LUK 7:16 Iwe oanongeer noa ra igin mesag nge ra aepingepinga Deus. Iwe ra iura pwe, “Erhai profeta taegias iye a pwae me neeirh igina! Deus a itto epwe aemenewa naiun aeremas!”
LUK 7:17 Iwe miniwe kkepesaen Jesus a rheeoi fetaen noan oanongaen Judea me pwiuneoi kkewe oaron.
LUK 7:18 Iwe rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun John Baptist ra itto reen John nge ra aengaeni oanongaen minikkewe, iwe e faingiir riiurhai me neeiir
LUK 7:19 nge a aefengaar noa reen Soamwoon pwe repwe noa aeiyegiy pwe, “Een miniwe re iura pwe epwe itto, aere aeipwe wewweti erhai?”
LUK 7:20 Oatowe ra itto reen Jesus, nge ra iura pwe, “John Baptist e aefengagemaem to reemw pwe aeipwe itto aeiyegiug aere een miniwe re iura epwe itto, aere aeipwe wewweti erhai?”
LUK 7:21 Faer oatowe rhag Jesus a aecchipwaar towunepaen aeremas saengi mesemesaen aar semwaai, nge epwan oatowowuur aniu aenneew me wooar, nge e aeffetaar noa rhooa masparh.
LUK 7:22 A paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oaw sefaaen noa oawwa aengaeni John meeta kka oawwa weri me rongorong: rhooa masparh ra ffatenoa, rhooa pirhemae ra faaeraeg, rhooa kaenepaai ra gacch noa, rhooa saeningapiung ra rongorong, rhooa mae ra menawtae, nge Kkepas Mwamwaai we a fenai ngaeniir rhooa affayeo.
LUK 7:23 Ifa mwo wenepwuweer rhooa se tip mwaramwar reei!”
LUK 7:24 Weni mwirin aar rhooan pweipwogin kkepas kkewe naiun John ra noa, Jesus a kkepas ngaeniir aeremas kkewe reen wunuunun John: “Igine oawwa noa reen John noan desert we, meeta minne oaw niuwaennei pwe oawpwe noa weri? Efoarh fetin e mwoaroro reen aaeng?
LUK 7:25 Meeta minne oawnoa pwe oawpwe weri? Erhai mwaaen kka e memmengaag tae mengaag nning? Rhooa kkomwu re memmengaag tae taeppen minikkena imwu reno rhag noan imwaen king!
LUK 7:26 Aengaeniaei, meeta oawnoa pwe oawpwe weri? Erhai profeta? Ooa, ennetaen, oawwa weri erhai e taegias saengi erhai profeta.
LUK 7:27 Pwe John miniwe Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, ‘Deus a kkepas, ngaang ipwene fangetiw naeyi rhooan pweipwogin kkepas me weni mmwoamw pwe epwe noa maeneti ennepoamw.’
LUK 7:28 Ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe John ina e taegias saengiir aeremas towunap kka reno wooan soanop. Iwe nge manna oarosaen git me noan minna Mweoiun Deus ina e taegias saengi John.”
LUK 7:29 Oanongeer aeremas nge re rongorong miniwe; iir me rhooan iyoiyon tax kkewe re rongorong minikka mwaeniaen Deus nge e wenewen, iwe oanongeer noa ra noa paptismus reen John.
LUK 7:30 Iwe nge Pharisees me sinsein anniug kkewe rese tipaeni aaen Deus oatoat ngaeniir, iwe ina minne rese tipaeni no repwe paptismus reen John reen.
LUK 7:31 Jesus a pwan iura pwe, “Iwe, meeta ipwe aweweei ngaeniir aeremesaen mweoi e igina? E ifa wunuunuur?
LUK 7:32 Ra aeffitaeg ngaeniir rhag wonigaet kkewe remooat noan nenien chuwaai. Eew mwiirh nge re iyaekkepwas ngaeniir aaemweoi, ‘Aemaem aeiya pwai kker ngaenigaemi nge aaemi oawse maan! Aemaem aeiya arhiuwerhiuw, nge aaemi oawse saeng!’
LUK 7:33 John Baptist a itto, e aecchigipin nge ese pwan iun wine, nge aaemi oaw iura pwe, ‘Iiy eyor aniu aenneew wooan!’
LUK 7:34 A itto Naiun Aeremas, e mwommwongo nge e iun nge oaw iura pwe, ‘Oaw pipiiy mwaaen een! Iiy erhai mwaaen mwongonap me iun wine, nge maereyaereer rhooan iyoiyon tax me rhooa monofit!’
LUK 7:35 Iwe nge minna repiaen Deus a pwae noa pwe ennet reer aeremas kka re tapweei.”
LUK 7:36 Erhai Pharisee e tengaeg Jesus epwe noa mwongoon faaef reen, iwe Jesus a noa reen iimw we imwan a noa mooat tiw pwe repwene mwongo.
LUK 7:37 Noan aepinoamw we eno erhai rhooapwut monofit ee. Niewe e rongorong pwe Jesus e mwongo reen iimw we imwaen Pharisee we, iwe a pwigito eew neoningas,
LUK 7:38 iwe a noa iu mwirin Jesus oaron pirheen nge a saeng nge e oasopwutiw rhaniun mesan wooan pirheen Jesus. Iwe a aepaena ngaeni aennirhimwen nge a faeisongei miniwe pirheen Jesus, iwe a aepiti ngaeni neoningas.
LUK 7:39 Igiwe Pharisee we a weri miniwe nge a kkepastiw rhag wooan nge a iura pwe, “Ngaere igine ennet pwe erhai profeta, mwaaeneei nge epwe pwae ngaeni iyo rhooapwut een me meeta taeppen aeremas iye e itto geotteopa; pwe rhooapwut een iye erhai maan monofit!”
LUK 7:40 Jesus a kkepas nge a iura pwe, “Simon, eyor minne ipwe aengaeniug mwo.” Simon a iura pwe, “Ooa wo sinsei, aengaeniaei?”
LUK 7:41 Jesus a rhaepetae aan fioang, “Riiurhai mwaaen re monofit senaapiy me reen erhai rhooan fang senaapiy. Erhai e monofiti nimapwiugiuw faifayiun senaapiy silver, nge iwe erhai nimeig.
LUK 7:42 Esooar erhai rhooawe e e rhiuwen mmwenen aera minikkiwe monofitiir, iwe mwaaen we a oamoaw noa minikkewe monofitiir. Iwe ifa erhai neeiir ne epwe temoag aan aerhaengi mwaaen we?”
LUK 7:43 Simon a paniuwaeni pwe, “I maengi nge epwe mwaaen na e temoag minna e aar me reen monofitin.” Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennet reemw.”
LUK 7:44 Iwe a toagun ngaeni rhooapwut we nge a mwaenieniy ngaeni Simon, “Woweri rhooapwut een? Ngaang itto noan minne imwoamw, nge esooar rhaan e wo ngoatto pwe toatoan pirheei, nge iya faer toafi pirheei reen rhaniun mesan nge e aepaena ngaeni aennirhimwen.
LUK 7:45 Wose faeisongei aei reen oamw aewenimmwaeyaei, nge iiy iye esaaen iug noa mwo reen aan faeisongei pirheei saengi rhag oatowe i tooto.
LUK 7:46 Esooar tiikka e wofang pwe aepitaen rhimwei, nge iiy a faer aepiti ngaeni pirheei neoningas.
LUK 7:47 Iwe ina minne ipwe aengaeniug pwe, aerhaengerhaeng temoag e a pwaeri noa, ina a tiwegin pwe oanongaen minikkiwe monofitin nge a saenetaeg noa. Iwe nge iyo na e egius rhag monofit na e aessaenetaegiy nge ina e egius rhag aan aerhaengerhaeng.”
