LUK 19:5 Oatowe Jesus enoa itto pwiuneoi we, enoa fattae a weri Zacchaeus iwe a aengaeni pwe, “Mwetekkaeitiw Zacchaeus pwe ipwe no noan iimw we imwoamw raaeneei.”
LUK 19:6 Zacchaeus a teeo mwetekkaeitiw a itto aewenimmwa Jesus noan aan kker.
LUK 19:7 Oanongeer aeremas kkewe ra weri minikkewe a rhaepetae aar mwangiuniungiun pwe, “Mwaaen een epwene noa no noan imwaen erhai man monofit!”
LUK 19:8 Zacchaeus a iutae nge a aengaeni Soamwoon pwe, “Soawumwaer! Ngaang ipwene fang esoapw pisaegiy ngaeniir man affayeo, nge ngaere eyor mane i riugiuriug ngaeni nge ipwe aesefaaeni paniuwaen minikkena aan faaen faawu.”
LUK 19:9 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Menaw a toori imweei raaeneei, pwe pwan mwaaeneei nge pwan iiy teoteeon Abraham.
LUK 19:10 Manewe Naiun Aeremas e itto giut nge e itto aemenewaar rhooa mwaenirh noa.”
LUK 19:11 Nugunupaen aar aeremas aiussaening minikkeei nge Jesus a soapwei noa aan kkepas nge a fioangei ngaeniir eew fioangon awewe. Igina nge a aekkaerepa noa Jerusalem, nge rhooawe ra niuwaennei pwe miniwe Mweoiun Deus epwene oaropaen pwaeto.
LUK 19:12 A iura pwe, “Eno erhai mwaaen taegias epwene noa wooan eew faniuw taaw noa epwene noa no pwe king, nge mwirin a sefaaeneto nee pwugusan.
LUK 19:13 Weni mmwaen aan epwe noa a faingi fengaenniir rhooan akkiuneo kkewe naiun iwe seig, nge a ngaenneer eew tutuun gold nge a aengaeniir pwe, ‘Oaw giutta ngaere eyor minne oawpwe aemenewa ngaeni minneen igine ipwene noa.’
LUK 19:14 Iwe nge aeremas kkewe naiun nge re oapwuta, iwe ra fangenoa rhooan pweipwogin mwaenieer wooan faniuw we eew pwe, ‘Aemaem aeise tipaeni mwaaen een pwe epwe no pwe aemaem king.’
LUK 19:15 “Ra oatonongei mwaaen we pwe king nge a noa sefaaeneto. Iwe rhag nge a akkiuneo rhooan engaang kkewe naiun pwe repwe itto reen pwe epwe pipiiy a ifa nepaen minne ra aemenewa ngaeni senaapiy kkewe.
LUK 19:16 Iwe egommw a iura pwe, ‘Menap, a seig aan paer noa faiun gold minne iya aemenewa ngaeni iwe efai iwe wo ngaenneaei.’
LUK 19:17 Mwaaen we a iura pwe, ‘Wo igin mwamwaai. Een erhai rhooan akkiuneo we wo igin mwamwaai! Pwonno iga min paerhigerhig mwo nge wo aniugiuniug noan, een wopwene nemaeni seig aepinoamw.’
LUK 19:18 Rhooan akkiuneo we ariiurhaiun a noa itto a iura pwe, ‘Menap, a nimowu aan paer noa faiun gold minne iya aemenewa ngaeni iwe wo ngaenneaei.’
LUK 19:19 Iwe mwaaen we a iura pwe, ‘Een wopwene nemaeni nimowu aepinoamw.’
LUK 19:20 Iwe erhai a noa itto nge a iura pwe, ‘Menap, ieen faiun gold we noawumw i oapa noan eew mengaag.
LUK 19:21 I mesagiug pwe iga een erhai mwaaen sosoong. Wo pwigi minikka saapw oamw nge wo giniiy minikka saapw foatogiyoamw.’
LUK 19:22 Mwaaen we a aengaeni pwe, ‘Een erhai rhooan akkiuneo e aenneew! Minikkomwu mwaenioamw nge ipwene oamonofitiug wooan! Wo giuneei pwe ngaang erhai man sosoong, i pwigi mwo nge minikkena saapw aaei nge i giniiy uwaen irae kena ise foatogi.
LUK 19:23 Iwe meeta rhag wose ngoannong senaapiy we naeyi noan bank reen? Ina nge ipwe pwigi nge epwene yor menewan iga iya sefaaeneto.’
LUK 19:24 A aengaeniir rhooa kkewe re iu pwe, ‘Pwigi saengi mwaaen mwuun faiun gold na nge oawwa ngaenneei mwaaen we seig naiun faiun gold.’
LUK 19:25 Nge ra aengaeni pwe, ‘Menap, a fasiun seig naiun gold!’
LUK 19:26 A iura pwe, ‘Ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe, iyo a yor meeta aan nge repwe pwan fang ngaeni, nge iyo ese yor meeta aan nge repwe pwigi saengi mwo nge iwe egius iwe eyor reen.
LUK 19:27 Igina, nge rhooa kkewe rhooan kkoapwutoi ikkiwe rese tipaeni pwe ipwe no pwe aar king, oaw pwigiir to igeei, iwe oawwa itto niir tiw me weni mmwaei!’ ”
LUK 19:28 Mwirin aaen Jesus aepesa minneei, nge a gommw noa weni mmweer ra noa ngaeni Jerusalem.
LUK 19:29 Igiwe a aerepato Bethphage me Bethany me reen miniwe rhugun Olives nge a akkiuneeor noa riiurhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun
LUK 19:30 nge a aengaeniir pwe: “Oawnoa noan pwugos mwu mmwaemi; nge oatona oawpwe toonong nge oawpwe weri erhai donkey mwittig e feotaeg ina esaaen yor mwo erhai ne e waawa. Oaw pwaeisi oawwa pwigito igeei.
LUK 19:31 Ngaere igine aeremas e aeiineogaemi aere meeta oaw saeneti reen, oawwa aengaeni pwe Soamwoon e mwerhaen waawa.”
LUK 19:32 Ra noa nge oanongaen min kkewe Jesus e aengaeniir nge ewen ngaeni.
LUK 19:33 Igiwe ra pweppwaeisi ooas mwittig we nge manewe naiun a mwaenieniy ngaeniir, “Meeta oawwa pwaeisi noa reen?”
LUK 19:34 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Maasta e mwerhaen waawa”,
LUK 19:35 iwe ra pwigi noa donkey we reen Jesus. Ra iseni tae minikkewe mengaagiiur wooan, iwe ra iseni tae Jesus wooan.
LUK 19:36 Igiwe Jesus a faaeraeg nge aeremas ra mmeraeg tiw mengaagiiur wooan ennap we.
LUK 19:37 Igiwe a aerepato Jerusalem, pwiuneoi we ennap we e ittiw me reen rhugun Olives, rhooa towunap kkewe naiun rhooan kkayeo ra rhaepetae aar fang aan Deus aerhigerhig, nge re aekkepwas temoag tae reen aar aepingepinga Deus reen oanongaen manaman kkena ra weri.
LUK 19:38 Ra iura pwe, “Deus epwe aewenepwuwa king na e itto faaen itaen Soamwoon! Oapoas me wooai naaeng me nning ngaeni Deus na oarosaen taegias!”
LUK 19:39 Aaemweoi Pharisees reno noa pwuwa we ra aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Sinsei, mwaenieniy ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkomwu noawumw pwe resoapw oacchorong!”
LUK 19:40 Jesus a paniuwaeniir, “Ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe, aere igine repwe anniug, ina nge fai kaan minne repwe aekkepwas.”
LUK 19:41 Igiwe Jesus a aerepato aepinoamw we, nge oatowe eweri nge a saengiti,
LUK 19:42 nge a iura pwe, “Aetaemwo wogaen giuneei raaeneei meeta minne epwe pwigito oapoas! Nge igina een wosoapw mmwenen weri!
LUK 19:43 Eew oat epwe noa itto rhooan kkoapwutomw repwene roangeog noa, nge re aetippoag, nge ra pineyi saengiug oanongaen pwiuneoi.
LUK 19:44 Repwene oatoaropoag noa een me aeremas kkomwu noan minimwu neniemw; esooar efai faai kaan ne epwe notiw nenien, pwe iga een ese pwae ngaeniug oatowe Deus e itto pwe epwe aemenewoag!”
LUK 19:45 Jesus a noa noan Temple we nge a rhaepetae aan asiiur wow rhooan ameomeo kkewe reno noan,
LUK 19:46 a aengaeniir pwe, “E foatofoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus pwe Deus e aepesa pwe, ‘Temple e aaei nge imwaen maeipin.’ Nge aaemi oawwa ssiuweniy pwe nenien wopoor rhooa mwoarho!”
LUK 19:47 Oanongaen raaen nge Jesus e fenai noan Temple we. Soamwoonin patere me sinsein anniug me soamwooniir aeremas kkewe ra mwerhaen niiy noa,
LUK 19:48 nge ina rhag esooar eew meeta ne re giuneei pwe repwe feeori ngaeni, pwe igiwe oanongeer aeremas kkewe nge re tipaeni repwe aiussaening ngaeni minikkewe petenaen mwaenian.
LUK 20:1 Eraaen igiwe Jesus e fenai ngaeniir aeremas me noan Temple we, e fenaiuw Kkepas Mwamwaai we, nge soamwooniir patere, me sinsein anniug me fengaen me rhooa kkewe ra tugufaeyi ra noa itto
LUK 20:2 nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Meeta nemaenioamw pwe wopwe feeori minikkeei? Iyo a ngaenneog oamw nemenem?”
LUK 20:3 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ipwe aeiineogaemi eew kkepas aeiineo. Oaw aengaeniaei,
LUK 20:4 iya e itto aaen John nemenem pwe epwe paptismus fetaen: saengi Deus aere saengi aeremas?”
LUK 20:5 Ra rhaepetae aar aengimaw fengaen wooar, “Meeta sipwe iura? Aere sipwe iura pwe, ‘Saengi Deus,’ nge iiy epwe aeiineogirh pwe, ‘Nge meeta rhag oawse niugiuniug ngaeni John reen?’
LUK 20:6 Nge aere sipwe iura pwe, ‘Saengi aeremas,’ ina nge pwuwaen aeremas eei nge repwene teragirh, pwe iga re niugiuniug pwe John nge erhai profeta.”
LUK 20:7 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Aeise giuneei iga e itto me ee.”
LUK 20:8 Iwe nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ina nge ngaang isoapw pwan aengaenigaemi iya iga i pwigi me ee nemaeniaei pwe ipwe feeori minikkeei.”
LUK 20:9 Iwe Jesus a aeni eew fioang awewe ngaeniir aeremas kkewe. “Eno erhai mwaaen a foatogi eew maetaen grape, nge a ngaenneer aaemweoi rhooan maat pwe repwe aefaenniy. Iwe rhag nge a saei taaw noa.
LUK 20:10 Enoa itto oatowe repwe giniiy uwaen waniwan kkewe, a fangenoa erhai rhooan akkiuneo pwe epwe noa pwigi wiwiin me reen uwaen maat kkewe. Nge rhooan maat kkewe ra wirhiy nge ra aesefaaeni noa nge esooar meeta e pwigi.
LUK 20:11 Iwe a pwan fangenoa erhai rhooan akkiuneo; rhooan maat kkewe ra pwan noa wirhiy nge ra feeori ngaeni aekkaew wegitaeg aessaew nge re aesefaaeni noa nge esooar meeta e pwigi.
LUK 20:12 A pwan fangenoa aeiniurhaiun rhooan akkiuneo kkewe; rhooan maat kkewe ra pwan oawoasu nge re aerheiwow niugiun maat we.
LUK 20:13 Manewe aan maat we a iura pwe, ‘Meeta minne ipwene feeori? Maeni ipwene fangenoa aeterhaeng e naeyi; e tiwegin nge repwe aesirowu!’
LUK 20:14 Nge igiwe rhooan maat we ra weri, ra pwiungiuw fengaenniy wooar pwe, ‘Ieei mwaaen we naiun mwaaen we aan maat eei iwe epwe pwugusaeni minneei. Oaw itto sipwe niiy noa, pwe sipwe pwigi minne pwugusaen pwe pwugusarh!’
LUK 20:15 Iwe ra oatorawow niugiun maat we nge ra niiy noa.” Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta manewe aan maat we epwe feeori ngaeniir rhooan maenemaen kkewe?
LUK 20:16 Epwe itto a itto niir noa mwaaen kkewe, nge a ngaenneer aaemweoi maat we.” Igiwe aeremas ra rongorong minneei nge ra iura pwe, “Aapw saapw ina!”
LUK 20:17 Jesus a wegitaeg ngaeniir nge a aeiineeor pwe, “Iwe ina nge meeta awewen miniwe noan Pwapwior we e Santus? ‘Fai we rhooan kaiu iimw re aerheei noa, nge faer ina fai we egin yor ipitan me mmwaen oanongan.’
LUK 20:18 Oanongeer rhooakka repwe ppiungiutiw wooan faai een nge repwe mwetoarotoar noa; nge aere faai een epwe ppiungiutiw wooan erhai, epwe aepettatiw.”
LUK 20:19 Sinsein anniug me soamwoonin patere kkewe ra mwerhaen repwe torofi Jesus, pwe igiwe re giuneei pwe fioangoor miniwe a aengaeniir; nge igiwe re mesagiiur aeremas kkewe.
LUK 20:20 Iwe ra weti ngaeni eew oat ne repwe mmwenen torofi. Ra fang ngaeniir aaemweoi mwaaen senaapiy pwe repwe noa feeoriir noa pwe iir aaemweoi mwaaen wenewen, iwe ra fangenoa iir pwe repwe noa oatupwu Jesus pwe repwe torofi reen aan kkepas pwe epwe mmwen pwe repwe fangenoa iiy reen Governor reen Rome ina eyor maemaewan.
LUK 20:21 Iwe aeremas kkewe ra aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Sinsei, aei giuneei pwe minikkomwu wo aepesa nge e wenewen. Aei giuneei pwe een wose aefaenniy wunuunun erhai me erhai, nge wa fenaiuw wenewenen nee tipaen Deus ngaeniir aeremas.
LUK 20:22 Aengaenigemaem, e mwamwaai aarh sipwe fang tax ngaeni Soamwoonin Rome, aere aapw?”
LUK 20:23 Jesus e metefaaegini oatupwutupw we aar nge a aengaeniir pwe,
LUK 20:24 “Pwaerito efai senaapiy silver. Mesaen iyo me itaen iyo imwu eno wooan?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Soamwoonin Rome.”
LUK 20:25 Jesus a iura pwe, “Iwe ina nge oaw ngaenneei Soamwoonin Rome meeta aaen Soamwoonin Rome, nge oaw ngaenneei Deus meeta aaen Deus.”
LUK 20:26 Iwe esooar meeta ne emmwen pwe repwe torofi Jesus reen petenaen kkepas kkewe e paniuwaeni ngaeniir me weni mmweer rhooa towunap we, iwe ra anniug noa rhag pwe ra mwaar reen sefaaenin kkepas kkewe aan.
LUK 20:27 Aaemweoi Sadducees, iwe re iura pwe esooar menaw sefaaen me reen mae, ra itto aengaeni Jesus pwe,
LUK 20:28 “Sinsei, Moses minne e foatogi anniug eei pwe aemaem: ‘Aere erhai mwaaen a mae nge esooar naiun wooan rhooapwut we pwiuniuwan, ina nge mwaaen we pwiin epwe pwiuniuwaeni rhooapwut we pwe epwe yor naiun pwe epwe ffai pwe naiun mwaaen we a mae.’
LUK 20:29 Reno fiusiuman pwipwi; mwaaen we e tugufaeyi a pwiuniuwaeni nge emae noa nge esooar naiun.
LUK 20:30 Iwe ariiurhaiun a pwan pwiuniuwaeni rhooapwut we,
LUK 20:31 pwan ina rhag iwe aeiniurhaiun. Oanongeer me fiusiuman nge ina rhag miniwe ewen ngaeniir. Remae noa nge esooar naiiur.
LUK 20:32 Mwirin noan, nge rhooapwut we a maenoa.
LUK 20:33 Iwe igina, wooan raaenin na manimae repwene menaw sefaaen, iyo me neeiir epwe pwiuniuwaeni rhooapwut we? Pwe igiwe rhooawe fiusiuman nge re pwiuniuwaeni niewe.”
LUK 20:34 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Mwaaen me rhooapwuton faaen mweoiuw nge re rhooan ngaenne,
LUK 20:35 iwe nge mwaaen me rhooapwut kena ra ffin tae pwe repwe menaw sefaaen iwe nge ra no noan mweoi na epwe noa itto nge ina resoapw rhiuwen pwiuppwiuniuw.
LUK 20:36 Iir repwene weei rhag angkenus pwe resoapw mmwenen mae. Ra no pwe naiun Deus pwe ra menaw sefaaen me reen maenoa.
LUK 20:37 Moses a aeffeta noa pwe manimae nge re menaw sefaaen tae. Me reen petenaen fioangon waniwan we e ppwunuwow aengaet me reen iwe e aepesa kkepesaen Soamwoon pwe, ‘aaen Abraham Deus, aaen Isaac Deus, me aaen Jacob Deus.’
LUK 20:38 Pwe iiy minne aar Deus rhooakka re menaw nge soapw rhooakka ra mae, pwe me reen nge oanongeer aeremas nge re menaw me reen.”
LUK 20:39 Aekkaaemweoi me neeiir sinsein anniug we ra mwaenieniy tae, “Sinsei, e igin gacch aessefaaenin kkepas we oamw!”
LUK 20:40 Pwe iir ra mesag pwe repwe aeiineo mwo nge eew kkepas aeiineo.
LUK 20:41 Jesus a aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta emmwen pwe re iura pwe Kristus nge teoteeon David reen?
LUK 20:42 Pwe David wooan oanongan nge e iura me noan pwapwior we Psalms, ‘Soamwoon a aengaeniaei Soamwoon: Mooat tiw peig mwaaeneei
LUK 20:43 toori aaei ipwe iseniir tiw rhooan oapwutoag faaen pirhemw pwe repwe no pwe nenien pirhemw.’
LUK 20:44 David e faingi pwe iiy ‘Soamwoon’; iwe nge e ifa wusun nge Kristus epwe no pwe teoteeon David?”
LUK 20:45 Igiwe aeremas re aiussaening ngaeni nge Jesus a aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe,
LUK 20:46 “Oaw aefaennigaemi reen sinsein anniug kkewe, re aerhaengi aar faaeraeg fetaen faaen mengaagiiur min enaenaei, nge re aerhaengi aar aeremas repwe aewenimmwaar me aesirowuur me noan imwaen chuwaai, nge re fini rhag neniy kkena nenieer rhooa taegias me noan wutteer Jews me pwiuneoi mwamwaai me noan gupwun.
LUK 20:47 Re oapwurhaar rhooapwut kkewe ra mae pwiuniuweer, nge ra pirifa saengiir pwuguseer, nge ra oangona ngaeniir aeremas aar maeipin enaei! Iwe nge aegaeregaeriir ina epwene igin waeiraes!”
LUK 21:1 Jesus a fan fetaen nge a weriir rhooa naiwiis pwe ra iseis nong aar maenigaech noan nenien maenigaech me noan Temple we,
LUK 21:2 iwe nge a pwan weri erhai rhooapwut mwaenene a maenoa pwiuniuwan a iseis nong riiufai manfaifai pwe aan maenigaech.
LUK 21:3 Nge a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe maenigaech na rhooapwut mwaenene we efang ina e temoag saengi aar oanongeer aeremas towunap kkewe.
LUK 21:4 Pwe oanongeer nge re iseni nong nusegin wiineer; nge rhooapwut een inamwo iga e igin affayeo nge efang oanongaen minikkena eno reen.”
LUK 21:5 Aaemweoi me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe re fiffioangei Temple we reen nningen faai kkewe eno wooan me niffang kkewe aar aeremas ngaeni Deus. Nge Jesus a iura pwe,
LUK 21:6 “Oanongaen minikka oawwa weri, ina eyor eew oat ina epwe noa itto nge esooar efai faai kaan ne epwe notiw nenien; oanongan noa nge repwene toaropotiw.”
LUK 21:7 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Sinsei, ineeta epwe wen minneei? Meeta na epwe wen nge epwe pwaeri ngaenigemaem pwe minikkeei nge epwene wen?”
LUK 21:8 Jesus a iura pwe, “Oaw aefaennigaemi; oawteorh tupw. Towunepeer aeremas repwene itto faaen itaei nge repwene aepesa pwe, ‘Ngaang minne iiy! A ieei oatowe!’ Nge oawsoapw tapweer.
LUK 21:9 Oawsoapw mesag igine oawpwe rongorong kkepesaen moawun me fitigogon weni faniuw; ikkeei minikka epwe mmwaen wen, iwe nge saapw reen a arapeto ne soapwonoan.”
LUK 21:10 A pwan soapwei noa a pwan iura pwe, “Faniuw me faniuw nge repwene fiiow fengaen, eew mweoi me eew mweoi repwene moawun fengaen.
LUK 21:11 Epwene yor fanemwar tettemoag, me naengeta, me semwaai temoag me oanongaen pwiuneoi; epwene yor mini ariuriu me aemmesag ittiw me weei naaeng.
LUK 21:12 Ina rhag nge weni mmwaen minikkeei epwene wen, ina repwene torofigaemi nge ra aewwaeiraesigaemi; ra pwigigaemi noa noan wutteer Jews pwe oawpwene noa apwiung iwe nge oawnoa kanepwus; repwene pwigigaemi weni mmweer king me soamwoon pwe faaen itaei.
LUK 21:13 Nge a ieei oaton aaemi oawpwe aepesa Kkepas Mwamwaai we.
LUK 21:14 Oawpwe fasiun oamoannatae nee tipaemi pwe oawsoapw aiunaengiy aaemi noa saenetigaemi,
LUK 21:15 pwe ngaang ipwe ngaennegaemi mwaeniaemi me repiaemi nge esooar erhai rhooan kkoapwutomi epwe mmwen epwe appaniuwaeni aere paniuwaeni mwaeniaemi.
LUK 21:16 Aaemi ina inaemi me semaemi, pwiimi, perhaengiyaemi, me maereyaeremi, minne repwe fangenoa aaemi. Nge aaemweoi aaemi ina repwene nigaemi noa.
LUK 21:17 Oanongeer aeremas nge repwene oapwutaegaemi noa pwe faaen itaei.
LUK 21:18 Ina rhag ina eyaen mwo aennirhimwemi nge esoapw ppiung noa.
LUK 21:19 Oaw oarhorho, nge ina nge oawpwe menaw.
LUK 21:20 “Igine oawpwe weriir sonotaw aar pwaeniaeniy noa Jerusalem, ina nge oawwa giuneei pwe a arap oaton aan epwene ffeir noa.
LUK 21:21 Iwe rhooawe reno Judea repwe fattapwetae weei rhug; rhooawe reno nee aepinoamw repwe siusaengi, rhooawe reno neman nge resoapw ittiw no nee aepinoamw.
LUK 21:22 Pwe ikkinaan raaenin kena raaenin aegaeregaer, nge minikkeei epwe pwaeritae minikkiwe mwaeniaen Pwapwior we e Santus e aepesa.
LUK 21:23 Epwe ifa mwo aar affayeo rhooapwut pwoopwo me ikka re nayigit noan oaton naan! Temoagon aewwaeiraes epwene itto weni faniuw, nge aaen Deus aegaeregaer epwene itto wooar aeremas kaan.
LUK 21:24 Aaemweoi repwene mae wooan saeitan nge aaemweoi repwene pwigiir noa wooan aekkaaemweoi faniuw; nge re Gentiles ina repwene itto pwuraegraeg wooan Jerusalem toori aan moanno noa minna oatoor.
LUK 21:25 “Epwene yor eew aeginn epwene wen ngaeni aenet me meram me fiiu. Nge wooan soanop nge towunepaen faniuw repwene maegin no noan aewwaeiraes, repwene mesagiu piungpiungiun noa me pwuurtaen saaet.
LUK 21:26 Aeremas repwene niyoarorhrorh reen aar mesag noan aar wetiwet ngaeni meeta epwe wen ngaeni faeinaengiy, pwe minikkena maemaewaen noan naaeng repwene mwagiut saengi nenieer.
LUK 21:27 Noan oatonaan nge miniwe Naiun Aeremas epwene pwaeto me noan naengemaan reen maemaewan me nningen.
LUK 21:28 Oatona epwe wen minikkeei, nge oawwa iutae nge oawwa saeregi tae rhimwemi, pwe menewaemi ina a arapeto.”
LUK 21:29 Jesus a aengaeniir fioangon awewe een: “Oaw maengiy efoarh waniwan fig me oanongaen waniwan kkewe aaemweoi.
LUK 21:30 Nge oawpwe weri minikkena rheon pwe a pwiugiuw wow, oawwa giuneei pwe a arapeto neraeg.
LUK 21:31 Epwan ieei rhag taeppen, igine oawweri minikkeei pwe a wen, ina nge oawwa giuneei pwe arapeto minna Mweoiun Deus.
LUK 21:32 “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe oanongaen minikkeei nge epwe wen weni mmwaen iga aeremesaen igina repwe maenoa.
LUK 21:33 Naaeng me soanop repwe soapwonoa, nge aaei kkepas esoapw soapwonoa.
LUK 21:34 “Oaw aefaennigaemi pwe oawte igin gupwun me oappwunaas me aaemi aiunaengiy menaen menaw eei, nge epwe tooto raaenin naan nge epwe rhiuwen torofigaemi rhag
LUK 21:35 taeppen iga oawyo noan taefirh. Pwe minneei ina epwe wen ngaeniir oanongeer aeremesaen noan faeinaengiy.
LUK 21:36 Ina oawpwe aefaennigaemi nge oaw maeipin noa rhag pwe epwe yor maemaewaemi noan oatonaan epwe wenewen minikkeei iwe me aaemi noa iutae me weni mmwaen mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas.”
LUK 21:37 Jesus aeni raaenin kkeei reen aan fenai noan Temple we, nge enoa nee oatofaaef, nge a noa wooan rhugun Olives.
LUK 21:38 Nee oatosor moawugowug nge oanongeer aeremas ra maegeto noan Temple we pwe repwe aiussaening ngaeni aan fenai.
LUK 22:1 A arapeto oaton gupwunon fenoawa we esooar yeast reen, iwe regaen iura pwe Passover.
LUK 22:2 Soamwoonin patere me sinsein anniug kkewe re mesagiiur aeremas iwe ra kiukkiutta eew oat ne repwe niiy noa Jesus noan mwoanomwoan.
LUK 22:3 Saetan a itinong nee tipaen Judas, pwan itan Iscariot, iwe erhai me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai.
LUK 22:4 Judas a noa mwaenieniy ngaeniir soamwoonin patere kkewe me soamwooniir poosun Temple we reen wunuunun aan epwe fang ngaeniir Jesus.
LUK 22:5 A gacch nee tipeer rhooawe iwe ra iura pwe repwene fang senaapiy reen miniwe epwene feeori.
LUK 22:6 Judas a tipieew ngaeni miniwe iwe a rhaepetae aan kiukkiutta eew oaton ne egacch pwe epwe fangenoa menewaen Jesus nge aeremas resoapw giuneei.
LUK 22:7 A itto raaenin gupwunon fenoawa we esooar yeast reen, igiwe regaen ninni sheep pwe mwongoon Passover.
LUK 22:8 Jesus a fangenoa Peter me John a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawnoa oamoannatae mwongoon Passover we aarh.”
LUK 22:9 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Iya iga wo mwerhaen pwe aeipwe noa oamoannatae me ee?”
LUK 22:10 A paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oaw itinong nee aepinoamw, nge erhai mwaaen na epwe pweipwog ruumen rhaan ina epwe itto rhuungigaemi. Oawwa tapweei noa noan iimw na epwe noa toonong noan,
LUK 22:11 nge oawwa aengaeni mwaaen na imwan iimw naan pwe: ‘Sinsei e aeiineo ngaeniug pwe, Ifa sengkin na rhooan kkayeo kena naeyi me ngaang aeipwe mwongoon Passover me ee?’
LUK 22:12 Ina epwene pwaeri ngaenigaemi eew sengkin faeregit ina wooan tae, ina e fasiun moannotae noan, nge ina igina oawpwene noa oamoannatae me ee.”
LUK 22:13 Ra noa rhooawe ra noa weri pwe oanongaen minikkewe Jesus e aengaeniir nge ewen ngaeni, iwe ra noa oamoannatae mwongoon Passover me ee.
LUK 22:14 Enoa toori oatowe nge Jesus a mooat tiw reen table we reer oapostonus kkewe naiun.
LUK 22:15 A aengaeniir pwe, “A igin noa tipaei pwe sipwe aeni fengaenniy mwongoon Passover eei weni mmwaen aaei ipwe toonong noan aaei aewwaeiraes!
LUK 22:16 Pwe ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe, isoapw rhiuwen mwongonoa mwongo eei toori oatona epwe pwae noa oanongaen minna faan minna mwongoon Passover me noan minna Mweoiun Deus.”
LUK 22:17 Iwe Jesus a pwigi eew kkap, a fang aan aerhigerhig ngaeni Deus, nge a iura pwe, “Oaw pwigi minneen pwe oawpwe amakkiu fengaenniy woami.
LUK 22:18 Ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe saengi igina a noa nge isoapw iun no wine een toori tooton minna Mweoiun Deus.”
LUK 22:19 Iwe a pwigi fenoawa we a fang aan maeipinen aerhigerhig, iwe a giniiy nge a ngaenneer nge a iura pwe, “Ieen minne oanongaei, iye ipwene fangenoa pwe aegin aaemi. Oawpwe feeori minneen pwe ipwe gaen memmaeng ngaenigaemi.”
LUK 22:20 Pwan taeppen rhag miniwe efeeori igiwe a noa moanno noa mwongo we nge pwigi kkap we nge a iura pwe, “Ieen miniwe kkepaen ppwon ffeo we aaen Deus iye reen minne cchaei, iye epwene nipinoa pwe aegin aaemi.
LUK 22:21 “Iwe nge oaw pipiiy! Pwe mwaaen we epwe fangenoa tinnimaei iye eno reei oaron table eei!
LUK 22:22 Mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas ina epwene mae noa noan aaen affeeor Deus, iwe nge ifa mwo aenneewan ngaeni mwaaen na e fangenoa tinnimaen!”
LUK 22:23 Iwe rhag nge ra maegetae aeiineo fengaen wooar iyo erhai neeiir na epwe mmwenen feeori minneei.
LUK 22:24 Rhooa kkayeo kkewe ra itto aengiingi fengaen wooar iyo na oarosaen taegias.
LUK 22:25 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “King kena soamwooniir re Gentiles ina eyor maemaeweer wooar, iwe nge iir soamwoon kaan nge iir minne re iura pwe ‘iir maereyaereer aeremas.’
LUK 22:26 Nge aaemi esoapw ieei wusumi; oawpwe faer feeori pwe iyo na oarosaen taegias epwe faer weer rhag maan wonigaet, nge soamwoon repwe weer rhag rhooan akkiuneo.
LUK 22:27 Iyo na oarosaen taegias, manna emooat tiw pwe epwe mwongo aere manna e inet mwongo? Manewe emooat tiw minna e taegias. Ngaang iye ino neeimi nge ngaang minne i inet mwongo.
LUK 22:28 “Oawwa nonno reei noan oanongaen aaei waeiraes;
LUK 22:29 nge eweei rhag igiwe manewe Semaei a ngaenneaei maemaewaei pwe ipwe nemenem, nge ngaang ipwe pwan ngaennegaemi iiy maemaewaei.
LUK 22:30 Aaemi oawpwe mwongo me iun me reen table e aeinoa minna Mweoiuy, iwe nge aaemi oawpwe mooat wooan minikkena nenieer soamwoon oawpwe nemaeniir aeinang kkewe seig me ruwowu ikkiwe aaen Israel.
LUK 22:31 “Simon, Simon! Aiussaening! A fasiun saenetaeg pwe Saetan epwe soatonigaemi, pwe epwe aeyimweoiuw noa rhooa mwamwaai me rhooa aenneew, taeppen rhag iga rhooan maat regaen aeyimweoiuw noa wheat saengi peeon.
LUK 22:32 Nge ngaang i maeipinoag een Simon, pwe oamw niugiuniug esoapw ppiung noa. Nge oatonoa wopwe noa toagun ngaeniaei nge wa aemaewaar rhooa kkomwu pwiimw.”
LUK 22:33 Peter a paniuwaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, ngaang iya oamoannatae ipwe tapweog reen kanepwus me oamw mae!”
LUK 22:34 Jesus a iura pwe, “I aengaeniug Peter, pwe esoapw keokkeok maniug nee pwongiy toori oatona wopwe iura faaen enuuw pwe wose giuneaei.”
LUK 22:35 Jesus a aeiineeor rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Oatowe i aefengaegaemi noa nge esooar aaemi pwetoaw, tutu me nokka, nge eyor minne esooar reemi?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Esooar mwo.”
LUK 22:36 Jesus a iura pwe, “Nge igina, iyo eyor aan pwetoaw aere tutu nge epwe pwigi; nge iyo esooar naiun saeitan, epwe chuwaiuw noa mengaagiun pwe epwe meoni efoarh saeitan.
LUK 22:37 Pwe ipwe aengaenigaemi pwe Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, ‘Iiy ina a pwan aeffitaeg ngaeniir rhag rhooakkena re aenneew,’ ina epwe nnetaen wen ngaeniaei, pwe iga minikka kkepesaei ikka e foatofoat nge ikka a pwae noa pwe ennet.”
LUK 22:38 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra iura pwe, “Emwaeri! Soamwoon, riiufoarh saeitan ikka!” Nge iya iura pwe, “A toaw!”
LUK 22:39 Jesus a nigiti aepinoamw we nge a noa ngaeni miniwe rhugun Olives, igiwe e fasiun gaen noa e, nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra pwan tapweei noa.
LUK 22:40 Igiwe ra toori pwiuneoi we, nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw maeipin pwe oawte ppiungiunong noan sessoat.”
LUK 22:41 A nigitiir iwe a sooar mwet taaw saengiir egius, a noa foatotiw pwe a maeipin.
LUK 22:42 A iura pwe, “Semaei, aere wo mwerhaen nge wa arhiuwa saengiaei kkepaen waeiraes ee. Nge soapw minne tipaei, pwe minna tipoamw minna epwe mmwen.”
LUK 22:43 Erhai angkenus naaeng a itto reen a itto aemaemaewa tae.
LUK 22:44 Noan aan igin waeiraes egius mwo nge e aetemaegin reen aan maeipin, moaniyoanon e ssopwetiw nee ppweon nge a weei rhag sossopwun ccha.
LUK 22:45 Enoa iutae me reen maeipin, a sefaaen noa reer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun nge a noa weriir pwe ra maiur, ra gin mmaniuniu reen aar nee tip cchoaw.
LUK 22:46 A aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta oawwa maiur reen? Oaw rhimwitae oawwa maeipin pwe oawte ppiungiunong noan sessoat.”
LUK 22:47 Jesus e rhiuwen mwaenieniy nge a noa itto eew pwuwaen aeremas, Judas minne e mmweer, iwe erhai me neeiir rhooawe seig me riiurhai a war. A itto reen Jesus a itto faeisongei.
LUK 22:48 Nge Jesus a iura pwe, “Judas, faeisong mwu oamw minimwu wopwene fangenoa tinnimaen Naiun Aeremas reen?”
LUK 22:49 Oatowe rhooan kkayeo kkewe reno reen Jesus ra giuneei miniwe epwene wen, nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Soamwoon, aeipwe mmwenen nainai saeitan kka naimaem?”
LUK 22:50 Erhai me neeiir e pwigi fena rhooan akkiuneo we naiun Soamwoonin Patere iwe gopiy noa peig mwaaenen saeningan.
LUK 22:51 Iwe nge Jesus a iura pwe, “Iug noa, a gacch nepaen!” A geotteopa saeningaen mwaaen we iwe a gacch noa.
LUK 22:52 Jesus a aengaeniir rhooawe soamwoonin patere me soamwooniir poosun Temple we me mwaaen tugufaeyi kkewe re itto pwe repwe itto torofi, “Meeta oawnoa itto faaen saeitan me soapwon irae reen, pwe iga aetae ngaang erhai man mwoarho?
LUK 22:53 I nonno reemi oanongaen raaen noan Temple we, nge esooar aaemi torofiaei. Iwe nge igina minne a oatomi, pwe iga maemaewaen pwoong roorh a nemenem.”
LUK 22:54 Ra torofi Jesus ra pwigi noa noan iimw we imwaen Soamwoonin Patere; nge Peter epwan tettapweer to me itaaw.
LUK 22:55 Effooan eew aengaet noan wororaen iimw we, nge Peter a itto mooat tiw oaroor rhooawe re feroangoroangei noa aengaet we.
LUK 22:56 Igiwe erhai rhooapwut rhooan engaang a weri pwe emooat oaron aengaet we, a fan wenewen ngaeni nge a iura pwe, “Pwan mwaaen een nge rhoaniuwaen Jesus!”
LUK 22:57 Nge Peter e iura pwe, “Rhooapwut mwuun, ngaang ise giuneei mwaaen na!”
LUK 22:58 Ese mmwaei mwo nge erhai mwaaen a pwan weri Peter nge a pwan iura pwe, “Pwan een erhai rhoaniuwan!” Nge Peter a iura pwe, “Mwaaen mwuun, soapw ngaang!”
LUK 22:59 Epwe eew awa me mwirin nge erhai mwaaen a pwan kkepas ngaeni pwe, “Ennetaen pwe mwaaen een rhoaniuwaen Jesus, pwe iga iiy pwan erhai re Galilee!”
LUK 22:60 Peter a paniuwaeni pwe, “Mwaaen mwuun, ise giuneei meeta mwu wo iyaekkepesa!” Iwe rhag nge igiwe e rhiuwen mwaenieniy nge a keokkeok noa maniug we.
LUK 22:61 Soamwoon a wegitaeg a fan wenewenei Peter, iwe nge Peter a maengiy meeta we Soamwoon e aengaeni, “Weni mmwaen epwe keokkeok maniug nee pwongiy, nge een wopwe aepesa faaen enuuw pwe wose giuneaei.”
LUK 22:62 Peter a toowow a igin noa saeng.
LUK 22:63 Mwaaen kkewe re posuw Jesus ra aeni fetaeneei aegekkaei nge re wirhiy.
LUK 22:64 Ra pwaniuw noa mesan nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Aegina! Iyo we e wirhiug?”
LUK 22:65 Egin towunap kkepas aenneew kka repwan aengaeni.
LUK 22:66 Enoa itto raaenin we, nge tugufaeyi me soamwoonin patere me sinsein anniug ra mwiirh fengaen, nge ra pwigito Jesus me weni mmweer.
LUK 22:67 Ra aengaeni pwe, “Aengaenigemaem, een minne Kristus?” A paniuwaeni, “Aere i aengaenigaemi nge oawsoapw niugiuniug ngaeniaei;
LUK 22:68 iwe aere i aeiineogaemi eew kkepas aeiyeg, oawsoapw paniuwaeni.
LUK 22:69 Iwe nge saengi igina a noa, miniwe Naiun Aeremas epwene mooat peig mwaaenen Deus na oarosaen maemaew.”
LUK 22:70 Ra maegin iura pwe, “Ina nge een minne Naiun Deus?” Nge a paniuwaeniir, “Aaemi minimwu oaw iura pwe ngaang.”
LUK 22:71 Ra iura pwe, “Esooar no ne si rhiuwen weti pwe epwe itto pwaeritae aenneewan! Giirh wooan oanongarh nge sia rongorong miniwe e iura!”
LUK 23:1 Rhooa towunap we ra maegin iutae ra paeninoa Jesus weni mmwaen Pilate,
LUK 23:2 iwe a rhaepetae aar oaturu Jesus me ee: “Aemaem aeiweri mwaaen een pwe e oatupwuur aeremas, egaen iura pwe resoapw fang tax ngaeni Soamwoonin Rome, nge epwan iura pwe iiy miniwe Kristus, iwe erhai king.”
LUK 23:3 Pilate a aeiineow pwe, “Een minne aar king re Jews?” Jesus a paniuwaeni, “Een minimwu wo aepesa.”
LUK 23:4 Pilate a aengaeniir soamwoonin patere kkewe me aeremas kkewe pwe, “Esooar meeta minne i giuneei pwe teren mwaaen een.”
LUK 23:5 Nge ra egius mwo nge re aengimaaw tae, “Reen aan fenai minne a rhaepiy tae fiiow nepeteer aeremas me wooan oanongaen Judea. Erhaepetae me Galilee iwe nge igina a toorito igeei.”
LUK 23:6 Igiwe Pilate a rongorong minneei, nge a aeiyeg pwe, “re Galilee mwaaen een?”
LUK 23:7 Igiwe a pwae ngaeni pwe Jesus e itto me pwiuneoi we Erotes e nemaeni, iwe a fangenoa Jesus reen Erotes, iwe iiy epwan no Jerusalem reen oatowe.
LUK 23:8 Erotes a igin kker igiwe a weri Jesus, pwe igiwe a fasiun rongorong kkepesaen Jesus nge e tipaeni pwe epwe weri rhag me mweoiuwe. E tipaeni pwe epwe weri aaen Jesus feeori aekkaew kkeman.
LUK 23:9 Iwe Erotes a aeiyegiy Jesus aekkaew kkepas aeiyeg, nge Jesus ese paniuwaeni.
LUK 23:10 Soamwoonin patere kkewe me sinsein anniug kkewe ra toonong nge ra aetemaeginiy pwe repwe oamonofitiy Jesus.
LUK 23:11 Erotes me sonotaw kkewe naiun ra aeni aegekkaei Jesus iwe nge refeeori ngaeni aekkaew min aenneew; iwe ra iseni tae eew mengaag nning wooan iwe nge ra fang sefaaen noa reen Pilate.
LUK 23:12 Noan raaenin we rhag nge Erotes me Pilate ra maereyaer noa; nge igiwe mmwan nge re aenneew fengaen.
LUK 23:13 Pilate a faingi fengaenniir soamwoonin patere, me mwaaen kkewe me rhooa towunap we,
LUK 23:14 nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw pwigito mwaaen een reei nge oaw iura pwe e oatupwuur aeremas. Igina iya pipiiy gacchiuw me igeei nge esooar minne iweri pwe oawpwe oamonofitiy wooan.
LUK 23:15 Erotes mwo nge esooar minne e oamonofitiy ngaeni, iwe a aesefaaenito reerh. Esooar meeta ne mwaaen een efeeori nge epwe mae reen.
LUK 23:16 Iwe ipwene aengaeniir pwe repwene wirhiy nge ra saeneti noa.” [
LUK 23:17 Noan oanongaen gupwunon Passover nge Pilate egaen saeneti noa erhai rhooan kanepwus ngaeniir aeremas.]
LUK 23:18 Rhooanap we ra aekkepwas rhag pwe, “Niiy noa! Saeneti ngaenigemaem Barabbas!” (
LUK 23:19 Barabbas e kanepwus reen aan aeffiiowuur aeremas noan aepinoamw we me aan nni menaw aeremas.)
LUK 23:20 Pilate e mwerhaen epwe saeneti noa Jesus iwe a pwan tingoar sefaaen ngaeniir pwuwa we.
LUK 23:21 Nge iir ra faer aekkepwas sefaaen pwe, “Kurusuw noa! Kurusuw noa!”
LUK 23:22 Aeinuwaen aaen Pilate kkepas ngaeniir a iura pwe, “Meeta monofit na efeeori? Ngaang esooar minne iweri pwe efeeori ne sipwe niiy noa reen! Ipwene aengaeniir pwe repwe wirhiy nge ra saeneti noa.”
LUK 23:23 Nge iir egius mwo nge re aekkepwas temoag tae pwe repwe kurusuw noa Jesus, enoa oarosan noa nge ina miniwe ra feeori.
LUK 23:24 Iwe Pilate a feeori ngaeni Jesus meeta we aar aeremas tingoar.
LUK 23:25 Pilate a saeneti noa mwaaen we re tipaeni, iwe re kanepwusa pwe e aeffiiow aeremas me nni menaw aeremas, nge Jesus a iseni ngaeniir pwe repwe feeori ngaeni minna re tipaeni.
LUK 23:26 Sonotaw kkewe ra paeninoa Jesus, igiwe ra feffaaeraeg noa, ra rhuungi erhai re Cyrene itan Simon iwe e itto saengi eew soapw. Ra torofi iwe ra ngaettae kurus we wooan, nge ra feeori pwe epwe aiufera kurus we me mwirin Jesus.
LUK 23:27 Eew pwuwaen aeremas towunap ra tettapwei noa mwirin; aekkaerhai rhooapwut reno neeiir ra saengiti.
LUK 23:28 Jesus a wegitaeg ngaeniir nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Rhooapwuton Jerusalem! Oawsoapw saengitiaei, pwe oawfaer saengiti gaemi me aetekkomwu naimi.
LUK 23:29 A ikkitto raaennekena aeremas repwene iura pwe, ‘Ra wenepwu rhooapwut kkena esooar naiiur, esaaen yor mwo aar nainai, nge esaaen yor mwo aar atiut!’
LUK 23:30 Ina oatona aeremas repwene aengaeni rhug pwe, ‘Piungtiw woamaem!’ nge re aengaeni taeiit pwe, ‘Oapaegemaem!’
LUK 23:31 Pwe ngaere minikkeei a wenewen iga e rhiuwen arawaraw waniwan, nge epwe ifa wusun igine a ppwass?”
LUK 23:32 Riiurhai mwaaen, rhooan kanepwus, ra pwan paeniir wow repwe noa niir noa me reen Jesus.
LUK 23:33 Renoa itto reen pwiuneoi we regaen iura pwe “Peopeoi Rhimw”, ra itto kurusuw noa Jesus me ee, fengaen me rhooan kanepwus kkewe riiurhai, erhai me peig mwaaenin nge erhai me peig rhooapwuton.
LUK 23:34 Jesus a iura pwe, “Semaei, oamwusaar noa! Rese metaf reen minikka refeeori.” Re aekkaerh dice pwe repwe inetiy minikkewe mengaagiun wooar.
LUK 23:35 Aeremas ra iun oawruru soamwooniir Jews kkewe ra gaen aeni fetaeneei aegekkaei: “A aemenewaar aaemweoi; iwe nigiti ngaeni epwe aemenewa oanongan ngaere ennetaen pwe iiy Kristus we Deus e fini!”
LUK 23:36 Sonotaw kkewe ra pwan aeni fetaeneei aegekkaei: ra itto reen ra ngaenneei wine kkewe emwaenn,
LUK 23:37 nge ra iura pwe, “Aemenewa oanongoamw ngaere ennetaen pwe een soamwooniir Jews!”
LUK 23:38 Wooan tae rhimwen nge effoat pwe: “Ieen minne Kingaen Jews.”
LUK 23:39 Erhai me neeiir rhooan kanepwus kkewe e kurus a gaen aessaewa pwe: “Saapw een miniwe Kristus? Aemenewoag nge wa pwan aemenewaegemaem!”
LUK 23:40 Nge mwaaen we erhai a soong ngaeni a iura pwe, “Wose mesagiu Deus? Oamw mae epwan aeffitaeg ngaeni rhag aan.
LUK 23:41 Iwe nge giirh ina efin pwe sipwe kurus pwe paniuwaen aenneew kena giirh sifeeori; nge iiy esooar min aenneew ne efeeori.”
LUK 23:42 Iwe nge a aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Maengiaei, Jesus, igine wopwene noa itto noan nemenem na oamw!”
LUK 23:43 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Iya ppwoneei ngaeniug raaeneei pwe een wopwe no reei noan Paradise.”
LUK 23:44 Saengi nugunupaen oanowas nge aenet esa ttin no nge a rorhappiung noa faniuw we enoa gona enuuw konook; iwe nge mengaag we e tteoraeg noan Temple we mwo nge a taeringatiw faaen ruwowu.
LUK 23:46 Jesus a aekkepwas noa nge a iura pwe, “Semaei! Iya iseni nong minne ngeoniuy noan poawumw!” E iura rhag minneei nge a nurh noa aan ngasangas.
LUK 23:47 Soamwoonin sonotaw we eweri miniwe a wen, iwe a aepingepinga Deus, nge iwe a iura pwe, “Ennet pwe erhai aeremas mwamwaai mwaaen we!”
LUK 23:48 Igiwe aeremas kkewe re maegeto pwe rhooan oawruru miniwe a wen, igiwe ra weri, ra sefaaen noa nee iimw, nge ra tugutuguw aiungeer reen aenneewaen tipeer.
LUK 23:49 Oanongeer rhooa kkewe re giuneei Jesus, fengaen me rhooapwut kkewe re tapweeito me Galilee, renoa iun oawruruto me itaaw.
LUK 23:50 Eno erhai mwaaen itan Joseph iwe re Arimathea, eew aepinoamw me noan Judea. Iiy erhai mwaaen mwamwaai nge essoar, e wewweti rhag itton minna Mweoiun Deus. Inamwo igiwe iiy erhai rhooan Council we, nge ese tipieew ngaeni niunniuwaen we aar me miniwe ra feeori.
LUK 23:52 A noa reen Pilate nge a noa tingoar miniwe oanongaen Jesus.
LUK 23:53 A noa pwinititiw miniwe oanongaen nge a tiugiumi noa noan mengaag pwerh we, nge a oawnanong noan paeyi we iwe ekken wow neeiin faai, iwe esaaen yor mwo manimae ne etonong noan.
LUK 23:54 Wooan Aenimowu miniwe, a gin egius rhag nge epwene itto Sabbath.
LUK 23:55 Rhooapwut kkewe re tapweei mwirin Jesus me Galilee ra tapweei noa Joseph ra noa weri paeyi we me wunuunun aaen miniwe oanongaen Jesus won noan.
LUK 23:56 Ra sefaaen noa nee iimw ra noa oamoannatae aar waningas me neoningas pwe repwe noa aepiti miniwe oanongaen Jesus. Wooan Sabbath ra aseoseo, pwe ina miniwe e foatofoat noan Anniug we.
LUK 24:1 Sunday nee oatosor moawugowug nge rhooapwut kkewe ra mwet noa reen paeyi we, nge re pweipwog noa neoningas kkewe re oamoannatae.
LUK 24:2 Ra noa weri fai we pwe a mwagiut saengi aesemaen paeyi we,
LUK 24:3 iwe ra toonong noan paeyi we; nge rese rhuungi miniwe oanongaen Soamwoon Jesus.
LUK 24:4 Ra riu reen meeta we a wen, iwe rhag nge riiurhai mwaaen igin marettin mengaagiiur ra iu me oaroor.
LUK 24:5 Reen aar igin mesag, rhooapwut kkewe ra foatotiw nee ppweon, nge mwaaen kkewe ra aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta faan aaemi giutta mwaaen e menaw me neeiir rhooa mae reen?
LUK 24:6 Esa nono igeei; a menaw sefaaen tae. Oaw maengiy meeta we e aengaenigaemi igiwe eno noan Galilee:
LUK 24:7 ‘Mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas ina epwene toonong nee paiiur rhooa monofit, repwe kurusuw noa, nge mwirin enuuw raaen epwe menaw sefaaen tae.’ ”
LUK 24:8 Iwe nge ra maengiy noa meeta kkewe Jesus e aepesa,
LUK 24:9 ra sefaaen saengi paeyi we, ra noa fioangei ngaeniir rhooawe seig me erhai rhooan kkayeo me pwan oanongeer rhooawe aaemweoi.
LUK 24:10 Rhooapwut kkewe iwe Maria Magdalene, Joanna, me Maria we inaen James; iir me rhooapwut kkewe aaemweoi ra aengaeniir oapostonus kkewe minikkewe a wen.
LUK 24:11 Nge oapostonus kkewe ra maengiy pwe meeta we rhooapwut kkewe re aepesa nge min ffeeoretae rhag, iwe rese niugiuniug ngaeniir.
LUK 24:12 Nge Peter a iutae rhag nge a fattapw noa reen paeyi we; a pwoarotiw nge a weri pwe a mengaag kkewe rhag. Iwe a mwet sefaaen noa nee iimw nge a mwaar reen meeta we a wen.
LUK 24:13 Noan raaenin we rhag nge riiurhai mwaaen kkewe rhoaniuwaen Jesus ra faaeraeg ngaeni eew soapw itan Emmaus, iwe epwe fisuuw miles saengi Jerusalem,
LUK 24:14 iwe nge regaen mwaenieniy fengaen wooar reen oanongaen meeta kkewe a wen.
LUK 24:15 Igiwe re kekkepas me fioangei minikkewe, nge Jesus a noa arapeto reer iwe a itto faaeraeg eew noa meyiir;
LUK 24:16 nge ra weri nge rese giuneei pwe Jesus miniwe.
LUK 24:17 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta mwu oaw iyaepesa fengaenniy, wooan aaemi feffaaeraeg noa?” Iwe ra iunoa, ra mas affayeo noa.
LUK 24:18 Erhai me neeiir, itan Cleopas, a aeiineow pwe, “Een rhag me neeiir waseona wooan Jerusalem minne wose giuneei meeta kka a wewwen noan raaenin kkewe a noa?”
LUK 24:19 “Meeta kena?” a aeiyeg. Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Minikkewe ewen ngaeni Jesus re Nazareth we. Mwaaeneei nge erhai profeta, iwe Deus me oanongeer aeremas nge re giuneei pwe eyor maemaewan noan oanongaen meeta kka e iura me feeori.
LUK 24:20 Soamwoonin patere me mwaaen kkewe aarh ra fangenoa pwe repwe noa niiy noa, iwe me kurusuw noa.
LUK 24:21 Nge aeiya iseni aemaem aepiniugiuniug wooan pwe iiy minne epwene saeneti noa Israel me noan aenneew! Nge soapw ina rhag, pwe a enuuw raaen mwirin aan wen minikkewe.
LUK 24:22 Aaemweoi rhooapwut kkewe rhoaniuwarh minne re ariugemaem; renoa reen paeyi we nee oatosor moawugowug,
LUK 24:23 nge rese weri miniwe oanongan. Ra sefaaeneto nge ra iura pwe aaemweoi angkenus repwae ngaeniir nge ra aengaeniir pwe iiy a menaw sefaaen tae.
LUK 24:24 Aaemweoi aemaem ra noa reen paeyi we nge ra noa weri pwe oanongaen meeta kkewe rhooapwut kkewe re aepesa nge ennet, pwe rese weri minna oanongan.”
LUK 24:25 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “A ifa mwo pwurhomi, me mmwaeyin aaemi niugiuniug ngaeni oanongaen meeta profeta kkewe re iura!
LUK 24:26 Pwe esoapw faer ieei wusun aaen Kristus waeiraes reen minikkeei weni mmwaen aan noa toonong noan minna nningen?”
LUK 24:27 Iwe Jesus a aemmetefa ngaeniir meeta kkewe kkepesan me noan oanongaen Pwapwior we e Santus, rhaepetae me noan mini pwapwioron Moses me oanongaen minikkewe foatogieer profeta kkewe.
LUK 24:28 Igiwe ra arapeto reen soapw we re faaeraeg ngaeni, Jesus a feeori pwetae epwe faaeraeg saengiir;
LUK 24:29 nge iir ra ammwarhiu sefaaeniy, ra iura pwe, “Notiw remaem, epwene oaropaen pwoong nge iye a rorhappiung noa.” Iwe a toonong pwe epwene notiw reer.
LUK 24:30 Iwe a mooat tiw pwe epwene mwongo reer, a pwigi fenoawa we, nge a maeipina; a giniiy fenoawa we nge a ngaenneer.
LUK 24:31 Iwe egius mwo nge eppwun noa meseer nge ra giuneei pwe iiy, iwe rhag nge e soano saengiir.
LUK 24:32 Ra iura fengaenniy pwe, “Meeta ese weei rhag ppwunon aengaet me noan tiparh, igiwe e mwaenieniy ngaenigirh me wooan ennap reen aan aemmetefa ngaenigirh meeta we e foatofoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus?”
LUK 24:33 Ra iutae rhag ra noa Jerusalem, ra noa rhuungi rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me erhai me rhooawe aaemweoi,
LUK 24:34 ra iura pwe, “A menaw sefaaen Soamwoon! A pwae ngaeni Simon!”
LUK 24:35 Rhooawe riiurhai ra itto fioangei ngaeniir miniwe ewen me wooan ennap, me wunuunun aar giuneei pwe iiy Soamwoon igiwe a giniiy fenoawa we.
LUK 24:36 Oatowe rhooa kkewe riiurhai re rhiuwen mwaenieniy, nge Soamwoon e rhiuwen iunoa rhag me neeiir nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oapoas epwe no reemi.”
LUK 24:37 Ra igin mesag pwe ra maengiy pwe ra weri erhai aniu.
LUK 24:38 Nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Meeta oawwa aiuraeg reen? Meeta oawtip mwaramwar fetaen reen?
LUK 24:39 Oaw pipiiy paeyi me pirheei, pwe oawpwe weri pwe ngaang minneen. Oaw geotteopayaei, pwe oawpwe giuneei, pwe esooar aniu ne egaen yor fitigon me rhiun, nge oawpwe weri pwe eyor wooai.”
LUK 24:40 Igiwe e aepesa minneei nge a pwaeri ngaeniir paiun me pirheen.
LUK 24:41 Nge iir resaaen niugiuniug rhag, reen aar igin kker me tip mwaramwar; iwe a aeiineeor pwe, “Eyor minne sipwe mwongo me igeei?”
LUK 24:42 Iwe ra ngaenneei egiufet iig appwerh,
LUK 24:43 iwe e pwigi nge a aengi me weni mmweer aeremas kkewe.
LUK 24:44 Iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Ikkeei minikkewe i fasiun aengaenigaemi oatowe i rhiuwen no reemi: oanongaen minikkewe effoat pwe wunuunuy noan Oasoapwosoapw we aaen Moses, me minikkewe foatogieer profeta kkewe, iwe me noan pwapwioron Psalms nge epwe nnet.”
LUK 24:45 Nge a sugi noa aar niunniuwaen pwe repwe metefaaegini oawton Pwapwior we e Santus,
LUK 24:46 nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Ieen miniwe effoat: Kristus epwe affayeo nge a menaw sefaaen mwirin eoniuraen,
LUK 24:47 nge noan minna itan nge kkepas we kkepesaen toagun saengi monofit iwe me sessaenin monofit epwe fenaiuw ngaeniir oanongaen faniuw, epwe rhaepetae me Jerusalem.
LUK 24:48 Aaemi rhooan pwaeritae oanongaen minikkeei.
LUK 24:49 Iwe nge ngaang ipwene aefengatiw woami meeta we mwaaen we Semaei e ppwoneei. Nge aaemi oawpwe no rhag nee aepinoamw toori aan ittiw woami maemaew na wooai naaeng.”
LUK 24:50 A pwigiir wow me noan aepinoamw we toori noa Bethany, igiwe a aeititae paiun nge a aepiniir noa.
LUK 24:51 Nugunupaen aan aepiniir nge a nigitiir pwe a noa weei naaeng.
LUK 24:52 Iir ra oassoara iiy nge ra sefaaen noa Jerusalem, reen aar igin kker,
LUK 24:53 nge ra no rhag noan Temple we reen aar fang ngaeni Deus aan aerhigerhig.
JOH 1:1 Noan oatowe pweoneotaen faeinaengiy nge Kkepas we a fasiun no; Kkepas we eno reen Deus, nge Kkepas we ina iiy Deus.
JOH 1:2 Saengi rhag ne pweoneotaen nge Kkepas we a no reen Deus.
JOH 1:3 Oanongaen meeta Deus a feeori nge e itto me reen; esooar eew aegiaeg ne ese ffeeor me reen.
JOH 1:4 Iiy Kkepas eei minne efang menaw, nge iiy menaw eei minne e aesseremaar aeremas.
JOH 1:5 Iiy seram we e aesserema roorh, nge roorh ese oarorha seram.
JOH 1:6 Deus a fang naiun rhooan pweipwogin kkepas, erhai mwaaen itan John,
JOH 1:7 iwe a itto pwe epwe aengaeniir aeremas wunuunun seram we, pwe oanongeer rhooakka repwe rongorong kkepas we nge repwe niugiuniug.
JOH 1:8 Iiy wooan oanongan saapw iiy seram we; iiy e itto pwe epwe itto aepesa kkepesaen seram we.
JOH 1:9 Ieei minne oanongonniuwan seram, seram we epwe itto noan faeinaengiy pwe epwe ttin tiw wooar oanongeer aeremas.
JOH 1:10 Kkepas we a no wooan faeinaengiy, iwe inamwo iga Deus efeeori faeinaengiy me reen, nge faeinaengiy ese giuneei.
JOH 1:11 Iiy e itto wooan sipegin faniuwan, nge sipegin aeremesaen faniuwan rese aetiwa.
JOH 1:12 Aekkaaemweoi re aetiwa nge re niugiuniug ngaeni; iwe ikkeei a aeitaar pwe iir naiun Deus.
JOH 1:13 Rese no pwe naiun Deus reen aar wupwutiw, nge saapw tipaen aeremas ngaere tipaen erhai mwaaen, pwe faer saengi tipaen Deus.
JOH 1:14 Iiy Kkepas we a itto no noa pwe aeremas, iwe a itto nonno neeirh, nge a sseog noa reen ffayeo me min nnet. Sa weri nningan, nning we mwaaen we Seman e ngaenneei pwe iga iiy rhag Naiun.
JOH 1:15 Iiy John e aepesa wunuunun. Aan aekkepwas aegini pwe, “Ieen iiy mwaaen we i aekkaepesa pwe, ‘Iiy epwe itto mwiriy, nge iiy e taegias me mmwaei, pwe iya fasiun no me weni mmwaen aaei supw.’ ”
JOH 1:16 Me reen temoagon ffayeo na aan a aewenepwuwagirh faaen fiteig oanongarh, a aewenepwuwagirh noa rhag.
JOH 1:17 Deus a fang oasoapwosoapw kkewe ngaeni Moses, nge faayeow me nnet e itto me reen Jesus Kristus.
JOH 1:18 Esaaen yor mwo faaen eew ne erhai a weri Deus. Pwe mwaaen na rhag Naiun, ina iiy rhag Deus, nge eno rhag wenepeigin minna Seman, nge iiy minne a giuneei noa wunuunun.
JOH 1:19 Soamwoonin Jews me noan Jerusalem ra aefengaar noa aaemweoi patere me Levites repwe noa aeiineow John pwe, “Een iyo?”
JOH 1:20 John ese oapa iiy iyo pwe a faer aeffeta noa nge a iura pwe, “Saapw ngaang Kristus.”
JOH 1:21 Iwe ra aeiineow pwe, “Iwe nge een iyo? Een Elijah?” John a iura pwe, “Aapw, saapw ngaang.” Nge ra pwan aeiineow pwe, “Een Profeta we?” Nge iiy a pwan paniuwaeniir pwe, “Aapw.”
JOH 1:22 Nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Iwe aengaenigemaem ngaere een iyo. Pwe aeipwe noa aengaeniir mwaaen kkewe refangeto aemaem. Meeta wopwe iura reen mmwenemw?”
JOH 1:23 Aessefaaenin kkepas we aaen John a aepesa miniwe mwaeniaen profeta we Isaiah: “Ngaang ‘aeremas we i iyaekkepwas me noan desert pwe: Aewenewena ennap na ennepaei Soamwoon!’ ”
JOH 1:24 Rhooan pweipwogin kkepas kkewe Pharisees re aefengaar,
JOH 1:25 ra aeiineow John pwe, “Ngaere saapw een Kristus, ngaere Elijah, ngaere Profeta we, iwe meeta faan wonoa paptismus aeremas reen?”
JOH 1:26 John a paniuwaeniir, “Ngaang i paptismus reen rhan, nge e iu erhai me neeimi nge oawse giuneei.
JOH 1:27 Ina aeremas na epwe itto me mwiriy, nge ngaang ese fin ipwe pwaeisi geeogeeon nokkaan.”
JOH 1:28 Oanongaen minikkeei nge ewen me Bethany ina eno peig na eotiw me reen pwupwu we Jordan, peig we John e paptismus fetaen ee.
JOH 1:29 Sorotaen raaenin we eraaen nge John a weri Jesus pwe a ikkitto, nge a iura pwe, “Inaan iiy Sheep we Naiun Deus, iwe e arhiuwa noa monofitin faeinaengiy!
JOH 1:30 Een iiy mwaaen we igaen aepesa mmwenen iwe i iura pwe, ‘Erhai mwaaen ina epwe itto mwiriy, nge iiy e taegias me mmwaei, pwe iya fasiun no me weni mmwaen aaei supw.’
JOH 1:31 Ngaang ise giuneei aere epwe iiy iyo, nge ngaang iya itto nge iya itto paptismus reen rhaan pwe epwe pwae ngaeniir re Israel ngaere iiy iyo.”
JOH 1:32 Iwe John a pwaeritae pwe, “Ngaang iweri Espritu Santus e ittiw me noan naaeng nge eweei erhai dove iwe a ittiw no noa wooan.
JOH 1:33 Ngaang ise giuneei aere epwe iiy iyo, nge Deus, iwe efangeto ngaang pwe ipwe ittiw paptismus reen rhaan, nge a aengaeniaei pwe, ‘Wopwe weri Espritu Santus aan ittiw no wooan erhai mwaaen; iiy mwaaen we epwe paptismus reen Espritu Santus.’ ”
JOH 1:34 John a iura pwe, “Iya weri, iya aengaenigaemi pwe iiy minne Naiun Deus.”
JOH 1:35 Mmasetae nge John me riiurhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra pwan itto iu igiwe,
JOH 1:36 nge a weri aaen Jesus faaeraeg noa. A iura pwe, “Een iiy Sheep we Naiun Deus.”
JOH 1:37 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe riiurhai re rongorong miniwe e aepesa nge ra ttapw noa mwirin Jesus.
JOH 1:38 Jesus enoa toagun, a weri aar tapweto me mwirin, iwe a aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta oaw kiukkiutta?” Ra paniuwaeni, “Wo nonno iya Rabbi?” (Wewen nge “Sinsei”.)
JOH 1:39 Nge iya iura pwe, “Oaw itto oawpwe noa weri.” (Epwene aerepaen faawu konook nee oatofaaef.) Ra tapweei noa ra noa weri igiwe eno nonno ee, iwe ra nonoa reen noan raaenin we.
JOH 1:40 Erhai mwaaen kkewe nge itan Andrew, iwe pwiin Simon Peter.
JOH 1:41 Enoa rhag noa giutta mwaaen pwiin Simon, nge a aengaeni pwe, “Aeiya rhuungi Messiah.” (Wewen nge “Kristus”).
JOH 1:42 Iwe ra pwigi noa Simon reen Jesus. Jesus a fan ngaeni nge a iura pwe, “Een Simon we naiun John, wopwene itaeni Cephas.” (Iteei nge e aeffitaeg ngaeni rhag Peter, wewen nge “faai.”)
JOH 1:43 Mmasetae nge Jesus a maengiy epwene noa Galilee. Enoa nge a rhuungi Philip nge a aengaeni pwe, “Itto tapweaei!” (
JOH 1:44 Philip nge re Bethsaida, aepinoamw we Andrew me Peter re nonno ee.)
JOH 1:45 Philip a noa weri Nathanael nge a aengaeni pwe, “Aeiya weri mwaaen we Moses e foatogi wunuunun noa pwapwioron anniug we nge iwe profeta kkewe repwan foatogi wunuunun. Iiy Jesus we naiun Joseph, iwe saengi Nazareth.”
JOH 1:46 Nathanael a aeiineo pwe, “Yor min mwamwaai ne epwe itto me Nazareth?” Philip a iura pwe, “Itto pwe wopwe noa weri!”
JOH 1:47 Igiwe Jesus a weri aaen Nathanael aan ikkito a fioangei wunuunun pwe, “Ieen iiy erhai oanongonniuwaen re Israel; esooar eew min oatupwutupw ne eno wooan!”
JOH 1:48 Nathanael a aeiineow pwe, “E ifa wusun nge wa giuneaei?” Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaang i weriug pwe womooat faaen waniwan we fig, weni mmwaen aaen Philip faingiug.”
JOH 1:49 Nathanael a iura pwe, “Sinsei, een minne Naiun Deus! Een minne Kingaen Israel!”
JOH 1:50 Jesus a iura pwe, “Oamw rhag niugiuniug iga i aengaeniug pwe i weriug igiwe wono faaen fig we? Eyor aaemweoi minikka wopwe naaen itto weri ikka e taegias saengi minneei!”
JOH 1:51 Nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: oawpwe weri aan susu noa naaeng nge oawwa weriir angkenus kkewe Naiun Deus aar ittae me ittiw wooan mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas.”
JOH 2:1 Riiuraaen me mwirin nge a yor eew appwiuniupai me noan aepinoamwon Cana me noan Galilee. Rhooapwut we inaen Jesus eno ee,
JOH 2:2 nge Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun repwan feffai repwe noa reen apwiuppwiuniuw we.
JOH 2:3 Igiwe a ros noa wine, rhooapwut we inaen Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “A ros noa aar wine.”
JOH 2:4 Jesus a iura pwe, “Een wosoapw aengaeniaei meeta ipwe feeori, pwe minna oatoi ina esaaen itto.”
JOH 2:5 Rhooapwut we inaen Jesus a aengaeniir rhooan akkiuneo kkewe pwe, “Oawfeeori ese tiwegin minikkena e aengaenigaemi.”
JOH 2:6 Jews eyor aar oasoapwosoapwon aenimenim, ina faaen miniwe eno wonowu ruumen rhaan, nge eew ruume kkewe nge epwe pwigi oawton riiuweig ngaeni eniig neosaening.
JOH 2:7 Jesus a aengaeniir rhooan akkiuneo kkewe pwe, “Oaw oawuta ruume kaan reen rhaan.” Nge ra oawuta minikkewe asseogiu noa,
JOH 2:8 nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Iwe igina oaw itifi aekkaew reen rhaan oawwa pwigi noa reen manna e soamwooniy gupwun eei.” Iwe ra pwigi noa reen rhaan kkewe,
JOH 2:9 nge igina nge rhaan kkewe a ffeeor noa pwe wine, nge mwaaen we a nnaeri. Ese giuneei igine wine kkewe e itto me ee (nge rhooan akkiuneo kkewe re ifi rhaan kkewe re giuneei); iwe a faingi bridegroom we
JOH 2:10 a aengaeni pwe, “Oanongeer aeremas regaen gommwaen iseis wow wine nneo, nge aeremas re pwunaas noa nge renaaen iseis wow wine kka ese nneo. Nge wa gaen noa iseni wine na oarosaen mwamwaai pwe epwe noa no pwe oarosan!”
JOH 2:11 Jesus a feeori aeyewaen kkeman me noan Cana me noan Galilee; a pwaeri noa minna nningen, nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra niugiuniug ngaeni.
JOH 2:12 Mwirin minneei nge Jesus me rhooapwut we inan me pwiin me rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra noa Capernaum ra noa no e noan fitiraen.
JOH 2:13 Akkarap oaton gupwunon Passover, we re Jews regaen oagupwuna, iwe Jesus a noa Jerusalem.
JOH 2:14 Noan Temple we a noa rhuungiir aeremas pwe re chuwaai fetaen wakke, sheep, pigeons, iwe me rhooan ssiuwen senaapiy repwan mooat reen aar table.
JOH 2:15 A feeori eew soapwoi saaen pwe naiun wuwoaw, iwe a aenewaar wow maan me noan Temple we, sheep me wakke; a aerheppa table kkewe aar rhooan aetittinen senaapiy me aeperessa noa naiiur manfaifai;
JOH 2:16 iwe a aengaeniir rhooan chuwaiun pigeons kkewe, “Oaw pwigin wow me igeei! Enemmwaen mwo aaemi pwigi minne imwaen mane Semaei pwe nenien aaemi imwaen chuwaai!”
JOH 2:17 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun a maeng ngaeniir meeta we effoat noan Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, “Deus, rhaengin minna imwoamw ina eweei pwerhin aengaet me nee rhiuy.”
JOH 2:18 Soamwooniir Jews ra itto aeiineow pwe, “Meeta eew kkeman wopwe feeori nge epwe pwaeri ngaenigemaem pwe eyor maemaewoamw pwe wopwe feeori minikkeei?”
JOH 2:19 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw oatoaropaetiw Temple eei, nge noan eoniuraen ipwe feeori sefaaeniy.”
JOH 2:20 Nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Wopwe feeori sefaaeniy noan eoniuraen? Temple eei effeeor noan faaeig me wonowu raeg!”
JOH 2:21 Nge Temple we Jesus e fioangei nge iwe ina miniwe oanongan.
JOH 2:22 Iwe igiwe enoa menaw sefaaen tae, rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra maengiy noa pwe e iura minneei, iwe ra niugiuniug ngaeni Pwapwior we e Santus me miniwe mwaeniaen Jesus.
JOH 2:23 Igiwe Jesus eno Jerusalem reen gupwunon Passover, ra towunap rhooa e ra niugiuniug igiwe ra weri kkeman kkewe efeeori.
JOH 2:24 Iwe nge Jesus ese niugiuniug ngaeniir, pwe iiy e giuneei nee tipeer oanongeer noa.
JOH 2:25 Esooar ipitaen pwe repwe aengaeni wunuunuur aeremas, pwe iiy e giuneei meeta kkewe eno nee tipeer.
JOH 3:1 Eno erhai soamwooniir re Jews mwaaen itan Nicodemus, iiy erhai Pharisee.
JOH 3:2 Eew pwongin a noa reen Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Rabbi, aei giuneei pwe een erhai sinsei aefengayaen Deus. Esooar erhai ne epwe mmwenen ffeeor kkeman kkomwu wogaen feeori, ngaere Deus ese no reen.”
JOH 3:3 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: esooar erhai ne epwe weri minna Mweoiun Deus igine ese supw sefaaen.”
JOH 3:4 Nicodemus a aeiineo pwe, “Epwe ifa wusun aaen erhai mwaaen tugufaeyi epwe supw sefaaen? Iiy esoapw mmwenen sefaaen nong noan upwaen miniwe inan pwe epwe oaruwowwan aan supw sefaaen!”
JOH 3:5 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: esooar erhai ne epwe toonong noan minna Mweoiun Deus aere ese supw me reen rhaan me Espritu Santus.
JOH 3:6 Erhai ne esupw saengi aeremas nge naiun aeremas, nge ne esupw saengi Espritu Santus nge ina iiy naiun.
JOH 3:7 Oawsoapw riu reen iga i aengaenigaemi pwe oawpwe supw sefaaen.
JOH 3:8 Aaeng ina ese tiwegin igine e aengiaeng noa ee; oaw rongorong ngiungiun, nge oawse giuneei iga e itto me ee aere iya iga epwe noa ee. E ina wusuur reer rhooakka resupw to me reen Espritu Santus.”
JOH 3:9 Nicodemus a aeiineo pwe, “Epwe ifa wusun aan mmwen minneei?”
JOH 3:10 Jesus a paniuwaeni, “Een erhai sinsei taegias me wooan Israel nge wose giuneei minneei?
JOH 3:11 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaeniug minna wenewenen: aei aepesa minikka aei giuneei nge aei pwaeritae minikkena aeiweri, nge aaemi oawse rongorong aemaem kkepas.
JOH 3:12 Oawse niugiuniug ngaeniaei iga i aengaenigaemi minikka mmwenei noan faeinaengiy; nge epwe ifa wusun aaemi niugiuniug ngaeniaei iga ipwe aengaenigaemi minikkena mmwenei noan naaeng?
JOH 3:13 Esaaen yor mwo erhai ne enoa naaeng, pwe aeggaen minna rhag Naiun Aeremas, iwe e ittiw me naaeng.”
JOH 3:14 Wunuunun aaen Moses saeregi tae sowufaeng goanoorh we wooan eew irae me noan desert we, epwe pwan ina rhag wusun aaen aetaegiasa tae mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas,
JOH 3:15 pwe ina nge oanongeer aeremas kka re niugiuniug ngaeni nge repwe toori menaw na esooar iaenin.
JOH 3:16 Reen aaen Deus igin aerhaengi faeinaengiy, a fangetiw mwaaen erhai we Naiun, pwe oanongeer aeremas kka re niugiuniug ngaeni nge resoapw maenoa nge repwe toori menaw na esooar iaenin.
JOH 3:17 Deus ese fangetiw mwaaen we Naiun noan faeinaengiy pwe epwe ittiw apwiungiu, pwe epwe faer ittiw aemenewa.
JOH 3:18 Iyo kka re niugiuniug ngaeni mwaaen we Naiun Deus nge resoapw apwiung; nge iyo kena rese niugiuniug ngaeni nge ra fasiun no noan apwiung, pwe iga rese niugiuniug ngaeni mwaaen erhai we Naiun Deus.
JOH 3:19 Epwe ieei wunuunun apwiung: seram a itto noan faeinaengiy nge aeremas re aerhaengi roorh me mmwaen seram, pwe iga aar feoffeeor nge e aenneew.
JOH 3:20 Iyo kka re feoffeeor aenneew nge ikkina re oapwuta seram, resoapw itto noan seram, pwonno feoffeeor aenneew kkena refeeori ete pwaetae.
JOH 3:21 Nge iyo kkena refeeori minikkena e wenewen nge repwe itto noan seram, pwonno seram epwe pwaeritae pwe minikkena refeeori nge e tapweei minikkena tipaen Deus.
JOH 3:22 Mwirin minneei nge Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra noa Judea, a noa notiw reer pwe a noa paptismus fetaen aeremas.
JOH 3:23 Iwe nge John Baptist eno pwe epwan paptismus fetaen noan Aenon, ese taaw saengi Salim, pwe iga e igin ssow rhaan me ee. Aeremas ra noa reen pwe a paptismus aeginiir. (
JOH 3:24 Minneei nge weni mmwaen igiwe John enoa kanepwus.)
JOH 3:25 Aaemweoi rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun John ra aengimaw ngaeni erhai re Jew reen wunuunun aar iir re Jews oasoapwosoapwon aenimenima oanongeer.
JOH 3:26 Ra noa reen John nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Sinsei, wo maengiy rhag mwaaen we eno reemw me peig na epeig me reen pwupwu we Jordan, iwe wo fioangei kkepesan? Igina nge a paptismus fetaen nge oanongeer aeremas nge ra maeg noa reen!”
JOH 3:27 John a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Esooar erhai ne epwe yor eew meeta reen pwe aeggaen igine rhag Deus epwe fang ngaeni.
JOH 3:28 Aaemi minikkomwu naeyi rhooan pwaeritae, reen iga ngaang iura pwe, ‘Saapw ngaang Kristus, pwe ngaang minne Deus egommwaen aefengaeyaei to me mmwan.’
JOH 3:29 Bridegroom ina rhooan ngaenne aaen bride na; nge niewe maereyaeren mwaaen we e appwiuniupai, e iu oaron nge a kker igiwe a rongorong mwaeniaen mwaaen we. E ieen wunuunun oanongonniuwaen aaei kker.
JOH 3:30 Iiy epwe taegias noa nge ngaang ipwe sessoanotiw.”
JOH 3:31 Mwaaen we e ittiw me weei naaeng minne oarosaei taegias saengiir oanongeer aeremas. Iyo na e itto me wooai soanop nge iiy naiuy soanop ina epwe aepesa mmwenen soanop, nge iyo we e ittiw me naaeng nge iiy minne oarosaen taegias saengiir oanongeer aeremas.
JOH 3:32 E aepesa minne eweri me e rongorong, nge esooar ne e aiussaening ngaeni.
JOH 3:33 Nge iyo e aetiwa kkepas e aan, iwe nge iiy e pwaeritae pwe Deus nge ennet.
JOH 3:34 Iyo we Deus a fang nge e aepesa oanoon Deus, pwe Deus a oawunusa ngaeni oanongonniuwaen minna Ngeoniun.
JOH 3:35 Deus we Seman e igin aerhaengi mwaaen na Naiun iwe a fang ngaeni oanongaen minna mamaawan.
JOH 3:36 Iyo na e niugiuniug ngaeni mwaaen we Naiun nge epwe toori menaw na esooar ssiaaenin; nge iyo ese niugiuniug ngaeni mwaaen we Naiun nge esoapw yo ngaeni menaw na esooar ssiaaenin, nge epwe no rhag noan aaen Deus aegaeregaer.
JOH 4:1 Pharisees kkewe ra rongorong pwe ra towunap rhooan kkayeo kka Jesus a paptismusaar me mmwaen John nge a pwigiir pwe naiun rhooan kkayeo. (
JOH 4:2 Nge minna wenewenen, nge saapw Jesus pwe faer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun minne re paptismusaar.)
JOH 4:3 Iwe nge igiwe Jesus a rongorong meeta we re aepesa, a siusaengi Judea a sefaaen ngaeni Galilee;
JOH 4:4 nge noan faaeraeg noa we aan nge epwan toonong noan Samaria.
JOH 4:5 Noan Samaria a noa reen eew aepinoamw itan Sychar, igaan nge ese taaw saengi maat we Jacob e ngaenneei Joseph iwe naiun.
JOH 4:6 Rhanniunim we aaen Jacob eno ee, iwe Jesus a itto mooat tiw epwe a mmaniuniu reen aan aeggaesaeisaei. A aerepa nugunupaen oanowas.
JOH 4:7 Erhai rhooapwuton Samaria a itto pwe epwe itto ifiif rhan, nge Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Ngoatto egius rhan pwe iuniumaei.” (
JOH 4:8 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun re soano pwe renoa nee aepinoamw pwe renoa chuwaai mwongo.)
JOH 4:9 Rhooapwut we a aengaeni pwe, “Een erhai Jew, nge ngaang erhai re Samaria — e ifa wusun nge wa tingoareaei iuniumoamw rhaan?” (Re Jews resoapw iun nong noan aar kkap me mwongo nong noan aar saepiy re Samaria.)
JOH 4:10 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Aere wo giuneei meeta e Deus efang me iyo e etingoareog iuniuman rhaan, nge wo tingoar ngaeni nge iiy epwe ngaenneog minna rhaniun menaw.”
JOH 4:11 Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Menap, esooar oamw pwaecchi nge rhanniunim een iye e igin nennoan. Iya iga wopwe pwigi rhaniun menaw me ee?
JOH 4:12 Jacob we rhaepetomaem minne efang ngaenigemaem rhanniunim ee; iiy me aetekkewe naiun me naiun maan nge oanongeer nge re iun saengi rhan eei. Meeta, een wo iura pwe wo taegias saengi Jacob?”
JOH 4:13 Jesus a paniuwaeni, “Rhooakka re iun me reen rhan eei nge repwe moar sefaaen,
JOH 4:14 nge rhooa kena re iun me reen rhan na ngaang ipwe ngaenneer nge esooar faaen eew ne repwe moar. Rhan na ipwe ngaenneer ina epwene no pwe rhaepeton eew rhan ina epwene ngaenneer rhaniun menaw na esooar ssiaaenin.”
JOH 4:15 Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Menap, ngaenneei aei rhan na! Ina nge isoapw rhiuwen moar no nge isoapw rhiuwen itto no igeei pwe ipwe itto ifiif rhan.”
JOH 4:16 Jesus a aengaeni, “Wonoa faingi mwaaen we rhooan ngaenne oamw nge wa sefaaeneto.”
JOH 4:17 Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Esooar rhooan ngaenneaei.” Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennet minimwu wo iura pwe esooar rhooan ngaenne oamw.
JOH 4:18 Een wa moannon appwiuniupai ngaeniir nimman mwaaen, iwe nge mwaaen na wono reen igina ina soapw oanongonniuwan rhooan ngaenne oamw. Wo aengaeniaei minna wenewenen kkepas.”
JOH 4:19 Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Iya weri pwe een erhai profeta, menap.
JOH 4:20 Re Samaria kkewe rhaepetoi re itto maeipin ngaeni Deus me wooan rhug eei, nge aaemi Jews oaw iura pwe Jerusalem minne sipwe maegin maeipin ngaeni Deus me ee.”
JOH 4:21 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Rhooapwut mwuun, niugiuniug ngaeniaei, eyor eew oat ina epwe noa itto nge aeremas resoapw maeipin ngaeni no minna Semaei me wooan rhug eei aere noan Jerusalem.
JOH 4:22 Aaemi re Samaria oawse giuneei iyo mwu oawgaen maeipin ngaeni; nge aemaem re Jews aei giuneei mane aeigaen maeipin ngaeni, pwe iga menaw na esooar ssiaaenin ina e itto me reer re Jews.
JOH 4:23 Nge oatona epwe itto ina a fasiun no igeei, reen minna maemaewaen Espritu Santus nge aeremas repwene maeipin ngaeni Deus, nge repwene feeori maeipin kkena e wenewen ina e tipaeni.
JOH 4:24 Deus ina ngeon, maemaewaen minne epwe mmwen pwe aeremas repwe maeipin ngaeni nge ina epwe noa reen Deus noan minna e wenewen.”
JOH 4:25 Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Ngaang i giuneei pwe Kristus epwe itto, oatona epwe itto, epwe aengaenigemaem oanongaen aegiaeg.”
JOH 4:26 Jesus a paniuwaeni, “Ngaang iiy minne i mwaenieniy ngaeniug.”
JOH 4:27 Oatonaan nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun Jesus ra sefaaen, nge iir ra igin riu pwe e mwaenieniy ngaeni erhai rhooapwut. Nge esooar erhai neeiir ne e aeiineow rhooapwut we, “Meeta wo tipaeni?” aere aeiyegiy Jesus pwe, “Meeta wo mwaenieniy ngaeni rhooapwut na reen?”
JOH 4:28 Rhooapwut we a nigiti ruumen rhan we aan, nge a sefaaen noa nee aepinoamw, nge a aengaeniir aeremas kkewe ee pwe,
JOH 4:29 “Oaw itto pipiiy mwaaen ee e aengaeniaei oanongaen meeta kkewe i feoffeeori. Oaw maengiy nge iiy minne Kristus?”
JOH 4:30 Iwe ra nigiti aepinoamw we nge ra noa reen Jesus.
JOH 4:31 Noan oatonaan nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe re iyaeffaenipirhe ngaeni Jesus pwe, “Sinsei, angi egiufet meeta!”
JOH 4:32 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaang eyor aenaei mwongo ina aaemi oawse giuneei mmwenen.”
JOH 4:33 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra aeiyeg fengaen wooar, “Eyor mwo mane e pweipwog to mwongo reen?”
JOH 4:34 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Mwongo na aenaei ina ipwe tapweei tipaen manna efangeto ngaang, pwe ipwe oamoanna noa engaang na e ngaenneaei pwe ipwe feeori.
JOH 4:35 Eyor eew mwaeniaemi iwe oawgaen iura pwe, ‘Faawu rhag meram nge a oaton gin.’ Nge ipwe aengaenigaemi, oaw pipiiy gacchiuw maat kaan; foat kaan ikka a maaw pwe sipwene giniiy!
JOH 4:36 Iyo na a giniiy uwaen foat kaan ina a pwigi paniuwaen nge a ioni fengaenniy uwaen foat kaan pwe aegin menaw na esooar ssiaaenin; iwe iyo we efoat me iyo we egin nge repwe kker fengaen.
JOH 4:37 Pwe ennetaen kkepas we regaen iura pwe, ‘Erhai epwe foat nge erhai a giniiy uwaan.’
JOH 4:38 Iya fangenoa aaemi pwe oawpwe noa giniiy uwaen foat kena soapw foatogiyaemi; aaemweoi minne re engaang ee, nge aaemi oawwa pwigi wenepwuwaen aar engaang.”
JOH 4:39 Re towunap re Samaria kkewe reno noan aepinoamw we ra niugiuniug ngaeni Jesus pwe igiwe rhooapwut we e aengaeniir pwe, “E aengaeniaei oanongaen minikkewe iya moannon feoffeeori.”
JOH 4:40 Iwe re Samaria kkewe ra itto reen iwe ra aeffaenipirheei pwe epwe notiw reer, iwe Jesus a notiw reer noan riiuraaen.
JOH 4:41 Repwan towunap rhooakka re niugiuniug pwonno reen miniwe mwaenian,
JOH 4:42 ra aengaeni rhooapwut we pwe, “Aeiya niugiuniug igina, nge saapw igiwe wo aengaenigemaem, pwe iga aemaem wooan oanongaemmaem aeiya rongorong mwaenian, iwe aeiya giuneei pwe iiy miniwe rhooan aemenewa faeinaengiy.”
JOH 4:43 Mwirin aan no aegini riiuraaen igiwe, nge Jesus a nigiti iwe a noa Galilee.
JOH 4:44 Pwe iiy wooan oanongan miniwe e iura pwe, “Profeta nge esooar aesirowuur me noan sipegin faniuweer.”
JOH 4:45 Oatowe enoa toori Galilee, aeremas ra itto aewenimmwa, pwe igiwe renoa tapweei gupwunon Passover me Jerusalem, nge ra weri oanongaen minikkewe efeeori me reen gupwun we.
JOH 4:46 Iwe Jesus a sefaaen noa Cana me noan Galilee, pwiuneoi we efeeori rhaan pwe wine. Erhai aeremesaen aam eno ee nge mwaaen na naiun nge e semwaai me noan Capernaum.
JOH 4:47 Igiwe e rongorong pwe Jesus a itto me Judea pwe epwene noa Galilee, a noa reen nge a aengaeni pwe epwe noa mwo Capernaum pwe epwe noa aecchipwa aetena naiun, pwe epwene oaropaen mae.
JOH 4:48 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Esooar faaen eew ne erhai me neeimi epwe niugiuniug pwe aeggaen igine rhag eweri kkeman me min ariuriu.”
JOH 4:49 Aeremesaen aam we a iura pwe, “Menap, itto tapweaei weni mmwaen aetena naeyi epwe mae noa.”
JOH 4:50 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Wonoa, aetena noawumw epwene menaw!” Mwaaen we a niugiuniug ngaeni miniwe mwaeniaen Jesus iwe a noa.
JOH 4:51 A faaeraeg noa nge a noa rhuungiir slave kkewe nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Aetewe noawumw epwe menaw!”
JOH 4:52 A aeiineeor fitowu konook minne aetewe naiun etakketae. Iwe nge iir ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Epwe eew konook nee oanowesaen naeneew pwe iwe esa pwerhikkar no ginin.”
JOH 4:53 Iwe rhag nge miniwe semaen aetewe a maengiy noa pwe ina oatowe Jesus e aengaeni pwe, “Aetewe noawumw epwe menaw.” Iwe iiy me oanongeer rhooan famini we aan ra niugiuniug ngaeni.
JOH 4:54 A ieei minne oaruwowwaen kkeman Jesus a feeori weni mwirin aan itto me Judea ngaeni Galilee.
JOH 5:1 Mwirin minneei nge Jesus a noa Jerusalem pwe epwe noa tapweei gupwunon eew pwoong kkewe aar re Jew.
JOH 5:2 Oaron eew rhan kken e aerepa minna aesemaen Jerusalem itan Sheep Gate ina nimowu pwerantaan; nge noan kkepesaen Hebrew nge Bethzatha.
JOH 5:3 E towunap rhooa semwaai rewon faaen pweranta kkewe — rhooa parh, rhooa pirhemae, me rhooa maemerhoar. [Re wewweti rhan we pwe epwe mwagiutiugiut,
JOH 5:4 pwe faaen aekkaew nge angkenusun Soamwoon e ittiw noan rhan we iwe a gupeti. Nge iyo na egommwaen toonong noan rhan we weni mwirin aan gupetaeg, nge esaer noa ese tiwegin semwaai ne e aeni.]
JOH 5:5 Erhai mwaaen eno ee a eniig me wanuuw raeg aan semwaai.
JOH 5:6 Jesus a weri pwe ewon noa rhag igiwe, nge e giuneei pwe a ssiunaei aan semwaai; iwe a aeiineow pwe, “Wo mwerhaen wopwe takketae?”
JOH 5:7 Mwaaen we a iura pwe, “Menap, ngaang esooar mane epwe iseniaei nong noan rhan mwuun igine a mwagiutiugiut; i aetemaegin pwe ipwe toonong nge erhai e itto gommw noa me mmwaei.”
JOH 5:8 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Rhimwitae wa pwigi minimwu giemw nge wa faaeraeg noa.”
JOH 5:9 Oatowe rhag nge etakk noa mwaaen we; nge e pwigi rhag miniwe gien nge a faaeraeg noa faan. Minneei nge ewen wooan Sabbath,
JOH 5:10 iwe soamwooniir Jews kkewe ra aengaeni mwaaen we a takk noa pwe, “Sabbath minneei, ese gacch ngaeni aarh Oasoapwosoapw pwe wopwe pweipwog fetaen giemw.”
JOH 5:11 Mwaaen we a paniuwaeni pwe, “Mwaaen we e aecchipwaeyaei tae e aengaeniaei pwe ipwe pwigi minne giei nge iya faaeraeg noa.”
JOH 5:12 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Iyo mwaaen na e aengaeniug pwe wopwe feeori minna?”
JOH 5:13 Nge mwaaen we a takketae ese giuneei aere iyo we e aecchipwatae, pwe igiwe re igin towunap aeremas igiwe, iwe Jesus a yo noa.
JOH 5:14 Enoa mwirin minneei nge Jesus a noa rhuungi mwaaen we me noan Temple we nge a aengaeni pwe, “Wa weri pwe wa takk igina; wosoapw oamonofit no, wopwe ina rhag nge eew min aenneew epwe wen ngaeniug.”
JOH 5:15 Mwaaen we a noa aengaeniir rhooawe soamwooniir Jews pwe Jesus miniwe e aecchipwatae.
JOH 5:16 Iwe a rhaepetae aar aewwaeiraesi Jesus pwe igiwe e aecchipwaar tae rhooa semwaai wooan Sabbath.
JOH 5:17 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Mwaaen na Semaei ina e engaang ffoarh noa rhag, iwe nge ngaang ipwan engaang.”
JOH 5:18 Egius mwo nge rhooawe soamwooniir Jews ra gin mwerhaen pwe repwe niiy reen miniwe mwaenian; a fasiun fereei miniwe oasoapwosoapwon Sabbath, nge a pwan iura pwe Deus nge Seman taeppei nge a aeffitaegiy ngaeni pwe iiy Deus.
JOH 5:19 Iwe Jesus a paniuwaeniir, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: esooar minne mwaaen na Naiun epwe mmwenen feeori rhag wooan oanongan; efeeori rhag minikkena eweri pwe mwaaen na Seman efeeori. Minikkena mwaaen we Seman efeeori nge ina minikkeei na mwaaen we Naiun epwe pwan feeori.
JOH 5:20 Pwe mwaaen we Seman nge e aerhaengi mwaaen we Naiun nge e pwaeri ngaeni oanongaen meeta kkewe iiy efeeori. Epwe pwaeri ngaeni mwo nge minikkena e temoag saengi me mmwaen ieei, iwe aaemi oawpwe mwaar reen.
JOH 5:21 Pwan taeppen rhag iga mwaaen we Seman e aemenewaar tae rhooa mae, epwan ina rhag mwaaen na Naiun epwe fang menaw ngaeniir rhooakkena e tipaeniir.
JOH 5:22 Nge mwaaen we Seman nge esoapw pwan apwiungiu mwo nge erhai aeremas. A fang ngaeni mwaaen na Naiun oanongaen maemaewan pwe epwe apwiungiiur aeremas,
JOH 5:23 iwe ina nge oanongeer aeremas nge repwe aesirowu minna Naiun, taeppen rhag aar aesirowu minna Seman. Iyo na ese aesirowu minna Naiun nge ina ese aesirowu minna Seman ina efangeto iiy.
JOH 5:24 “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: iyo kena re rongorong ngaeni minikkena mwaeniaei nge re niugiuniug ngaeni iiy iyo na efangeto ngaang nge repwe menaw foarhofoarh. Iir resoapw apwiung, pwe ra fasiun nigiti mae ra noa ngaeni menaw.
JOH 5:25 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: oatowe ina a itto, a fasiun no igeei, nge rhooa mae repwene rongorong minna mwaenian minna Naiun Deus, nge rhooakkena re rongorong repwe menaw sefaaen.
JOH 5:26 Taeppen rhag iga mwaaen na Seman rhaepin menaw, taeppen rhag minneei a pwan feeori minna Naiun pwe rhaepin menaw.
JOH 5:27 Nge a fasiun ngaenneei minna Naiun maemaewan pwe epwe apwiung, pwe iga iiy minne Naiun Aeremas.
JOH 5:28 Oawsoapw riu reen minneei, pwe a itto oatowe oanongeer manimae nge repwene rongorong mwaenian,
JOH 5:29 nge ra maegewow me noan paeyieer: rhooa feoffeeor mwamwaai repwene menaw tae, nge rhooa feoffeeor aenneew ra noa apwiung.
JOH 5:30 “Saapw tipaei rhag iya feeori minikkeei; Ngaang i apwiungiiur rhag kka Deus e aengaeniaei, iwe aaei apwiung ina e wenewen, pwe iga ngaang ise feeori minna i tipaeni pwe ifeeori minna tipaeniaen iyo na efangeto ngaang.
JOH 5:31 “Aere igine ngaang i pwaeritae kkepesaei, ina nge repwe iura pwe minikka mwaeniaei nge ese nnet.
JOH 5:32 Iwe nge eyor erhai ina epwe mmwenen aepesa kkepesaei, nge ngaang i giuneei pwe minna e aepesa reen minna mmwenei nge ina ennet.
JOH 5:33 John miniwe oawfang pwe rhooan pweipwogin kkepas, nge iiy e aepesa minna e wenewen.
JOH 5:34 Saapw menaen epwe yor naeyi aeremas rhooan pwaeritae; i aepesa rhag minneei pwe aaemi oawpwe menaw.
JOH 5:35 John iwe eweei rhag eew oappwun, iwe eppwun nge e seram, nge aaemi nge noan eew oat nge oawkker pwe oawpwe no noan sereman.
JOH 5:36 Iwe nge ngaang eno erhai naeyi rhooan pwaeritae ina e taegias saengi mwo nge John: minikka ifeeori, me minikka mwaaen na Semaei e ngoatto pwe ipwe feeori, oanongaen minikkeei nge e aepesa mmwenei pwe mwaaen na Semaei minne efangeto ngaang.
JOH 5:37 Mwaaen na Semaei ina efangeto ngaang, iiy epwan pwaeritae kkepesaei. Esaaen yor mwo aaemi rongorong mwaenian me weri mesan,
JOH 5:38 aaemi oawse iseni minna mwaenian noan tipaemi, pwe aaemi oawse niugiuniug ngaeni iyo na iiy efangeto.
JOH 5:39 Aaemi oaw aeraegi Pwapwior we e Santus, pwe oaw niuwaennei pwe oawpwe weri menaw na esooar ssiaaenin me ee. Nge iiy Pwapwior kka e santus ina re aepesa kkepesaei!
JOH 5:40 Nge inamwo oawse mwerhaen pwe oawpwe itto reei pwe oawpwe menaw foarhofoarh.
JOH 5:41 “Ngaang ise giutteon aeremas repwe oassoaraeyaei.
JOH 5:42 Pwe ngaang i giuneei wunuunumi, pwe esooar ffayeon Deus me noan pwunnomi.
JOH 5:43 Ngaang itto faaen itaen minna Semaei, nge aaemi oawse aetiwaeyaei; iwe ngaere aekkaerhai re itto faaen iteer nge aaemi oawpwe aetiwaar.
JOH 5:44 Oaw tipaeni pwe oawpwe gaen oassoara fengaennigaemi rhag, oawse giutta minne epwe yor ssoaromi me reen ina iiy noa rhag minne Deus; epwe ifa wusun rhag nge oawwa niugiuniug ngaeniaei?
JOH 5:45 Oawsoapw niuwaennei pwe ngaang minne ipwe oamonofitigaemi reen mwaaen na Semaei. Pwe Moses iwe oawgaen aeni aepiniugiuniug iiy minne epwe oamonofitigaemi.
JOH 5:46 Pwe ngaere igine oaw niugiuniug ngaeni Moses, nge oawpwe niugiuniug ngaeniaei, pwe igiwe iiy e foatogi minna wunuunuy.
JOH 5:47 Pwonno igiwe oawse niugiuniug ngaeni miniwe e foatogi, nge epwe ifa wusun aaemi niugiuniug ngaeni mwaeniaei?”
JOH 6:1 Weni mwirin minneei nge Jesus a noa noan meoneoiniuniun Galilee (aere meoneoiniuniun Tiberias).
JOH 6:2 Eew pwuwaen aeremas e tettapwei, pwe igiwe ra weri kkeman kkewe efeeori reen aan aecchipwaar rhooa semwaai.
JOH 6:3 Jesus a ittae wooan eew rhug a ittae mooat tiw reer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun.
JOH 6:4 Oatowe oaton gupwunon Passover a arapeto.
JOH 6:5 Jesus efaaen fetaen nge a weri eew pwuwaen aeremas pwe ra feffaaeraeg to reen, iwe a aeiineow Philip pwe, “Iya iga sipwe mmwenen chuwaai mwongo me ee, pwe aeremas kaan repwe mwongo?” (
JOH 6:6 E aepesa minneei pwe epwe soatoni Philip; iwe nge minna iiy ina a fasiun giuneei minne epwe feeori.)
JOH 6:7 Philip a iura pwe, “Inamwo igine epwe paer saengi riiuwapwiugiuw faiun silver eyor nge esoapw pwan toaw paniuwaenin fenoawa pwe erhai nge e angi egius.”
JOH 6:8 Andrew pwan erhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun, iwe pwiin Simon Peter, a iura pwe,
JOH 6:9 “Erhai aet iye eno niffai fenoawa barley me riiurhai iig reen. Iwe nge esoapw toaw mwo nge wooar rhooanap eei.”
JOH 6:10 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Aengaeniir oanongeer aeremas pwe repwe mooat tiw.” (Egin ssow fetin igiwe.) Iwe nge oanongeer aeremas ra mooat tiw; akkarap nimingeras nepeer mwaaen kkewe.
JOH 6:11 Jesus a pwigi fenoawa we, a fang ngaeni Deus aan aerhigerhig, a inetiy wooar aeremas kkewe remooat. Pwan ina miniwe efeeori ngaeni iig we, iwe aeremas ra mwongo nepaen minne re tipaeni.
JOH 6:12 Igiwe ra mat noa, a aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Oaw pwigi oanongaen nuseg, sisoapw oasonopa mwo nge egiufet.”
JOH 6:13 Iwe ra pwigi nusegin fenoawa barley kkewe, ngoannong noan seig me ruwowu rhiug.
JOH 6:14 Igiwe ra weri kkeman we Jesus efeeori, rhooa kkewe ra iura pwe, “Ennetaen pwe ieei iiy profeta we epwe itto noan faeinaengiy!”
JOH 6:15 Jesus a giuneei pwe repwene torofi pwe repwe feeori noa pwe king, iwe iiy rhag a pwan noa neeiin taeiit kkewe.
JOH 6:16 Enoa nee oatofaaef rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun Jesus ra maegetiw ngaerhen meoneoiniun we,
JOH 6:17 ra teeotae rhiun efoarh pwoot ra seraeg noa noan meoneoiniun we pwe repwe noa ngaeni Capernaum. Enoa pwoong noa, nge Jesus esaaen tooto mwo reer.
JOH 6:18 Enoa oatonaan nge a kekkaein noa rhag aaeng nge a iutae mesaei saaet.
JOH 6:19 Igiwe epwe enuuw aere faawu miles aar rhooan kkayeo kkewe fatiun, nge ra weri aaen Jesus faaeraegto weei saaet, enoa arap ngaeni pwoot we nge ra mesag.
JOH 6:20 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw mesag pwe iye ngaang!”
JOH 6:21 Nge re ateeotae rhiun pwoot we, nge ese mmwaei mwo nge ra toori faniuw igiwe re nennoa ngaeni ee.
JOH 6:22 Mmasetaen iwe eraaen, pwuwaen aeremas we eno peig we epeig ra giuneei pwe efoarh rhag pwoot eno igiwe. Ra giuneei pwe Jesus ese tapweer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun, pwe iir rhag miniwe renoa.
JOH 6:23 Aekkaew pwoot saengi Tiberias re tooto pwiuneoi we pwuwaen aeremas we re mwongo fenoawa me ee, mwirin aaen Soamwoon fang aerhigerhig.
JOH 6:24 Igiwe pwuwaen aeremas we enoa weri pwe Jesus e soanono igiwe, fengaen me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun, ra teeotae rhiun pwoot kkewe iwe ra noa Capernaum, ra noa giutta fetaeneei.
JOH 6:25 Igiwe aeremas kkewe ra weri Jesus me reen peigin meoneoiniun we, ra aengaeni pwe, “Sinsei, ineeta minne wo tooto igeei?”
JOH 6:26 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: oaw giuttayaei pwe iga oawwa mat noa pwe oawwa mwongo fenoawa, nge soapw reen aaemi metaf reen kkeman kkewe ifeeori.
JOH 6:27 Oawsoapw engaang ngaeni mwongo kkena epwe mmwenen aenneew noa; nge oawpwe faer engaang ngaeni mwongo kkena epwe noa ffoarh ngaeni minna menaw na esooar ssiaaenin. Ieen mwongo e mwaaen na Naiun Aeremas epwe ngaennegaemi, pwe iga Deus, ina Seman, a aeffeta noa pwe a fini pwe iga efin tipaen reen.”
JOH 6:28 Iwe ra aeiineow pwe, “Iwe meeta minne aeipwe feeori nge a mmwen aeipwe feeori minikkena Deus e tipaeni?”
JOH 6:29 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Minna Deus e tipaeni pwe oawpwe feeori, ina oawpwe niugiuniug ngaeni manna efangeto.”
JOH 6:30 Ra iura pwe, “Meeta kkeman kena wopwe feeori pwe aeipwe weri nge aeipwe niugiuniug ngaeniug? Meeta minne wopwe feeori?
JOH 6:31 Rhaepeto kkewe aemaem re mwommwongo manna me noan desert, taeppen rhag miniwe Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, ‘A ngaenneer fenoawa ittiw me naaeng pwe repwe mwongo.’ ”
JOH 6:32 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: miniwe we Moses e ngaennegaemi nge saapw fenoawa ittiw me naaeng; manna Semaei minne efang ngaenigaemi minna oanongonniuwaen fenoawa ittiw me naaeng.
JOH 6:33 Pwe fenoawa we Deus efang, ina iiy iyo we e ittiw me naaeng ina a aemenewa faeinaengiy.”
JOH 6:34 Iir ra aengaeni pwe, “Menap, ngaennegemaem fenoawa eei oanongaen oat.”
JOH 6:35 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ngaang minne fenoawaen menaw. Rhooakka re itto reei resoapw rhiuwen pecchai no; nge rhooakka re niugiuniug ngaeniaei resoapw moar no.
JOH 6:36 Iwe i aengaenigaemi pwe oawwa weriaei nge oawse niugiuniug.
JOH 6:37 Rhooakkena mwaaen na Semaei e ngaenneaei, repwe itto reei. Esooar faaen eew ipwe toagun saengi manna e itto reei,
JOH 6:38 pwe ise ittiw me naaeng pwe ipwe ittiw feeori minna aaei mwerhaen, pwe ipwe feeori aaen mwerhaen manna efangeto ngaang.
JOH 6:39 Aaen mwerhaen manna efangeto ngaang ina esoapw ppiung saengiaei mwo nge erhai me neeiir rhooawe e ngaenneaei, pwe ipwe faer aemenewaar tae oanongeer wooan minna oarosaen raaen.
JOH 6:40 Pwe mwaaen na Semaei ina e mwerhaen pwe oanongeer aeremas kena reweri minna Naiun nge re niugiuniug ngaeni iwe nge repwe menaw foarhofoarh. Nge ipwe aemenewaar tae wooan minna oarosaen raaen.”
JOH 6:41 A rhaepetae aar aeremas ngiuniungiuniuw pwe igiwe e iura pwe, “Ngaang fenoawa we e ittiw me naaeng.”
JOH 6:42 Nge ra iura pwe, “Ieen iiy mwaaen we naiun Joseph, aere? Si giuneei seman me inan. Nge ifa wusun nge e iura pwe e ittiw me naaeng?”
JOH 6:43 Jesus a paniuwaeniir, “Oawsoapw ngiuniungiun rhag woami.
JOH 6:44 Esooar ne epwe mmwenen itto reei pwe aeggaen igine rhag mwaaen na Semaei ina efang to ngaang minne e pwigiir to reei; iwe nge ipwe aemenewaar tae wooan minna oarosaen raaen.
JOH 6:45 Profeta kkewe re foatogi pwe, ‘Oanongeer aeremas nge Deus epwe aerrepiaar.’ Oanongeer rhooai rongorong ngaeni Semaei nge re reepiy me reen, nge re itto reei.
JOH 6:46 Ise iura pwe oanongeer aeremas nge reweri minna Semaei; pwe iyo na e itto me reen Deus ina rhag aeremas na a fasiun weri manna Semaei.
JOH 6:47 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: iyo na e niugiuniug, ina epwe menaw foarhofoarh.
JOH 6:48 Ngaang minne fenoawaen menaw.
JOH 6:49 Rhooa kkewe rhaepetomi re mwongo manna me noan desert, nge remae noa.
JOH 6:50 Iwe nge fenoawa na e ittiw me naaeng ina ese tiwegin ne e mwongo nge esoapw mae.
JOH 6:51 Ngaang minne fenoawa na e ittiw me naaeng. Aere oaw angi fenoawa een, nge oawpwe toori menaw na esooar ssiaaenin. Fenoawa e ipwe ngaennegaemi ina fitigoi, ina epwe fang pwe faeinaengiy epwe menaw.”
JOH 6:52 Iwe rhag re Jew kkewe erhaepetae aar aengimaaw fengaen. Ra aeiineow pwe, “Epwe ifa wusun aan ngaennegirh fitigon pwe sipwe mwongo?”
JOH 6:53 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: aere oawse angi minna fitigon mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas nge oaw iun me reen cchaan, nge esoapw yor menewaemi.
JOH 6:54 Iyo kena re mwongo fitigoi nge re iun cchaei, nge repwe menaw foarhofoarh, ipwe aemenewaar tae wooan minna oarosaen raaen.
JOH 6:55 Pwe minne fitigoi ina oanongonniuwaen mwongo, iwe nge minne cchaei ina oanongonniuwaen menaen iun.
JOH 6:56 Iyo kena re mwongo minna fitigoi nge re iun me reen minna cchaei nge iir reno noan ngaang nge ngaang ino noan iir.
