JOH 6:57 Saam na e menaw efangeto ngaang, iwe ngaang ipwan menaw pwe aegin iiy. Epwe pwan ina rhag pwe iyo kena re angi fitigoi repwe pwan menaw pwe aegin ngaang.
JOH 6:58 Iwe ieen iiy fenoawa we e ittiw me naaeng; ese weei taeppen iiy fenoawa we rhaepeto kkewe aaemi re mwongo nge faeiyegius noa nge remae noa. Nge iyo kena re mwongo fenoawa een nge repwe menaw noa rhag.”
JOH 6:59 Jesus e aepesa minikkeei igiwe e fenai noan wutt we wutteer Jews me Capernaum.
JOH 6:60 Towunepeer rhooa kkewe rhoaniuwaar re rongorong minneei nge ra iura pwe, “E igin waeiraes aerrepiei. Iyo na epwe mmwenen aiussaening ngaeni?”
JOH 6:61 Rese aengaeni nge Jesus e giuneei miniwe re ngiuniungiuniuw, iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Minne ifeeori a aetippaegaemi ina oawwa nigiti noa aaemi niugiuniug?
JOH 6:62 Ngaere pwetae oawweri mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas aan sefaaen tae reen pwiuneoi we e fasiun no ee?
JOH 6:63 Espritu na aaen Deus minne efang menaw; esooar ipitaen minne maemaewaen aeremas. Pwe kkepas kka iya ngaennegaemi nge kkepesaen Ngeon me menaw.
JOH 6:64 Nge ina rhag aaemweoi aaemi oawse giuneei.” (Saengi rhag rhaepetaen nge Jesus e giuneei iyo kena rese niugiuniug, me iyo na epwe fangenoa tinnimaen.)
JOH 6:65 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ieei faaen iiy miniwe i aengaenigaemi pwe esooar aeremas kka repwe mmwenen itto reei pwe igine rhag mwaaen na Semaei efeeori pwe epwe mmwen pwe repwe itto.”
JOH 6:66 Iwe aegin minneei, re towunap rhooa kkewe rhoaniuwaen Jesus ra sefaaen resa mwerhaen tapweei noano.
JOH 6:67 Iwe a aeiineeor rhooan kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai, “Iwe nge aaemi, oawpwan mwerhaen noa?”
JOH 6:68 Simon Peter a paniuwaeni, “Soamwoon, nge iyo aeipwene noa reen? Eno reemw kkepas na efang menaw na esooar ssiaaenin.
JOH 6:69 Iwe igina aei niugiuniug nge aei giuneei pwe een miniwe wo santus iwe wo itto me reen Deus.”
JOH 6:70 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ngaang miniwe i finigaemi tae seig me riiurhai, aere saapw ngaang? Nge ina rhag ina erhai me neeimi nge mwuniaan!”
JOH 6:71 A aepesa kkepesaen Judas, iwe naiun Simon Iscariot. Pwe Judas, inamwo igiwe iiy erhai rhooawe seig me riiurhai, nge epwene fangenoa tinnimaen Jesus.
JOH 7:1 Mwirin minneei nge Jesus a no fetaen rhag noan Galilee; ese tipaeni pwe epwe noa fetaen noan Judea pwe igiwe soamwooniir Jews ra mwerhaen repwe niiy noa.
JOH 7:2 Oaton Gupwunon Penaes a arapeto,
JOH 7:3 iwe mwaaen kkewe pwiin Jesus ra aengaeni pwe, “Wone nigiti igeei pwe wopwene noa Judea, pwe rhooakka rhoaniuwoamw repwe weri minikka wa feeori.
JOH 7:4 Aeremas rese oapa minikka repwe feeori igine re tipaeni pwe repwe pwae noa, nge iga wa feoffeeori minikkeei, pwaeri ngaeni faeinaengiy pwe repwe giuneog!” (
JOH 7:5 Mwaaen kkewe mwo pwiin nge rese niugiuniug ngaeni.)
JOH 7:6 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Esaaen oato mwamwaaiun pwe ipwe noa. Aaemi ese tiwegin eew oat nge efin ngaenigaemi.
JOH 7:7 Faeinaengiy ese mmwen epwe oapwutaegaemi, nge ngaang e oapwutaeyaei, pwe iga ngaang i aengaeni rhag pwe minikka feoffeeoriiur iga e aenneew.
JOH 7:8 Oawnoa aaemi oawpwe noa tapweei gupwun na. Ngaang isoapw noa tapweei gupwun na pwe esaaen itto mwo minna oatoi.”
JOH 7:9 E aengaeniir minneei iwe a notiw noan Galilee.
JOH 7:10 Mwirin aar mwaaen kkewe pwiin noa tapweei gupwun we iwe nge Jesus a pwan noa; ese pwaeri noa aan noa, pwe eyopo noa rhag.
JOH 7:11 Rhooa kkewe soamwooniir Jews ra giutta fetaeneei rhag me faaen gupwun we. Ra aeiineow pwe, “Ifa iiy wonowe?”
JOH 7:12 Ra igin towunap rhooan mwangiuniungiun me noan pwuwa we. Aaemweoi ra iura pwe, “Erhai aeremas gacch.” Nge aekkaaemweoi re iura pwe, “Aapw, pwe e oatupwutupw aeremas.”
JOH 7:13 Aeremas rese fioangei fetaeneei pwe re mesagiiur soamwooniir Jews.
JOH 7:14 A nugunupan noa aan epwene moann gupwun we nge Jesus a noa noan Temple we iwe a noa rhaepiy tae aan fenai.
JOH 7:15 Rhooa kkewe soamwooniir Jews ra igin riutae ra iura pwe, “E ifa wusun nge mwaaeneei nge e giuneei minikkeei nge esooar aan suguun?”
JOH 7:16 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Minikka i fenaiuw nge saapw aaei fenai pwe e itto me reen Deus, iwe efangeto ngaang.
JOH 7:17 Iyo na e mwerhaen epwe feeori minna tipaen Deus nge epwe giuneei pwe aere minikka i fenaiuw nge e itto me reen Deus, ngaere ngaang iya aepesa wow mwaeniaei wooan oanongaei.
JOH 7:18 Iyo kka iir re aepesa wow mwaenieer wooan oanongeer nge iir re giutta rhag ssoaron iteer. Nge iyo na e mwerhaen giutta ssoaron iyo na efangeto iiy ina e wenewen, esooar eew min oatupwutupw reen.
JOH 7:19 Moses e ngaennegaemi anniug we, ngaere? Nge esooar erhai me neeimi ne e tapweei. Nge meeta oawwa mwerhaen pwe oawpwe niaei noa reen?”
JOH 7:20 Nge pwuwa we a paniuwaeni pwe, “Eyor mwuniaan woamw. Iyo na e mwerhaen epwe niug noa?”
JOH 7:21 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ifeeori eew kkeman nge oanongaemi nge oawwa maegin riutae reen.
JOH 7:22 Moses a akkiuneogaemi pwe oawpwe circumcise aegini naimi aetemwaaen (nge iwe saapw Moses pwe rhooawe rhaepetomi miniwe rerhaepiy tae), iwe oawwa circumcise aegini erhai aetemwaaen wooan Sabbath.
JOH 7:23 Ngaere re circumcise aegini erhai aetemwaaen wooan Sabbath pwe minni ete fereei anniug we aaen Moses, nge meeta oawwa soong wooai iga i aecchipwatae erhai aeremas wooan Sabbath reen?
JOH 7:24 Oawsoapw apwiung aeremas reen meeta na oawweri, pwe oawpwe apwiung reen minna e wenewen.”
JOH 7:25 Aaemweoi re Jerusalem ra iura pwe, “Saapw ieen mwaaen we soamwoon kkewe re mwerhaen repwe niiy noa?
JOH 7:26 Pipiiy! A kkepas neeiir rhooanap, nge esooar meeta minne re iura reen! Meeta, re giuneei pwe iiy Kristus?
JOH 7:27 Nge aere Kristus enoa itto, esooar erhai ne epwe giuneei aere iiy aeremesaen iya. Nge oanongarh nge si giuneei iya iga mwaaen een e itto me ee.”
JOH 7:28 Iwe Jesus a feffenai noan Temple we, a kkepas temoag tae nge a iura pwe, “Oaw oanongonniuwaen giuneaei me iga i itto me ee? Saapw ngaang minne tipaei pwe ipwe itto. Nge iiy iyo na efangeto ngaang ina e wenewen. Aaemi oawse giuneei,
JOH 7:29 nge ngaang i giuneei, pwe iga itto me reen nge iiy efangeto ngaang.”
JOH 7:30 Iwe rhooawe ra menaen repwe torofi, nge esooar mane e anngaeni, pwe igiwe esaaen gona mwo oaton.
JOH 7:31 Nge towunepeer rhooawe re niugiuniug ngaeni me noan pwuwa we ra iura pwe, “Oatona epwe itto Kristus, epwe ssow kkeman kka epwe feeori me mmwaen mwaaen een?”
JOH 7:32 Pharisees reno noan pwuwa we ra rongorong aar aeremas ngiuniungiuniuw kkepesaen Jesus, iwe iir me soamwooniir patere kkewe ra fangenoa aaemweoi poos repwe noa torofi.
JOH 7:33 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ipwene no egius rhag reemi, nge iya noa reen iyo we efangeto ngaang.
JOH 7:34 Oawpwe giuttayaei nge oawsoapw rhuungiaei, pwe aaemi oawsoapw mmwenen noa iga ipwe noa ee.”
JOH 7:35 Rhooa kkewe soamwooniir Jews ra aeiineo fengaen wooar, “Iya iga epwe noa ee nge sisoapw mmwenen weri? Epwene noa wooan eew aepinoamwon Greece igiwe aeremas kkewe naiurh reno ee, iwe a noa fenaiuw ngaeniir re Greeks?
JOH 7:36 Nge e iura pwe sipwe noa giutta nge sisoapw rhuungi, nge sisoapw mmwenen noa iga epwe no ee. Meeta faan minna e iura?”
JOH 7:37 Oarosan raaenin gupwun we e igin yor ipitan, Jesus a iutae nge a kkepas temoag tae, “Iyo ne a moar epwe itto reei,
JOH 7:38 iwe nge iyo ne e niugiuniug ngaeniaei epwe iun. Pwe iwe Pwapwior we e Santus e iura pwe, ‘Rhan we efang menaw epwe pwuutiw me wenepeigin.’ ”
JOH 7:39 Jesus e kkepesaen mmwenen Espritu, pwe aeremas kka ra niugiuniug ngaeni nge repwene pwigi. Noan oatonaan nge Espritu esaaen fang mwo pwe iga Jesus esaaen toonong mwo noan minna nningen.
JOH 7:40 Aaemweoi aeremas kkewe noan pwuwa we re rongorong aan aepesa miniwe nge ra iura pwe, “Mwaaeneei nge oanongaen pwe iiy Profeta we!”
JOH 7:41 Aaemweoi re iura pwe, “Iiy minne Kristus!” Nge aaemweoi re iura pwe, “Kristus esoapw itto me Galilee!
JOH 7:42 Pwapwior we e Santus nge e iura pwe, ‘Kristus nge teoteeon king David nge epwe supw me Bethlehem, aepinoamw we David eno ee.’ ”
JOH 7:43 Iwe a yor aeiyaegin nee finaen aeremas me reen pwuwa we pwonno faan ngaeni iiy Jesus.
JOH 7:44 Aaemweoi ra mwerhaen torofi, nge esooar mane emmwenen angetae paiun wooan.
JOH 7:45 Igiwe renoa sefaaen poos kkewe, soamwooniir patere kkewe me Pharisees ra aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta oawse pwigito reen?”
JOH 7:46 Poos kkewe ra iura pwe, “Esaaen yor erhai ne eweei aaen kkepas mwaaen een!”
JOH 7:47 Pharisees kkewe ra aeiineeor pwe, “Aaemi mwo nge epwan oatupwugaemi?
JOH 7:48 A yor mwo erhai soamwoon kaan aere Pharisees pwe re niugiuniug ngaeni?
JOH 7:49 Pwuwa eei nge ese giuneei anniug kkewe aaen Moses, iwe iir ra no faaen aaen Deus aegaeregaer!”
JOH 7:50 Erhai Pharisee itan Nicodemus, mwaaen we a fasiun noa mwo reen Jesus. A aengaeniir pwe,
JOH 7:51 “Noan aarh Anniug nge sisoapw mmwenen oamonofiti erhai iga sisaaen apwiungiiur mwo pwe sipwe giutta meeta na efeeori.”
JOH 7:52 Ra iura pwe, “Iwe, nge een erhai rhooan Galilee? Aeraegi Pwapwior we e Santus pwe wopwe giuneei pwe esooar profeta e ikkitto me Galilee.” [
JOH 7:53 Iwe erhai nge enoa reen imwan.
JOH 8:1 Iwe nge Jesus a noa wooan rhugun Olives.
JOH 8:2 Nee oatosor moawugowugon raaenin we eraaen nge a noa noan Temple we. Ra maegeto aeremas reen, a mooat tiw pwe a fenai ngaeniir.
JOH 8:3 Sinsein anniug me Pharisees kkewe ra pwigito erhai rhooapwut iwe re torofi pwe e maiur ngaeni pwiuniuwaen erhai, ra itto aiuw noa me weni mmweer oanongeer.
JOH 8:4 Ra aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Sinsei, rhooapwut een re torofi pwe e mwoarho pwiuniuwan.
JOH 8:5 Noan aarh oasoapwosoapw nge Moses e iura pwe taeppen rhooapwut een nge sipwe tera pwe epwe mae. Iwe igina nge meeta een wopwe iura?”
JOH 8:6 Re aepesa minneei pwe repwe aegina Jesus pwe repwe oamonofitiy wooan. Iwe nge iya pwoarotiw a ittiw foatofoat fetaen wooan ppweon reen aiuttiun.
JOH 8:7 Reen oatowe ra iu igiwe pwe ra kkepas aeiyeg ngaeni, a fattae nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Iyo erhai me neeimi ne esooar monofitin nge iiy minne epwe aerheei minna mesaemmwaen faai.”
JOH 8:8 A pwan pwoar sefaaen tiw a pwan ittiw foatofoat fetaen wooan ppweon.
JOH 8:9 Igiwe ra rongorong minneei nge a erhai me erhai neeiir ra siussiu noa, rhaepetae me wooar rhooa kkewe re tugufaeyi. Iwe a noa rhag noatiw Jesus me rhooapwut we e iu.
JOH 8:10 A fattae nge a aengaeni pwe, “Ra maegenoa iya? Esooar erhai ne enotiw pwe epwe oamonofitiug?”
JOH 8:11 Rhooapwut a paniuwaeni nge a iura pwe, “Esooar menap.” Jesus a iura pwe, “Iwe ina pwan ngaang nge isoapw oamonofitiug. Wonoa nge wosoapw rhiuwen feeori no eew monofit.”]
JOH 8:12 Jesus a pwan mwaenieniy sefaaen ngaeniir Pharisees kkewe, a iura pwe, “Ngaang minne seremaen faeinaengiy. Iyo noa epwe tapweaei nge epwe no reen minna seremaen menaw, iwe nge esooar faaen eew ne epwe faaeraeg noan rorhappiung.”
JOH 8:13 Pharisees kkewe ra aengaeni pwe, “Meeta kkomwu wo iura igina nge kkepesaen oamw pwaeritae wunuunumw; nge minikkomwu wo iura nge ese nnet.”
JOH 8:14 Jesus a iura pwe, “Inamwo iga ngaang i aepesa sipegin kkepesaei, iwe nge minne i aepesa ina e wenewen, pwe iga i giuneei iga itto me ee iwe nge i giuneei iya iga ipwene noa ee. Aaemi oawse giuneei iga i itto me ee aere iga ipwe noa ee.
JOH 8:15 Aaemi oaw aeni rhag aar aeremas apwiung; nge ngaang esooar mane i apwiungiu.
JOH 8:16 Pwe ngaere igine ipwe apwiungiiur aeremas, iwe nge ipwe apwiungiiur noan wenewen, pwe iga saapw ngaang rhag minne ifeeori minneei; pwe mwaaen na Semaei ina efangeto ngaang epwan tapweaei.
JOH 8:17 Pwe eno noan Oasoapwosoapw we aaemi pwe ngaere riiurhai rhooan pwaeritae e aeffitaeg mwaenieer iwe ina nge minna re aepesa nge e wenewen.
JOH 8:18 Ngaang i aepesa mmwenei wooan oanongaei, iwe nge mwaaen na Semaei iwe efang to ngaang, epwan aepesa mmwenei.”
JOH 8:19 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Pwe ifa mwaaen na Semoamw?” Jesus a iura pwe, “Aaemi oawse giuneaei iwe oawse pwan giuneei mwaaen na Semaei. Aere igine oaw giuneaei ina nge oawpwan giuneei mwaaen na Semaei.”
JOH 8:20 Oanongaen minikkeei nge Jesus e aepesa igiwe e fenai noan Temple we, noan pwiuneoi we eno kakoonaen niffang kkewe ee. Nge esooar ne e torofi pwe igiwe esaaen itto mwo minna oaton.
JOH 8:21 Jesus a pwan aengaeniir pwe, “Ngaang ipwene noa; oawpwe giuttayaei nge oawpwe maenoa noan aaemi monofit. Oawsoapw mmwenen noa iga ipwe noa ee.”
JOH 8:22 Iwe mwaaen kkewe soamwooniir Jews ra iura pwe, “E iura pwe sisoapw mmwenen noa iga epwe noa ee. E iura minneen pwe iiy epwe sipegin niiy noa oanongan?”
JOH 8:23 Jesus a iura pwe, “Aaemi oaw itto me reen faniuw efaan, nge ngaang itto me reen ina weei naaeng. Aaemi oawno noan faeinaengiy, nge ngaang ise itto me reen faeinaengiy.
JOH 8:24 Ina faaen minne i aengaenigaemi pwe oawpwe maenoa noan aaemi monofit reen. Oawpwe maenoa noan aaemi monofit igine oawse niugiuniug pwe ‘Ngaang ina Ngaang’.”
JOH 8:25 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Een iyo?” Jesus a iura pwe, “Miniwe i aengaenigaemi me rhaepetaen.
JOH 8:26 Ngaang e igin ssow minne ipwe aepesa reen mmwenemi, iwe me minne ipwe oamonofitigaemi wooan. Nge iyo na efangeto ngaang ina e wenecchar, nge ngaang iya aengaeni faeinaengiy minikkena ngaang iya rongorong saengi.”
JOH 8:27 Iir rese metefaaegini pwe Jesus a fioangei ngaeniir mmwenen minna Semaen.
JOH 8:28 Iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “Oatona oawpwe aetaegiasaetae mwaaen na Naiun Aeremas, ina nge oawpwe giuneei pwe, ‘Ngaang ina Ngaang’; nge ina oawpwe giuneei pwe ngaang saapw tipaei rhag iya feeori minikkeei, pwe ngaang i aepesa rhag minna mwaaen na Semaei e aengaeniaei pwe ipwe aepesa.
JOH 8:29 Nge iyo na efangeto ngaang ina eno reei; esaaen nigitiaei mwo; pwe iga ngaang ifeeori rhag meeta kena iiy e tipaeni.”
JOH 8:30 Re towunap rhooa kkewe re rongorong aaen Jesus aepesa minikkeei nge ra niugiuniug ngaeni.
JOH 8:31 Iwe Jesus a aengaeniir Jews kkewe re niugiuniug ngaeni pwe, “Ngaere oaw tapweei aaei fenai, aaemi minne oanongonniuwaen naeyi rhooan kkayeo;
JOH 8:32 oawpwe giuneei minna e wenewen nge minna e wenewen epwe saenetigaemi.”
JOH 8:33 Ra iura pwe, “Aemaem minikka teoteeon Abraham, iwe nge esaaen yor mwo ne e pwigigemaem pwe aemaem pwe naiun rhooan akkiuneo. Iwe meeta faaen miniwe wo iura pwe, ‘Oawpwene saenetaeg reen’?”
JOH 8:34 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: oanongeer rhooakka re monofit nge ina iiy naiun monofit rhooan akkiuneo.
JOH 8:35 Rhooan akkiuneo ina esoapw mmwenen no noa pwe naiun eew famini, iwe nge aetemwaaen emmwenen no noa pwe naiun famini ne esooar iaenin.
JOH 8:36 Aere igine mwaaen na Naiun Deus epwe saenetigaemi, iwe nge oawpwe oanongonniuwaen saenetaeg.
JOH 8:37 Ngaang i giuneei pwe aaemi nge teoteeon Abraham. Iwe nge aaemi oawwa menaen oawpwe niaei noa, pwe oawse mwerhaen aetiwa minikka mwaeniaei.
JOH 8:38 Ngaang i aepesa meeta minne mwaaen na Semaei a pwaeri ngaeniaei, nge aaemi oawfeeori minikkena manna semaemi e aengaenigaemi.”
JOH 8:39 Ra iura pwe, “Mwaaen na semmaem nge Abraham.” Jesus a iura pwe, “Ngaere igine oanongonniuwaen aaemi naiun Abraham, ina nge oawpwe pwan feeori minikkewe iiy epwan feeori.
JOH 8:40 Minna rhag ngaang ifeeori ina i aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen ina i rongorong me reen Deus, nge aaemi oawwa menaen oawpwe niaei noa. Esooar taeppen minneei ne Abraham efeeori!
JOH 8:41 Aaemi oawfeeori meeta na semaemi efeeori.” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Deus ina iiy rhag minne Semmaem, nge aemaem pwiungiuncheraen naiun.”
JOH 8:42 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Ngaere igine Deus minne oanongonniuwaen Semaemi, nge oawpwe aerhaengiaei, pwe iga ngaang i itto me reen Deus iwe igina ngaang iya no igeei. Saapw tipaei rhag iya noa ittiw, pwe iiy minne e fangetiw ngaang.
JOH 8:43 Meeta oawse metefaaegini minne i iura reen? Faan ina pwe iga oawse mwerhaen rongorong ngaeni aaei fenai.
JOH 8:44 Aaemi naiun miniwe semaemi, iwe Saetan, oaw mwerhaen tapweei minna aaen mwerhaen minna semaemi. Saengi rhag rhaepetaen nge iiy rhooan niiy menaw nge esaaen yor mwo faaen eew eno noan wenewen, pwe iga esooar wenewen nee tipan. Igine epwe oatupwutupw, iwe nge efeeori minna fasiun aan feoffeeor, pwe iiy fasiun erhai man oatupwutupw, nge iiy minne semaen oanongaen oatupwutupw.
JOH 8:45 Iwe nge i aengaenigaemi minna e wenewen, iwe ina faan minne oawse niugiuniug ngaeniaei reen.
JOH 8:46 Iyo erhai neeimi ne epwe mmwenen pwaeritae pwe i monofit? Ngaere igine i aengaenigaemi minna e wenewen, iwe nge meeta oawse niugiuniug ngaeniaei reen?
JOH 8:47 Iyo na e itto me reen Deus ina e rongorong ngaeni minna mwaeniaen Deus. Iwe nge aaemi oawse itto me reen Deus, iwe ina faan minimwu oawse rongorong reen.”
JOH 8:48 Ra aeiineow Jesus pwe, “Ese nnet ngaenigemaem igiwe aei iura pwe een erhai re Samaria nge eyor mwuniaan woamw?”
JOH 8:49 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ngaang esooar mwuniaan wooai. Ngaang i oassoara manna Semaei, nge aaemi oawse oassoaraeyaei.
JOH 8:50 Ngaang ise giutteon aaei ssoar wooan oanongaei. Nge a yor erhai ina e kiukkiutta aaei ssoar nge e wenewen aan apwiung.
JOH 8:51 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: erhai ne epwe tapweei aaei fenai nge esooar faaen eew ne epwe mae.”
JOH 8:52 Ra aengaeni pwe, “Igina aeiya oanongonniuwan giuneei pwe eyor mwuniaan woamw! Abraham emae noa nge profeta kkewe repwan mae noa, iwe nge een wo iura pwe erhai ne e tapweei oamw fenai nge esooar faaen eew ne epwe mae.
JOH 8:53 Manewe semmaem Abraham iwe a mae; nge een wo iura pwe wo taegias me mmwaen Abraham? Nge profeta kkewe mwo nge repwan mae noa. Wo niuwaennei pwe een iyo?”
JOH 8:54 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Aere igine ngaang rhag i oassoaraeyaei wooan oanongaei, nge ssoar naan esoapw yor ipitan. Manna e oassoaraeyaei ina manna Semaei — ina iiy mwaaen we oaw iura pwe aaemi Deus.
JOH 8:55 Aaemi oawse fasiun giuneei, iwe nge ngaang i giuneei. Ngaere igine i aengaenigaemi pwe ise giuneei, ina nge ipwene oatupwugaemi. Iwe nge ngaang i giuneei, iwe nge i tapweei minna mwaenian.
JOH 8:56 Manewe semaemi Abraham a pwapwa reen aan epwe weri oaton aaei itto; a weri iwe nge a kker nee tipan.”
JOH 8:57 Ra aengaeni pwe, “Esaaen toori mwo nimeig raeg raegimw nge wa iura pwe woweri Abraham?”
JOH 8:58 Jesus a paniuwaeniir, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: weni mmwaen aan supw Abraham, ‘Ngaang ina Ngaang’.”
JOH 8:59 Iwe ra pweipwog faai pwe repwe tera, iwe nge Jesus a mwoan saengiir nge a siusaengi Temple we.
JOH 9:1 Igiwe Jesus a feffaaeraeg noa nge a weri erhai mwaaen esupwuto nge eparh mesan.
JOH 9:2 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra aeiineow pwe, “Sinsei, monofitin iyo minne mwaaen efeeori pwe epwe wupwutiw nge eparh mesaen? Monofitin aere monofitin inan me seman?”
JOH 9:3 Jesus a paniuwaeniir, “Aan masparh saapw menaen aan monofit aere aar inan me seman. Eparh mesan pwe epwe pwaeri noa minna mamaawan aaen Deus engaang wooan.
JOH 9:4 Iga e rhiuwen raaen sa feeori aaen engaang manna efangeto ngaang; akkarapto pwoong nge esooar ne epwe rhiuwen mmwenen engaang.
JOH 9:5 Iga e rhiuwen no noan faeinaengiy nge ngaang minne seremaen faeinaengiy.”
JOH 9:6 Mwirin aan aepesa minneei nge Jesus a oattuffa tiw nee ppweon a tonaeni fengaenniy me ppweon we iwe a toafi ngaeni mesaen mwaaen we
JOH 9:7 iwe nge a aengaeni pwe, “Wonoa wa noa woraes noan rhaan na Siloam.” (Faaen itaen rhaan we nge “Fang”) Iwe mwaaen we a noa, a noa woraes, a sefaaeneto pwe a ffat noa mesan.
JOH 9:8 Rhooan no oaron me rhooa kkewe reweri aaen mwaaen we tingoar maaw fetaen rhag ammwenen ra aeiineo pwe, “Saapw ieei mwaaen we e mooaton tingoar maaw fetaen rhag?”
JOH 9:9 Aaemweoi re iura pwe, “Ooa, ina iiy,” Nge aaemweoi ra iura pwe, “Aapw, saapw iiy; eweei rhag pwe iiy mwaaen we.” Nge iiy mwaaen we a iura pwe, “Ngaang iiy mwaaen we.”
JOH 9:10 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Ifa wusun rhag nge a ffatenoa mesoamw?”
JOH 9:11 Iiy mwaaen we a iura pwe, “Mwaaen we itan Jesus e pwigi aekkaew ppweon a toafitae wooan mesaei, iwe a aengaeniaei pwe ipwe noa noan rhaan we Siloam pwe ipwe noa woraes. Iwe iya noa, nge igiwe rhag i woraes, nge a ffat noa mesaei.”
JOH 9:12 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Ifa iiy?” Nge a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ngaang ise giuneei.”
JOH 9:13 Iwe ra pwigi noa mwaaen we eparh mwo mesan reer Pharisees kkewe.
JOH 9:14 Raaenin we Jesus efeeori ppweon kkewe pwe epwe aecchipwa ngaeni mwaaen masparh we nge eew Sabbath.
JOH 9:15 Iwe Pharisees kkewe ra pwan aeiineow mwaaen we wunuunun aan ffat noa mesan. Nge a aengaeniir pwe, “E toafitae ppweon wooan mesaei; iya noa woraes iwe igina a ffat noa mesaei.”
JOH 9:16 Aaemweoi Pharisees kkewe ra iura pwe, “Mwaaen we efeeori minneei nge ese itto me reen Deus, pwe iiy ese tapweei oasoapwosoapwon Sabbath.” Nge aaemweoi re iura pwe, “Nge epwe ifa wusun aaen erhai mwaaen monofit epwe mmwenen aan feeori minikkeei?” Iwe a yor giniginin nee fineer.
JOH 9:17 Nge Pharisees kkewe ra pwan aeiineow sefaaeniy mwaaen we pwe, “Wo iura pwe iiy minne e aecchipwa oamw masparh — iwe meeta wopwe iura reen mmwenen?” Mwaaen we a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Iiy erhai profeta.”
JOH 9:18 Mwaaen kkewe soamwooniir Jews rese mwerhaen repwe niugiuniug pwe mwaaen we e masparh mwo nge igina a pwan ffat noa mesan, toori igiwe ra faingiir rhooawe inan me seman,
JOH 9:19 nge ra aeiineeor pwe, “Naimi mwaaen een? Oaw iura pwe esupwutiw nge eparh mesan; nge e ifa wusun rhag nge a ffat noa mesan?”
JOH 9:20 Rhooawe inan me seman ra iura pwe, “Aei giuneei pwe iiy naimaem, iwe nge aei giuneei pwe esupw nge eparh mesan.
JOH 9:21 Iwe nge aeise giuneei e ifa rhag wusun nge a ffat noa mesan, iwe nge aeise giuneei iyo e aeffeta noa mesan. Oaw aeiineow, pwe imwu a reepiy, iwe imwu epwene mmwenen aesefaaeni aeiineo mwu aaemi!”
JOH 9:22 Rhooa kkewe inan me seman re aepesa minneei pwe igiwe re mesagiiur rhooawe soamwoonin Jews, ikkiwe iir ra fasiun tipieew pwe erhai ne e iura pwe Jesus minne Kristus iwe nge repwe aerheei wow me noan wutteer Jews.
JOH 9:23 Ina faaen miniwe inan me seman re iura pwe, “A reepiy, oaw aeiineow!”
JOH 9:24 Pharisees kkewe a oaruwowwaen aar faingi mwaaen we eparh mesan nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Wopwe aekkepan faaen mesaen Deus pwe wopwe aepesa minna e wenewen! Aei giuneei pwe mwaaen e aecchipwoag nge erhai mwaaen monofit.”
JOH 9:25 Mwaaen we a iura pwe, “Ngaang ise giuneei aere erhai mwaaen monofit aere saapw. Nge eew minne i giuneei: eparh mwo mesaei nge igina nge a ffat noa.”
JOH 9:26 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Meeta minne efeeori ngaeniug? E ifa wusun aan aeffeta noa mesoamw?”
JOH 9:27 A paniuwaeniir pwe, “Iya moannon aengaenigaemi, nge aaemi oawse aiussaening. Meeta faaen oawpwe pwan rongorong sefaaen ngaeni reen? Meeta, maeni faer aaemi mwo nge oaw mwerhaen pwe oawpwe no pwe naiun rhooan kkayeo?”
JOH 9:28 Ra kkepas aenneew ngaeni nge ra aengaeni pwe, “Een mini naiun aeremas we rhooan kkayeo; pwe aemaem nge naiun Moses rhooan kkayeo.
JOH 9:29 Aemaem aei giuneei pwe Deus e mwaenieniy ngaeni Moses; nge mwaaen na, aeise giuneei mwo nge igine e itto me ee!”
JOH 9:30 Mwaaen we a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Aeina mwo amwaraeran minna! Oawse giuneei iya iga e itto me ee, nge iiy e aeffeta noa mesaei!
JOH 9:31 Si giuneei pwe Deus ese aiussaening ngaeniir rhooa monofit; nge e aiussaening ngaeniir rhooakka re aesirowu iwe me refeeori minikkena aan mwerhaen.
JOH 9:32 Saengi rhag rhaepetaen faeinaengiy nge esaaen yor mwo erhai ne si rongorong pwe e aeffeta noa perhaen mesaen erhai e esupwuto nge e fasiun parh.
JOH 9:33 Aere igine mwaaeneei ese itto me reen Deus, nge esoapw mmwen ngaeni mwo nge eew minikka efeeori.”
JOH 9:34 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Wosupw nge woffooan tae noan monofit — iwe nge wa menaen pwe wopwe itto fenaiugimaem?” Iwe rhag nge re aerheei wow me noan wutteer Jews we.
JOH 9:35 Igiwe Jesus a rongorong pwe ra aerheei wow mwaaen we me noan wutteer Jews we, enoa rhuungi mwaaen we nge a aeiineow pwe, “Wo niugiuniug ngaeni mwaaen na Naiun Aeremas?”
JOH 9:36 Mwaaen we a paniuwaeni pwe, “Menap, aengaeniaei mwaaen e iiy, ina nge ipwe niugiuniug ngaeni!”
JOH 9:37 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Wa fasiun weri, pwe iiy minne e mwaenieniy ngaeniug igina.”
JOH 9:38 Iwe mwaaen we a foatotiw me mmwaen Jesus nge a aengaeni pwe, “Ngaang i niugiuniug, Soamwoon!” iwe a foatotiw weni mmwaen Jesus.
JOH 9:39 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ngaang i ittiw noan faeinaengiy pwe ipwe ittiw aettiweginiy wunuunuur aeremas, pwe rhooakka reparh repwe ffat noa, iwe nge rhooakka reffat repwe parh noa.”
JOH 9:40 Aaemweoi Pharisees kkewe reno reen nge re rongorong aan aepesa minneei, nge ra aeiineow pwe, “Wo iura pwe aemaem mwo nge aeipwan masparh?”
JOH 9:41 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ngaere igine oawparh, ina nge oawse no noan monofit, nge igomwu oaw iura pwe oawffat ina nge aaemi oawno noan monofit.”
JOH 10:1 Jesus a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: mwaaen na ese toonong me noan aesemaen gurun sheep we pwe etonong me eew pwiuneoi, nge iiy erhai maan mwoarho me esooaw piraf.
JOH 10:2 Aeremas na etonong me noan aesemaen gurun sheep we nge ina rhooan neginegin sheep kkewe.
JOH 10:3 Rhooan poosun guruwe epwe sugi ngaeni asam, nge iir sheep kkewe repwe rongorong mwaeniaen igine epwe faingi iteer nge a wummwuur wow niugiun.
JOH 10:4 Igiwe a paeniir wow, nge ina epwe gommw memmweer, nge sheep kkewe ra tapweei mwirin pwe iga ra aeginna mwaenian.
JOH 10:5 Esooar erhai ne repwe tapweei; pwe repwe faer fattapw saengi aeremas we, pwe iga rese aeginna ttigin mwaenian.”
JOH 10:6 Jesus a fioangei ngaeniir fioangon awewe eei, nge iir rese metefaaegini faan.
JOH 10:7 Jesus a pwan aengaeniir pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen, pwe ngaang minne aesemeer sheep kkewe.
JOH 10:8 Oanongeer rhooa kkewe regommwoto me mmwaei nge iir maan mwoarho me soaw piraf, pwe sheep kkewe rese rongorong mwaenieer.
JOH 10:9 Ngaang minne asam. Iyo kka re itto toonong me reei nge repwe menaw; repwe itto toonong nge retowow nge repwe rhurhu mwongo.
JOH 10:10 Maan mwoarho we ina e itto rhag pwe epwe mwoarho me nni me oatoaropa. Ngaang itto pwe aegin oawpwe menaw — ina menaw na oarosaen mwamwaai.
JOH 10:11 “Ngaang rhooan neginegin sheep kkewe e mwamwaai, iwe i mwerhaen mae noa faaen iteer sheep kkewe.
JOH 10:12 Mwaaen we refang paniuwan pwe rhooai neginegiir sheep kkewe, nge iir sheep kkewe nge saapw pwan naiun. Epwe weri rhag itton erhai wolf nge epwe fattapw saengiir sheep kkewe; iwe wolf we a itto niir nge re peraseras noa.
JOH 10:13 Mwaaen we refang rhag paniuwaen pwe rhooan neginegin sheep kkewe, ina e fattapw noa pwe iga ese tepaar sheep kkewe pwe saapw naiun.
JOH 10:14 Ngaang rhooan neginegin sheep kkewe e mwamwaai. Mwaaen na Semaei e giuneaei nge ngaang i giuneei mwaaen na Semaei, ina epwan ina wusun pwe ngaang i giuneer naeyi sheep nge sheep kka naeyi repwan giuneaei. Ngaang ipwe fangenoa menewaei faaen iteer.
JOH 10:16 Epwan no aekkaerhai sheep ikka naeyi iga re soano noan guru eei. Ipwan pwigiir to, nge iir repwe rongorong mwaeniaei nge ra itto no pwe eew cchon sheep, nge erhai rhag rhooai neginegiir.
JOH 10:17 “Mwaaen na Semaei e aerhaengiaei pwe iga i mwerhaen fangenoa menewaei, pwe ipwe mmwenen pwan pwigi sefaaeniy.
JOH 10:18 Esooar ne epwe pwigi saengiaei menewaei. Ngaang minne ipwe sipegin fangenoa. Eyor maemaewaei aaei ipwe sipegin fangenoa, nge eyor maemaewaei aaei ipwe pwan pwigi sefaaeniy. Ieei minne mwaaen na Semaei e ammwir ngaeniaei pwe ipwe feeori.”
JOH 10:19 Iwe a pwan yor ginigin nepeteer aeremas pwe reen kkepas kkeei.
JOH 10:20 E towunap rhooakka re iura pwe, “Eyor mwuniaan wooan! A mmang noa! Meeta oaw rhiuwen aiussaening ngaeni reen?”
JOH 10:21 Nge aekkaaemweoi re iura pwe, “Mwaaen eyor mwuniaan wooan nge ese mmwen epwe ieen wusun mwaenian! Epwe ifa wusun aaen mwuniaan aeffeta noa meseer rhooa parh?”
JOH 10:22 A oaton nefaeng, nge a toori oaton gupwunon oatonongon Temple we me Jerusalem.
JOH 10:23 Jesus e faaeraeg fetaen faaen pweranta we regaen iura pwe Pwerantaen Solomon me reen Temple we,
JOH 10:24 iwe aeremas ra maegeto reen ra aeiineow pwe, “Epwe ifa ssiunaein oamw aeppaeti fetaenegemaem? Aengaenigemaem minna wenewenen: aere een minne Kristus?”
JOH 10:25 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ngaang iya fasiun aengaenigaemi, nge aaemi oawse niugiuniug ngaeniaei. Minikka igaen feeori reen maemaewaen minna Semaei ina egaen pwaeritae mmwenei;
JOH 10:26 nge aaemi oawse niugiuniug, pwe iga aaemi saapw aaemi naeyi sheep.
JOH 10:27 Sheep kka naeyi re aiussaening ngaeni minikka mwaeniaei; ngaang i giuneer nge iir re tapweaei.
JOH 10:28 I ngaenneer menaw na esooar ssiaaenin nge esooar faaen eew ne repwe mae. Esooar erhai ne epwe mmwenen torofiir saengiaei.
JOH 10:29 Meeta na manna Semaei e ngaenneaei, ina e taegias saengi oanongaen aegiaeg, nge esooar erhai ne emmwenen epwe torofiir noa me noan paiun manna Semaei.
JOH 10:30 Manna Semaei me ngaang nge aei eew rhag.”
JOH 10:31 Iwe rhag nge aeremas ra pwan pweipwog faai pwe repwe tera.
JOH 10:32 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “E igin ssow min mwamwaai kka i itto feeori me weni mmwaemi iga manna Semaei efang ngaeniaei pwe ipwe feeori; ifa me neeiin minikkaan minne oaw tipaeni pwe oawpwe terayaei reen?”
JOH 10:33 Ra iura pwe, “Aeise mwerhaen aeipwe teroag reen mini mwamwaai kka wofeeori, pwe faer reen oamw fioang aenneewa Deus! Een rhag erhai aeremas nge wa itto feeoriug noa pwe een Deus!”
JOH 10:34 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Effoat noan oasoapwosoapw we aaemi pwe Deus e iura pwe, ‘Aaemi minikka deus.’
JOH 10:35 Si giuneei pwe minna Pwapwior we e Santus e iura nge ennet nge esooar iaenin; iwe Deus e faingiir aeremas kenaan pwe iir deus, aeremas kenaan nge ikkina aeremas kkewe efang mwaenian ngaeniir.
JOH 10:36 Iwe nge ngaang, manna Semaei minne e finiaei iwe a fangeto ngaang noan faeinaengiy. Iwe epwe ifa wusun rhag oawwa mmwenen iura pwe i fioang aenneewa Deus iga iura pwe ngaang Naiun Deus?
JOH 10:37 Aere ise feeorin minikkena minna Semaei e mwerhaen ipwe feeori, iwe ina nge oawsoapw niugiuniug ngaeniaei.
JOH 10:38 Nge aere ifeeorin, nge inamwo oawse niugiuniug ngaeniaei, ina nge engaang kka aaei mwo nge oawpwe niugiuniug ngaeni, pwe aegin oawpwe giuneei gacchiuw pwe minna Semaei eno reei nge ino reen minna Semaei.”
JOH 10:39 Ra pwan aegina aar repwe torofi Jesus, nge ennus noa me noan paiiur.
JOH 10:40 Jesus a pwan sefaaen noa noan pwupwu we Jordan, pwiuneoi we e paptismus John me ee, iwe a noa no ee.
JOH 10:41 Re towunap aeremas ra itto reen, ra iura pwe, “John esooar aeginn ne egaen feeori, iwe oanongaen minikka e aepesa pwe kkepesaen mwaaen een nge ennet.”
JOH 10:42 Iwe re towunap aeremas kkewe reno igiwe ra niugiuniug ngaeni.
JOH 11:1 Erhai mwaaen itan Lazarus iwe eno Bethany a semwaai noa. Bethany itaen eew aepinoamw iwe Maria we pwiin Martha re nonno ee. (
JOH 11:2 Ieen iiy Maria we e aekkitiw neoningas wooan pirheen Soamwoon nge a toafi noa chogin reen aennirhimwen; nge man semwaai we Lazarus nge mwengeyan.)
JOH 11:3 Rhooapwut pwipwi kkewe ra fangenoa eew kkepas reen Jesus nge re iura pwe, “Soamwoon, maereyaer aecchaeng we oamw iye a semwaai.”
JOH 11:4 Igiwe Jesus a rongorong miniwe nge a iura pwe, “Amwiucchiunoan semwaai een nge saapw reen maenoan Lazarus; minneei nge a wen pwe epwe pwaeri noa minna nningen Deus, pwe ina nge mwaaen na Naiun Deus epwe yo ngaeni minna nningen.”
JOH 11:5 Jesus e aerhaengi Martha me miniwe pwiin me Lazarus.
JOH 11:6 Igiwe e itto kkepas we reen Jesus pwe Lazarus a semwaai, iwe a pwan no aegini mwo riiuraaen.
JOH 11:7 Iwe a aengaeni rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun pwe, “Sa pwan sefaaen noa Judea.”
JOH 11:8 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Sinsei, esaaen ssiunaei mwo aar aeremesaen iginaan menaen repwe teroag, nge wa pwan mwerhaen sefaaen noa?”
JOH 11:9 Jesus a iura pwe, “Eraaen nge seig me ruwowu awa noan, aere? Iwe rhooakkena re faaeraeg noan seremaen raaen ina resoapw toroppiung, pwe ra weri minna seremaen faeinaengiy.
JOH 11:10 Iwe nge aere re faaeraeg nee pwoong nge repwe toroppiung, pwe esooar seram.”
JOH 11:11 Jesus e aepesa miniwe nge a pwan iura pwe, “Lazarus we maereyaererh nge a maiur noa, ipwene noa pwe ipwe noa faingitae.”
JOH 11:12 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra iura pwe, “Soamwoon, ngaere igine e maiur, nge iiy ina epwe cchipw sefaaen noa.”
JOH 11:13 Jesus e aengaeniir pwe Lazarus a maenoa, nge iir re maengiy pwe e kkepesaen aan maiur.
JOH 11:14 Iwe Jesus a aeffeta ngaeniir pwe, “Lazarus a mae,
JOH 11:15 nge aegin aaemi minne egacch tipaei iga ise no reen Lazarus, pwe aaemi oawpwe niugiuniug. Sa noa reen.”
JOH 11:16 Thomas (iwe repwan gaen iura pwe Nippwei) a aengaeniir rhooa kkayeo kkewe aaemweoi pwe, “Oawsa tapweei noa Sinsei pwe sipwe noa rhag mae nong wooan!”
JOH 11:17 Igiwe enoa tooto Jesus a itto weri pwe a fapwoong mwirin aan nipwaenipw noa Lazarus.
JOH 11:18 Bethany nge ese yo mwo nge ruwowu miles saengi Jerusalem,
JOH 11:19 iwe nge re igin towunap re Judea rhooan itto emwaeriir Maria me Martha reen maen mwaaen we mwengeyeer.
JOH 11:20 Igiwe Martha a rongorong pwe Jesus a itto, a itiwow pwe a itiwow rhuungi, nge Maria eno rhag nee iimw.
JOH 11:21 Martha a aengaeni Jesus pwe, “Soamwoon, aere igine wono igeei nge mwaaen e mwengeaei esoapw mae!
JOH 11:22 Nge i giuneei pwe igina mwo nge Deus epwe ngaenneog ese tiwegin minne wo tingoareei.”
JOH 11:23 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Mwaaen mwu mwengeyoamw epwe menaw sefaaen tae.”
JOH 11:24 Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Ngaang i giuneei pwe wooan minna oarosaen raaen nge epwe menaw sefaaen tae.”
JOH 11:25 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Ngaang minne menaw sefaaen me menaw. Iyo kka re niugiuniug ngaeniaei nge repwe menaw, inamwo igine ra mae noa;
JOH 11:26 iwe iyo kka re menaw nge re niugiuniug ngaeniaei nge esooar faaen eew ne repwe mae. Wo niugiuniug ngaeni minneei?”
JOH 11:27 Rhooapwut we a iura pwe, “Ooa, Soamwoon! Ngaang i niugiuniug pwe een Kristus iwe Naiun Deus iwe epwe itto noan faeinaengiy.”
JOH 11:28 Mwirin aaen Martha aepesa minneei, a sefaaen a noa faingi mwoanomwoanei Maria we pwiin. A aengaeni pwe, “Sinsei a no igeei, iwe nge e aekkaeyiyeg een.”
JOH 11:29 Igiwe Maria e rongorong miniwe, a iutae rhag nge a gucchuwow reen Jesus. (
JOH 11:30 Jesus esaaen toori mwo aepinoamw we, pwe e rhiuwen no igiwe Martha e rhuungi me ee.)
JOH 11:31 Rhooawe reno reen Maria noan iimw we ra pwan tapweei wow igiwe e iutae pwe epwene noa. Re niuwaennei pwe epwene noa reen paeyi we pwe epwe noa saeng me ee.
JOH 11:32 Maria enoa tooto igiwe Jesus eno ee, igiwe rhag eweri, nge e foatotiw me weni mmwan a aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, aere igine wo fasiun no igeei nge mwaaen we mwengeaei esoapw mae!”
JOH 11:33 Jesus eweri aan saeng, me pwan aeremas kkewe repwan tapweeito aar pwan saeng; iwe a gin tiwto waeiraesiy nee tipan me aenneewaen nee rhiun.
JOH 11:34 A aeiineeor pwe, “Iya iga oaw paeia me iya?” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, itto wopwe noa weri.”
JOH 11:35 Jesus a saeng.
JOH 11:36 Aeremas kkewe ra iura pwe, “Oawweri nepaen aan aerhaengi!”
JOH 11:37 Aaemweoi ra iura pwe, “Iiy miniwe e aeffeta noa mesaen erhai masparh, aere? Esoapw mmwen aan epwe feeori pwe esoapw mae Lazarus?”
JOH 11:38 A pwan gin tiwto aenneewaen nee tipaen Jesus, igiwe a noa reen paeyi we, iwe eew ngat me peigin eew rhug, iwe eno eew fai temoag reen asaeman.
JOH 11:39 Jesus a akkiuneeor pwe, “Peniy noa fai mwu!” Martha iwe mwengeyaen mwaaen we a mae a iura pwe, “Soamwoon, epwene aenneew pwoon, pwe a fapwoong pwongin aan nipwaenipw noa!”
JOH 11:40 Jesus aengaeni pwe, “Isaaen aengaeniug pwe wopwe weri minna nningen Deus igine wo niugiuniug?”
JOH 11:41 Ra peniy noa fai we. Jesus a fattae naaeng nge a iura pwe, “Wa aerhigerhig Semaei, reen oamw aiussaening mwaeniaei.
JOH 11:42 I giuneei pwe wogaen aiussaening ngaeniaei rhag, nge i aepesa minneei pwe aegiir aeremas kka igeei, pwe repwe niugiuniug pwe een minne wofangeto ngaang.”
JOH 11:43 Mwirin aan aepesa minneei nge a kkepas temoag noa, “Lazarus, toowow!”
JOH 11:44 A toowow, nge e rhiuwen tiugiutiug noa rhag paiun me pirheen reen mengaag iwe epwan yor mengaag tiugiutiug ngaeni mesan. Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw pwaeisi noa nge oawwa nigiti noa.”
JOH 11:45 Towunepeer rhooawe re itto reen Maria ra weri meeta we Jesus efeeori, iwe ra niugiuniug ngaeni.
JOH 11:46 Iwe nge aekkaerhai iir ra noa ngaeniir Pharisees kkewe iwe ra aengaeniir meeta kkewe Jesus efeeori.
JOH 11:47 Iwe Pharisees me soamwooniir patere kkewe ra rhungaeni council we iwe ra iura pwe, “Meeta sipwene feeori? Oaw pipiiy oanongaen kkeman kka mwaaeneei a feeorin!
JOH 11:48 Ngaere igine sipwe nigiti noa rhag pwe epwe ieei wusun, oanongeer aeremas nge repwene niugiuniug ngaeni, nge manekka soamwoonin Rome repwe itto fereei noa Temple e aarh me minne faniuwarh!”
JOH 11:49 Erhai me neeiir itan Caiaphas, iiy miniwe Soamwoonin Patere noan raeg we, a iura pwe, “A inamwo pwurhomi!
JOH 11:50 Oawse giuneei pwe egacch ngaenigaemi igine erhai emae noa faaen iteer rhooa towunap, mmwaen igine oanongeer aeremas repwe toaroporop noa?”
JOH 11:51 Ese tipan rhag wooan oanongan pwe epwe aepesa minneei; pwe iga iiy miniwe Soamwoonin Patere noan raeg naan, iwe e aepesa pwe Jesus epwe mae noa faaen iteer re Jews,
JOH 11:52 nge saapw faaen iteer rhag, pwe pwan minni epwe oarhuur nong rhag noan eew tipieew oanongeer aeremas kka naiun Deus ikka re meganagan fetaen.
JOH 11:53 Saengi raaenin we a noa, soamwooniir Jews kkewe ra feeori noa aar niunniuwaen pwe repwe niiy noa Jesus.
JOH 11:54 Iwe Jesus esa pwaeri noano aan faaeraeg fetaen me wooan Judea, iwe a noa reen eew pwiuneoi iwe eno oaron desert we, reen eew aepinoamw itan Ephraim, a noa no ee iiy me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun.
JOH 11:55 Oaton gupwunon Passover we a arapeto, re towunap aeremesaen aepinoamw kkewe ra maegeto Jerusalem pwe repwe itto feeori engaengaen aenimenimen weni mmwaen gupwun we.
JOH 11:56 Ra kiukkiutta Jesus, nge igiwe ra rhu me noan Temple we ra aeiineo fengaen wooar pwe, “Meeta oaw maengiy? Ennetaen esoapw itto tapweei gupwun eei, aere?”
JOH 11:57 Soamwoonin patere me Pharisees kkewe ra fasiun aetiwenig ngaeniir aeremas pwe aere yor e eweri Jesus, nge a iura, pwe repwe noa torofi.
JOH 12:1 Wonowu raaen me weni mmwaen Passover, nge Jesus a noa Bethany, iwe pwugusaen Lazarus, mwaaen we e aemenewaetae me reen mae noa.
JOH 12:2 Ra oamoannatae eew mwongoon faaef pwe aan, iwe Martha a tipaengiir reen feeoriun; Lazarus iwe erhai mwaaen kkewe emooat reen Jesus reen table we.
JOH 12:3 Maria a pwigi eew neoningas e igin cchoaw paniuwaen a aekkitae wooan pirheen Jesus, iwe ooa toafi noa chogin pirheen reen aennirhimwen. Miniwe pwongesaen neowe a rheeoi noa noan iimw we.
JOH 12:4 Erhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun itan Judas Iscariot — mwaaen we epwe fangenoa tinnimaen — a iura pwe,
JOH 12:5 “Meeta rese chuwaiuw noa neoningas een reen eniupwiugiuw silver iwe nge ra ngaenneer man affayeo minna senaapian?”
JOH 12:6 E iura miniwe nge saapw iga e faayeeor man affayeo pwe iga iiy erhai man mwoarho. Iiy minne pweipwog tutuun senaapiy nge egaen piraf naiun senaapiy me reen.
JOH 12:7 Jesus a iura pwe, “Oawsoapw amwagiutiu, nigiti pwe epwe iseni meeta kkomwu aan pwe ammwenen raaenin na ipwe nipwaenipw noa reen.
JOH 12:8 Pwe rhooa affayeo repwe fasiun yor reemi oanongaen oat, nge ngaang isoapw no rhag reemi oanongaen oat.”
JOH 12:9 Re towunap aeremas ra rongorong pwe Jesus eno Bethany iwe ra noa igiwe, soapw pwonno rhag reen Jesus nge pwonno repwe pwan weri Lazarus, iwe Jesus e aemenewaetae me reen mae noa.
JOH 12:10 Iwe soamwoonin patere kkewe ra feeori noa aar niunniuwaen pwe repwe pwan niiy noa Lazarus,
JOH 12:11 pwonno reen Lazarus minne ra igin towunap Jews kka ra toagun saengiir ra noa niugiuniug ngaeni Jesus.
JOH 12:12 Mmasetaen iwe eraaen, eew pwuwa temoag a itto tapweei miniwe gupwunon Passover pwe ra rongorong pwe Jesus a itto noan Jerusalem.
JOH 12:13 Iwe ra pweipwog to paeneaei niu pwe repwene itiwow aewenimmwei Jesus, nge ra gaen aekkepwas pwe, “Aepingepinga Deus! Deus epwe aewenepwuwa aeremas na epwe itto faaen itaen Soamwoon! Deus epwe aewenepwuwa king na aar re Israel!”
JOH 12:14 Jesus enoa rhuungi erhai donkey a teeotae wooan, taeppen rhag miniwe Pwapwior we e Santus iwe e iura pwe,
JOH 12:15 “Wosoapw mesag, een aepinoamwon Zion! Emwaeri, a itto king we noawumw, iye e waawa erhai donkey mwittig.”
JOH 12:16 Noan oatowe nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun rese metefaaegini miniwe; nge oatowe enoa menaw sefaaen Jesus a ittiw noan nningen nge ra naaen maengiy pwe ina miniwe Pwapwior we e Santus e iura reen, nge e ina wusun miniwe refeeori ngaeni.
JOH 12:17 Rhooa kkewe reno reen Jesus oatowe e faingiwow Lazarus me noan miniwe paeian nge a aemenewa sefaaeniy tae iwe ra aepesa fetaeneei miniwe a wen.
JOH 12:18 Ina faaen miniwe pwuwa we a itiwow rhungaeni pwe iga ra rongorong wunuunun kkeman we efeeori.
JOH 12:19 Iwe Pharisees kkewe ra iura fengaenniy wooar pwe, “Oawwa weri pwe esooar mwo nge eew meeta ne emmwen ngaenigirh! Oaw pipiiy, oanongaen faeinaengiy nge a tapweei!”
JOH 12:20 Aaemweoi re Greeks reno neeiir rhooawe renoa Jerusalem repwe noa maeipin oaton gupwunon Passover.
JOH 12:21 Ra noa reen Philip (erhai re Bethsaida e nonno Galilee), iwe ra aengaeni pwe, “Menap, aei mwerhaen rhuungi Jesus.”
JOH 12:22 Philip a noa a aengaeni Andrew, iwe iir ra noa aengaeni Jesus.
JOH 12:23 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Awa we iye a itto igina pwe miniwe Naiun Aeremas epwene pwae noa minna nningen.
JOH 12:24 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: ngaere efai faiun wheat ese ppiungtiw nee ppweon nge a mae noa, nge epwe no rhag pwe efai faiun. Iwe ngaere epwe mae noa ina nge epwe towunap uwaan.
JOH 12:25 Rhooakka re aerhaengi meneweer nge epwe ppiung saengiir, nge rhooakka rese aerhaengi meneweer me noan faeinaengiy ina epwe yo ngaeniir menaw na esooar iaenin.
JOH 12:26 Iyo na e mwerhaen epwe engaang ngaeniaei epwe tapweaei, pwene naeyi rhooan engaang epwe no reei iga ino ee. Iwe nge minna Semaei epwe fang ssoar ngaeniir ikkina re engaang ngaeniaei.
JOH 12:27 “Igina a waeiraes nee tipaei — meeta ipwe iura? Ipwe iura pwe, ‘Semaei, wosoapw aefengato oaton eei wooai?’ Nge ina rhag ina faaen aaei itto, pwe ipwe toonong noan oaton affayeo eei.
JOH 12:28 Semaei, pwaeri noa nningen minna itoamw!” Nge eew mangiungiu a ittiw naaeng, “Iya fasiun pwaeri noa nningen, nge ipwe rhiuwen feeori sefaaeniy.”
JOH 12:29 Pwuwa we re iu igiwe re rongorong mangiungiu we, nge aaemweoi ra iura pwe pacch, aaemweoi re iura pwe, “Erhai angkenus minne e mwaenieniy ngaeni!”
JOH 12:30 Iwe nge Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Saapw aegin ngaang minne mangiungiu naan ittiw me noan naaeng reen, pwe aegin aaemi.
JOH 12:31 Igina a itto oatowe faeinaengiy epwene apwiung; nge igina mwaaen e soamwoonin faeinaengiy epwene asiuw me wooan nenien.
JOH 12:32 Aere iya aetaegiasaetae saengi faeinaengiy, nge ipwene pwigiir to oanongeer aeremas reei.” (
JOH 12:33 Noan aan aepesa minneei, nge a aepesa wunuunun mae na epwe aeni.)
JOH 12:34 Pwuwa we a iura pwe, “Aemaem anniug e aengaenigemaem pwe Kristus epwe menaw foarhofoarh. Epwe ifa wusun oamw iura pwe mwaaen na Naiun Aeremas epwe aetaegiasaetae? Iyo iiy minne Naiun Aeremas?”
JOH 12:35 Jesus a iura pwe, “Iiy seram we epwe no faeiyegius fetaen mwo neeimi. Oaw soapwei noa aaemi faaeraeg iga seram e rhiuwen no reemi, pwe roorh ete gonaegaemi; pwe erhai ne e faaeraeg nee roorh nge esoapw giuneei igine e faaeraeg noa ee.
JOH 12:36 Iwe oawpwe niugiuniug ngaeni seram naan, noan faei oaton aan no reemi, pwe aaemi oawpwe no pwe aeremesaen ne seram.” Mwirin aaen Jesus aepesa minneei, a nigitiir pwe a noa wop saengiir.
JOH 12:37 Inamwo igiwe a feeori oanongaen kkeman kkeei me weni mmweer, nge rese niugiuniug ngaeni,
JOH 12:38 pwe aegin miniwe mwaeniaen profeta Isaiah epwe pwae noa iwe e iura pwe, “Soamwoon, iyo e niugiuniug ngaeni kkepas we aeiya aepesa? Nge iyo na Soamwoon e pwaeri ngaeni minna maemaewan?”
JOH 12:39 Iwe rese mmwenen niugiuniug, pwe igiwe Isaiah epwan iura pwe,
JOH 12:40 “Deus a aeperha noa meseer nge a oarorha noa noan tipeer, pwonno meseer ete weriwer nge nee tipeer ese metaf, nge resoapw toagun ngaeniaei, aaen kkepas Deus, nge ngaang ipwe aemaemaewaar tae.”
JOH 12:41 Isaiah e aepesa minneei pwe igiwe a weri minna nningen Jesus iwe a fioangei kkepesan.
JOH 12:42 Oateen mwo nge re towunap soamwooniir Jews ra niugiuniug ngaeni Jesus; nge pwonno reer Pharisees kkewe minne esooar minne re aepesa, pwe rete aerheer wow me noan wutteer Jews.
JOH 12:43 Re aerhaengi pwe aeremas repwe aepingepingaar mmwaen aaen Deus epwe aepingepingaar.
JOH 12:44 Jesus a kkepas temoag tae nge a iura pwe, “Iyo na e niugiuniug ngaeniaei nge ese niugiuniug ngaeniaei rhag, pwe pwan iyo na efangeto ngaang.
JOH 12:45 Nge iyo na eweriaei nge epwan weri iyo na efangeto ngaang.
JOH 12:46 Ngaang itto noan faeinaengiy pwe eew seram, pwe iyo na e niugiuniug ngaeniaei esoapw no noan rorhappiung.
JOH 12:47 Rhooakka re rongorong mwaeniaei nge rese tapweei, isoapw apwiungiiur. Ngaang ise itto ipwe itto apwiungiu faeinaengiy, pwe itto pwe ipwe aemenewa.
JOH 12:48 Iyo kena rese aetiwaeyaei nge rese aetiwa mwaeniaei nge eno erhai ina epwe itto apwiungiiur. Iir ina repwe apwiung reen minikka petenaen mwaeniaei wooan minna oarosaen raaen!
JOH 12:49 Wenewenen minikkeei, pwe saapw tipaei rhag wooan oanongaei, pwe mwaeniaen minna Semaei ina efangeto ngaang, nge e ammwir ngaeniaei meeta ipwe iura me aepesa.
JOH 12:50 Nge ngaang i giuneei, pwe oasoapwosoapw e aan epwe pwigito menaw na esooar iaenin. Iwe meeta i iura nge ina minna manna Semaei e aengaeniaei pwe ipwe iura.”
JOH 13:1 Igina nge a eraaen me weni mmwaen miniwe gupwunon Passover. Jesus a giuneei pwe a itto oaton aan epwene nigiti faeinaengiy pwe epwene noa reen miniwe Seman. Iiy e fasiun gin aerhaengiir rhooakka noan faeinaengiy ikka naiun, nge e aerhaengiir toori noa amwiucchiun aan menaw.
JOH 13:2 Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra mwongoon faaef. Nge Saetan a fasiun iseni nong nee tipaen Judas, mwaaen we naiun Simon Iscariot, pwe epwe fangenoa tinnimaen Jesus.
JOH 13:3 Jesus e giuneei pwe mwaaen we Seman nge efang ngaeni oanongaen mamaaw; e giuneei pwe iiy e itto me reen Deus nge epwene sefaaen ngaeni Deus.
JOH 13:4 Iwe a iutae me reen table we, a iseni tiw mengaagiun niugiun, nge a geonitae eew toawun nugunupan.
JOH 13:5 Iwe a aekkinong rhaan noan eew saepiy nge a rhaepetae aan toafi pirheer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun, nge e aepaena ngaeni toawun we e geeogeeo nugunupan.
JOH 13:6 A itto reen Simon Peter, nge Peter a aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, wopwe toafi pirheei?”
JOH 13:7 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Igina wose metefaaegini minne ifeeori, nge faeiyegius noa nge wopwe naaen metaf.”
JOH 13:8 Peter a iura pwe, “Esooar faaen eew ne wopwe toafi pirheei!” Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Aere igine ise toafi pirhemw nge wosoapw nono pwe een naeyi rhooan kkayeo.”
JOH 13:9 Simon Peter a aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, ina nge saapw pirheei rhag minne wopwe toafi! Wopwe pwan toafi paeyi me rhimwei!”
JOH 13:10 Jesus a iura pwe, “Rhooakka ra tiutiu nge a nimegacch noa wooar, nge resoapw tiutiu no pwe pirheer rhag epwe tiutiu. Oanongaemi nge oawwa aenimenim — nge erhai rhag ese aenimenim.” (
JOH 13:11 Jesus a fasiun giuneei iyo epwene fangenoa tinnimaen; ina faaen miniwe e iura pwe, “Oanongaemi nge oawwa aenimenim — nge erhai rhag ese aenimenim.”)
JOH 13:12 Weni mwirin aaen Jesus toafi pirheer, a iseni sefaaen tae minikkewe mengaagiun nge a noa mooat sefaaen tiw reen table we. A iura pwe, “Oaw metaf reen miniwe ifeeori ngaenigaemi?
JOH 13:13 Oaw faingi ngaeniaei pwe Sinsei me Soamwoon, nge efin pwe oawpwe ina wusun ngaeniaei, pwe iga ina minna ngaang.
JOH 13:14 Ngaang, aaemi Soamwoon me Sinsei, nge iya toafi pirhemi. Iwe nge aaemi oawpwan toafi pirheen erhai me erhai me neeimi.
JOH 13:15 I aweri ngaenigaemi minneen pwe oawpwe giuneei, pwe oawpwe feeori wunuunun meeta we ifeeori ngaenigaemi.
JOH 13:16 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: esooar slave ne e taegias saengi aan maasta, nge esooar rhooan pweipwogin kkepas ne e taegias saengi iyo na e akkiuneo.
JOH 13:17 Iga oawwa giuneei minneei, ifa mwo aaemi kker igine oawpwene noa pomwoni!
JOH 13:18 “Ngaang ise kkepas reemi oanongaemi; i giuneer iyo kka i finiir. Iwe nge miniwe mwaeniaen Pwapwior we e Santus epwe pwae noa iwe e iura pwe, ‘Mwaaen we e mwongo reei a appaniuwaeniaei.’
JOH 13:19 Igina i aengaenigaemi minneei weni mmwaen epwe wen, pwe epwe noa wen nge oaw niugiuniug pwe, ‘Ngaang ina ngaang.’
JOH 13:20 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: iyo e aetiwa iiy iwe i aefenga e aetiwaeyaei; nge iyo e aetiwaeyaei epwan aetiwa iyo na efangeto ngaang.”
JOH 13:21 Weni mwirin aaen Jesus aepesa minneei a igin cchoaw nee tipan iwe a iura pwe, “Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen, pwe erhai me neeimi epwene fangenoa tinnimaei.”
JOH 13:22 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra wegitaeg fengaen wooar pwe resa metaf reen miniwe e iura.
JOH 13:23 Erhai me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe, mwaaen we Jesus e igin aerhaengi, iwe emooat oaron Jesus.
JOH 13:24 Simon Peter a cchimw ngaeni nge a iura pwe, “Aeiineow ngaere iyo mwu e iyaekkepesa?”
JOH 13:25 Iwe rhooan kkayeo we e aeppwaenaeg ngaeni Jesus nge a aeiineow pwe, “Soamwoon, iyo na?”
JOH 13:26 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ieei ipwene rhirinong fenoawa een nge iya ngaenneei; nge ina manna iiy.” Iwe a rhirinong fenoawa we nge ngaenneei Judas we naiun Simon Iscariot.
JOH 13:27 Igiwe rhag Judas e pwigi fenoawa we nge Saetan a toonong noan pwunnon. Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Mwetekkaei, wonoa feeori minna wopwe feeori!”
JOH 13:28 Esooar erhai neeiir rhooawe oaron table we ne e metefaaegini faaen miniwe Jesus e aengaeni.
JOH 13:29 Iwe nge pwonno igiwe Judas miniwe rhooan pweipwogin tutuun senaapiy, aaemweoi rhooan kkayeo kkewe re niuwaennei pwe Jesus e aengaeni pwe epwe noa a noa chuwaiuw aemwetaen gupwun we, aere ngaenneer rhooa affayeo eew aegiaeg.
JOH 13:30 Judas e pwigi rhag fenoawa we nge a noa. A nee pwoong miniwe.
JOH 13:31 Mwirin aaen Judas noa nge Jesus a iura pwe, “Igina epwene pwae noa nningen mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas; nge minna nningen Deus ina epwene pwae noa pwe aegin iiy.
JOH 13:32 Iwe ngaere minna nningen Deus epwaetae me reen, iwe Deus wooan oanongan epwe pwan pwaeritae nningen mwaaen we Naiun Aeremas, nge epwe feeori igina rhag.
JOH 13:33 Aaemi naeyi, a egius mmwaai rhag nge ipwene nigitigaemi. Oawpwene giuttayaei; iwe nge igina ipwene aengaenigaemi miniwe i aengaeniir soamwoonin Jews, ‘Oawsoapw mmwenen noa iga ipwene noa ee.’
JOH 13:34 Iwe igina ipwene ngaennegaemi eew anniug ffeo: oaw aerhaengi fengaennigaemi. Taeppen rhag aaei aerhaengigaemi, iwe aaemi oawpwe aerhaengi fengaennigaemi.
JOH 13:35 Aere igine oaw aerhaengi fengaennigaemi, ina nge oanongeer aeremas repwe giuneei pwe aaemi minikkewe naeyi rhooan kkayeo.”
JOH 13:36 Simon Peter a aeiineow pwe, “Soamwoon, wopwene noa iya?” Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Wosoapw mmwenen tapweaei noa igina ngaang ipwe noa ee, epwe mwirin noa nge oawpwapw tapweto mwiriy.”
JOH 13:37 Peter a aeiineow pwe, “Soamwoon, meeta isoapw mmwenen tapweog noa iginaan reen? Ngaang iya moannotae pwe ipwe mae noa faaen itoamw!”
JOH 13:38 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Wa moannotae pwe wopwe mae noa faaen itaei? Ennetaen, ipwe aengaeniug minna wenewenen, pwe weni mmwaen aan epwe keokkeok maniug nge epwe faaen enuuw oamw iura pwe wose giuneaei.”
JOH 14:1 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oawsoapw aiuraeg. Oaw niugiuniug ngaeni Deus nge oawpwan niugiuniug ngaeniaei.
JOH 14:2 Egin towunap neniy me noan iimw na imwaen manna Semaei, nge ipwene noa oamoannatae neniemi me ee. Aere ese nnet minneei nge isoapw aengaenigaemi.
JOH 14:3 Epwe weni mwirin aaei noa oamoannatae minna neniemi, nge iya sefaaen pwe ipwe itto pwigigaemi, pwe oawpwe noano pwiuneoi na ngaang ino ee.
JOH 14:4 Oaw giuneei ennap na epwe noa reen pwiuneoi na ipwe noa ee.”
JOH 14:5 Thomas a aengaeni pwe, “Aemaem aeise giuneei igomwu wopwe noa ee; iwe epwe ifa wusun nge aeipwe giuneei minna ennepan?”
JOH 14:6 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaang minne ennap me ennet me menaw; esooar ne enoa reen minna Semaei igine ese sefaaen me reei.
JOH 14:7 Igina iga oawwa giuneaei, oawpwene pwan giuneei manna Semaei, iwe saengi igina a noa, oawwa giuneei iwe me oawwa weri iiy iyo.”
JOH 14:8 Philip a aengaeni pwe, “Pwaeri ngaenigemaem manna Semoamw, ina rhag aemaem mwerhaen.”
JOH 14:9 Jesus a iura pwe, “A igin ssiunaei aaei no reemi oanongaemi; iwe nge een Philip wosaen pwan giuneaei mwo? Mane a weriaei nge ina nge a pwan weri manna Semaei, nge meeta wo iura pwe, ‘Pwaerito remaem manna Semoamw’?
JOH 14:10 Wosaen niugiuniug mwo pwe ngaang ino reen manna Semaei nge manna Semaei eno reei? Petenaen kkepas kkewe i aengaenigaemi nge ese itto me reei. Pwe manna Semaei ina eno reei, ina efeeori aan engaang.
JOH 14:11 Oaw niugiuniug ngaeniaei reen ikka i aepesa pwe ngaang ino reen manna Semaei nge manna Semaei eno reei. Ngaere oawse niugiuniug ngaeni ina, ina nge oaw niugiuniug ngaeni minikkewe ifeeori.
JOH 14:12 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: iyo kena re niugiuniug ngaeniaei ina repwe feeori minikkena ifeeori — ooa, epwe faer tettemoag minikka iir repwe feeori pwe, iga ngaang ipwene noa reen manna Semaei.
JOH 14:13 Nge ese tiwegin meeta kka oawpwe tingoar faaen itaei nge ipwe feeori, pwonno nningen Semaei epwe pwae noa me reen minna Naiun.
JOH 14:14 Ina ngaere oaw tingoar pwe ipwe feeori eew meeta, nge ipwe feeori.
JOH 14:15 “Aere oaw aerhaengiaei, oawpwe tapweei oasoapwosoapw kka aaei.
JOH 14:16 Ipwe tingoareei manna Semaei, nge ina epwe ngaennegaemi erhai pwe Rhooan Tipaengigaemi, nge epwe no reemi e esooar iaenin.
JOH 14:17 Ina manna Espritu, ina epwe pwaeri minikkena e wenewen pwe wunuunun Deus. Aeremesaen faeinaengiy ese mmwen epwe aetiwa, pwe iga ese weri me iga ese giuneei. Iwe nge aaemi oaw giuneei, pwe iga eno reemi nge eno neeimi.
JOH 14:18 “Aere ipwene noa, nge esoapw aaemi noa rhag; pwe ipwe sefaaen to reemi.
JOH 14:19 A egius rhag nge faeinaengiy esoapw rhiuwen weriaei no, nge aaemi oawpwe weriaei; pwe iga ngaang i menaw iwe aaemi oawpwan menaw.
JOH 14:20 Epwe noa itto raaenin naan, oawpwene giuneei pwe ngaang ino reen manna Semaei nge aaemi oawno reei, taeppen rhag iga ngaang ino reemi.
JOH 14:21 “Rhooakka eno oasoapwosoapw e aaei reer nge re tapweei, ikkina rhooakkena re aerhaengiaei. Semaei e aerhaengiir rhooakkena re aerhaengiaei; ngaang ipwan aerhaengiir nge ipwe pwan pwae ngaeniir.”
JOH 14:22 Judas (saapw Judas we Iscariot) a iura pwe, “Soamwoon, epwe ifa wusun oamw wopwe pwae ngaenigemaem nge wosoapw pwae ngaeni faeinaengiy?”
JOH 14:23 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Rhooakka re aerhaengiaei nge repwe tapweei aaei fenai. Semaei epwe aerhaengiir, nge Semaei me ngaang aeipwe itto aeiya itto no reer.
JOH 14:24 Rhooakkena rese aerhaengiaei ina resoapw tapweei aaei fenai. Iwe fenai kkewe oawwa rongorong ikkina saapw aaei, pwe e itto me reen manna Semaei iwe efangeto ngaang.
JOH 14:25 “I aengaenigaemi minikkeei iga i rhiuwen no reemi.
JOH 14:26 Manna Rhooan Tipaengigaemi, ina Espritu Santus ina manna Semaei efangeto faaen itaei, pwe epwe itto kapwiung ngaenigaemi oanongaen meeta, pwe oawpwe maengiy oanongaen meeta kkewe iya aengaenigaemi.
JOH 14:27 “Oapoas minne iya nigititiw reemi; ina oapoas na aaei ina iya ngaennegaemi. Niffang na aaei ina esoapw weei niffang na aaen faeinaengiy. Oawsoapw aiuraeg nge oawsoapw mesag.
JOH 14:28 Oawwa rongorong aaei aengaenigaemi pwe, ‘Ipwene noa, nge ipwe sefaaeneto reemi.’ Aere oaw aerhaengiaei nge oawpwe kker iga ipwene noa reen manna Semaei; pwe iiy e taegias saengiaei.
JOH 14:29 Igina iya aengaenigaemi minikkeei weni mmwaen epwe wen, pwe igine epwene wen, iwe nge oawpwe niugiuniug.
JOH 14:30 Esoapw ssiunaei aaei kkepas ngaenigaemi, pwe manewe soamwoonin faeinaengiy epwene itto. Esooar maemaewan wooai,
JOH 14:31 pwe faeinaengiy epwe giuneei pwe ngaang i aerhaengi manna Semaei; ina faaen minne ifeeori oanongan meeta kka e iura pwe ipwe feeori. “Oaw itto, oawsa siusaengi pwiuneoi eei.
JOH 15:1 “Ngaang minne oanongonniuwaen aeggaen grape we, nge manna Semaei minne rhooan foat.
JOH 15:2 E gopiy noa oanongaen rae kka eno wooai ikka esooar uwaan, nge a maeneti ikkina e uwwa pwe epwe towunap wow uwaan.
JOH 15:3 Iwe aaemi oawwa fasiun fin reen fenai kkewe iya aengaenigaemi.
JOH 15:4 Oawpwe no rhag reei nge ngaang ipwe pwan no rhag reemi. Ese mmwen eew rae epwe uwa aere epwe iiy noa rhag; nge epwe uwa aere epparh ngaeni miniwe rhaepin. Epwan ina rhag wusumi pwe oawsoapw uwa igine oaw soano reei.
JOH 15:5 “Ngaang minne grapevine we, iwe nge aaemi raaen. Iyo kka reno reei nge ngaang ino reer, epwe igin towunap uwaar; pwe esooar meeta oawpwe feeori igine i soano reemi.
JOH 15:6 Rhooakka re soanotiw reei nge repwe taeppen raaen irae kka e aekkaerh wow a noa ppwass noa; rae kena ina regaen ioni fengaenniy ra aerheei tae wooan aengaet pwe repwe ppwun noa.
JOH 15:7 Aere oawno reei nge minikka petenaen mwaeniaei eno reemi, ina nge ese tiwegin minne oaw tingoar nge epwe yo ngaenigaemi.
JOH 15:8 Nningen manna Semaei ina epwe pwae noa igine a igin ssow uwaemi; iwe epwe ieei wusun aaemi oawpwene no pwe naeyi rhooan kkayeo.
JOH 15:9 Ngaang i aerhaengigaemi eweei rhag aaen minna Semaei aerhaengiaei; oawno rhag noan aerhaengerhaeng e aaei.
JOH 15:10 Aere oaw tapweei oasoapwosoapw kka aaei oawpwe no rhag noan aaei aerhaengerhaeng, taeppei rhag aaei tapweei rhag aaen manna Semaei oasoapwosoapw iwe iye ino rhag noan aan aerhaengerhaeng.
JOH 15:11 “Iya aengaenigaemi minikkeei pwe epwe kker nee tipaemi, iwe nge kker na aaemi epwe wunus.
JOH 15:12 Ieen minne aaei oasoapwosoapw ngaenigaemi: oaw aerhaengi fengaennigaemi, taeppen rhag aaei aerhaengigaemi.
JOH 15:13 Aerhaengerhaeng na e oarosaen taegias ina oawpwe fang ngaeniir maereyaeremi ina oawpwe fang noa menewaemi pwe faan ngaeniir.
JOH 15:14 Aaemi maereyaerei igine oawfeeori meeta kka i akkiuneogaemi.
JOH 15:15 Isa faingigaemi no pwe slave, pwe slave rese giuneei meeta aar maasta efeeori; iya faingigaemi pwe aaemi maereyaerei, pwe iga iya aengaenigaemi oanongaen minikka i rongorong me reen manna Semaei.
JOH 15:16 Oawse finiaei; ngaang i finigaemi nge iya akkiuneogaemi pwe oawpwe noa pwe epwe gin noa ssow noa uwaemi, taeppen uwa kena esoapw meoyiur noa. Iwe manna Semaei epwe ngaennegaemi ese tiwegin meeta oaw tingoar faaen itaei.
JOH 15:17 Iwe ieen oasoapwosoapw we i aengaenigaemi: oaw aerhaengi fengaennigaemi.
JOH 15:18 “Aere igine faeinaengiy e oapwutaegaemi, nge oawpwe maengiy rhag pwe ngaang minne epwe mwaaen oapwutaeyaei.
JOH 15:19 Aere aaemi naiun faeinaengiy, ina nge faeinaengiy epwe aerhaengigaemi pwe iga aaemi naiun. Nge ngaang i finigaemi me noan faeinaengiy, iwe aaemi soapw naiun faeinaengiy; ina faaen minne faeinaengiy e oapwutaegaemi reen.
JOH 15:20 Oaw maengiy rhag miniwe i aengaenigaemi: ‘Esooar slave ne e taegias saengi aan maasta.’ Aere aeremas re aewwaeiraesiaei iwe ina nge repwe pwan aewwaeiraesigaemi; aere re tapweei fenai kka aaei iwe ina nge repwe pwan tapweei fenai kka aaemi.
JOH 15:21 Repwe feeori ngaenigaemi oanongaen minikkeei pwe iga aaemi naeyi; pwe iga rese giuneei iyo na efangeto ngaang.
JOH 15:22 Aere ise itto mwaenieniy ngaeniir nge ina resoapw monofit; iwe igina esooar no minne repwe rhiuwen tipi ngaeni reen aar monofit.
JOH 15:23 Iyo na e oapwutaeyaei epwan oapwuta manna Semaei.
JOH 15:24 Resoapw monofit aere ise feeori me neeiir meeta kkewe aeremas resaaen feeori mwo; nge igina iga iya feeori nge ra weri meeta kkewe ifeeori, iwe ra oapwutaeyaei noa me manna Semaei.
JOH 15:25 Minneen e fasiun ffeeor to pwe minni epwe pwae noa meeta we e foatofoat noan aar anniug pwe ennet: ‘Ra oapwutaeyaei ne esooar faan.’
JOH 15:26 “Manewe Rhooan Tipaengiaemi ina epwe itto — Espritu ina epwe pwaeritae minikkena e wenewen pwe wunuunun Deus nge iiy e itto me reen manna Semaei. Ipwene fangeto iiy reemi saengi manna Semaei, iwe nge iiy epwe aepesa wunuunuy.
JOH 15:27 Iwe aaemi mwo nge oawpwe aepesa wunuunuy, pwe igiwe oawno reei saengi rhag rhaepetaen.
JOH 16:1 “Iya aengaenigaemi minneei pwe ete ppiung noa aaemi niugiuniug.
JOH 16:2 Repwe asiugaemi wow me noan wutteer Jews, nge epwe noa gona oatona nge rhooakkena re ninnigaemi ina iir repwene niuwaennei pwe ra feeori eew engaang kkena aaen Deus.
JOH 16:3 Aeremas repwe feeori minikkeei pwe iga rese weri manna Semaei aere ngaang.
JOH 16:4 Iwe nge iya fasiun aengaenigaemi minneei, pwe epwe noa itto oatona repwe noa feeori ngaenigaemi iwe nge emaeng ngaenigaemi minikka iya aengaenigaemi. “Ise aengaenigaemi minikkeei rhaepetaen pwe igiwe i rhiuwen no reemi.
JOH 16:5 Iwe nge igina ipwene noa reen iyo na efangeto ngaang, iwe nge erhai mwo me neeimi nge ese aeiineo iya ipwe noa ee.
JOH 16:6 Nge igina iga iya aengaenigaemi, iwe ina oawpwene nee tip cchoaw noa.
JOH 16:7 Nge i aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: pwe efaer mwamwaai igine ipwe nigitigaemi, pwe ngaere ise noa nge manewe Rhooan Tipaengigaemi esoapw itto reemi. Iwe nge ngaere igine inoa, ina nge ipwe noa fangeto reemi.
JOH 16:8 Nge oatonoa epwe noa itto, ina epwe pwaeri ngaeniir aeremesaen faeinaengiy pwe rerug reen wunuunun monofit iwe me wunuunun minikka epwiung iwe me wunuunun aaen apwiung Deus.
JOH 16:9 Rerug reen monofit, pwe iga rese niugiuniug ngaeniaei;
JOH 16:10 rerug reen wunuunun minikka epwiung, pwe iga ngaang ipwene noa reen manna Semaei iwe nge oawsoapw rhiuwen weriaei no;
JOH 16:11 iwe nge rerug reen wunuunun apwiung, pwe iga manna soamwoonin faeinaengiy nge a fasiun no noan aegaeregaer.
JOH 16:12 “E rhiuwen gin towunap minikka ipwe aengaenigaemi, iwe nge ina rhag maeni epwene igin cchoaw pwut ngaenigaemi.
JOH 16:13 Iwe ngaere epwe noa itto Espritu ina nge e pwaeritae minikka e wenewen pwe wunuunun Deus, iwe nge epwe aeiti ngaenigaemi oanongaen minikkena ennet. Soapw mwaenian wooan oanongan minikka epwe aepesa, pwe epwe aepesa meeta kena e rongorong, nge epwan aepesa meeta kka epwan itto.
JOH 16:14 Epwene ngaenneaei nning, pwe epwene pwigi minikka i aepesa iwe nge a itiwow aengaenigaemi.
JOH 16:15 Oanongaen minikka aaen manna Semaei nge aaei; iwe ina faaen minne iura pwe Espritu epwe pwigi meeta i aepesa nge a aengaenigaemi.
JOH 16:16 “A faeiyegius rhag nge oawsoapw weriaei no, nge epwe pwan faeiyegius noa nge oawpwene weriaei.”
JOH 16:17 Aekkaerhai me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra aeiineo fengaen wooar, “Iwe meeta faaen minneei? E iura pwe a faeiyegius rhag nge sisoapw weri no, nge epwe pwan faeiyegius noa nge sa pwene weri; iwe nge epwan iura pwe, ‘Pwe iga ipwene noa reen manna Semaei.’
JOH 16:18 Iwe nge meeta faaen minne, ‘a faeiyegius rhag’? Sise giuneei faaen meeta kka e iukkiura!”
JOH 16:19 Jesus e giuneei meeta kkewe re mwerhaen aeiineow, iwe a aengaeniir pwe, “I aengaenigaemi pwe, ‘A faeiyegius rhag nge oawsoapw weriaei no, nge epwe pwan faeiyegius noa nge oawwa weriaei.’ Ieen miniwe oaw aekkaeyiineo fengaen woami?
JOH 16:20 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: oawpwe saeng nge aenneew noa nee tipaemi, iwe nge faeinaengiy epwene gacch tipan; aaemi oawpwene cchoaw nee tipaemi, iwe nge aaemi nee tip cchoaw epwe ssiuwen ngaeni kker.
JOH 16:21 Igine epwe timenaw erhai rhooapwut, a igin nee tip cchoaw reen aan affayeo; iwe nge oatona enoa supw aetewe a maniuwegi noa aan affayeo pwe a igin kker, pwe a supwuto erhai wonigaet noan faeinaengiy.
JOH 16:22 E ieei pwan wunuunumi: igina oawwa nee tip cchoaw, iwe nge ipwan weri sefaaenigaemi rhag, nge minikkena nee tipaemi epwene pwan igin kker, esooar erhai ne epwe mmwenen pwigi saengigaemi.
JOH 16:23 “Epwe noa itto raaennenaan, esooar minne oawpwe aeiineowaei. Ennetaen, ipwe aengaenigaemi minna wenewenen: manna Semaei epwe ngaennegaemi ese tiwegin meeta oaw aeiineo faaen itaei.
JOH 16:24 Toorito igina, esaaen yor meeta ne oaw tingoar faaen itaei; oaw tingoar nge epwe yo ngaenigaemi, pwe epwe wunus noa aaemi kker.
JOH 16:25 “Iya gaen aengaenigaemi minikkaan noan fioangon awewe. Iwe nge epwe noa itto eew oat ina isoapw rhiuwen fioang awewe ngaenigaemi no, ipwene aeffeta noa aaei kkepas ngaenigaemi reen mmwenen minna Semaei.
JOH 16:26 Epwe noa itto raaennenaan, nge oawpwe tingoar ngaeni faaen itaei; nge ngaang ise iura pwe ipwe tingoar ngaeni reen mmwenemi,
JOH 16:27 pwe iiy mwo manna Semaei nge e aerhaengigaemi. E aerhaengigaemi pwe iga oaw aerhaengiaei, iwe nge oaw niugiuniug pwe ngaang itto me reen Deus.
JOH 16:28 Ngaang itto me reen Deus, iwe iya itto noan faeinaengiy; iwe igina ipwene nigiti faeinaengiy iwe nge iya sefaaen noa reen manna Semaei.”
JOH 16:29 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra aengaeni pwe, “Igina nge a ffat mwaenioamw, inamwo ikka wose aeyae fioangon awewe.
JOH 16:30 Igina aei giuneei pwe wo giuneei oanongaen aegiaeg; esooar ipitaen aar aeremas kkepas aekkaeyiyeg ngaeniug. Reen minneei minne aeiya niugiuniug pwe een wo itto me reen Deus.”
JOH 16:31 Jesus a paniuwaeniir pwe, “Oawwa niugiuniug igina?
JOH 16:32 A itto oatowe iye a no igeei, oatowe erhai me erhai aaemi epwene mwetoar, erhai nge enoa nee pwugusan, nge ngaang oawpwene nigitiaei tiw. Nge esoapw ngaang noa rhag, pwe manna Semaei iye eno reei.
JOH 16:33 Iya aengaenigaemi minneei pwe oawpwe nonoan oapoas reen aaemi rhu ngaeniaei. Faeinaengiy epwe affayeogaemi. Oaw aemenetaegaemi! Pwe ngaang iya appiungiu faeinaengiy!”
JOH 17:1 Weni mwirin aaen Jesus oamoanna noa minneei nge a fannoa naaeng nge a iura pwe, “Semaei, a tooto oatowe. Fang ngaeni mwaaen we Noawumw nningen, pwe aegin mwaaen na Noawumw epwe fang ngaeniug nningen.
JOH 17:2 Pwe een wa ngaenneei mamaaw pwe epwe aeni noa wooar oanongeer aeremas, pwe aegin epwe fang ngaeniir aeremas kena wo ngaenneei menaw na esooar iaenin.
JOH 17:3 Nge wewen menaw na esooar iaenin ina repwe giuneog, pwe een rhag minne oanongonniuwaen Deus, nge repwe pwan giuneei Jesus Kristus iwe wo fangetiw.
JOH 17:4 Iya pwaeri noa nningeomw me wooan feoniufan; nge iya oamoanna noa engaang we wo ngaenneaei.
JOH 17:5 Semaei, igina fang ngaeniaei nningei me faaen mesoamw, taeppen rhag nning we i aeni me reemw weni mmwaen aan ffeeor faeinaengiy.
JOH 17:6 “Iya pwaeri itoamw ngaeniir iyo kkewe wa ngaenneaei me noan faeinaengiy. Iir noawumw, nge wa fangeto reei pwe naeyi. Re tapweei mwaenioamw,
JOH 17:7 iwe igina ra giuneei pwe oanongaen minikkewe wofang ngaeniaei nge e itto me reemw.
JOH 17:8 Iya fang ngaeniir kkepas we wo ngaenneaei, iwe nge iir ra pwigi; ra giuneei pwe ennet pwe ngaang itto me reemw, iwe nge re niugiuniug pwe een minne wo aefengaeyaei to.
JOH 17:9 “Ngaang i maeipinaar. Ngaang ise maeipina faeinaengiy pwe i maeipinaar rhooawe wofang ngaeniaei, pwe iir noawumw.
JOH 17:10 Oanongaen minikka aaei nge oamw, nge oanongaen minikka oamw nge aaei; nge a pwae noa nningei me reer.
JOH 17:11 Iwe igina iya itto reemw; ngaang isoapw nono noan faeinaengiy, iwe nge iir repwe no noan faeinaengiy. Semaei ina e santus, aefaenniir reen kkemenaen minna itoamw, itiwe wo ngaenneaei, pwe aegin pwe repwe eew rhag, taeppen iga een me ngaang si eew rhag.
JOH 17:12 Igiwe ino reer, nge i aemmwenaar faaen kkemenaen minna itoamw, itiwe wo ngaenneaei. I aefaenniir nge erhai mwo me neeiir nge ese mwaenirh noa, pwe aeggaen mwaaen we rhag e fasiun itto pwe epwe mwaenirh noa — pwe epwe nnet noa miniwe noan Pwapwior we e Santus.
JOH 17:13 Iwe igina iya itto reemw, iwe nge i aepesa minikkeei me noan faeinaengiy pwe repwe iseni kker na aaei reer.
JOH 17:14 Iya fang ngaeniir kkepas we oamw, iwe nge faeinaengiy a oapwutaar, pwe iga iir saapw naiun faeinaengiy, taeppen rhag iye saapw ngaang naiun faeinaengiy.
JOH 17:15 Ngaang ise tingoareog pwe wopwe pwigiir wow me noan faeinaengiy, pwe ifaer tingoareog pwe wopwe aefaenniir me reen Man Aenneew we.
JOH 17:16 Taeppen rhag iga ngaang saapw naiun faeinaengiy, iwe iir saapw naiun faeinaengiy.
JOH 17:17 Aeyimweoiiur wow reemw noan wenewen; mwaenioamw nge e wenewen.
JOH 17:18 Iya fang wow iir noan faeinaengiy, taeppen een igiwe wofang to ngaang noan faeinaengiy.
JOH 17:19 Pwonno reer minne iya aeyimweoi wow oanongaei reemw, pwe pwonno iir repwe pwan fang wow oanongeer reemw noan wenewen.
JOH 17:20 “Ngaang ise maeipinaar rhag, pwe ipwan maeipinaar iyo kena re niugiuniug ngaeniaei pwe reen petenaen minikkena mwaenieer.
JOH 17:21 Semaei, i maeipin pwe iir repwe eew rhag, nge iir repwe no reerh, taeppen rhag iga wono reei nge ngaang ino reemw, pwe iir repwe eew rhag, pwe ina nge faeinaengiy epwe niugiuniug pwe een wofang to ngaang.
JOH 17:22 Ngaang iya fang ngaeniir nning we wo ngaenneaei, pwe aegin iir repwe eew, taeppen rhag iga een me ngaang si eew rhag:
JOH 17:23 ngaang ino reer, iwe nge een wono reei, pwe aegin iir repwe oanongonniuwaen eew rhag, pwe aegin faeinaengiy epwe giuneei pwe een minne wofangeto ngaang, iwe een wo aerhaengiir taeppen rhag oamw aerhaengiaei.
JOH 17:24 “Semaei, wa ngaenneaei to iir reei, nge ngaang i mwerhaen repwe no reei iga ino ee, pwe repwe weri minna nningei, nning we wofang ngaeniaei; pwe een wo fasiun aerhaengiaei to rhag me weni mmwan aan epwe feor noa faeinaengiy.
JOH 17:25 Semaei we wo oanongonniuwaen ennet, faeinaengiy ese giuneog, iwe nge ngaang i giuneog, nge rhooa eei re giuneei pwe een minne wofangeto ngaang.
JOH 17:26 Ngaang iya pwaeri itoamw ngaeniir, nge ipwan sessoapwei noa rhag, pwe aegin aerhaengerhaeng na oamw ngaeniaei epwe no reer, ina nge ngaang ipwan no reer.”
JOH 18:1 Weni mwirin aaen Jesus aeni maeipin eei, iwe iiy me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra noa reen rhan pwupwu we Kidron. Eno eew maat pwiuneoi we, iwe Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ra noa ee.
JOH 18:2 Rhooan a fang tinnimae we Judas e giuneei pwiuneoi we, pwe a gin towunap aaen Jesus me rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun renoa rhu me ee.
JOH 18:3 Iwe Judas a noa noan maat we, iiy me cchon sonotaweer Rome kkewe, iwe me aaemweoi poosun Temple we, aefengayeer soamwoonin patere me Pharisees kkewe; re itto fengaen me nimeer me oappwun me tiun.
JOH 18:4 Jesus e fasiun giuneei oanongaen meeta epwene wen ngaeni, iwe a faaeraeg ngaeniir nge a aeiineeor pwe, “Iyo mwu oaw kiukkiutta?”
JOH 18:5 Ra iura pwe, “Jesus re Nazareth.” Nge a iura pwe, “Ngaang ieei.” Rhooan a fang tinnimae we Judas e iugiu reer.
JOH 18:6 Oatowe Jesus e aengaeniir pwe, “Ngaang ieei,” nge ra mer sefaaen iwe ra ppiungtiw wooan ppweon.
JOH 18:7 Jesus a pwan aeiineeor pwe, “Iyo mwu oaw kiukkiutta?” Ra iura pwe, “Jesus re Nazareth.”
JOH 18:8 Jesus a iura pwe, “Iya moannon aengaenigaemi pwe ngaang iiy. Iwe ngaere ngaang minne oaw kiukkiuttayaei, ina nge oawpwe nigitiir noa ikka aaemweoi.” (
JOH 18:9 Jesus e aepesa minneei pwe menaen kkepas we e aengaeniir epwe pwae noa: “Semaei, esooar mwo erhai me neeiir rhooawe wo ngaenneaei ne e mwaenirh saengiaei.”)
JOH 18:10 Simon Peter, iwe e pwigi epeo saeitan, e waeititae rhag a gopiy noa peig mwaaenen saeningaen erhai rhooan akkiuneo kkewe naiun Soamwoonin Patere we. Itaen rhooan akkiuneo we nge Malchus.
JOH 18:11 Jesus a aengaeni Peter pwe, “Iseni noa saeitan mwu noawumw! Wo niuwaennei pwe isoapw iuniumi kkepaen affayeo mwu manna Semaei efang ngaeniaei?”
JOH 18:12 Iwe sonotawaen Rome kkewe me soamwoon kkewe aar fengaen me poos kkewe aar Jews ra torofi Jesus iwe ra geoni noa,
JOH 18:13 iwe ra pwigi noa reen Annas. Iiy minne semaen rhooan ngaenne aaen Caiaphas, iwe iiy minne Soamwoonin Patere noan raegin we.
JOH 18:14 Caiaphas minne e aengaeniir soamwoonin Jews kkewe pwe egacch igine erhai aeremas epwe mae noa faaen iteer rhooa towunap.
JOH 18:15 Simon Peter me erhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe re tettapw noa weni mwirin Jesus. Iiy rhooan kkayeo we erhai iwe e fasiun gin me reen Soamwoonin Patere we, iwe a tapweei noa Jesus niugiun wororaen iimw we imwaen Soamwoonin Patere we,
JOH 18:16 iwe nge Peter iwe e iu rhag reen aesemaen iimw we. Iwe rhooan kkayeo we erhai a sefaaen wow niugiun a noa itiwow kkepas ngaeni rhooapwut we reen wororaen iimw we, iwe a noa paeni nong Peter.
JOH 18:17 Rhooapwut we reen aesemaen iimw we a aengaeni pwe, “Saapw pwan een erhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe rhoaniuwaen mwaaen naan?” Peter a iura pwe, “Aapw, saapw ngaang.”
JOH 18:18 E patapat noan oatowe, iwe rhooan akkiuneo kkewe me poos kkewe ra sonitae eew aengaet iwe ra iu roangoroangei noa pwe re aepwerhikkeraar. Iwe Peter a faaeraeg noa reer iwe a noa aepwerhikkera oanongan.
JOH 18:19 Soamwoonin Patere we a aeiyegiy Jesus wunuunun rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun me fenai kkewe aan.
JOH 18:20 Jesus a iura pwe, “Oanongaen aaei mwaenieniy ngaeniir rhooa towunap; me aaei fenai nge isooaw no rhag noan wutteer Jews kkewe me Temple we, pwiuneoi we oanongeer aeremas regaen itto aemmweoiu ee. Esooar faaen eew ne i mwaenieniy nge i mwaenieniy noan mwoanomwoan.
JOH 18:21 Iwe ina nge meeta faan oawwa aeiineowaei reen? Aeiineeor rhooawe re aiussaening ngaeniaei. Aeiineeor meeta we i aengaeniir — iir re giuneei meeta kkewe i aepesa.”
JOH 18:22 Oatowe Jesus e aepesa minneei, nge erhai me neeiir poos kkewe a pigiri nge a aengaeni pwe, “Meeta e ina wusun oamw kkepas ngaeni man mwu Soamwoonin Patere reen!?”
JOH 18:23 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Aere eyor eew min mwaerhei ne i aepesa nge wa aengaeniir rhooa eei minne iiy. Iwe ngaere epwiung minne i aepesa, iwe nge meeta faaen oamw peosepaeyaei?”
JOH 18:24 Iwe Annas a fangenoa iiy reen Caiaphas Soamwoonin Patere we, nge e rhiuwen geeogeeo noa rhag.
JOH 18:25 Peter iwe e rhiuwen iu igiwe pwe e aepwerhikkera oanongan. Iwe ra aengaeni pwe, “Saapw pwan een erhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun mwaaen naan?” Iwe Peter a iura pwe, “Saapw ngaang.”
JOH 18:26 Erhai me neeiir slave kkewe naiun Soamwoonin Patere we, iwe re pwugusaen mwaaen we Peter e gopiy noa saeningan, a iura pwe, “Pwe ise weriug me reen noan maat we?”
JOH 18:27 Iwe Peter a pwan iura pwe, “Saapw ngaang.” Iwe rhag nge e keokkeok noa maniug we.
JOH 18:28 Nee oatosor moawugowug rhag nge ra pwigi Jesus me reen imwaen Caiaphas iwe ra pwigi noa reen imwaen governor. Soamwooniir re Jew kkewe rese toonong noan imwaen governor, pwe rete nimaenneew noa nge epwe yo aar repwe mwongo mwongoon Passover we.
JOH 18:29 Iwe Pilate a toowow niugiun a itiwow aeiineeor pwe, “Meeta minne oaw oamonofitiy aeremas een wooan?”
JOH 18:30 Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Aeisoapw pwigito reemw igine esooar eew min aenneew ne efeeori.”
JOH 18:31 Pilate a aengaeniir pwe, “Iwe ina nge aaemi oaw pwigi iwe oawwa noa apwiungiu reen aaemi anniug.” Ra paniuwaeni pwe, “Esooar aemaem mamaaw pwe aeipwe niiy noa erhai.” (
JOH 18:32 A wen minneei pwe epwe pwaetae miniwe mwaeniaen Jesus igiwe e aemmetefa wunuunun mae na epwe aeni.)
JOH 18:33 Pilate a sefaaen nong noan iimw we imwan nge a faingi Jesus. A aeiineow pwe, “Een minne aar king re Jews?”
JOH 18:34 Jesus a iura pwe, “Kkepas aeiyeg na e itto me reemw, aere aaemweoi minne re aengaeniug mmwenei?”
JOH 18:35 Pilate a iura pwe, “Wo niuwaennei pwe ngaang erhai re Jew? Sipegin noawumw aeremas me soamwoonin patere kkomwun minikkomwu re pwigiug to reei. Meeta wa feeori?”
JOH 18:36 Jesus a iura pwe, “Minna Mweoiuy ina ese itto me reen faeinaengiy; pwe ngaere minna Mweoiuy e itto me reen faeinaengiy, nge rhooakkena rhoaniuwaei repwe moawun faaen itaei pwe ete mmwenen aar iseniaei nong noan paiiur soamwoonin Jews. Aapw, minna Mweoiuy ese no igeei!”
JOH 18:37 Iwe Pilate a aeiineow pwe, “Iwe een erhai king?” Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Een minne wo iura pwe ngaang erhai king. Faaen aaei supw me aaei noa itto noan faeinaengiy ina faaen ngaeni rhag eew aegiaeg, ipwe itto aepesa minna wenewen. Ese tiwegin iyo na e tipaeni wenewen, nge epwe rongorong ngaeniaei.”
JOH 18:38 Pilate a aeiineow pwe, “Iwe meeta minna wenewen?” Pilate a sefaaen wow reer rhooawe niugiun nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Esooar meeta iweri pwe teren mwaaen een.”
JOH 18:39 Nge eew kkomi, iwe ngaang igaen fasiun aessaenetaegiy erhai rhooan kanepwus noan gupwunon Passover. Oaw mwerhaen ipwe saeneti ngaenigaemi mane aar king Jews?”
JOH 18:40 Ra paniuwaeni reen aar aekkepwas tae, “Aapw, saapw iiy! Aei tipaeni Barabbas!” (Barabbas iwe erhai rhooa mwoarho.)
JOH 19:1 Iwe Pilate a pwigi noa Jesus ra noa woawuti.
JOH 19:2 Sonotaw ra fiti eew mwaer saengi irae towfanfan nge ra ngaettae wooan rhimwen; iwe ra pwigi eew mengaag siungiurhoan enaenaei pwe mengaagiun
JOH 19:3 nge ra itto reen nge ra iura pwe, “Sirow woamw, Kingaen Jews!” Nge regaen faaeraeg ngaeni nge re pigiri sepan.
JOH 19:4 Pilate a pwan sefaaen nge a pwan aengaeni pwuwa we pwe, “Oaw pipiiy, ipwene paeni wow reemi pwe oawpwe weri pwe ngaang esooar meeta ne iweri pwe teren mwaaen een.”
JOH 19:5 Iwe Jesus a toowow nasam nge e mwaermwaer irae towfanfan we nge e memmengaag mengaag siungiurhoan enaenaei we. Pilate a aengaeniir pwe, “Ieen iiy mwaaen we!”
JOH 19:6 Oatowe soamwooniir patere kkewe me soamwoonin Temple we reweri nge ra aepwesaegini pwe, “Kurusuw noa! Kurusuw noa!” Pilate a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw pwigi aaemi pwe oawpwe noa kurusuw noa. Ngaang esooar minne iweri pwe teren mwaaen een.”
JOH 19:7 Pwuwa we a pwan paniuwaeni pwe, “Eyor aemaem oasoapwosoapw nge e iura pwe epwe mae, pwe iga e iura pwe iiy Naiun Deus.”
JOH 19:8 Oatowe Pilate a rongorong miniwe, a kkaein noa aan mesag.
JOH 19:9 A pwan sefaaen nong noan iimw we imwan a pwan aeiineow Jesus pwe, “Wo itto me iya?” Jesus ese paniuwaeni.
JOH 19:10 Pilate a aengaeni pwe, “Wose mwerhaen mwaenieniy ngaeniaei? Maengiy pwe ngaang minne eyor maemaewaei pwe ipwe saenetiug noa aere ipwe kurusug noa.”
JOH 19:11 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Eyor rhag maemaewoamw wooai pwe iga Deus e ngaenneog. Ina minne aeremas we efang noa menewaei ngaeniug ina epwe igin temoag monofit na aan.”
JOH 19:12 Igiwe Pilate a rongorong miniwe, a giutta epwe ifa wusun aan saeneti noa Jesus. Iwe nge pwuwa we a pwan aekkepwas aegini pwe, “Aere igine wo saeneti noa nge saapw een maereyaeren Soamwoonin Rome we! Erhai ne e iura pwe iiy king nge ina nge a appaniuwaeni minna soamwoonin Rome!”
JOH 19:13 Igiwe Pilate a rongorong petenaen kkepas kkewe iwe a paeni wow Jesus nasam iwe a mooat tiw wooan miniwe nenien soaw apwiung iwe regaen iura pwe “Taeyif”. (Iwe nge noan kkepesaen Hebrew nge “Gabbatha”.)
JOH 19:14 A aerepa nugunupaen oanowas noan raaenin we weni mmwaen Passover. Pilate a aengaeniir aeremas kkewe pwe, “Ieen iiy king we naimi!”
JOH 19:15 Nge iir ra aekkepwas pwe, “Niiy noa! Niiy noa! Kurusuw noa!” Pilate a aeiineeor pwe, “Oaw mwerhaen ipwe kurusuw noa king e aaemi?” Soamwooniir patere kkewe ra iura pwe, “Esooar aemaem king pwe Soamwoonin Rome rhag!”
JOH 19:16 Iwe Pilate a ateeow nong Jesus noan paiiur pwe repwene noa kurus noa. Iwe rhooawe ra pwigi noa Jesus.
JOH 19:17 E itiwow a aiufera kurus we aan a itto reen eew pwiuneoi itan “Nenien Peopeoi rhimw”. (Noan Hebrew nge “Golgotha”.)
JOH 19:18 Pwiuneoi we ra kurus noa me ee; nge repwan kurusuur noa riiurhai mwaaen, erhai iir nge eno me epeig, iwe nge Jesus eno nepeteer.
JOH 19:19 Pilate a foatogi eew pwapwior nge a iseni tae wooan kurus we. E iura pwe, “Jesus aaen Nazareth, iiy minne Kingaen Jews.”
JOH 19:20 Re igin towunap rhooan aeraegi pwapwior we, pwe iga pwiuneoi we Jesus e kurus noa me ee nge ese taaw saengi aepinoamw. Pwapwior we nge e foatofoat noa Hebrew, Latin me Greek.
JOH 19:21 Man kkewe soamwooniir patere ra aengaeni Pilate pwe, “Wosoapw foatogi pwe ‘king reer Jews’, pwe wopwe faer foatogi pwe ‘Mwaaen een e iura pwe, Ngaang minne king reer Jews.’ ”
JOH 19:22 Pilate a aengaeniir pwe, “Minne iya foatogi nge ina minna epwe foat.”
JOH 19:23 Weni mwirin aar sonotaw kkewe kurusuw noa Jesus, ra pwigi minikkewe mengaagiun iwe ra itto giniiy wooar faaen faawu, erhai sonotaw nge epeo. Ra pwan pwigi mengaag enaenaei we, iwe effeeor saengi epeo mengaag nge esooar oarhurhun teteen.
JOH 19:24 Sonotaw kkewe ra iura fengaenniy pwe, “Sisoapw fereei; sipwe aekkaerh dice iyo ne epwe pwigi.” A wen minneei pwe epwe nnet miniwe Pwapwior we e Santus, iwe e iura pwe: “Re inetiy minikka mengaagiuy wooar nge re aekkaerh dice reen mengaag enaenaei we mengaagiuy.” Iwe nge ina miniwe sonotaw kkewe refeeori.
JOH 19:25 Rhooakka re igin iu arap ngaeni miniwe kurusun Jesus, nge manewe inan, manewe pwiin inan, Maria we pwiuniuwaen Clopas, me Maria Magdalene.
JOH 19:26 Jesus a weri miniwe inan me rhooan kkayeo we naiun iwe e igin aerhaengi pwe re iu; a aengaeni miniwe inan pwe, “Ina iiy mwaaen we noawumw.”
JOH 19:27 Iwe nge a aengaeni rhooan kkayeo we pwe, “Ina iiy minimwu inoamw.” Iwe saengi oatowe a noa, rhooan kkayeo we a pwigi niewe pwe epwe noa no reen noan iimw we imwan.
JOH 19:28 Jesus a giuneei pwe oanongaen meeta nge a moann; pwe epwe nnet miniwe eno noan Pwapwior we e Santus, nge a iura pwe, “Ngaang iya moar.”
JOH 19:29 Eew saepiy eno pwiuneoi we ne e sseogiun wine kkewe emwaenn; ra rhirinong eew faerewa noan, ra ngaettae wooan efoarh raaen hyssop, ra seigi tae reen ewan.
JOH 19:30 Jesus a iuniumi wine we nge a iura pwe, “A moann!” Jesus a aiuneorhimw tiw rhag nge a fangetae ngeoniun.
JOH 19:31 Iwe man kkewe soamwooniir Jews ra tingoareei Pilate pwe epwe fang ngaeniir pwe repwe gopiy pirheer mwaaen kkewe re kurusuur noa, iwe me repwe aetiweer tiw me wooan kurus kkewe. Re tingoar miniwe pwe igiwe a aenimowu, nge rese mwerhaen pwe rhooa kkewe repwe no rhag wooan kurus wooan Sabbath, pwe igiwe Sabbath we epwe itto nge e igin ssoar.
