JOH 19:32 Iwe sonotaw kkewe ra noa gopiy pirheen mwaaen we erhai, iwe me pwan iwe erhai, iwe re kurusuur noa reen Jesus.
JOH 19:33 Nge igiwe re itto reen Jesus, ra weri pwe a fasiun mae, iwe resa gopiy no pirheen.
JOH 19:34 Iwe nge erhai me neeiir sonotaw kkewe a pwigi wopwaei we a towuuw ngaeni wenepeigin Jesus, iwe a pwupwu noa ccha me rhaan. (
JOH 19:35 Aeremas na eweri minneei a fioangei fetaeneei pwe oawpwe niugiuniug. Miniwe e aepesa nge e wenewen, nge iiy e giuneei pwe e aepesa minna e wenewen.)
JOH 19:36 A wen minneei pwe epwe nnet miniwe noan Pwapwior we e Santus, iwe e iura pwe, “Eew mwo rhiun nge resoapw gopiy.”
JOH 19:37 Nge epwan yor eew miniwe noan Pwapwior we e Santus iwe e iura pwe, “Aeremas ra oawruru mwaaen we re towuuw.”
JOH 19:38 Mwirin minneei nge Joseph, erhai re Arimathea, a aeiineow Pilate aere epwe mmwenen pwigi miniwe oanongaen Jesus. (Joseph iwe erhai naiun Jesus rhooan kkayeo, nge ese aekkefaet fetaen, pwe e mesagiiur soamwoon kkewe aar Jews.) Pilate a aengaeni pwe epwe mmwenen pwigi oanong we. Iwe Joseph a noa pwigi oanong we.
JOH 19:39 Nicodemus, iwe egommwaei noa sengaeri Jesus nee pwoong, a tapweei noa Joseph iwe nge e pwigi epwiugiuw poawunon waningas tonaaen myrrh me aloes pwe angesan.
JOH 19:40 Iwe mwaaen kkewe riiurhai ra pwigi oanong we, iwe ra tiugiumi noa noan mengaag pwerhepwerh fengaen me waningas kkewe, e tapweei wunuunun kkoor Jews reen aar nipwaenipw.
JOH 19:41 Yor eew maat pwiuneoi we re kurusuw Jesus me ee, iwe nge eno paeyi ffeo esaaen yor mwo mane e nipwaeni nong noan.
JOH 19:42 Ra iseni nong rhag miniwe oanongaen Jesus igiwe pwonno igiwe a eraaen rhag me weni mmwaen Sabbath, iwe me igiwe paeyi we e arap.
JOH 20:1 Nee oatosoraei Sunday, igiwe e rhiuwen pwoong, nge Maria Magdalene a noa reen paeyi we, iwe nge a noa weri pwe fai we tittin aesemaen paeyi we a mwagiut saengi miniwe nenien.
JOH 20:2 A fattapw noa reen Simon Peter me rhooan kkayeo we erhai, mwaaen we Jesus e igin aerhaengi, nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Ra pwigi noa Soamwoon me noan paeyi we, nge aeise giuneei igine ra pwigi noa ee!”
JOH 20:3 Iwe Peter me rhooan kkayeo we erhai ra noa reen paeyi we.
JOH 20:4 Iir me riiurhai nge re fattapw ppag noa, nge rhooan kkayeo we erhai enang me mmwaen Peter, iwe a gommwonoa gona paeyi we.
JOH 20:5 A pwoar tiw iwe a weri mengaag pwerhepwerh kkewe, iwe nge ese teogach nong noan paeyi we.
JOH 20:6 Simon Peter epwan mwiriy to, e itto rhag itto teeo foar nong noan paeyi we. A weri mengaag pwerhepwerh kkewe pwe ewon
JOH 20:7 fengaen me mengaag we geeogeeon rhimwen Jesus. Ese rhunong neeiin mengaag kkewe aaemweoi pwe iiy e oawunnu noa rhag.
JOH 20:8 Nge iwe rhooan kkayeo we erhai, iwe egommwaen gonoa paeyi we, iiy a pwan toonong; a weri iwe a niugiuniug. (
JOH 20:9 Resaaen metefaaegini mwo reen miniwe eno noan Pwapwior we e Santus iwe e iura pwe iiy epwe menaw saengi mae noa.)
JOH 20:10 Iwe rhag nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra pwan sefaaen noa nee pwuguseer.
JOH 20:11 Maria e rhiuwen iu saeng niugiun paeyi we. Igiwe e rhiuwen sessaeng, a pwoar tiw pwe a fan nong noan paeyi we
JOH 20:12 iwe a weriir riiurhai angkenus re mengaag pwerh ffat noa rhag, remooat igiwe eno miniwe oanongaen Jesus ee, erhai emooat reen rhimwen nge erhai reen pirheen.
JOH 20:13 Ra aeiineow pwe, “Rhooapwut mwuun, meeta wosaeng reen?” A paniuwaeniir pwe, “Ra pwigi noa aaei Soamwoon nge ise giuneei igine ra pwigi noa ee!”
JOH 20:14 Enoa toagun sefaaen nge a weri Jesus pwe e iu igiwe; nge ese giuneei pwe Jesus.
JOH 20:15 Jesus a aeiineow pwe, “Rhooapwut mwuun, meeta wosaeng reen? Iyo mwu wo kiukkiutta?” Niewe e niuwaennei pwe rhooan maat we, iwe a aengaeni pwe, “Menap, ngaere wa pwigi noa iwe nge wopwe aengaeniaei igine wonoa iseni noa ee, pwe ipwe noa iya noa pwigi.”
JOH 20:16 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Maria!” Niewe a toagun ngaeni nge a iura noan kkepesaen Hebrew pwe “Rabboni!” (Faan nge “Sinsei”.)
JOH 20:17 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Wosoapw kkemwarh tae wooai, pwe ngaang isaaen ittae mwo reen miniwe Semaei. Iwe nge wopwe sefaaen noa reer rhooawe pwiiy nge wa aengaeniir pwe ngaang ipwene sefaaen noa reen miniwe Semaei me Semeer, aaei Deus me aar Deus.”
JOH 20:18 Maria Magdalene a noa aengaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe pwe a weri Soamwoon, nge a pwan aengaeniir meeta we Soamwoon e aengaeni.
JOH 20:19 A nee oatofaaef noan iiy Sunday we, nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra mweoiu fengaen, iwe ra noakkei noa asam pwe igiwe re mesagiiur Soamwoonin Jews kkewe. Jesus a itto iunoa neeiir, nge a iura pwe, “Oapoas epwe no reemi.”
JOH 20:20 Mwirin aan aepesa minneei nge a pwaeri ngaeniir noan paiun me miniwe wenepeigin. Rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra igin kker tae igiwe ra weri Soamwoon.
JOH 20:21 Jesus a pwan aengaeniir pwe, “Oapoas epwe no reemi. Taeppen Semaei a fangeto ngaang, iwe ngaang iya fangenoa aaemi.”
JOH 20:22 Iwe Jesus a nngastiw wooar iwe nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Epwe no Espritu Santus woami.
JOH 20:23 Aere oaw saeneti monofitiir aeremas nge epwe saenetaeg; nge aere oawse saeneti nge esoapw saenetaeg.”
JOH 20:24 Erhai me neeiir rhooa kkayeo kkewe seig me riiurhai itan Thomas (iwe regaen iura Nippwei), e soano reer reen oatowe Jesus e itto.
JOH 20:25 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe aaemweoi ra aengaeni pwe, “Aeiya weri Soamwoon!” Thomas aengaeniir pwe, “Aekkaen igine iweri nepeyin kinesaen chiufan kkewe noan paiun nge iya aeitinong aiuttiuy noan ginesaen paiun me tugunong noan ginas we wenepeigin, iwe nge ipwe naaen niugiuniug.”
JOH 20:26 Enoa eew week me mwirin, rhooan kkayeo kkewe ra pwan rhu fengaen me nee iimw, iwe nge Thomas a no reer. Asam kkewe nge e noak, iwe nge Jesus e itto a itto iunoa neeiir nge a aengaeniir pwe, “Oapoas epwe no reemi.”
JOH 20:27 Nge a aengaeni Thomas pwe, “Aeiti nong aiuttiumw iga, iwe wa pipiiy minikka paeyi; iwe nge wa aeitito poawumw pwe wopwe tugunong noan minne wenepeigi. Wone iugiu noa mwo me oamw se niugiuniug, iwe wone niugiuniug!”
JOH 20:28 Thomas a paniuwaeni pwe, “Aaei Soamwoon nge aaei Deus!”
JOH 20:29 Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Wo niugiuniug rhag iga woweriaei? Ifa mwo aar kker rhooakka re niugiuniug nge rese weriaei!”
JOH 20:30 Egin towunap kkeman kka Jesus a feeori weni mmweer rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun ikka ese foat noan pwapwior eei.
JOH 20:31 Iwe nge ikkeei a foatotiw pwe aegin pwe oawpwe niugiuniug pwe Jesus minne Kristus, Naiun Deus, iwe nge noan aaemi niugiuniug ngaeni oawpwe weri menaw.
JOH 21:1 Weni mwirin minneei nge Jesus a pwan pwae ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun reen meoneoiniun we Tiberias. E ieen wusun aan pwae ngaeniir.
JOH 21:2 Simon Peter, Thomas (iwe regaen iura pwe Nippwei), Nathanael (erhai re Cana me noan Galilee), mwaaen kkewe naiun Zebedee, iwe me riiurhai rhooan kkayeo kkewe naiun Jesus re sseoiu fengaen.
JOH 21:3 Simon Peter a aengaeniir ikkiwe aaemweoi pwe, “Ipwene noa fita.” Rhooa kkewe ra aengaeni pwe, “Aemaem aeipwe tapweog.” Iwe ra noa wooan eew pwoot, nono e nee oatosor noa nge erhai mwo iig nge rese nipaeni.
JOH 21:4 Enoa taetae aenet, nge Jesus a iu ngaerhen nooamw we, nge rhooan kkayeo kkewe rese aeginna pwe Jesus.
JOH 21:5 Iwe a aeiineeor pwe, “Mwaaen kkomwun, eyor minne oaw nipaeni?” Ra iura pwe, “Ese erhai mwo.”
JOH 21:6 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Aerheitiw wuug mwu naimi me peig mwaaenen pwoot na, nge ina nge oawpwe nipaeni aekkaerhai.” Iwe ra aerheitiw wuug we wenepeigin pwoot we, nge resa mmwenen taiuw no, pwe a sseog noa reen iig.
JOH 21:7 Iwe nge rhooan kkayeo we Jesus egin aerhaengi a aengaeni Peter pwe, “Soamwoon minna!” Igiwe Peter e rongorong pwe Soamwoon miniwe nge e geonitae rhag minikkewe mengaagiun wooan (pwe iwe e aetiwa noa mwo) iwe nge ennus noa nee set.
JOH 21:8 Rhooan kkayeo kkewe aaemweoi ra itto mwoarhoisaet rhiun pwoot we, ra pwan tettaiuw nong wuug we pwe iwe a sseog noa reen iig. Rhooawe rese pwan taaw saengi faniuw, maeni epwe epwiugiuw iyaach taaw noar.
JOH 21:9 Renoa tiw tae mwoarhoisaet, ra weri aengaet we eyor iig me fenoawa wooan.
JOH 21:10 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw pwigito fitiman iig kkomwu oawnaen nipaeni.”
JOH 21:11 Simon Peter a itiwow wooan pwoot we, a noa taiuw nong wuug we a sseogiun iig tettemoag, ina epwiugiuw nimeig me eoniurhai nepan; inamwo igiwe a igin sseog nge ese ffeir wuug we.
JOH 21:12 Jesus a aengaeniir pwe, “Oaw itto mwongo.” Erhai mwo me neeiir rhooan kkayeo kkewe nge ese mmwen pwe repwe aeiineow pwe, “Een iyo?” pwe igiwe re giuneei pwe Soamwoon miniwe.
JOH 21:13 Jesus a faaeraeg noa, a noa pwigi fenoawa we nge a ngaenneer; a pwan ngaenneer iig kkewe.
JOH 21:14 Iwe a ieei aeinuwaen aaen Jesus pwae ngaeniir rhooan kkayeo kkewe weni mwirin aan menaw tae.
JOH 21:15 Weni mwirin aar moannon mwongo, Jesus a aengaeni Simon Peter pwe, “Simon mwu naiun John, aerhaengerhaeng mwu oamw ngaeniaei, e temoag saengi aar rhooa kkomwu aaemweoi aerhaengiaei?” A paniuwaeni pwe, “Ooa Soamwoon, een wo giuneei pwe ngaang i aerhaengiug.” Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Aemmwenaar naeyi sheep.”
JOH 21:16 Oaruwowwan Jesus a pwan aengaeni pwe, “Simon mwu naiun John, wo aerhaengiaei?” A paniuwaeni pwe, “Ooa Soamwoon, wo giuneei pwe i aerhaengiug.” Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Aefaenniir sheep kka naeyi.”
JOH 21:17 Aeinuwan Jesus a pwan aeiineow, “Simon naiun John, wo aerhaengiaei?” A aenneew nee tipaen Peter pwe igiwe a faaen enuuw aaen Jesus aeiineow pwe, “Wo aerhaengiaei?” Iwe a aengaeni pwe, “Soamwoon, wo giuneei oanongaen meeta, wo giuneei pwe i aerhaengiug!” Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Aemmwenaar sheep kka naeyi.
JOH 21:18 Ennetaen, ipwe aengaeniug minna wenewenen: oatowe wo rhiuwen anian, wopwe memmengaag tae rhag nge wonoa ese tiwegin igine wopwe noa ee; nge iga wa tugufaeyi, ina wopwe aeiti wow poawumw nge erhai a geoniug noa a wummwug noa igina wose mwerhaen wopwe noa ee.”
JOH 21:19 (Jesus e aepesa minneei, pwe e aeffeta noa epwe ifa wusun aaen Peter epwe mae nge epwe fang ngaeni Deus minna nningen.) Iwe nge Jesus a aengaeni pwe, “Tapweto mwiriy!”
JOH 21:20 Peter e toagun sefaaen mwirin nge a weri rhooan kkayeo we erhai iwe Jesus e igin aerhaengi — iwe e aeppwaenaeg ngaeni Jesus nupwaen aar mwongoon faaef nge a aeiineow pwe, “Soamwoon, iyo epwene fangenoa tinnimaem?”
JOH 21:21 Igiwe Peter eweri, iwe a aeiineow Jesus pwe, “Soamwoon, nge e ifa wusun mwaaen een?”
JOH 21:22 Jesus a paniuwaeni pwe, “Ngaere i mwerhaen pwe epwe no toori aaei noa sefaaeneto, nge pwan meeta faan ngaeniug? Een tapweto mwiriy!”
JOH 21:23 Iwe a teeo fetaen kkepas neeiir rhooawe rhoaniuwaen Jesus pwe rhooan kkayeo we nge esoapw mae noa. Nge Jesus ese iura pwe esoapw mae; pwe e iura pwe, “Ngaere i mwerhaen pwe epwe no toori aaei noa sefaaeneto, nge pwan meeta faan ngaeniug?”
JOH 21:24 Iiy rhooan kkayeo we minne e aepesa minikkeei, iiy minne e foatogin tiw; iwe nge si giuneei pwe minikka e aepesa nge ikka e wenewen.
JOH 21:25 Iwe nge epwan igin ssow aekkaew minikka Jesus epwan feeori. Iwe ngaere igine oanongan nge foatofoatotiw, iwe nge maeni faeinaengiy mwo nge esoapw faer iiy pwapwior kenaan noan.
